VNṬ_1,1–1,3^1^1	namaḥ vighghna pramathanāya nānā sat guṇa ratna rāśi kiraṇa dhvasta andhakāra ssadā yaḥ nānāvidha sattva vāṃchita phala prāpti artha m atti udyataḥ tad niḥśeṣa jagat hita udaya parannatu a āri amañju śriyam vāda nyāya vibhāgaḥ eṣa vimalaḥ saṅkṣiptaḥ ārabhyate yad prayojana rahitam tat prekṣā pūrvva kāribhiḥ nna ārabhyate yathā bali tvac darśana viniścaya ādikam aprayojanañca idam prakaraṇam iti āśaṃkāvataḥ tadāśaṃkā parijihīrṣayā prayojana pradarśanāya nyāya vādinam ityādi vākyam upanyastavān katham punar anena vākyena asya prayojanam upadarśyate iti āstāṃtāvat etat 
VNṬ_1,1–1,3^1^2	 arthaḥ tu vyākhyāyate nyāyaḥ trirūpa liṅga lakṣaṇā yuktiḥ nīyate prāpyate vivakṣita artha siddhiḥ anena iti kṛttvā atas eva trividham liṅgam ityādinā trirūpam eva liṅgam anantaram vakṣyati tad abhidhāyi vacanam iti apare tamvaditum śīlam yasya sa tathā uktaḥ tam api nigṛhṇanti parājayante iti arthaḥ nigṛhṇantu nāma anyāya vādi namparājaya adhikaraṇat tvāt eva nyāya vādi nantu anigraha arham api yat nigṛhṇanti etat na sambhāvyate para utkarṣa vyāra upadhiyaḥ tu tam api parājayante iti sambhāvanāyām api śabdaḥ samuccaya arthaḥ atiśayat yotana arthaḥ vā keṣu 
VNṬ_1,3^2	 nigṛhṇanti iti āha vādeṣu sādhana dūṣaṇa saṃśabditeṣu vicāreṣu iti yāvat vivādeṣu itikvacid pāṭhaḥ tatra viruddhā vādāḥ vivādā steṣu iti vyākhyeyam virudvāḥ ca katham sādhana dūṣaṇa saṃśabditānām vicārāṇa an ta d vi ruddha artha sādhana pravṛttattvāt kathampunar nyāya vādinam asatsu asiddhi ādiṣu hetu doṣeṣu nigṛhṇantī tyāha asat vyayavastha upanyāsaiḥ asatām asādhūnām vyavasthāḥ asatyaḥ vā vyavasthāḥ sadbhiḥ kutsi tattvāt tāḥ ca phala jāti a sannigraha sthāna lakṣa ṇāstāsām upanyāsāḥ prayogaḥ taiḥ iti vigrahaḥ ke punar ahrīkāḥ te evam vidhāḥ iti āha śaṭhāḥ dhūrtāḥ māyāvinaḥ para sampattau= īrṣyā lavaḥ iti yāvat yasmāt tam tathā nigṛhṇanti iti tasmāt tad niṣedha artham teṣām śaṭhāna anteṣām vā asat vyavasthā upanyāsānāntasya vā nigrahasya trayāṇām vā niṣedhaḥ nirāsaḥ tad arthan tad nimittam idam prakaraṇam ārabhyate saḥ e vā arthaḥ asya iti vigrahītavyam 
VNṬ_1,3^3	 tad niṣedhe ca kṛte samyak vicāraḥ pravartate tad pūrvakaḥ ca sarvaḥ puruṣa arthaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ āsanna viṣayiṇā tu antar viparivartti prakaraṇam idam āparām ṛṣati antar tantu ātmanā pariniṣpanna tvāt anyathā apariniṣpanna ātmatayā asanna tva abhāvāt idam śabda prayogaḥ na syāt ārabhyate iti vartamāna kāla nirdeśaḥ katham iti ced vartamāna sāmīpye vartamāna vat ve ti vacanāt sambandhaḥ api abhidhānīyaḥ eva anyathā bāla unmatta pralāpa vat agrāhyam idam prekṣā pūrva kāriṇām bhavet iti ced sattyam etat prayojana antarga tattvāt pṛtha ga sau na abhihitaḥ tathā hi tat niṣedha artham idam ārabhyate tatas ca etad prayojanam anena prakaraṇena sādhyate tathā ca prayojana prakaraṇayoḥ sādhya sādhana lakṣaṇaḥ sambandhaḥ iti sūcitam ye tu anye kriyā nantarī ādi lakṣaṇāḥ sambandhāḥ te na vācyāḥ eva prakaraṇa kriyāyām anaṅga bhū tattvāt 
VNṬ_1,3^4	 tathā hi teṣu satsu api prayojana abhāve na ārabhyate eva prakaraṇam asatsu api ca teṣu sati prayojane prārabhyatas eva tasmāt prakaraṇa ārambhasya prayojana anvaya vyatireka anuvidhānāt prayojanam eva abhidhānīyam prekṣā pūrva kāriṇā tasmin= ca abhihite sambandha upyuktaḥ eva bhavati iti manyate na anavadhārita prakaraṇa śarīrāḥ pravartante prekṣāvantaḥ tasmāt prayojana vat pravṛtti aṅga tvāt prakaraṇa śarīram api vaktvyam eva iti ced evam etat prayojana vākyena tu abhihita tvāt na eva tat api sambandha vat pṛthak abhidhānam arhati yatas tat niṣedha artham idam ārabhyate iti uktam atas ca tatniṣe dhas asya śarīram iti uktam bhavati yadā ca etat niṣedha artham idam ārabhyate tadā pūrvakaḥ hetuḥ asiddhaḥ pratipramāṇa dvayañca anena sūcitam prārabdha vyamidamprakaraṇam prekṣā avatāsati sāmarthye grāhyam vā prayojanava tvāt sambandhava tvāt ca tad anya śāstra vat iti svabhāva hetuḥ 
VNṬ_3,1^1	 evam abhidhāya prayojanam sakala prakaraṇa artha saṃgrāhakam śloka māhaa sādhana aṅvacanam ityādinā asādhana aṅga vacanam adoṣa udbhāva nañca dvayoḥ vādi prativādi noḥ yathākramam nigraha sthānam parājaya adhikaraṇam anyat tu iti etat heya vyatiriktam akṣapāt apa rikalpitam pratijñā saṃnyāsa ādikam vakṣyamāṇam nigraha sthānam na yuktam iti kṛtvā na iṣyate nigraha sthānam iti varttate ayam tāvat samāsena śloka arthaḥ iṣṭasya ityādinā vibhāgam ārabhate iṣṭaḥ arthaḥ anittyaḥ śabdaḥ ityādi sādhyat tvena īpsitaḥ tasya siddhiḥ pratipattiḥ sādhanam tat anena bhāvasya sādhanoyam sādhana śabdaḥ tāvat asmin vyākhyāne abhipretaḥ na tu karaṇa sādhanaḥ iti darśayati tasya sādhanasya iṣṭa artha siddhi lakṣaṇam asya aṅgam kintat iti āha nirvartta kaṃjanakam anena aṅga śabdam vyācaṣṭe 
VNṬ_3,1^2	 kāraṇa paryāyoyam atra aṅga śabdaḥ na avayava paryāyaḥ iti arthaḥ tat ca sādhana aṅgam iha niścita trairūpyam liṅgam ucyate asya sādhana aṅgasya vacanam trirūpa liṅga ākhyānam tasya sādhana aṅgasya avacanam anuccāraṇam anabhidhānam yat tat asādhana aṅga vacanam anena etat kathayati asādhana aṅgasya pakṣa upanayana ādeḥ vacanam asādhana aṅga vacanam iti nai va pratipattavyam asmin vyākhyāne kintu sādhana aṅgasya eva avacanam asādhana aṅga vacanam iti tat asādhana aṅga vacanam vādinaḥ nigraha sthānam tat etena ślokasya pūrvva bhāgam vivṛṇoti kathampunar sādhana aṅgasya anuccāraṇam bhavati nigraha sthānam ca iti āha tat abhyupagamya iti tat iti iṣṭam sādhyam abhyupagamya aham etat sādhayāmi iti pratijñayā pratibhayā karaṇa bhūtayā tūṣṇīm bhāvāt apratibhā atra pūrvva adhi gata artha vismaraṇam stambhi tattvañca gṛhyate 
VNṬ_3,2	 anena sarvu athā sādhana aṅgasya āvacanam āha abhidhāne vā yadi na samarthitam tadā uktam api aanūktam eva sva kārya akaraṇāt iti abhiprāyavān āha sādhana aṅgasya asamarthanāt vā iti tat abhyupagamya itivartate vā śabdaḥ purvvā apekṣayā vikalpa arthaḥ sādhana aṅgasya asamarthanam triṣu api rūpeṣu niścaya apradarśanam tasmāt tūṣṇīmbhāvāt asamarthanāt ca sādhana aṅgasya anuccāraṇam tatas ca pratijñāta artha akāraṇāt vādinaḥ nigraha adhikaraṇa miti prakṛtena sambandhaḥ kvacid tu vādinā eti pāṭhaḥ tatra tad śabdena prakṛtam anuccāraṇam saṃbadhyate 
VNṬ_3,3^1	 kathampunar sādhana aṅga asamarthanambhavati yena tad viparyayena asamarthanāt pratijñāta artha akāraṇāt vādinaḥ nigraha adhikaraṇattvam iti kadācid kaścid brūyāt iti etat parijihīrṣuḥ ādi prasthānam āracayati trividham eva ityādinā tri prakāram eva liṅgam aṅgaṅkaraṇam kasya asiddheḥ pratipatti rūpāyāḥ kasya siddheḥ iti āha apratyakṣasyā parokṣasya anumeya bhūtasya vastunaḥ iti yāvat avadhāraṇañcaturādi vyavacchedam ācaṣṭe trividham eva iti niyamaḥ katham ayam iti ced yasmāt vidhi pratiṣedha rūpa tayā dvidhā sādhyam vyavasthitam vidhiḥ ūpañca sadbhā varūpaṅkāraṇa rū pamvā bhavat bhavet na anyat tatra hetoḥ pratibandha ayogāt na hi artha antarasya akāryasya sadbhāve aparasya sadbhāvaḥ yuktaḥ paṭa sadbhāvaḥ iva uṣṭrasya na api arthāṃtarasya akāraṇasya nivṛttau= akāryasya anyasya ca nivṛttiḥ yuktimatī uṣṭre nivṛttau= iva paṭasya 
VNṬ_3,3^2	 na ca anvaya vyatireka vikalasya āgamakattvam yuktam paṭasya api uṣṭra gama kattva prasaṅgāt svabhāva bhūta dharma sadbhāve tu svabhāva bhūtasya anyasya sadbhāvaḥ yuktaḥ na hi svabhāvaḥ svambhauvamparityajya vartte tad svabhāvat tva abhāva prasaṅgāt tad nivṛtta auca nivṛttiḥ kāryasya api bhāve kāraṇasya bhāvaḥ yuktaḥ tad nivṛttau ca nivṛttiḥ anyathā tena vinā api bhāvāt kāryam eva tat tasya na syāt tad anya vat tasmāt svabhāva kāraṇa bhūta sādhya bhedāt dvidhā eva vidhi rūpam sādhyam tatra eva hetoḥ pratibandhāt svabhāva bhūtañca sādhyam svabhāva hetuḥ sādhayati kāraṇa bhū tañca kārya hetuḥ iti abhyupeyam pratiṣedham api upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta anupalabdhiḥ eva sādhayati na anyā yathā tathā vistareṇa pratipādayiṣyati tat idam iha saṃkṣiptam artha tattvam viṣaya vyapekṣayā viṣayiṇaḥ liṃgasya vyavasthā viṣayaḥ ca vidhiḥ pratiṣedhaḥ vā bhavet 
VNṬ_3,3^3	 vidhau= api artha antaram vā vidhīye tān artha antaram vā artha antara vidhau= api kārya kāraṇam anubhayam vā sādhyate kārya pratipādana ipi kāraṇa sāmānyam vā amegha ādi vyāvṛttam vastu mātram liṅga tvena ucyate kāraṇa viśeṣaḥ vā yaḥ apratibaddha sāmarthye megha ādiḥ pratiṣedhopi niṣedhya abhimatasya anupalambhena upalambhena vā pratipādyeta anupalambhepi upalambha nivṛtti mātra lakṣaṇaḥ vā bhavet tad tulya yoga avasthaḥ kevalā para padārtha upalambha rūpaḥ vā iti vikalpāḥ tatra nāvaśyam gambhīra dhvāna ādi yuktam api megha ādi kāraṇa mātram vṛṣṭi ādi kārya āvirbhāvakam antarā pratibandha sambhavena vyabhicārāt atas na kāraṇa mātram gamakam kāraṇa viśeṣāt api apratihata śakteḥ anantaram sambandha smṛti vyavahitāt anumeya vijñānāt prāk kāryam eva udbhūtam akṣa jñāna grāhyaṃbhavati iti na tasya api liṅga tvam kāryantu kāraṇa liṅgam yuktam tad avinā abhāvāt tad atikrame vā hetumat tām vilaṃghayet 
VNṬ_3,3^4	 anubhayam api asambandha anugamakam ati prasaṅga uvā anartha antaram api avyabhicāra aṅgamyate iti yuktimat niṣedha upyupalambhena na yujyate virodhāt katham hi nāma upalabhyate ca na asti ca iti upapadyate tad jñāna nivṛtti mātram api vyabhicāri eka jñāna saṃsargiṇaḥ tu kaivalya dṛṣṭeḥ asattā vyavahāraḥ yuktaḥ yadi hi syāt upalabhya sattvaḥ eva bhavet pramāṇañca yat anupapadyamāna viṣayam na tat viṣayi yuktam yathā vāji viṣāṇam anupapadyamāna viṣayañca ukta prakāreṇa svabhāva ādi syāt anya saṃyogya ādi para parikalpitam liṃgam iti vyāpaka anupalambhaḥ vaidharmyeṇa nīla ādi jñānam tat eva vā kārya ādi liṅgam naimittika śabda artha anupapattiḥ bādhikā kim evam siddham agamakattvam anyeṣām tathā hi viṣayitu aṅgamakattvam prakāśa kattvam ityādayaḥ paryāyāḥ tasmāt sādhyasya trividhat tvāt taṅgamakaḥ hetuḥ api trividhaḥ eva iti sthitam etat 
VNṬ_5,1^1	 kathantrividham iti āha svabhāvaḥ ityādi ca śabdaḥ svabhāva kārya apekṣayā samuccaya arthaḥ etat ca abhimata hetu pradarśanam svabhāva kārya anupalambha bhedāt trividham apratyakṣasya siddheḥ aṅgam na tu kāraṇa eka artha samavāyi viraḥ dhyā ādi bhadāt iti darśana artham nanu ca upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta anupalambhaḥ ca iti vaktavyam tasya evā pratyakṣasya siddheḥ vakṣyamāṇena nyāyena aṅgattva at na anupalambha mātrasya tat katham sāmāni eta uktam iti ced evam etat samarthita sādhana aṅga adhikārāt tu sāmānya śabda upyayam anupalambha śabda aupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta anupalambhaḥ eva varttate tathā hi sāmānya śabdāḥ api śabda antara sannidhānāt prakaraṇa sāmarthyāt ca viśeṣeṣu avatiṣṭhante yat āha na hi viśeṣa śabda sannidheḥ eva śabdānām viśeṣa avasthiti hetuḥ api tu prakaraṇa sāmarthya ādikam api iti yathā ca anupalambha mātrasya samarthita sādhana aṅgat tvam na sambhavati tathā uttaratra pratipādayiṣyati apratyakṣa siddhi hetu liṅga adhikārāt vā acodyam eva etat 
VNṬ_5,1^2	 kimpu nar asya trividhasya sādhana aṅgasya samarthanam yad viparyayāt asamartha nambhaviṣyati iti āha tasya ityādi sādhya śabda utra anityat tva ādi dharma mātrasya vācakaḥ avayava samudāya upacārāt na tu sādhya dharmi dharma samudāyasya vyāpteḥ eva abhāva prasaṅgātaḥ śabda ādi dharmmi viśiṣṭasya anittyat tva ādeḥ dṛṣṭānta dharmiṇī a bhāvāt vyāptim prasādhya anvaya vyatireka sādhakena pramāṇena anena anvaya vyatireka niścayau= uktau dharmiṇi jijñāsita viśeṣe śabda ādau bhāva sādhanam pakṣa dharmattva sādhakena pramāṇena sattva kathanam iti arthaḥ anena api pakṣa dharmat tva niścayaḥ uktaḥ kathampunar sarvvā upasaṃhāreṇa vyāptim prasādhya dharmiṇi bhāvaḥ kathyate iti atra udāharaṇam āha yathā ityādi tat sarvvami tyanena sarvvā upasaṃhāreṇa vyāpti pradarśan aṅkathayati kimartham vipratipatti nirāsa artham tathā hi pakṣa sa pakṣa apekṣayā antar vyāptiḥ bbahis vyāptiḥ ca pradarśya te iti eke vipratipannāḥ 
VNṬ_5,1^3	 tat ca na yuktam vastu balāya atattvāt vyāpteḥ pūrvva sādhyena vyārptim prasādhya paścāt dharmmiṇi sattvam kathayitavyam iti ayam īdṛśaḥ krama niyamaḥ kim atra asti na vā iti āha atra api ityādi atra iti mad mate sādhana aṅga samarthane vā api śabdaḥ avadhāraṇepratiṣedhe na ca sambandhanīyaḥ na eva kaścid ayam īdṛśaḥ krama niyamaḥ paripāṭi niyamaḥ iti yāvat kiṃkāraṇam iti āha iṣṭa artha siddheḥ ubhayatra aviśeṣāt iti vyāpti sādhana abhidhāna pūrvvaka dharmi bhāva sādhana abhidhāne dharmi bhāva sādhana abhidhāne dharmi bhāva sādhana abhidhāna pūrvvake vā vyāpti sādhana abhidhāne sādhya artha siddheḥ viśeṣa abhāvāt iti arthaḥ evama kūtam krama niyamaḥ hi kimartham āśrīyate sādhya sidhi artham yathā sādharmyavati dṛṣṭānta prayoge sādhyena eva hetoḥ avinābhāvaḥ pradarśyate na hetunā sādhyasya tathā vaidharmyavati sādhya abhāvaḥ eva hetoḥ abhāvaḥ kathyate na tu hetu abhāve sādhyasya kimartham 
VNṬ_5,1^4	 mābhūt hetoḥ sādhyena avinābhauvit tva apradarśanena iṣṭa artha siddheḥ asiddhiḥ viparyaya siddhiḥ ca iti yat āha evam hi hetoḥ sa pakṣaḥ eva sattvam sādhya abhāve ca asattvam eva śakyam darśayitum na viparyayāt iti yathā nitya tā akṛta kattvena nāśittvāt vā atra kārya tā syāt anuktā kṛtā vyāpit tu a niṣṭhaḥ ca samanvayaḥ iti tat atra yuktam krama samāśrayaṇaṃ iha tu vinā api anena abhimata artha siddhiḥ sampadyate iti sūvatan na kaścid krama niyamaḥ iti iṣṭa artha siddheḥ ubhayatra aviśeṣāt iti etat eva atra kutas iti ced āha yasmāt dharmiṇī ityādi sādhyena vyāptim prasādhya iti uktam prāk kimpunaḥ tad vyāpti sādhanam iti āha atra ityādi atra iti syabhāva hetau kārya anupalambhayoḥ tu paścāt vyāpti sādhanam abhidhā syāt viparyaye sādhyasya hetoḥ va rttamānasya sataḥ iti śeṣaḥ bādhakam pramāṇam yena sādhya viparyaye varttamānaḥ hetuḥ bādhyate tasya kathanam yat tat vyāpti sādhanam iti arthaḥ 
VNṬ_6,1^1	 kiṃpunaḥ tad vādhaka pramāṇa upadarśanam iti āha yadi na sarvvam vastu satkṛtakam ca iti pūrvva ukti hetu dvayam parāmṛṣati pratikṣaṇa vināśi syāt tadā asat eva syāt iti sambandhaḥ kutaḥakṣaṇikasya padārthasya krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā ayogāt tathā āha kṣaṇikattvena abhimatasya bhāvasya krameṇa tāvat artha kriyā na yujyate kārya nirvarttana yogyasya svabhāvasya sadā sattvāt anyathā paścāt api na kuryāt pūrvvasvabhāva apracyutaḥ purāvat sahakāriṇam āsādya karoti iti ced na anādheya ātmā atiśayasya pūrvvasvabhāva aparityāginaḥ saha kāriṣu apekṣā yogāt ādadhatti eva sahakāriṇaḥ tasya ātmā atiśayam iti ced na sahakāribhiḥ āhitasya atiśayasya tattva anyat tva ayogāt tathā hi na tāvat ayam ātmā atiśayaḥ tasya ātma bhūtaḥ tasya eva tat avyatirekāt ātma atiśaya vat sahakāri balāt utpatti prasaṅgāt evañca abhyupetam asya akṣaṇikattvam avahīyate vyatiriktaḥ eva sa tasmāt iti ced 
VNṬ_6,1^2	 bhavatu kintu tasmāt eva ātma atiśayāt kārya utpatteḥ tad avastham asya artha kriyāsu asāmarthyam iti durnnivāraḥ prasaṅgaḥ samāpatati sambandha upyanena katham iti vaḥ cintā viṣayam avatarati eva atiśaya balāt karoti iti atra api sahakāri apekṣā pakṣa uditaḥ doṣaḥ samartha svabhāvat tvāt anādheya atiśayat tvepi kuvinda ādi vat kiñcid apekṣya kārya janakaḥ iti ced na tat sāram na hi sahakāriṇaḥ pratyayāḥ tasya tāvat atiśayam ādhātum kṣamāḥ na ca api anupakārake bhāve apekṣā yuktim anupatati atiprasaṅgāt evañca sarvu akālam asya akārya jana kattva prasaṅgaḥ kuvinda ādīnām api tad svabhāvasya karaṇāt akārakasya vā tad svabhāvat tvāt ityādi hetuvindau= uktam iti na iha ucyate evantā vat krameṇa asya artha kriyā na yujyate na api yugapad tathā hi artha kriyā nivarttana yogya svabhāva adhyāsita mūrtiḥ saha eva asāvatas ca paścāt api tad rūpa viyogāt kāryam utpādayet anyathā udaya anantaram eva asya kṣayaḥ syāt na ca api akṣaṇikattvena upagatasya sakṛt kāryam utpadyamānam upalabhyate krama sambhava darśanāt 
VNṬ_6,1^3	 tat eva m aya makṣaṇikaḥ padārthaḥ krameṇa yugapad vā na kāñcid apyad artha kriyā mātrām aṃśatā upi kṣamaḥ nirvartayitum itti asattvam eva asya yadi nāma artha kriyā sā na yuktā taktim iti asattvam eva asya syāt iti āha artha kriyā ityādi artha kriyāyāḥ sāmarthyantadeva lakṣaṇam yasya sattvasya iti vigrahaḥ atas artha kriyā sāmarthya lakṣaṇāt sattvāt vyāvṛttam vyavacchinnam iti śruteḥ hetau tasmāt arthe vā katham punar idam avasīyate artha kriyā sāmarthyam sattva lakṣaṇam iti atas āha sarvva ityādi sarvu eṣām sāmarthyānām upākhyā śrutiḥ upākhyāyate anayā iti kṛtvā tasya avirahaḥ abhāvaḥ saḥ eva lakṣaṇam yasya nirupākhyasya sa tathā khyāyate atra api iti śruti hetau sarvu agrahaṇam ghaṭa ādīnām api kṣaṇikattvena abhimatānām viṣaya bhedena artha kriyā sāmarthya nirvṛtteḥ asti iti teṣām asattva vyavacchedāya na eva artha kriyā sāmarthyam sattva lakṣaṇam api tu sattā yogaḥ iti ced na sattāyāḥ abhā vāt 
VNṬ_6,1^4	 tad abhāvaḥ ca anyatra pratipāditaḥ iti na iha ucyate sattāyāḥ ca na eva sattvam prāpnoti sattā yoga abhāvāt niḥsāmānyāni sāmānyāni iti samayāt na ca svayam atad rūpāḥ padārtha ātmānaḥ svabhāva antara samparkkam āsāt ayanta upi tādrūpyam pratipadyante sphaṭika abhra paṭala ādayaḥ iva javākusuma ādi rūpam iti yaktiñcid etat tatu etāvat eva abhidhānīyam sarvu asāmarthya viraha lakṣaṇam nirupākhyam iti taktimanena upākhyā grahaṇena iti ced sūktam etat sarvvasām arthya rahitasya tu sāmarthya nibandhanasya kasyacid api śabdasya avṛtteḥ asat vyavahāra viṣayat tva khyāpanāya saṃjñāyāḥ ca anugata arthattva siddhi artham idam uktam iti gamyate yadi tu evam sādhya viparyaye heta utbādhaka pramāṇa upadarśanam na kriyate tatas kim syāt iti ced āha evam sādhanasya sādhya viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇān upadarśane satya nivṛttiḥ eva aśaṃkāyāḥ iti sambandhaḥ kā punar sā śaṃkā sa kṛtakaḥ vā syāt nityaḥ ca evam prakārāḥ 
VNṬ_8,1^1	 nanu vipakṣa hetoḥ vṛttiḥ na upalabhyate tat katham anivṛttiḥ iti āha adarśane pivṛtteḥ asya sādhanasya akṣa viparyaye sādhyasya hayupaskāraḥ kim iti evam api anivṛttiḥ iti āha virodha abhāvāt iti sādhana sādhya vipakṣayoḥ iti śeṣaḥ ayam asya abhiprāyaḥ yadi sādhanasya sādhya viparyasya ca parasparam virodhaḥ siddhaḥ syāt bhavet adarśana mātre te anyathā bādhakā siddhau saṃśayaḥ durnnivāraḥ syāt iti āśaṅkya āha na ca na eva sarvvā anupalabdhiḥ bādhikā pratiṣedhikā yuktā iti upaskāraḥ kasya bhāvasya sattvasya sādhya viparyaya īhetoḥ iti śeṣaḥ prakaraṇāt vaitat gamyate eva idam uktam bhavati 
VNṬ_8,1^2	 vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ eva sahabhāva bādhate hetoḥ sādhya abhāvena yathā pratipāditam prāk na api adarśana mātrāt vyāvṛttiḥ viprakṛṣṭa sarvu a darśinaḥ adarśanasya abhāva asādhanāt ityādinā tasmāt sūktam anyathā bādhakā siddhau saṃśayaḥ durnnivāraḥ syāt iti anena pūrvva uktam eva smārayati evañcai tad arthavat abhāva sādhanasya adarśanasya apratiṣedhāt iti uktam tatra bhavet kasyacid āśaṃkā kim anena abhāva sādhanasya iti viśeṣaṇena yāvatā sarvvam eva adarśanam abhāva sādhanam iti atas tad āśaṅkā vinivṛtti artham idam āha na ca ityādi atra ca śabdaḥ hi śabda arthe pratipattavyaḥ tasmiṃ na eva vā avadhāraṇe vyākhyānantu pūrvva vat 
VNṬ_9,1^1	 nanu ca bādhakasya eva pramāṇasya krama ākrama ayogasya asāmarthyena vyāptiḥ na siddhā tat katham tat svayam asiddha vyāptikam sat aparasya sattva ādeḥ hetoḥ vyāpti sādhane paryāptam pramāṇa antareṇa tatra vyāptiḥ sādhyate iti ced sā eva tarhi iyam anavasthā doṣāt iva anubadhnāti iti kadācid paraḥ brūyāt iti āśaṅkya sarvvam idam āha tatra ityādi tatra śabdaḥ vākya upanyāsa arthaḥ sāmarthyam yat vastu lakṣaṇam tad krama akrama yogena vyāptam siddham yatra sāmarthyam tatra krama ākramābhyām artha kriyayā abhavitavyam iti anena ākāreṇa tat eva kutas iti ced āha prakāra antara asagbhavāt yasmāt anyat kramākrama vyatiriktam prakāra antaram na asti tasmāt yatra idam sattva lakṣaṇam artha kriyā sāmarthyam tatra avaśyam ca krama ākramābhyām artha kriyayā bhavitavyam nanu ca kramākramābhyām anyaḥ rāśiḥ na asti iti etat eva katham siddham krama ākramayoḥ anyonya parihāra sthita lakṣaṇattvena tṛtīya prakāra vyatireka tvāt 
VNṬ_9,1^2	 bhāva abhāva vat iti brūmaḥ bhavatu evam sa tu krama yaugapadya rūpaḥ eva iti kutas iti ced kaḥ tahari anyaḥ bhavatu kaścid bhavet iti ced kimarthantarhi mahati anartha saṅkaṭe patitosi yadidantayā tad rūpa abhidhāna īpya samarthosi yadi nāma sāmarthyam krama akrama yogena vyāptam siddham tathā apikim siddham iti ced āha tena sāmarthyasya kramākrama yogena vyāpta tvena vyāpakasya dharmasya kramākrama yogasya anupalabdhiḥ akṣaṇike padārthe abhyupagate sāmarthyam bādhate nirākaroti iti arthaḥ tathā hi ayam krama akrama yogaḥ tasya sāmarthyasya vyāpakaḥ tatas ca asya nivṛtta avaśyam eva sāmarthyasya api nivṛttiḥ anyathā ayam asya vyāpakaḥ eva na prāpnoti yasmāt tat vā ādhate iti tasmai tkrama yaugapadyā yogasya vyāpaka abhāvasya karma bhūtasya sāmarthya abhāvena vyāpya abhāvena karttṛ bhūtena vyāpti siddheḥ kāraṇāt na anavasthā prasaṅgaḥ 
VNṬ_10,1^1	 evam svabhāva hetoḥ sādhana aṅga samarthanam abhidhāya adhunā nigamayati evam ityādinā evañca yadi na samarthanam kriyate tat eva tad vādinaḥ parājayam āvahati iti prāk pratijñātam eva ayojayati tasya asamarthanam ityādinā kasmāt evam prārabdha artha asādhanāt iti na hi asamarthitam sādhanam ārabdham artham sādhayitum samartham vivāda ābhāḥ vapra saṅgāt tathā hi sāru vajña jñāna sādhane saṃskāra utkarṣa bhedena sambhave prakarṣa paryanta vṛttayaḥ prajñā ādayaḥ guṇāḥ sthira āśraya vartti sakṛt yathā kathaṃcid āhita viśeṣam vinā ahetuḥ ātmani iti yadi tarhi bādhaka pramāṇa upadarśanena hetoḥ vyāptiḥ prasādhyate tathā satti anavasthā bhavataḥ prāpnoti iti āśaṃka apanodanāya pūrvvapakṣam āracayan= āha atra api ityādi atra iti bādhake pramāṇe 
VNṬ_10,1^2	 adarśanam apramāṇayataḥ tava na adarśana mātrāt hetoḥ vyatireka niścayaḥ iti anena ākāreṇa na kevalam maule hetau= iti api śabdaḥ kim pūrvvasya api maulasya hetoḥ avyāptiḥ prāpnoti iti kriyā padam kiṅkāraṇam krama yaugapadyā yogasya vā sāmarthyena vyāpti asiddhaḥ tathā hi yadi adarśana mātreṇa na vyatireka niścayaḥ tathā sati krama yaugapadyā yogaḥ ca bhaviṣyati sat lakṣaṇam sāmarthyañca bhaviṣyati kaḥ anayoḥ virodhaḥ iti atra eva bādhake pramāṇe vyāptiḥ na siddhāḥ yadi na ama atra na siddhā maula hetau= etat valena vyāptiḥ setsyati iti ced āha pūrvvasya api maulasya api hetoḥ avyāptiḥ prāpnoti iti adhyāhāraḥ tathā hi na svayam apramāṇakam bādhakam pramāṇam anyasya pramāṇam upakalpayitum alam prāmāṇya prasaṅgāt 
VNṬ_11,1^1	 yadi evam atra api tarhi vyāpake pramāṇe anyena vyāpakena pramāṇena vyāptiḥ niścīyate iti āha iha api na kevalam maula hetau= iti apinā āha punar sādhana upakrame satya navasthā bhavet tathā hi yat tat vādhake pramāṇe vyāpti prasādhana artham bādhakam pramāṇam ucyate tatra api vyāptiḥ anyena bādhakena pramāṇena sādhyāḥ yasmāt na tat api svayam apramāṇam itarasya prāmāṇyam karttu samartham iti etat tatra api śakyam vaktum tasya api anyena vyāptiḥ sādhyate iti ced yadi evam tatra api iyam eva vārtteṃti anavasthā bhavataḥ tathā sati prasajati evam samā racita pūrvvapakṣaḥ sāmpratam atra pratividhānam āha na abhāvasā dhanasya ityādi vyatireka sādhanattvena iti upaskāraḥ idam uktam bhavati 
VNṬ_11,1^2	 na sarvu amatra adarśanam pratikṣipyate vyatireka niścāyakasya vyāpaka anupalabdhi saṃjñakasya aniṣedhāt kintva darśana mātram iti yat āha yat adarśanam viparyayam abhāvam sādhayatī ti kasya hetoḥ kutra sādhya viparyaye tat adarśanam asya hetoḥ bādha kampramāṇam ucyate kasmāt viruddha pratyupasthāpanāt asya iti varttate tathā hi yasya krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā yogaḥ tasya sāmarthya lakṣaṇam sattvam na asti yathā bandhyā tanaya ādīnān tathā vā kṣaṇikānām api krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā ayogaḥ iti krama ākramābhyām artha kriyā ayogāt iti ayam vyāpaka anupalambhaḥ sattva ādityasya hetoḥ viruddham asat tvam sādhya viparyaye pratyupasthāpayat vādhakam pramāṇam ucyate evañca kṛtaka tva ādau= api yathāyogyam vācyam 
VNṬ_11,2^1	 kasmāt viruddha pratyupasthāpanāt asya tad vādhakampramāṇam ucyate iti āha evaṃhi sa hetuḥ sattva ādi lakṣaṇaḥ sādhya abhāve tasmin= asan= iti sidhyet yadi tatra sādhya abhāve bādhyate nirākriyatā kena sva viruddhena svarūpa viruddhena asattva ādinā iti yāvat kimbhūtena pramāṇavatā pramāṇa yuktena kasmāt evam asau tatra asastidhyati iti āha anyathā tatra sādhya viparyaye asya hetoḥ bādhakasya asiddhau sattyām saṃśayaḥ san= ca syāt nityaḥ ca ityādi durnivāraḥ syāt iti śeṣaḥ duḥkhena nivāryate iti durnivāraḥ durnniṣedhaḥ iti arthaḥ 
VNṬ_11,2^2	 bādhaka grahaṇena atra viruddhasya pratyupasthāpa kampramāṇaṃgṛhyate vādhaka pramāṇa pratyupasthāpitam vā hetu viruddham nanu ca anupalabdhi mātrāt eva sādhya viparyaye hetoḥ vyāvṛtti niścayāt asandigdhaḥ vyatirekaḥ bhaviṣyati taktimucya se śaṅkāyāḥ vyāvṛttiḥ bādhaka pramāṇa anupadarśane tu saḥ eva na sidhyati tat katham iyam nivartteta iti yadi nāma iyam āśaṅkā na vyāvarttate tatas kim iti āha tatas āśaṃkāyāḥ anivṛtte ranekāntikaḥ syāt hettvābhāsaḥ kasmāt vyatirekasi asādhya abhāve hetoḥ abhāva lakṣaṇasya sandehāt kāraṇāt sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttikaḥ syāt hetu ābhāse iti arthaḥ 
VNṬ_12,1	 kimpunar adarśana īpya nivṛttiḥ āśaṃkāyāḥ yāvatā tad adarśanam abhāvam sādhayati iti āha na api adarśana mātrāt vyāvṛttiḥ sādhya abhāve hetoḥ sidhyati iti vākya adhyāhāraḥ api śabdaḥ yasmāt arthe mātra grahaṇam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta adarśanasya vyavaccheda artham kutas etat viprakṛṣṭeṣu deśa kāla svabhāva viprakarṣaiḥ padārtheṣu cīnadāśarathi piśāca prabhṛtiṣu yat adarśanam tasya abhāva asādhanāt kasya abhāvam sādhayati iti ced prakṛtattvāt viprakṛṣṭānām iti gamyate 
VNṬ_12,2^1	 nanu samāsādita sakala padārtha vyāpi jānāti sa yasya adarśanam abhāvam viprakṛṣṭānām api sādhayati tat katham idam uktam iti āha asarvvadarśinaḥ iti sarvvan draṣṭum śīlam asya tatas nañā samāsaḥ kasmāt tasya api adarśanam abhāvat na sādhayati iti arvvāc darśanena puṃsā satām api keṣāñcid arthānām viprakṛṣṭānām adarśanāt idam āgūritam na iha sarvu adarśi darśanam samasta vastu sattām prāpnoti yena tad nivarttamānam artha sattām vṛkṣa vat śiṃsapām nivarttayet bhedāt na api tat tasyāḥ kāraṇam yena vahni vat dhūmam nivarttamānam nivarttayet tad abhāvepi bhāvāt iti bādhakam punar pramāṇam ityādi atra kecid evam pūrvvapakṣayanti kimpunar bādhakam pramāṇam yasya upadarśanena maulasya hetoḥ vyāpti pra tītiḥ bhavati iti āha bādhaka mpuna riti ādi 
VNṬ_12,2^2	 teṣa aṅkatham atra vyāpti sādhanam viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa upadarśanam yadi na sarvvam satkṛtakam vā pratikṣaṇam vināśi syāt ityādinā a traiva prāc arthasya abhihitattvāt punarukta doṣa prasaktiḥ na bhavati iti cintyam etat taiḥ eva iti alam para doṣa saṃkīrttanena tasmāt anyathā pūrvva pakṣyate yasya api tarhi bādhakampramāṇam asti tasya katham ayam adoṣaḥ iti atas āha bādhakam punar pramāṇam pravarttamānam asāmarthyam ākarṣati iti kriyā padam kīdṛśam asat lakṣaṇam katham pramāṇam yasya padārthasya krama yaugapadyā yogaḥ artha kriyāyāḥ iti adhyāhāryam na tasya kvacid kārye sāmarthyam yathā nabhastala aravindasya iti adhyāhāryaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ asti ca akṣaṇike bhāve sa krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyāyāḥ ayogaḥ iti evampravarttamānam tatas kiñjātam iti ced āha tena kāraṇena yena tat pravarttamānam asat lakṣaṇam asāmarthyam ākarṣayati yat satkṛta kamvā tat anityam eva iti sidhyati 
VNṬ_12,3^1	 evam api kim siddhambhavati iti āha tāvatā ca vā adhaka pramāṇa upadarśana mātreṇa sādhana dharma mātra anvayaḥ sidhyati iti varttate kena iti āha sādhya dharmasya karttari ca iyam ṣaṣṭhī pratipattavyā tena sādhya dharmeṇa sādhana dharma mātrasya anapekṣita hetu antara vyāpārasya anvayaḥ sidhyati iti vākya arthaḥ santiṣṭhate na tu evaṅkaraṇīyam sādhana dharma mātreṇa anvayaḥ sādhya dharmā iti evam hi sādhyam eva hetunā avinābhūtam jātam na hetuḥ iti hetoḥ agamakattvam bhavet tatas ca kaḥ guṇaḥ labhyate iti āha svabhāva hetu lakṣaṇañca siddham bhavati tāvatā ca iti varttate svabhāva hetu lakṣaṇañca tad bhāva mātrāt dharminisvabhāvaḥ pi pratyaya abhāve apunar yatna apekṣi tattvāt kaladhauta mala viśuddhi vat iti evamādayaḥ hetavaḥ pratilabdha sāmarthya atiśayāḥ santi eva te ca yadi asamarthitāḥ eva jñāpya samartham jñāpayeyuḥ tadā jaimini prabhṛtīnām vivāda abhāvaḥ eva bhavet 
VNṬ_12,3^2	 nanu etat eva na sambhāvyate yat paramārthataḥ samarthasya api hetoḥ abhidhāne nigraha arhaḥ asau= iti āśaṅkāyām sva abhiprāyam prakaṭayati vastutas samarthasya hetoḥ upādānepi sāmarthya pratipādanāt iti ayam asya bhāvaḥ yadi nāma anena paramārthataḥ samarthaḥ hetuḥ upāttaḥ tathā api tasya sāmarthyam sādhana aṅga asamarthanā anna pratipāditam anena iti asamartha kalpaḥ eva asau na hi arthasya para artha anumāne guṇa doṣa avadhi kriyete kintarhi vacanasya vaktuḥ ayathārtha abhidhānena upālambhāt atas eva yatra api arthasya guṇa doṣa avadhikriyete tatra api vacana dvāreṇa eva evam etat abhyupagantavyam anyathā kṣaṇikaḥ śabdaḥ iti etāvat mātram eva pratijñā vacanam abhidhāya sthātavyam tathā abhidhānāt eva abhimata artha siddheḥ iti 
VNṬ_13,1^1	 evam svabhāva hetau= upadarśya sādhana aṅga samarthanam idānīṅkārya hetau= āha kārya hetau= api ityādinā kimpunaḥ tat iti āha yat kāryam liṅgam dhūma ādi saṃjñakam kāraṇasya dahana ādeḥ sādhanāya upādīyate tasya dhūma ādeḥ tena dahana ādinā asaha kārya kāraṇa bhāva prasādhana liṅgi liṅgayoḥ hetu phala bhāva sādhanam eva yat tat eva kārya hetau sādhana aṅga samarthanam iti arthaḥ kena punar tayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ prasādhyate iti āha bhāva abhāva sādhana pramāṇābhyām iti bhāva abhāvau kārya kāraṇayoḥ sat asat te tayoḥ sādhane te ca te pramāṇe ca iti vyu tpatti kramaḥ sādhana śabdaḥ ca karaṇa sādhanaḥ bhāva abhāva sādhana pramāṇe ca pratyakṣa anupalambhaḥ yathākramam kathampunar pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ prasādhyate iti āha yathe tyādi idandhūm ādi saṃjñakam kāryam asmin dahane sati bhavati 
VNṬ_13,1^2	 upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam sat anupalabdham prāk iti vākya śeṣaḥ kāryaḥ anyathā dahanasya tatra dhūme vyāpāraḥ evana kathitaḥ syāt dahana sannidhānāt prāk api etat āsīt iti āśaṅkā sambhavāt yathā ukta anupalambha grahaṇe tu na eva iyam avatarati atas eva ca pramāṇa viniścayāḥ dā= api evam eva abhihitam iti anena ca pratyakṣa pramāṇa vyāpāraḥ uktaḥ tathā hi asmin sati idam bhavati iti pratyakṣeṇa etat gamyate samprati anupalambhasya vyāpāram nirdidikṣuḥ āha satsu api ityādi tasmāt dahanāt anyeṣu vidyamāneṣu api tathā tasya dhūmasya hetuṣu indhana anila ādiṣu samartheṣu satsu apī iti varttate cakāraḥ ca atra lupta nirdiṣṭaḥ pratipattavyaḥ samartheṣu ca iti tasya dahanasya abhāve na bhavati idam iti adhikṛtam iti evam iti asya arthe varttate vyavacchede vā tat anena gavāśu ādīnām tad deśa kāla sannihitānām api dhūma jananam prati kāraṇat tvad niṣiddham 
VNṬ_13,1^3	 yatas yadi te gavāśu ādayaḥ tasya kāraṇambhaveyuḥ tadā vyatīta īpi agnau teṣām sannihitattvāt dhūma utpatti prasaṅgaḥ indhana ādi kāraṇa antara apekṣāḥ te tasya janakāḥ bhavanti tatas yam aprasaṅgaḥ iti ced yadi evam tepi tatra sannihitāḥ eva iti na vyāvarttate prasaṅgaḥ iti dahanam api sahakāriṇam apekṣya tam janayanti tatas na yuktam idam iti ced nanu evam satyāya atandahanasya dhūma urtpattim prati kāraṇat tvam taktim idam ucyate pūrvvāpara vyāhataṅga vā aśu ādayaḥ eva tasya kāraṇat na dahanaḥ iti astu tarhi tasya api dahanasya kāraṇattu aṅga vāśu ādīnām api iti ced na yuktam etat tatra vyatireka gateḥ durghaṭa tvāt tathā hi apagateṣu api gavā ādiṣu sati ca dahane tatra indhana ādi kalāpe bhavati eva hutabhuj hetoḥ utpattiḥ yatas kāraṇa prabandhaṅkārya prabandhañca āśritya hetu phala bhāvaḥ cintyate bhāvānāṅkāraṇa prabandha pūrvvaḥ kārya prabandhaḥ iti 
VNṬ_13,1^4	 tat tu kṣaṇa bhedam na hi samāsādita jñāna atiśayānām ayam pūrvvaḥ kṣaṇaḥ ayam uttaraḥ iti viśeṣa avalambi jñānam udeti arvvāc darśibhiḥ ca adhikṛtya pramāṇa lakṣaṇam praṇayitam kṛpāvadbhiḥ yathoktam sāṃvyavahārikasya etat pramāṇasya rūpam uktam atra api pare vimūḍhāḥ visamvādayanti lokam iti vāsagṛha ādiṣu tarhi dahana abhāvepi dhūma sadbhāvāt vyabhicāraḥ iti ced bhūtasya api dahana prabandha pūrvvakat tvam asti eva sākṣāt pāramparya kṛtaḥ tu viśeṣaḥ avayanti ca vicchinna avicchinna darśana prabandhayoḥ ddhūma prabandhayoḥ vāsa gṛha ādi rasavatī pradeśa ādi bhāvinoḥ sphuṭam eva bhedam vicitra bhāva svabhāva viveka abhyāsa bala upajāta vidagdha buddhayaḥ iti bhedena api anumānam aviruddham ata eva deśa kāla ādi apekṣam anumānam kārya hetau viruddha kārya upalambhe ca uktam iṣṭam viruddha kāryepi deśa kāla ādi apekṣaṇam anyathā vyabhicāri syāt gati eva āsīta sādhanam iti 
VNṬ_15,1	 atha api kaścid vividha bhāva bheda pravicaya cāturya atiśaya śalāka unmīlita prajñā cakṣuṣṭvā ādayam jvalana janitaḥ dhūmaḥ ayam dhūma janitaḥ iti vivecayati tathā api na sutarām vyabhicāraḥ tathā hi na agni janyaḥ dhūmaḥ dhūmāt bhavati nirhetu kattva prasaṅgāt tathā ca yat uktam atas ca anagnitaḥ dhūmaḥ yadi dhūmasya sambhavaḥ śakra mūrdhnaḥ tathā astasya kena vāryeta sambhavaḥ ityādi 
VNṬ_15,2	 tat asāram iti api upekṣate tasmāt na teṣām gavāśu ādīnām tatra kāraṇattvam asti iti niścayaḥ samādhīyatām atas ca dahanaḥ eva tasya kāraṇam na aśva ādayaḥ iti sthitam etat tathā ca dahanasya kāraṇat tvam yojitam anvaya vyatirekābhyām yathā ukta prakārābhyām evam iṃdhana ādi sāmagryāḥ sarvasyāḥ kāraṇam yojayitavyam yadi vā eka vākya tayā eva vyākhyāyate satsu api tasmāt dahanāt anyeṣu samartheṣu tad hetuṣu iṃdhana ādiṣu asya abhāve na bhavati iti gavāśu ādīnām tu ahetuttvam vyatireka abhāva tayā yathā uktena vidhinā boddhavyam 
VNṬ_15,3	 nanu ca etat eva yuktam vaktum tad abhāvena bhavati iti atha kim artham satsu api tad anyeṣu samartheṣu tad hetuṣu iti ucyate iti ced āha evam hi ityādi yasmāt evam satsu apī ityādinā abhidhīyamānaḥ asya dhūmasya tad kārya tvam agnikāryat tvam samarthitam niścitam asandigdham bhavati anyathā yadi evam na upadarśyate kevalam tad abhāvena bhavati iti upadarśyate tadā tad abhāvena bhavati iti upadarśane kriyamāṇenyasya api tu gavāśvādeḥ indhana ādeḥ ca tatra agni śūnya bhū bhāge abhāve sati sandigdham asya agneḥ sāmarthī ambhavati iti kutas kāraṇa bhāva niścayaḥ iti samudāya arthaḥ tatas eva āha satsu hi samartheṣu tad hetuṣu kārya anutpattiḥ kāraṇa antara vikalpam sūcayatī ti sandigdham asya anyathā sāmarthyam iti etat eva anya ttatra ityā dinā sūcayati tatra dhūma aśva kārye anya deva aśva ādi yat indhana ādi samarthan tada bhāvāt tat na bhū tandahana śūnya deśe asya svabhāvāt tat na jātam iti ku toyam niścayaḥ iti arthaḥ 
VNṬ_16,1	 yadi anyat tatra samarthanta da bhāvāt tat na jātam etat nivṛttau nivṛttiḥ tarhi asya katham iti ced āha etat nivṛttau= ityādi etasya agneḥ nnivṛttau dhūma nivṛttiḥ yeyam dhūmasya sā yadṛcchā samvādaḥ kākatālī yanyāyena iti arthaḥ yadā tu satsu apī iti kriyate tadā sarvu eṣām tatra sannipātāt etasya eva nivṛttau= asya nivṛttiḥ iti niścayāt na yadṛcchā samvādaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ 
VNṬ_16,2	 kim vat etat nivṛttau nivṛttiḥ yadṛcchā samvādaḥ iti āha mātṛ vivāha etyādi mātuḥ vivāhaḥ ucitaḥ ācaritaḥ yasmin deśe sa tathā tatas deśa śabdena saha viśeṣaṇa samāsaḥ tatra sa ca janma āśrayat tvāt upacārāt janma utpattiḥ yasya tasya pārasīka deśa bhāvi na yāvat deśa antare mālavakāḥ dideśe yathā abhāvaḥ mātṛ vivāha abhāve yadṛcchā samvādaḥ tadvat atra api tathā hi mṛd viśeṣa abhāvāt deśa antare tasya abhāvaḥ na tu mātṛ vivāha abhāvāt iti kākatālīyaḥ tad abhāve tasya abhāvaḥ iti evañca etat 
VNṬ_16,3	 athavā anyathā vyākhyāyate yathā idam dhūma ādi kāryam asmin= agni indhana ādi kāraṇa kalāpe sati bhavati vākya adhyāhāraḥ tu pūrvva vat kāryaḥ tasya prayojanam tat eva avagantavyam idam pratyakṣa vyāpāra saṅkīrttanam satsu api ityādinā anupalambhasya tad anyeṣu punar tasmāt agni ādi kāraṇa kalāpāt anyeṣu gavāśu ādiṣu samartheṣu tad hetuṣu asya agni ādi kāraṇa kalāpasya abhāve na bhavati etat ca parama tāpekṣam uktam na tu teṣān tad hetuttvam asti yadi punar te tasya hetavaḥ syuḥ tadā tad kalāpa sannidheḥ prāk api paścāt iva dhūma utpāda prasaṅgaḥ tad sāpekṣa tayā tad kṛta kattvam teṣām iti ced āyātam tarhi tasya kalāpasya kāraṇat tvam 
VNṬ_16,4	 bhavatu tarhi ubhayoḥ api na naḥ kācid kṣatiḥ iti ced na vyatireka gataḥ tatra durghaṭa tvāt iti uktam yathā apagateṣu api sarvu eṣu teṣu tasmim kalāpe sati bhavati eva tasya sambhavaḥ iti tad abhāve na bhavati iti vācyam tat kim artham satsu api iti ādi uktam iti ced āha evam hī tyādi anyathā tasya kalāpasya abhāve na bhavati iti upadarśane tasya api gavāśvādeḥ tatra abhāve sati sandigdhamasya kalāpasya sāmarthyam bhavet yatas anyat gavāśu ādi tatra śaktam tad abhāvāt tat na bhūtam etasya kalāpasya nivṛttau nivṛttiḥ yadṛcchā samvādaḥ śeṣam pūrvvayat 
VNṬ_17,1	 eva aṅkārya kāraṇa bhāva niścaya upāya vidhim uktvā prakṛtam upasaṃharati evam ityādinā evam yathā uktena vidhinā tad dhūma ādi tasya vahni ādeḥ kāryam samarthitam niścitaṃsidhyati bhavati yat eva asamarthitam asandigdham sidhyati niścīyate athavā evam pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām samarthitaṃsat tat tasya kāryam sidhyati 
VNṬ_17,2	 yadi nāma sidhyati tat kibhiti āha siddham sat sva sambhavena ātma sannidhānena tad sambhavam tasya kāraṇasya sannidhānam sādhayati deśa kāla ādi apekṣayā iti ādhyāha rttavyam etat uktam bhavati kārya kāraṇa bhāva niścayāḥ tiddham tat utpatti lakṣaṇa prativastu yatra evam atādṛśa upalabhyate tatra eva sva sattā mātreṇa deśa kāla ādi apekṣayā tat svakāraṇaṅgamayati iti kiṃkāraṇam iti āha kāryasya kāraṇa avyabhicārāt iti anyathā hi tat tasya kāryam eva na syāt tat vyabhicārāt na hi yat vyatirekeṇayat bhavati tat tasya kāryam yuktam kuṇḍalam iva keyūrasya iti abhisandhiḥ 
VNṬ_17,3	 nanu yadi nāma dhūmaḥ agni kāryat tvat na vyabhicarati anyasya tu aṅkura ādeḥ sva kāraṇaiḥ eva bīja ādibhiḥ avyabhicāraḥ iti kutas etat iti āha avyabhicāre ca ityādi i damuktambhavati yadā dhūmasya sva kāraṇa avyabhicāraḥ tad utpatteḥ siddhaḥ tadā bīja ādibhiḥ ātmīyaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ saha aṅkura ādīnām sarvu akāryāṇām sadṛśaḥ avyabhicāra nyāyaḥ tathā ahitepi yathā ukta prakārābhyām pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām tad kārya tayā siddhāḥ santaḥ tad avyabhicāriṇaḥ siddhyanti etad sādhana aṅga samarthanam kārya hetau etad viparītañcā samarthanam tad vādinaḥ parājaya adhikaraṇam iti darśayan= āha evam ityādi evam iti pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyām yathā ukta prakāra abhyāṅkārya hetau= api na kevalam pūrvva uktena prakāreṇa svabhāva hetau= asamartha namvādinaḥ parājaya sthānam iti api śabdaḥ kasmāt evam iti āha asamarthitam ityādi asamarthite tasmin kārya kāraṇa bhāva īliṅga liṅginoḥ liṅgasya vā tad kāryat tve ārabdha artha āsiddheḥ iti kriyā padam ārabdhaḥ arthaḥ kāraṇasya sattā sādhanam tasya asiddheḥ tad parājaya sthānam iti prakṛtena sambandhaḥ 
VNṬ_17,4	 etat eva kutas iti āha artha antarasya dhūma ādeḥ bhāve sattve tasya anyādeḥ bhāva niyama abhāvāt niyama grahaṇam yadṛcchā samvāda nirāsa artham artha antarasya api tad bhāve pratibaddha svabhāvasya bhāve bhavati eva tad bhāva niyamaḥ iti atas āha tad bhāva apratibaddha svabhāvasya iti tad bhāve agni ādi bhāve apratibaddhaḥ anāyattaḥ svabhāvaḥ asya iti vigrahaḥ etat ca artha antarasya bhāve tad bhāva niyama abhāvāt iti etasya kāraṇam avagantavyam prayogaḥ punar yaḥ artha antara bhūtaḥ yasmin na pratibaddha svabhāvaḥ tasya bhāve na tad bhāva niyamaḥ tat yathā nūpurasya bhāve mukuṭasya artha antara bhūtaḥ ca ayam dhūma ādiḥ apratibaddha svabhāvaḥ tasmin= agni ādau= iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ vyāpaka viru ddha upalabdhi vidhinā vā hetu artha kalpanā tadbhāva apratibaddha svabhāvat tvam eva kutas iti āha kāryat tva asiddhe riti etat punar asamarthite tasmin ni ti boddhavyam tat ca paramārthataḥ tena kārya hetuḥ eva upāttasttat yadi nāma tad kāryantena na samarthitam tathā hi katham asau nigṛhītaḥ iti āha vastutas kāryasya api upādāna pratipādanāt iti tad kāryatvasya iti viśeṣaḥ 
VNṬ_18,1	 evam kārya hetau= api sādhana aṅga samarthanam abhidhāya anupalabdhau= āha anupalabdhau= api samarthana miti sambandhaḥ sādhanāṅsya iti adhyāhārya kim punar tat iti āha anupalabdhi sādhanam kim yasya kasyacid na iti āha upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya iti dṛśya svabhāvasya na anyasya iti yāvat upalabdhiḥ jñānam upalabdhi śabdasya bhāva karaṇa sādhana tayā jñāna paryāyat tvāt tasyāḥ lakṣaṇaṅkāraṇam lakṣaṇa śabdasya karaṇa sādhana tvena kṛtaka abhidhāyit tvāt tat ca pratyaya antara sākalyam svabhāva viśeṣaḥ ca tad vyāptasya anupalabdhiḥ tasyāḥ sādhanam pratipādanam iti vyutpatti kramaḥ 
VNṬ_18,2^1	 katham evaṃvidhasya anupalabdhiḥ iti ced na udyate tasya tatra evet yapitu anyatra tad jātīyasya kasya punar evam vidhasya anupalabdhiḥ prasādhyate iti āha pratipattuḥ prativādinaḥ yadi ca upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptāḥ piśācādayopi bhavanti tad jātīyānāṃanyeṣām prabhāvavatā vā taktinteṣām api anupalabdhi sādhanam sādhana aṅga samarthanambhavati na iti āha pratipattuḥ etat uktam bhavati yaḥ eva asau pratipādyaḥ tasya eva yat upalabdhi lakṣaṇañca āyāti tasya eva anupalabdhi sādhanam na anyasya iti kim punar kāraṇam evamprakārasya eva anupalabdhi sādhanam na anyasya iti āha tādṛśyāḥ eva anupalabdheḥ asat vyavahāra siddheḥ iti 
VNṬ_18,2^2	 a nupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta anupalabdheḥ saṃśaya hetu tayā agamakattvāt iti bhāvaḥ asat vyavahāra siddheḥ iti vacanam asat vyavahāraḥ eva tayā sādhyate na tu abhāvaḥ svabhāva anupalabdheḥ svayam abhāva rūpa tvāt iti pradarśana artham asat vyavahāra graha ṇañca upalakṣaṇa artham tena asat jñāna śabdau= api grāhyau etat punar kutas avasīyate iti ced āha anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya arthasya pratipattuḥ pratyakṣam tat eva upalabdhiḥ tasya anivṛttau= api satyām abhāva asiddheḥ abhāva grahaṇam abhāva vyavahāra śabda jñāna upalakṣaṇam upalabdhi lakṣaṇañca jñāna parigraheṇa tad pramita vastu vyudāsāya kā punar iyam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptiḥ yat yogāt upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptaḥ iti ucyate iti āha tatra ityādi 
VNṬ_18,2^3	 tatra śruti vacana upanyāsa arthāḥ svabhāva viśeṣaḥ kim iyat eva na iti āha kāraṇa antara sākalyañca tasmāt svabhāva viśeṣa ādyāni anyā nikāraṇāni indriya manaskāra ādīni tāni kāraṇa antarāṇi teṣām sākalyam sāmagryam svabhāva viśeṣa apekṣayā samuccaya arthaḥ cakāraḥ kaḥ punar ayam svabhāva viśeṣaḥ iti āha svabhāvaḥ ityādi yadi ayam trividhena viprakarṣeṇa vyavadhānena deśa kāla svabhāva lakṣaṇena na viprakṛṣṭam merurām a sura ādi rūpa vat svabhāva viśeṣaḥ ucyate tam eva spaṣṭayati yat ityādinā na ātma rūpaḥ anātma rūpaḥ para rūpaḥ iti arthaḥ sa ca asau pratibhāsaḥ ca tasya vivekaḥ abhāvaḥ tena ākāreṇa yat pratipattuḥ pratyakṣan tatra apratibhāsitum śīlam yasya rūpasya svabhāvasya tad rūpantatha uktam 
VNṬ_18,2^4	 athavā rūpa śabdena saha viśeṣaṇa samāsaḥ kāryaḥ sati upalambha pratyaya antarasā kalyaḥ iti upaskriyate yaḥ sajātīya vijātīya rahitena ātmanā pratibhāsate sva jñāne tad anya kāraṇa samavadhāne sati sa svabhāvaḥ iti yāvat tādṛśaḥ iti trividha vipra karṣā viprakṛṣṭa rūpaḥ padārthaḥ tathā anātma rūpa pratibhāsa vivekena pratipattṛ pratyakṣa pratibhāsena āśayena anupalabdhaḥ sa na asat vyavahārasya viṣayaḥ bhavati asat vyavahāra pratipatti yogyaḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ vidyamāna upīndriyasya ālokasya manaskārasya vā abhāvāt na upalabhyate tādṛśaḥ tat katham asat vyavahāra viṣayaḥ bhavati iticed āha satsu anyeṣu upalambha kāraṇeṣu iti 
VNṬ_20,1^1	 nanu aviprakṛṣṭopi ghaṭa ādiḥ upalambha kāraṇa antara samavadhānepi ca santāna vipariṇāma apekṣa tvāt na upalabhyate na hi hetu antara sannidhānam iti sva phala utpādana anuguṇaḥ pariṇāmaḥ bhavati kāraṇasya tathā hi satyām api pṛthivī bīja jala ādi sāmagryām ati bahunā eva kālena tāla bījasya sva kārya udaya anukūlā pariṇatiḥ bhavati śaṇa ādi bījasya tu anantaram eva tathā atra api bhaviṣyati iti kiñca anyat prabhāvavatā yoge piśāca māya ākāra ādinā adhiṣṭhitaḥ bhavati yadā ayam bhāvaḥ tadā vidyamānā upi na upalabhyate tat katham uktam tādṛśaḥ satsu anyeṣu upalambha kāraṇeṣu anupalabdhaḥ asat vyavahāra viṣayaḥ iti nūnambhavāḥ nnyāya vindau= api akṛta pariśramaḥ tathā hi atra uktam svabhāvaḥ yaḥ satsu anyeṣu upalambha kāraṇeṣu san pratyakṣaḥ eva bhavatī ti 
VNṬ_20,1^2	 yaḥ ca ayam santāna pariṇāmam apekṣate yaḥ ca prabhāvavatā adhiṣṭhitaḥ sa svabhāva viśeṣaḥ eva na bhavati sakala tad anya upalambha pratyaya samavadhān epi sva rūpa viṣaya upalambha janaka tvāt tathā evaṃvidhasya pi śācā ādi svabhāva aviśiṣṭa rūpasya abhāva vyavahāra viṣaya tā sādhyate kintā rhi indriyāṇi upalambha pratyaya antara sannidhāne yaḥ san pratyakṣaḥ eva bhavati tasya na evantarhi sarvathā abhāvaḥ sādhitaḥ bhavati iti ced suṣṭu anukūlam ācarasi yatas anantaram eva uktam yaḥ eva ayam anupahata indriya ādi sākalye darśana patham upayāti tasya ca tad sākalye anupalambhesya ca vyavahāra viṣaya tā sādhyate na tu piśāca ādi svabhāva aviśiṣṭa rūpasya iti 
VNṬ_20,1^3	 na ca tathāvidhasya api sakala tad anya upalambha pratyaya samavadhāne anupalabdhasya astitvam yuktam anupalabdheḥ eva ayogāt upalambha janane kasyacid apekṣaṇīyasya abhāvāt pramāṇa viniścaye tu spaṣṭīkṛtam eva idam na kārya kāle abhāva pratipatte riti ādinā etena eva yat ekena avaśyam sāmagri sākalya īpi pariṇāmaḥ tāla gaṇa bīja vat ityādinā sa tam atiśaya vat matimataḥ manāk api anavagacchantaḥ ca udya cuñcavaḥ ca ūcuduḥ tatra sarvaṃmayam duḥsthitam veditavyam iti alam apratiṣṭhita bāla pralāpaiḥ iti viramyate tasmāt upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta anupalabdhiḥ eva abhāva vyavahāra sādhanī iti sthitam etat 
VNṬ_20,1^4	 yatas ca etat evam tatas tasmāt kāraṇāt anyathā sati liṅge samavāyaḥ upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta anupalabdhim uktvā yat anyat asat vyavahāra sādhanam anupalabdhi mātram liṅgam upādīyate tadā tasmin sati saṃśayaḥ bhavati na asti asat vyavahāra niścayaḥ upalabdhi nivṛttau= api artha abhāva āsiddheḥ iti samudāya arthaḥ yadi vā tatas dṛśya anupalambhāt liṅgāt sakāśāt anyathā sati liṅge saṃśayaḥ iti vyākhyātavyam tasmāt śabdaḥ tu pūrva madhyā harttavyam athavā tatas upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptāda nyathā tad vihīne saṃśaye sati tad liṅgaḥ iti vyākhyeyam kā punar atra anupalabdhau vyāptiḥ iti āha atra api ityādi evam vidham iti dṛśyam sat anupalabdham sarvu agrahaṇam sarvvā upasaṃhāreṇa vyāpti pradarśana artham 
VNṬ_21,1^1	 nanu yadi nāma kasyacid viṣāṇa ādeḥ śaśa mastaka ādau= upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta anupalabdhasya asat vyavahāra viṣaya tā anyena api sāmānye viśeṣī evaya vidravya saṃyoga vibhāga ādinā tathāvidhena tathā bhavitavyam iti kutas ayam niyamaḥ iti atas āha kasyacidi tyādi kasyacid upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anupalabdhasya śaśa viṣāṇa ādeḥ asataḥ a sat vyavahāra viṣayestyabhyupagame asat vyavahāra ādi viṣayaḥ asan= iti uktaḥ tad lakṣaṇā viśeṣāt iti tasya asataḥ lakṣaṇam nimittam yathā ukta anupalabdhiḥ lakṣaṇa śabdaḥ ca karaṇa sādhanaḥ tasya aviśiṣṭa tvāt sāmānya viśeṣa avayavidravya ādau= iti vākya śeṣaḥ etat uktambhavati śaśa viṣāṇa ādeḥ api asat vyavahāra viṣayat tvam kasmāt iṣyate 
VNṬ_21,1^2	 yathā ukta anupalambhasya tad nimittasya sadbhāvāt iti ced yadi evam sāmānya viśeṣa tā tasya asti iti kasmāt tathā sat vyavahāra viṣaya tvat na abhyupagamyate anyathā tatra api tat syāt ced na hi puruṣa icchā vaśāt hetau viṣaya pravibhāgaḥ yuktaḥ iti na hi ityādinā etat eva vyanakti evaṃvidhasya dṛśyasya sattve anupalabdhasyā satva anabhyupagamaḥ iti asat vyavahāra ādi viṣaya tvāt na abhyupagamaḥ iti arthaḥ asatva śabdena asat vyavahāraḥ viniścayaḥ tasya upalakṣaṇam yukta upalambhasya tasya evā nupalambhanam pratiṣedha hetuḥ ityādi ced anyatra śaśaśṛṅga abhāve daṇḍena puruṣasya yogaḥ saḥ eva iti arthaḥ na hi evaṃvidhasya dṛśyasya cakṣuḥ ādi śūnyeṣu upalambha kāraṇeṣu sa anupalabdhiḥ bhavati 
VNṬ_21,2	 kintarhi upalabdhiḥ eva bhavati iti pratiṣedha dvayena āha anyasya upalabdhi pratyayasya kasyacivapekṣaṇīyasya abhāvāt iti bhāvaḥ tat anena prakṛtam eva spaṣṭayati anupalabhyamānam tu īdṛśam iti upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptat na asti tasmāt etāvat sātra upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta anupalabdhi mātrat nimittam yasya asat vyavahārasya sa tathā khyātaḥ tad anena asat vyavahārasya ananya nimitta tām āha etat eva kutas iti āha anyasya ityādi yathā ukta anupalabdhim apāsya anyasya nāstitva vyavahāra nimittasya abhāvāt iti samuccaya arthaḥ 
VNṬ_22,1^1	 nanu ca yasya yatra na kiñcid sāmarthyam asti tat asat vyavahāra viṣayaḥ yathā nabhastale kamalam tathā abhimatepi deśa ādau= abhimatasya bhāvasyana kiñcid sāmarthyam asti iti sarvu asāmarthya vivekaḥ eva na astitva vyavahārasya nimittam bhaviṣyati etaktimasaṃbaddham eva udghāṭita śirobhiḥ abhidhīyate anyasya tad nimittasya abhāvāt iti kadācid kaścid brūyāt iti tat matam āśaṃkate sarvu asāmarthya vivekaḥ nimittam iti cedi ti atra samādhim āha evam ityādinā 
VNṬ_22,1^2	 evaṃmanyate su uktam etat sarvu asāmarthya vivekaḥ nimittam iti kintu saḥ eva sarvu asāmarthya vivekoyam padārthaḥ katham avagataḥ yathā uktām anupalabdhim apāsya yena sarvu asāmarthya vivekaḥ asya asat vyavahārasya nimittam bhaviṣyati na ca asau= ajñātaḥ eva tasya nimittambhavitum arhati jñāpaka hetu adhikārāt kasmāt sarvvasāmarthya vivekinaḥ yathā ukta anu palambhena eva pratītiḥ iti āha anyasya tad pratipati upāyasya abhāvāḥ diti yadā tu yathā ukta anupalabdhyā tasya sarvu asāmarthya vivekinaḥ pratītiḥ bhavati tadā tad pratipattausatyām asat vyavahāraḥ bhavati iti tasmāt idam yathā ukta anupalambhanam tasya asat vyavahārasya animittam ucyate 
VNṬ_22,2^1	 punar api paronyasya tad nimittasya abhāva ādityasya kadācid ayukta tāmbrūyāt iti āśaṅkate buddhi vyapadeśaḥ ityādinā ayam asya abhisandhiḥ buddhi vyapadeśa artha kriyābhyaḥ sakāśāt tad vyavahāraḥ bhavati tathā hi tāḥ pravarttamāna avastu sattām sādhayanti tad bheda abhedau ca vastu bheda abhedau= iti āśayaḥ tāḥ ca nivarttamānāḥ sva nimittam sat vyavahāram nivartayanti agniḥ iva dhūmam tad nivṛtta auca asat vyavahāraḥ sat vyavahāra asat vyavahārayoḥ anyonya vyavaccheda sthita rūpa tvena eka tyāgasya apara upādānena antarīyaka tvāt 
VNṬ_22,2^2	 tatas ca buddhi ādi nivṛtta auca asat vyavahāra nimittam iti na idam yuktam vaktum anyasya ityādi atra api pratividhānam āha bhavatī tyādi yathā ukta pratibhāsā buddhiḥ pratipattṛ pratyakṣa pratibhāsi rūpa nirbhāsā yathā uktaḥ pratibhāsaḥ yasyāḥ iti vigrahaḥ uktañca yat anātma ityādinā tasyāḥ sakāśāt sat vyavahāraḥ bhavati sākṣāt vastu grahaṇāt tasya añca viparyayaḥ abhāvaḥ tasmin satya sat vyavahāraḥ bhavati satsu anyeṣu upalambha kāraṇeṣu iti vākya parisamāptiḥ kāryā anyathā saṃśaya utpatteḥ na hi vastu satvaḥ upalaṃbha pratyaya antarasākalye ca sā nivarttate iti niveditam etat puras asmābhiḥ iti bhāvaḥ 
VNṬ_22,2^3	 tavanena yadi evaṃvidhā buddhiḥ abhimatā tvayā tadā āvayoḥ aikamatyam eva tathā api na naḥ kiñcid aniṣṭam uktam syāta atha anyaḥ tadā vyabhicāraḥ iti darśayati tam eva vyabhicāran darśayan= āha pratyakṣa āviṣaya ityādinā liṅgāt jātāḥ liṅga jāḥ anumānam iti arthaḥ tasyāḥ sakāśāt sat vyavahāraḥ syāt parokṣe arthena kevalam anantara udita rūpāyāḥ sva grāhyaḥ iti apinā āha kim liṅga jāyāḥ sarvu asyāḥ sambhavati na iti āha kutaścid iti svabhāva kārya liṅga dvaya bala upajātāyāḥ iti arthaḥ anupalambhasya asat tā asat vyavahāra sādhaka tvāt iti bhāvaḥ 
VNṬ_22,2^4	 yadi nāma evam tatas katham vyabhicāraḥ iti ced āha asat vyavahāraḥ tu ityādi tad viparyaḥ iti tasyāḥ yathā ukta liṅga jāyā buddheḥ vinivṛttau= anaikāntikaḥ sandigdhaḥ iti arthaḥ kim kāraṇam viprakṛṣṭerthe deśa ādi viprakarṣaiḥ pratipattṛ pratyakṣasya pramāṇasya nivṛttau= api saṃśayāt kāraṇāt artha abhāvaḥ iti śeṣaḥ pratipattuḥ pratyakṣam iti ṣaṣṭhī samāsaḥ idañca prahīṇa sakala jñeya āvaraṇasya pratyakṣa nivṛttau tu asaṃdehaḥ eva iti kathanāya upāttam anyasya ca iti anumānasya āgamasya ca etat ca āgamasya prāmāṇyam abhyupagamya abhidhīyate na tu tasya prāmāṇyam asti 
VNṬ_23,1–23,3	 na antarīyaka tā bhāvāt śabdānām vastubhiḥ saha na artha siddhiḥ tatas te hi vaktṛ abhiprāya sūcakāḥ ḥ ityādi vacanāt ayam asya abhiprāyaḥ yadi nāma pramāṇa trayat nivṛttam apratyakṣa vastuni tathā api tat na asti iti kutoyat niścayaḥ tathā hi malaya na ganikuñja vartti dūrvvā pravāla patra prabhṛtayaḥ pramāṇa traya goca rabhāva atikrāntām mūrtim udvahantaḥ tiṣṭhanti na ca te na santi iti śakyam abhidhātum pramāṇa bhāvasya sakala viṣaya satva vyāpaka tva kāraṇa tva abhāvāt na ca tad rūpa vikala padārtha nivṛttau= anya nivṛtti niyamena ati prasaṅga doṣa upanipātāt itya āveditam etat purastāt yat āha śāstra adhikāra asambaddhāḥ bahavaḥ artha akṛta indriyāḥ aliṅgāḥ ca kathanta iṣām abhāvaḥ anupalambha tā iti 
VNṬ_24,1–24,2^1	 nanu ca atra liṅga jāyāḥ mateḥ asat vyavahāra hetuttvam niṣeddhum ārabdhantad viparyyayaḥ ityādi abhidhānāt tat kasmāt aprastutasya eva pratyakṣasya ca āgamasya ca upakṣepaḥ kṛtaḥ iti ced yuktam etat sarva pramāṇa nivṛtteḥ tu agamaka tva pradarśanena etad ekānta asambhava darśanāya uktam iti lakṣyate asya sudhiyaḥ abhisandhiḥ nanu idam uktam sat vyavahāra asat vyavahārayoḥ anyonya vyavaccheda sthita lakṣaṇa tve na eka abhāvasya apara bhāvanā antarīyaka tvāt viprakṛṣṭe tad nimitta abhāvāt sat vyavahāra nivṛttyā asat vyavahāraḥ iti satyam uktam eva etat na punar yuktam tathā hi parokṣe arthe sat vyavahāra nivṛttiḥ kathantad nimitta abha āvepi dvayoḥ api anayoḥ anupalabdhyoḥ sva viparyaya hetvabhāva bhāvābhyām sat vyavahāra pratiṣedha phala tvan tulyam ekatra saṃśayāt aparatra viparyayāt iti vacanāt saṃśayena iti ced yadi evam kathantarhi asat vyavahāra niścayaḥ tatra yuktim anupatati 
VNṬ_24,2^2	 yatra tu niścayena sat vyavahāra nivṛttiḥ tatra asat vyavahāra upi puktaḥ eva anyaḥ pravartana phalosi iti ukteḥ na ca abhāva rūpa vyavacchede bhāva anuṣaṅga usti niyamena na hi bandhyā tanaya nabhaḥ paṅkaja ādiṣu asat avasthatā bhavati pratiṣedhāt sat avastha tā bhavati pratiṣedha m ātrantu syāt tayoḥ ranyonya vyavacchedena avasthānāt tathā atra api apratyakṣe sat vyavahāra pratiṣedhāt na vidhi bhūtā sat vyavahāra anuṣaṅgaḥ tad vyavaccheda m ātrantu syāt tad bhāvasya tad bhāvasya anyonya parihāreṇa avasthita tvāt uktañca etat amala nyāya tatva prabodha udgata prajñā loka tiraskṛta aśeṣa paratīrthya pravāda dhvāntena dharma kīrtinā eva anitya nirātma tā ādi vyavacchedepi tat ca syāt ityādi na ityāḥ tāntāvat 
VNṬ_24,3^1	 adhunā sāmānya bhūtānām buddhi vyapadeśānām sat vyavahāra hetu tvam api na asti iti kathayan= āha na ca ityādi tatra ca yathākramam abhisambandhaḥ te sarvve buddhi vyapadeśāḥ na vastu sattām sādhayanti teṣām vā bheda abhedau na vastu bheda abhedayoḥ sattā sadbhāvam iti sarvu agrahaṇam kecid tu sādhayanti eva iti pradarśanāya kutas etat iti āha asatsu api atīta anāgata ādiṣu vṛtteḥ iti kriyā padam ādi śabdena vyoma utpala ādayaḥ parigṛhyante kathampunar viṣayam antareṇa teṣu teṣām vṛttiḥ yuktā iti ced āha kathaṃcid ta drūpa unubhavāhita vāsanā paripāka prabhāvāt iti arthaḥ teṣāñca vastu pratibandha abhāvāt iti bhāvaḥ 
VNṬ_24,3^2	 śaṅkha cakravartī ityādinā prakāreṇa tat anena vastu sattām sādhayanti iti etasya kāraṇam āha na anā ekām artha kriyā aṅka rtuṃśīlam yeṣām te tathā uktāḥ teṣu api ca vṛtteḥ kāraṇāt kimartham teṣu teṣām vṛttiḥ tad bhāva khyāpanāya teṣān nā anaika artha kriyā kāriṇā ambhāvaḥ tasya khyāpanāya nānā artha kriyā kāritvasya eka artha kriyā kāri tvasya ca kathana artham iti yāvat asti eva tarhi tasya vastunaḥ tatvam iti atas āha nānā eka ātma tāyāa bhāvepi tasya vastunaḥ iti adhyāhartavyam nānā eka rūpāṇa ambuddhi vyapadeśānām tat anena na vastu bheda abhedau sādhayanti iti sādhayati idam eva nidarśana pradarśanena saphalīkaroti rājā mahā sammataḥ idam atīta vṛtteḥ udāharaṇam 
VNṬ_24,3^3	 yathā iti ca adhyāhāryam śaṅkha cakravartī ityādi anutpanna vṛtteḥ śabdaiḥ viṣāṇam ityādi yadā upāttasya rūpam sa nidarśanañcakṣuḥ vijñāna janaka tvāt sa pratighaḥ ca sva deśe para utpatti pratibandhāt etat nānā artha kriyā kāriṣu vṛtteḥ iti etasya nidarśanam yasmāt tad cakṣuḥ vijñāna ādi kārya janaka tvāt eka rūpam api nānā rūpaiḥ sa nidarśana ādi śabdaiḥ viṣayīkriyate tasmāt na te vastu bheda sādhanāya alam ghaṭaḥ ca iti etat eka artha kriyā kāriṣu iti etasya udāharaṇan tathā hi bahavaḥ rūpa gandha rasa sparśā udaka dhāraṇa viśeṣa ādi kārya nirvarttana samartha tvāt abhinna samaiḥ taiḥ viṣaya tvena ātma sāktriyante tatas te nābha idam sādhayitum kṣamāḥ 
VNṬ_24,3^4	 tat ca atīta anāgata śaśa viṣāṇa ādiṣu tad pratipattiḥ na vastu sādhayati iti atipratītam etat atha katham idaṅgamyate sa nidarśana ādi buddhi śabdāna vastu bhedam sādhayanti iti atas prāha na hītyā di kasmāt eva atra vastuni rūpa ādau= upasaṃhārāt sa nidarśanam sa pratigham rūpam iti eva samāna adhikaraṇa tvāt itiyāvat anyathā bhinna adhikaraṇa tvāt vakula utpala kamala mālatī mallikā ādi śabdānām eva sāmānādhikaraṇyam eva na bhavet iti bhāvaḥ kaṇa bhakṣa akṣapāda mata anusāriṇaḥ tu mithyā darśana anurāga janita asat vikalpa mala upalipta antar locanāḥ sañcakṣate nānā viṣaya tvepi abhyupagamyamāne teṣām ekatra upasaṃhāraḥ aviruddhaḥ eva tad nimittānāṃsa nidarśana ādīn ān tatra rūpa ādau samavāyāt iti 
VNṬ_26,1	 tat etat sarvam eṣām avicārita ramaṇīya tayā vicāra vimardī kṣam atvāt paṇḍita jana hāsa kāri darśanam iti abhiprāyavāḥ na āha āyāse vatāya mityā di vata śabdaḥ anukaṃpāyāṅ kā asau= iti āha anekam sambandhinam sa nidarśana tva ādikam upakṛtya anupakāre tena teṣān tatra sambandhi tva ayogāt iti abhiprāyaḥ anekam sa nidarśana ādi śabdam tebhyaḥ sambandhibhyaḥ śaka asakāśāt ātmani saṃmārgayan= idama āyāsapatane kāraṇam 
VNṬ_26,2	 nanu sarūpa ādi bhāvaḥ yaiḥ śakti bhedaiḥ aneka sambandhinam upakaroti taiḥ eva śakti bhedaiḥ anekam buddhi ādi śabdam kinna utthāpayati yadi punar evam bhavet tadākaḥ guṇaḥ labhyate iti āha evam hayanena paramparā anusāra śramaḥ parihṛtaḥ bhavati iti śakti bhedaiḥ sambandhinam upakaroti tebhyaḥ ca śabdāḥ pravartanta iti ayamparampara anusaraṇa āyāsaḥ anena tapasvinā rūpa ādinā tyaktaḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ 
VNṬ_26,3^1	 nanu ca pratiniyatopi kārya śaktimantaḥ sarvvaḥ eva bhāvāḥ tvayā api etat avaśyam eva abhyupeyam anyathā kasmāt śāli bījaṃśālī aṅkuram eva utpādayati na yava aṅkura miti pareṇa abhiyuktena kim abhidhānīyam bhāva prakṛtim muktvā tasmāt tava padārtha prakṛti samāśrayaṇam eva śaraṇam anyathā asya doṣasya pariharttum aśakyatvāt etat ca na mama api rāja kula nivāritam tathā hi śakyam etatmayā api abhidhātum aneka sambandhi upakāraḥ eva tasya sāmarthyam nānā eka śabda utthāpanam iti ced satyam evam etat evantu manyate na tāvat sa nidarśana tva ādayaḥ santi krama yaugapadyābhyām artha kriyā tu anuprayogāt 
VNṬ_26,3^2	 upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta anāñca anupalambhāt na ca upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam sat anupalabhyamānam asti iti śakyate vaktum atiprasaṅgāt anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tāyām vā katham tad nibandhanāḥ pratyaya vyapadeśāḥ pravarttante go gavaya ādiṣu etena upalabdhānām api kṣaṇika tva ādi vat vyakti vyatiriktena anupalakṣaṇam pratyakṣam yasmāt sāmānyam yadi dṛṣṭam api avikalam bhinnam na saṃlakṣate bhāve tad bala bhāvinī bhavati sāyā śabda vṛttiḥ katham daṇḍya ādau na nibandhanasya na gatau dhī śabdayoḥ asti sā tasmāt asya kathañcid eva tat api te yuktyā na saṅgacchate 
VNṬ_27,1–27,3	 kiñca bhāvānām aikadeśyam prasajati bhavataḥ darśane sarvathā eṣām sattā deśāt abhedāt sakṛt idam athavā bhinna deśe nivṛttam vṛttau vā anekam etat na hi bhavati sakṛt sarvu athāḥ vṛtti bhājāṃtāla ādīnām phalānām bahuṣu bahuvidheṣu āśrayeṣu eka bhāvaḥ satve vā teṣāt na buddhi śabda utthāpana sāmarthyam anvaya vyatirekābhyām avadhāryate atas eva anupalabhyamāna tvāt pācaka ādiṣu api ca tad vyatirekeṇa api teṣām bhāvāt upapāditañca etat 
VNṬ_27,4–27,5	 pācaka ādiṣu abhinnena vinā api arthena vācakaḥ bhedāt na hetuḥ karma asya na jātiḥ karma saṃśrayāḥ ityādinā iti na iha ucyate na ca teṣām upakārya tvam asti nityatayā anādheya atiśaya tvāt na ca puruṣa abhiprāya anapekṣaḥ vyakti upakṛta sapratigha tva ādi sāmānya sāmarthya bhāvena upaneyaḥ vivakṣāya antu saṃmukhībhāvepi pravṛtti prāptaḥ puruṣa abhiprāya anurūpe vā saḥ eva astu niyāmakaḥ kim antar gaṃtṛbhiḥ sāmānyaiḥ tathā hi tad gata anvaya vyatireka anuvidhāna mā iva lakṣyate sāmānyānām na nityānām avyatireka tvāt 
VNṬ_27,6	 tasmāt sarvvam etat kudarśana samāśrayeṇa kalpanā mātram kalpanā casā eva kartavyā yā punar nna paryanuyogam arhati tatratyām kalpanāyām varam eva kalpanā doṣa abhāvāt guṇa sadbhāvāt ca iti syāt matam yuktā eva iyam kalpanā nahi ekasya nānā arthaka śabda utthāpane sāmarthyam asti iti yadi evam atra api brūmaḥ iti āha nānā śabda utthāpana asāmarthye nānā sambandhi upakāra upi mābhūt iti ekasya aneka upakāraka tva virodha abhyupagamāt iti abhisandhiḥ nitya tvāt sambandhinām anupakāraḥ abhyupetaḥ eva iti ced āha anupakāre hi teṣām sa nidarśana tva ādīna antena aṅgī kriyamāṇe tad sambandhitā na sidhyati na hi yaḥ yena na upakriyate heduḥ sa tasya samvandhi yuktaḥ himavā niva malaya gireḥ iti bhāvaḥ evantā vat para pakṣa nirākaraṇena sa nidarśana ādi śabdānām abhinna viṣaya tvam sādhitam te eva jaḍimnaḥ padam udvahantaḥ punar api paryanuyuñjate 
VNṬ_28,1	 nanu bhavatu nāmasa nidarśana ādi śabdānām abhinna viṣaya tvam atha katham avasīyate ghaṭa paṭa ādi śabdānām aneka artha viṣaya tvam iti yāvatā rūpa ādi vyatiriktam anyat eva avayavi dravyam asti tat eva ca ghaṭa paṭa ādi śabdaiḥ viṣayīkriyate tathā hi vicāra viṣaya āpannaḥ paṭaḥ tantubhyaḥ vyatiricyate bhinna kartṛka tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat tathā samasta vyasta pratyaya aviṣaya tvāt gavā ādi vat na hi tantavaḥ tantu samudāyaḥ iti vā paṭe pratyayaḥ duṣṭaḥ upāya antara sādhyat tvāt ca ghaṭa ādi vat bhinna deśa avasthitaiḥ ca kriyamāṇattvāt ghaṭa ādi vat eva bhinna parimāṇat tvāt ca vakula āmalaka bimba ādi vat atas ca pūrvva uttara kāla bhā vit tvāt bīja aṅkura ādi vat athavā paṭāt anye tantavaḥ tad kāraṇattvāt turya ādi vat tantu paṭayoḥ vā anyat tvam bhinna śaktimat tvāt jala anala ādi vat tathā idam aparam vicāra viṣaya āpannam indīvaraṅgandhā ādibhyaḥ atyanta bhinnanteṣām vyavacchedaka tvāt caitra ādi vat iha yadi asya vyavaccheda kantat tasmāt anyat tat yathā gopiṇḍāt caitraḥ iti etāni tad vyatireka sādhana pramāṇāni santi tat kathanta iṣām bhinna viṣaya tvam bhaviṣyati iti 
VNṬ_28,2^1	 tat etat api eṣām asat darśana abhiniveśa paṭala pracchādita antaḥkaraṇānām na alpīyasaḥ tamasaḥ durvilasitam iti āgūrya āha ghaṭaḥ iti api ca rūpa ādayaḥ eva eka artha kriyā kāriṇaḥ eka śabda vācyāḥ bhavantu kimartha antara kalpanayā iti kāryam iti upaskriyate na eva kiñcittasya tādṛśasya nīla ādi vyatirekeṇa anupalakṣaṇāt itya ākūtam asya yāni tu etāni tad pratipādanāya pramāṇāni uktāni tāni asiddha tā ādi doṣa duṣṭa tvāt nālam tad bheda sādhanāya iti bhotā nāma iva puratas chāyān dadhati iti manyate tathā hi na idam tāvat ādyam pramāṇam parīkṣyamāṇam pūrvvām api parīkṣām kṣamate yatotra vikalpa dvayam āvirbhavati anya avasthā avasthitebhyaḥ vā tantubhyaḥ paṭasya anya tvam sādhyate viśiṣṭa saṃsthāna avasthitebhyaḥ vā iti tatra na tāvat ayam ādyaḥ prakāraḥ sahate vicāra bhāra gauravam siddha sādhana tā doṣa anuṣaṅgāt yasmāt samadhigata samasta vastuyāthātathya su gata samaya naya samāśraya pravṛtti bala āsādita avadāta matayaḥ prasava anantara nirodha bhājaḥ sarvu abhāva aiti prakalpayanti 
VNṬ_28,2^2	 tatas ca tebhya unyat tvam iṣṭam eva iti siddha sādhya tā prasaṅga upanipāta piśācaḥ katham iva bhavantam na gṛhaṇāti dvitīya upi vikalpaḥ tīvra anala upataptaḥ iva upala tale talāni pādānām na pratiṣṭhām samāsādayam ti hetoḥ param pratyasiddha tvāt na hi viśiṣṭa sthāna avasthitebhyaḥ paṭasya bhinna kartṛka tvam param prati siddha paddhatim avatarati yohi tādṛś prakārebhyonya tvam abhāvāt eva na abhyupaiti sa katham iva bhinna kartṛka tvam abhyupagamiṣyati iti tad anantara abhihitam api pramāṇena samabhilaṣita manoratha paripūraṇāya alam hetu asiddheḥ yatas paṭaḥ iti tantuṣu eva sanniveśa viśeṣeṇa avasthiteṣu pratyayaḥ vartate tad vivikta rūpasya atyantam unmiṣita cakṣuṣā api adarśanāt sphaṭika ādau dṛṣṭam iti ced etat uttaratra niṣetsyāmaḥ yat tu idam upāya antara sādhya tvāt bhinna deśa avasthitaiḥ kriyamāṇa tvāt bhinna parimāṇa tvāt pūrva uttara kāla bhāvit tvāt bhinna śaktima tvāt ca iti 
VNṬ_29,1–29,3^1	 atra prathama sādhana abhihita vikalpa doṣaḥ tīvra āmarśa virakta locanaḥ iva arātiḥ tad sampadan na sahate prathame siddha sādhya tvam dvitīye hetu asiddha tā kṣaṇika tvāt viśiṣṭānām utpāda ubhim ataḥ yatas ḥ iti saṅgrahaślokaḥ yat ca id am uktam vicāra viṣayā pannam indīvaram ityādi tat api na saṅgacchate yasmāt indīvarasya gandhādayaiti in dīvara svabhāvāḥ gandha ādayaḥ madhu bhāvanā viśeṣa ādi kārya nirvarttana samarthāḥ iti yāvat aviśiṣṭa kārya sādhana ātmanā sāmānya bhūta gandha ādi śabdaiḥ prasiddha aviśiṣṭa kārya sādhana ākhyena viśeṣeṇa ye viśiṣṭāḥ te evam ucyante na punar atra anyat kiñcid iti artha āvarṇita lakṣaṇam dravyam asti tasya tādṛśaḥ anupalabdheḥ iti ukta prāyam tathā ca anena prakāreṇa teṣān tat vyavacchedakam bhavati iti teṣa anta dvyacchedakam ca na ca atyantaṃbhinnam iti kaḥ anayoḥ virodhaḥ iti sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttikaḥ hetuḥ pratibandha asiddhaḥ na hi dṛṣṭānta mātrāḥ tiddhiḥ asti sarvu asiddhi prasaṅgāt api ca śilāpu trakasya śarīram 
VNṬ_29,3^2–29,4	 rūpasya svabhāvaḥ iti atra api śilā putraka rūpayoḥ śarīra svabhāva vyavacchedaka tvam asti iti bhedaḥ tayoḥ api tatas prasajate na ca bhavati naiḥsvābhāvya prasaṅgāt tasmāt ayam etena anaikāntikaḥ sphuṭam eva bhavadbhiḥ abhidhānīyaḥ kiñca idam ati vikalaiḥ mithyā darśana saṃrāga piśāca āviṣṭa buddhibhiḥ kim indīvarasya gandhādaya iti ete śabdāḥ puruṣa abhiprāya vyāpāra nirapekṣāḥ eva vastu tatva nibandhanāḥ pravarttante kim vā yathā eva taiḥ prayujyante tathā eva vastutatvam anapekṣya tam artham asatkāreṇa pratipādayanti iti yadi ādyaḥ pakṣaḥ tadā sadādhvanana prasaṅgaḥ atīta ādiṣu anyatra ca puruṣe cchāvaśān niyojanan= abhavet na ca pravacana antara bhedeṣu artheṣu pravṛttiḥ prāpnoti na ca kasyāścid vācaḥ asatya artha tā syāt atha uttaraḥ tadā yeṣām vastu vaśāḥ vācaḥ na vivakṣā para āśrayāḥ ṣaṣṭhi vacana bheda ādi ca udyantān prati yuktimat yat āhuḥ yat yathā vācaka tvena vaktṛbhiḥ viniyamyate anapekṣita vāhaya arthantat tathā vācakamvacaḥ 
VNṬ_29,5^1	 tadā na puruṣa icchā bala pravṛtta śabda vaśāt arthata tvam vyavatiṣṭhate iti tada vasthaṃsan digdha vipakṣa vyatireka tvam hetoḥ iti etena etat api pratyuktam vipratipatti viṣaya āpannāt candanāt anye rūpa rasa gandha sparśāḥ heya tva ādayaḥ ca iti pratijānīmahe navī apadiśyamāna tvāt śilā tulā āḍhaka prasevikā vat iti tasmāt tad bhāva pratipādanāya na kiñcid pramāṇam asti iti sthitam etat asmākantu tad abhāva pramāṇa sādhakam pramā ṇam etat ye paraspara vyāvartta māna svabhāva avasthiti samāliṅgita śarīrāḥ te vyatirikta avaya vi dravya anugata mūrttim ātma atiśayam na ātmaśātkurvanti yathā bahavaḥ bhasma ādhārana lālā athūka ādayaḥ tathā ca yathā upadiṣṭa dharmavantaḥ tantu ādayaḥ iti svabhāva hetuḥ vaidharmyeṇa nabhaḥ paṅkaja ādayaḥ teṣān niḥsvabhāva tvāt paraspara vyāvarttamānānām apiyadi eka svabhāva anabhyupagame tasya teṣu sarvu ātmanā anyathā vā vṛtti ayogaḥ bādhakampramāṇam 
VNṬ_29,5^2	 kutas tat hi yugapad anekatra sarvu ātmanā varttamānam aneka ādhāra sthita ādheya vat anekattvam ātmanaḥ a numāpayati iti katham asya abhinna svabhāva tā yojyate eka avayava upalambha velā yāñca sakalasya tatra parisamāpta tvāt upalabdhi prasaṅgaḥ aneka avayava upalabdhi dvāreṇa upalambha katipaya avayava darśanepi syāt samasta avayava upalambha dvāreṇa upalabdhau sarvu akālam adarśana prasaṅgaḥ tasya ambha asvara madhya bhāgānām sakṛt anupalambhāt eka avayava kampe ca sarvu akampa ādi prasaṅgaḥ ca vācyaḥ na api eka deśena sāvayava tva prasaṅgāt eka deśān āñca anavasthā prasaṅgāt tepi hi tasya avayavāḥ iti pāṇi avayava vṛtteṣu api anyena varttitavyam ityādinā tad anya eka deśa abhāvavān ekaḥ kaścid avayavī vidyate tathā ca aṇu ādi samudāyaḥ eva astu konurodhaḥ sva ātma bhūteṣu avayaveṣu iti na vā kvacid api asau vṛttaḥ na hi eka deśāḥ pratyekam avayavī iti alam pratiṣṭhita mithyā pralāpaiḥ iti viramyate 
VNṬ_29,6^1	 tat evam etat parama tamalam ālā ucyamāna tīvratara arkka raśmi saṃpāta yogi hima śaila śilā śakala vat vilayam upayāti iti manyamānaḥ prāha kimartha antara kalpanayā iti sya āt i yattara āśā parasya na eva anekasya eka artha kriyā kāri tvam asti iti atas āha bahavaḥ pi hi ityādi kiṃvat cakṣuḥ ādi vat yathā rūpa āloka manaskāra cakṣuḥ ādayaḥ cakṣuḥ ādi vijñānam ekaṃrva kuvnti tathā rūpādayā upi udaka dhāraṇa viśeṣa ādikām ekām artha kriyā aṅkariṣyanti iti arthaḥ yatas ca etat evam tasmāt tasya eka artha kriyā sāmarthyasya khyāpanāyatatra rūpa ādau= ekasya paṭa ādi śabdasya niyogopi syāt iti etat yuktam paśyāmaḥ na kevalam ekārtha kriyā kāri tvam teṣām iti apiśabdena āha katham yuktam iti ced evam manyatekenacid prayojanena kecid śabdāḥ kvacid niveśyante tatra yat anekam ekatra upayujyate tat avaśyantatra codanīyam 
VNṬ_29,6^2	 tasya ca pṛthak kathañcodane ati gauravam syāt na ca asya ananya sādhāraṇam rūpam śakyam codayitum na api asya āyāsasya kiñcid sāphalyam kevalam anena yogyāḥ tatra terthāḥ codanīyāḥ ta ekena vā śabdena codyeran bahubhiḥ vā iti svātantryam atra vaktuḥ tat iyam ekā śrutiḥ bahuṣu vaktrabhiprāya vaśāt pravarttamānā na upālambham arhati na ca iyam aśakya pravarttamānāḥ icchā adhīna tvāt yadi hi na prayoktuḥ icchā katham iyam ekatra api vartteta icchāyām vā kaḥ enām bahuṣu api pratibaddhum samarthaḥ prayojana abhāvāt apravarttanam iti api na aśaṅkanīyam bhinneṣu api ekasmāt śabdāt pratītiḥ a tad prayojana bhedena yathā syāt iti ukta tvāt prayojanasya tasmāt su uktam asmābhiḥ yuktam paśyāmaḥ iti 
VNṬ_29,6^3	 yathā kathañcid vinā eva prayojanena lokaḥ śabdaṃprayuṃkte tatas na yuktam etat iti ced āha na ca niḥ prayojanāḥ lokasya artheṣu śabda yojane ti na hi vyasanam eva etat lokasya yat ayam asaṅgatam yat na prayujjānaḥ vā śabda antar khalu āsīt kintarhi sarvvaḥ eva asya ārambhaḥ prayojana sāpekṣaḥ prayojanañcetat ukta miti manyate tatra prayojanava tvena iti yathā rūpa gandha rasa ādayaḥ saha eka prayojanāḥ saṅkali tāḥ eka kārya kāriṇaḥ iti arthaḥ samavahitānām api kadācid kasyacid eva kārye vyāpāronyasya tu audāsīnyam itisyāt āśaṅkā saṃbhavaḥ tatas āha pṛthak vā iti vā śabdaḥ ca arthe sarvvaḥ eva vyāpāravantaḥ iti arthaḥ anye tu anyathā vyākhyānayanti vyākhyānañca ādaḥ dūṣayanti 
VNṬ_29,6^4	 tatra etasmin śabdaiḥ artha pratyāyana krame yerthāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ saha pṛthak vaika prayojanāḥ teṣām rūpa ādīnām saṃhitānām pṛthu budhnā udara ākāra saṃsthāpitānām ekam prayojanam yat uta madhu udaka ādi āharaṇam pṛthak vāteṣām eva pratyekam su ākāra jñāna jananam ekañca tad prayojanam ekatra dṛṣṭam yat tat anyatra na asti iti saha bhūtānām api kadācid audāsīnya darśanāt sarveṣām savya apāra tām ādarśayitum pṛthak vā iti abhihitam vā śabdaḥ ca samuccayaḥ iti anye kevalam atra eka prayojanāḥ iti abhidhānāt sarveṣān tathā bhāva pratītiḥ asti eva iti vyartham pṛthak vā iti syāt na ca ayam śabda arthaḥ iti yaktiñcid etat taiḥ prakaraṇam na lakṣitam tathā hi atra samudāya śabdasya eka vacana pravṛtyavirodhaḥ kathayitum ārabdhaḥ tatra kaḥ prastāvaḥ pṛthak va iti abhidhānasya 
VNṬ_32,1	 kevalam rūpa ādi śabdaḥ ca ayañjāti śabdaḥ tatra ca anya adṛśyā iva prakriyā bhaviṣyati yat tu idam uktam kevalam atra eka prayojanāḥ iti abhidhānāt sarvu eṣām tathā abhāva pratītiḥ asti eva iti tat api na yukti saṅgatam tathā hi para bala parājaya udyatānām eka prayojanavatu epi na tatra sarvve vyāpāravantaḥ bhavanti tadvat atra api bhavet atas eva ca syāt āśaṅkā sambhavaḥ iti vyākhyātam yadā tu sarvu eṣām eva sa vya apāra tā khyāpanāya pṛthak vā iti etat ucyate tadā apahnu ratam utsāryate tat etena eva aśabda artha tvam api pratyuktam iti yaktiñcid etat eva 
VNṬ_32,2^1	 astu vā etat api vyākhyānam yadi kathañcid vyavasthāpitum pāryate teṣā mevam vidhānām arthānāntasya eka artha kriyā kāriṇaḥ bhāvasya khyāpanāya ekoghaṭa ādi śabdaḥ yadi niyujyeta tadā kim syāt na kaścid doṣaḥ syāt guṇaḥ eva tu kevalaḥ labhyate iti āha tad artha kriyā śakte rabhinnāyāḥ khyāpanāya niyuktasya samudāya śabdasya eka vacana virodhopi na asti eva kutas yasmāt sa hitānām sā śaktiḥ ekā abhinnā na pratyekam na tu pṛthak bhūtānām iti arthaḥ iti tasmāt samudāya śabde tasmin= aikasmin ghaṭā dausamudāye vācye eka vacanam ghaṭaḥ iti bhavati iti śeṣaḥ 
VNṬ_32,2^2	 syāt iti vā vakṣyamāṇam kriyā padam nanvayaṅghaṭa ādi śabdaḥ gavā ādi śabda vat jāti śabdaḥ tat katham etat uktam iti ced satyam samudāya antara vṛti apekṣayā jāti śabda uyam rūpa ādi samudāyi apekṣayā tu samudāya śabda upi iti abhisandheḥ adoṣaḥ tathā hi trayī ā iva gatiḥ śabdānāṅkecit jāti śabdāḥ eva yathā sukha ādi śabdāḥ sukha ādeḥ anavayava tvāt kecid tu samudāya śabdāḥ eva yathā vindhya himavat sumeḥ u ādi śabdāḥ tad jātīya samudāya antara abhāvāt apare punar jāti samudāya śabdāḥ yathā ete eva ghaṭa ādi śabdāḥ samudāya antara samudāyi apekṣayā iti 
VNṬ_32,2^3	 evantā vat samudāya śabdeṣu vacana pravati avirodhaḥ uktaḥ atha kathan jāti śabdeṣu iti āha jāti śabdeṣu ityādi arthānām ghaṭāvīnām pratyekam sahitānāñca śakteḥ kāraṇāt nānā śaktiḥ ekā ca etat uktam bhavati yasmāt ekaḥ pi vṛkṣaḥ gṛha karaṇa ādi artha kriyā nirvarttanepi yogyaḥ bahavopi vṛkṣāḥ tatas ca teṣa aṅkevalānām api yogya tvāt anekā śaktiḥ samavahitānām api yogya tvāt ekā śaktiḥ eka pratyavamarśa pratyaya nibandhana tvena ekatva upacārāt yatas ca evam iti tasmāt yathākramam nānā śakti vivakṣāyām satyām bahuvacanam aneka tvāt śakteḥ vṛkṣāḥ iti bhavati 
VNṬ_32,2^4	 eka śakti vivakṣāya antu eka tvāt śabdaḥ eka vacana muktaḥ iti syāt tadā yadi eṣa niyamaḥ bhavadbhiḥ asat graha graha āveśa vyākulita cetobhiḥ iṣyate bahuṣu eva vācyeṣu bahuvacanam bhavati ekasmin= eva ca eka vacanam iti tat anena yadā api etat darśanam āśrīyate bahuṣu vahu vacanam bhavati dvi ekayoḥ dvivacana eka vacane iti tadā api na kaścid doṣaḥ iti darśayati bhavatā antu katham iti āha asmākam ityādi saṃketa baśāt śabdānāmbahuvacana antānān dārāḥ sikatāḥ pādāḥ guravaḥ ityādinā asati api bahu tve abhidheyasya vṛttiḥ 
VNṬ_33,1^1	 tathā asati api aneka tva īṣaṇṇa garī ṣaṣ pūlī vanam iti ādinā eka vacana antānām vṛttiḥ iti anabhiniveśaḥ eva kaḥ hi nāma sa cetanaḥ puruṣa abhiprāya mātra adhīna vṛttiṣu śabdeṣu abhiniveśam karttum utsahate iti bhāvaḥ para pakṣam pūrvapakṣayati na anekaḥ rūpa ādiḥ eka śabda utthāpane samarthaḥ iti ce diti na hi anekasya ekena sambandhaḥ yujyate iti kimi tyādinā parihāraḥ puruṣāṇām vṛttiḥ icchā tatra anapekṣāḥ santaḥ arthāḥ kim svayam śabdān utthāpayanti āhosvit puruṣaiḥ te vyavahāra artham artheṣu yathā kathañcid niyujyante iti vikalpa dvayam tatra puruṣaiḥ eva te yatheṣṭam niyujyante anyathā atītāḥ jātayoḥ darśana antara bhediṣu anyatra vā niyojanan na bha vediti bhāvaḥ 
VNṬ_33,1^2	 tatas ca svayam puruṣa icchā anapekṣāṇām arthānām śabda utthāpane sati bhāvasya śaktiḥ aśaktiḥ vā cintyeta nāma ekaḥ ityādinā asti eva tarhi svayam uttthāpanam iti ced āha na ca tat yuktam anantara uktāt kāraṇa trayāt iti abhiprāyaḥ tasmāt puruṣaiḥ teṣām śabdānām niyoga ūrtheṣu vinā api eka tva ādinā te puruṣāḥ yatheṣṭam ekatra api vahu vacana antam anekatra api ekavacana antam śabdam niyuñjīran= iti kaḥ tatra teṣu śabdeṣu upālambhaḥ na anekaḥ rūpa ādiḥ eka śabda utthāpane samartha iti ayam na eva kaścid kevala m ati bahula vyā moha vijṛmbhitam iti manyate syāt mataṅkim iti ekam śabdam anekatra niyuñjate iti āha nimitañca niyogasya uktam eva iti tad sāmarthya khyāpanāya tatra eka śabda niyogaḥ api syāt iti atra avasare 
VNṬ_33,1^3	 upacayam āha api ca ityādinā āśraya abhimatena iti avayavi dravyeṇa teṣa an tatra samavāya sambandhena sambandhāt katham sambandhaḥ na eva anekasya ekena saha sambandhaḥ virodha abhyupagamāt anyathā ekena śabdena api saha prāpnoti iti abhisandhiḥ paraḥ prāha na ce dayam ekena saha sambandha virodhāt kāraṇā deka śabdam rūpa ādiṣu na icchāmaḥ kintu a bhinnānām aviśiṣṭānām rūpa ādīna aṃghaṭa kambala paryaṅka ādiṣu nānāvidhā yā iyam artha kriyā jala dhāraṇa prāvaraṇa ādiḥ tasyāḥ virodhaḥ tathā ca tad sāmarthya khyāpanāya śabdasya virodhāt teṣāñcābhedaḥ tad āśraya dravya bheda abhāvāt etat eva sphuṭayati 
VNṬ_33,1^4	 te rūpa ādayaḥ e ka svabhāvāḥ santaḥ samudāya antare kamvala ādau yā iyam asambhāvinī udaka dhāraṇa viśeṣa ādi artha kriyā tām eva kuryuḥ tena kāraṇena tasyāḥ artha kriyāyāḥ prakāśanāya imām ete artha kriyām na te tad asambhāvinīm artha kriyā aṅkurvanti yathā te eva kambala gatāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ sajātīyebhyaḥ tathā ca ghaṭa gatāḥ api rūpa ādayaḥ kambala gatebhyaḥ rūpa ādibhyaḥ aviśiṣṭa svabhāvāḥ iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ evam anyatra apiyojyam iti iyam pūrvva pakṣa racanā atra uttaram āha bhavatu nāma ityādinā tat anena hetoḥ asiddhim udbhāvayati ayam atra arthaḥ na hi rūpa ādīnāṅ kambala ādiṣu abheda usti paraspara rūpa viviktānām eva pratyakṣa pramāṇa paricchedyat tvāt evañca sati idam pratyakṣam kim ena āmvāñchām upekṣate kimpraśne kṣepe vānā eva kṣantum arhati apākaroti iti 
VNṬ_33,1^5	 kiṃñca aniṣṭañceda masmābhiḥ ghaṭa kambala ādiṣu abhinnāḥ rūpa ādayaḥ iti kuto rūpa ādīnām pratisamudāyat tve hetu balāt anapekṣita dravyāṇām sva bheda abhyupagamāt tad anena abhyupagama dvāreṇa api asiddha tāñcodayati pūrvveṇa pratyakṣa dvāreṇa iti viśeṣaḥ punar api īrṣyāluḥ paraḥ prāha yadi anyaḥ eva rūpa ādibhyaḥ ghaṭaḥ syāt kim syāt iti na kaścid doṣaḥ syāt iti ākūtam na vayam mātsaryāt tam na icchāmaḥ kintu bhavati etāvat tvatra vaktavī asti iti āha tasya avayavinaḥ pratyakṣasya sataḥ cakṣuḥ sparśana indriya grāhya tayā abhyupagatattvāt arūpa ādi rūpasya rūpa gandha ādi svabhāva rahitasya iti arthaḥ guṇa dravyayoḥ bheda abhyupagamāt 
VNṬ_33,1^6	 tad vivekena rūpa ādi vivekena buddhau cakṣuḥ sparśana indriya jāyām pratibhāsane kim āvaraṇat na kaścid pratibandhaḥ iti arthaḥ na ca kaścid atyādareṇa apratihata karaṇa upi nirūpayat nīla madhura surabhi karkkaśa ādi vyatirekeṇa tad rūpam vivikta rūpam ghaṭa ādi dravyam upalabdhum īśaḥ iti manyate abiddhakarṇṇaḥ tu āha rūpa ādi agrahepi dravya grahaṇam asti eva yatas manda manda prakāśe a nupalabhyamāna rūpa ādikam dravyam upalabhyate aniścita rūpam gauḥ aśvaḥ vā iti nanu ca tatra api saṃsthāna mātram upalabhyate satyam upalabhyate na tu tad rūpa ādi ātmakam rūpa ādi ātmaka tve vā nīla pīta ādi viśeṣa grahaṇa prasaṅgaḥ tathā ayaskañcuka antargate puruṣe puruṣa rūpa ādi agrahepi puruṣa pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ rātrau ca valākā vyāmukta rūpa ādi agrahepi pakṣi pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ 
VNṬ_33,1^7	 tathā nīla ādi upadhāna bheda anuvidhāyinaḥ sphaṭika maṇeḥ sphaṭika rūpa ādi agrahepi sphaṭika pratyayaḥ tathā kaṣāya rūpeṇa paṭa rūpa abhibhave paṭa rūpa ādi agrahe api paṭa pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti tat etat sarvvam asya analpa kāla upacita kudarśana abhyāsa upajāta buddhi māndya vijṛmbhitam eva prakaṭayati vacaḥ tathā hi yat tāvat idam uktam manda mandāloke rātrau ca nīla ādi upadhāna sadbhāve ca tad rūpa ādi agrahepi dravyam upalabhyate iti tatra vaktavyam kīdṛśam tatra dravyam upalabhyate iti dṛśyate eva tat yādṛśam upalabhyate iti ced nanu śyāma rūpaṃmanda mandā loke rātrau ca tatra tat apulabhyate upadhānam rūpañca na ca tad rūpantat tādrūpye anantara udita pakṣa kṣaya prasaṅgāt 
VNṬ_33,1^8	 tad samīpa pārśva varttibhiḥ ca tathā anupa lambhāt na ca api anya ākāreṇa bodhena vastunaḥ avagatiḥ yasya kasyacid jñānasya sarvu avastu pariccheda kattva prasaṅgāt tasmāt bhrāntam etat jñānambhrānti vījāt sva upādānāt anādi ka ālīnāt nirviṣayam eva tathā pratibhāsi dvi candra ādi pratyaya vat upajāyate nirviṣayat tvepi pratiniyata deśa kāla bhāvi bhavati sva upādāna vāsanā prabodhaka bāhya adhipati pratyaya apekṣaṇāt dvi candra ādi jñāna vat eva bhrāntattva ipi artha avisamvādaḥ viśiṣṭa adhipati pratyaya sadbhāvāt maṇi prabhāyām maṇi bhrāntiḥ iva na ca artha avisamvādanāt eva asya sa viṣaya tvam yuktam anu mānena vyabhicārāt maṇi bhrāntyā ca tat eva dravyan tathā gṛhaṇāti tatonyasya nirviṣayat tvam iti ced 
VNṬ_33,1^9	 nanu na tat dravyantat rūpat na vāni ākāra anusyūtaḥ pratyayaḥ anyasya paricchedakaḥ iti uktam evañca sati sat viṣayat tve sati apekṣepi sat viṣayat tvam asti eva tathā hi samā api etat śakyam vaktuṃte eva nīla ādayaḥ tathā pratibhāsantaḥ iti asati bhrāṃti sandeha kāraṇe sa āloka avasthāyām yogya deśa avasthāne ca nirupadhāna avasthā yāñca na upalabhyate tat dravyam anātma rūpa pratibhāsi vivekena anyadā tu sati bhrānti sandeha kāraṇe niśā andhakāra avacchādita locana avasthāyām dūra deśa avasthāne sa upadhāna avasthāyāñca tad anya ākāra vivekena pratibhāsate iti konyaḥ bhautikāt vaktum arhati ayaskañcuka antargate puruṣa pratyayaḥ na pratyakṣaḥ kintarhi laigikaḥ 
VNṬ_33,1^10	 tathā hi puruṣa śarīra avayava samāśraya bala udbhūta viśiṣṭa saṃsthāna avasthita kañcuka darśanāt kārya liṃga jñānāt sambandha smaraṇa apekṣiṇaḥ kāraṇa bhūte tathāvidhe puṃsi puruṣoyam iti anantara mā iva pratyayaḥ samudbhūtim āsādayati atas eva ca aspaṣṭa ākārā sā pratītiḥ kaḥ ca ayam iti saṃśayaḥ ca bhavati tathāvidha saṃsthānasya ca kañcukasya uttpatteḥ puruṣa rūpa ādayaḥ eva hetavaḥ bhavanti na tu anyat avayavi dravyam tasya asiddheḥ asiddhasya ca kāraṇa tva abhyupagamā yogāt rūpa ādibhiḥ tu pratyakṣa anupalambhābhyāṅkārya kāraṇa bhāva siddheḥ teṣām eva kevalānān tathā sanniviṣṭānām upalambhāt paṭe tu kaṣāya mañjiṣṭhā ādi samparkāt artha antaram eva kevalantat tathā jātam īkṣyate na tu nānā rūpayoḥ dravyayoḥ saṃsargāt avibhāgāt tathā upalambhaḥ 
VNṬ_33,1^11	 punar tad dravya saṃsthāna sthiti kāraṇa vicchedāt tad nivṛttiḥ tad upādāna kāraṇa apekṣiṇaḥ ca jala pāvaka ādeḥ aparottpattiḥ iti etena ayaḥ golaka tad rūpa grahaṇepi tad pratyayaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ iti etat api pratisphuṭam tat evam dravyasya pratyakṣa tva asidheḥ yad uktaṅgava aśva mahiṣa varāha mātaṅga avimati adhikaraṇa bhāva āpannā rūpa ādi vyatiriktā iti eva ghoṣaṇā aindriyaka tve sati samasta rūpa ādi grāhaka vākya indriya anavacchedya tvāt prīti ādi vat iti tat apahastitam prayogāḥ punar yat dṛśyam sat sat vyatirekeṇa na upalabhyate tat tatas bhinnannābhyupeyat na asti iti vā abhyupagantavyam yathā nara śirasi viṣāṇanna upalabhyate ca dṛśyaṃsat nīla ādiṣu tad vyatirekeṇa sāmānya viśeṣa saṃyoga vibhāga paratva aparatva ādikam iti svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ
