VNṬ_33,1^12	 na asya siddhiḥ dṛśya tvena svayam abhyupagamāt tathārūpa ādi artha pañcaka vyatirikta tvena upagatam dravyan= a cakṣuḥ pratyaya avaseyam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta tvena upagata tve sati nīla ādi vastu rūpa virahāt śabda gandha rasa vat na ca tasmāt avyatiriktaḥ eva ayam tatra ca āyan doṣaḥ iti āgūrya āha sotiśayaḥ vyavaccheda lakṣaṇaḥ tasya atiśayavataḥ avasthātura ātma bhūtaḥ ananvayaḥ iti ekāntena nivartttamānaḥ vyāpaka tva abhāvāt pravartamānaḥ asan= ā iva kathat na svabhāva nānātvam sukha duḥkha dhīḥ ivākarṣati anvākarṣati eva iti arthaḥ prayogaḥ punar yaḥ yasya ātma bhūtaḥ sa tad nivṛttau= ekāntena nivarttate pravṛttau ca āsan= eva pravarttate yathā tasya eva atiśayasya ātmā 
VNṬ_33,1^13	 ātma bhūtaḥ ca atiśayasya atiśayavān iti svabhāva hetuḥ tatas ca tayoḥ avasthayoḥ avasthā āturnnānā tvam paraspara virodhi paryyādhyāsita tvāt sukha duḥkha vaditi svabhāva hetuḥ eva na vā sau= atiśayaḥ ananvayaḥ pravarttate nivarttate vā atas puru asmin pramāṇe sādhya vikala tvan dṛṣṭāntasya uttaratra tu asiddhiḥ hetoḥ iti ced āha sa anvaya tve ca atiśayasya nivṛtti pravṛtyoḥ aṃgīkriyamāṇe kā kasya nivṛttiḥ pravṛttiḥ vā iti na eva kācid kasyacid nivṛttiḥ pravṛttiḥ vā sarvasya sarvadā satvāt tathā ca sarvam sarvatra samupayujyeta ityādinā puronukrāntaḥ doṣonupayujyate iti abhiprāyaḥ upacayam āha yadi ca kasyacid svabhāvasya atiśaya ākhyasya pravṛttiḥ nivṛttiḥ vā iti svayam abhyanujñāyate tvayā 
VNṬ_33,1^14	 eka atiśaya nivṛtyā apara atiśaya uttpatyā vyavahāra bheda upagamāt iti abhidhānāt tat etat eva paraḥ tathāgata vacaḥ abhyāsa upajāta avadāta matiḥ bruvāṇaḥ na anumanyate bhadra mukhena bhavet evam yadi yathā āmayā pravṛtti nivṛttī abhyanujñāyete tathā tena api yāvatā asya niranvaya upajanana vināśa upagama sama tvād dravyasya āloka nīla ādi vat tad vyatirekeṇa apratibhāsanam abhinneṃdriya grāhya tvāt vā tadvat eva iti ataa āha pratibhāsamānāḥ ca vivekene dam nīlam idam surabhi madhuram karkaśam idam iti ca iti pratyakṣāḥ arthāḥ dṛśyante apṛthak deśa tvepi sati ke te rūpa ādayaḥ loka prasiddhyā ca id am uktat na tu teṣām abhinna deśa tvam asti sa pratighāḥ daśa rūpiṇaḥ iti vacanāt 
VNṬ_33,1^15	 tathā abhinna indriya grāhayatvepi vāta ātapa sparśa ādayaḥ iti yathākramam ca etat uttaram anena aikāntika tvam hetoḥ udbhāvayati upetya ca dharmi sambandham abhinna indriya grāhya tvasya vyabhicāraḥ uktaḥ na tu asau= asyā asti eka deśa asiddheḥ katham yatas na surabhi madhura ādayaḥ dravya grāhaka indriya grāhyāḥ sārva indriya tva prasaṅgāt dravyasya āloka nīla ādīnāṃ tu abhedaḥ eva yatas pradīpa ādi sannidhānāt prakāśa rūpāḥ eva tathāvidha svabhāva adhyāsita vapuṣaḥ te samudbhavanti na tu teṣām bhedaḥ asti iti sādhana vikalpa tā api dṛṣṭāntasya iti manyate tasmāt asya pratyakṣa tvam abhyupagacchadbhiḥ na bahis avaśyam rūpa ādi vivekena pratibhāsanam abhyupagantavyam anyathā pratyakṣa tva asiddheḥ 
VNṬ_33,1^16	 kutas yasmāt idam eva ityādi su bodham ayampunar ghaṭa ādiḥ bhavat bhīrūpa ādi vyatirekeṇa abhyupagataḥ kaḥ sāvamūlya dāna krayīyaḥ tat etena na ayam īdṛśaḥ loka vyavahāra paddhatim avatarati iti ācaṣṭe sa svarūpañca na utkarṣeṇa darśayati apratibhā samāna tva apratyakṣa tāñca svīkarttum icchati dārśanam spārśanañca dravyam iti siddhānte pāṭhāt iti etat ātma nirantara premāṇaḥ suhṛdaḥ pratyeṣyanti itti adhyāha rttavyam mūlya dāna krayā vidyantesya iti mūlya dāna krayī na tathā iti vṛttiḥ athavā kretum śīlam yasya asau krayī mūlya dānena kra yī na tathā katham etat iti āha yaḥ pratyakṣatām ityādi mūlya dānañcā atra svarūpa arpaṇam iti upahasati 
VNṬ_38,1^1	 nanu ca ekaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti pratyaya vyapadeśa sadbhāvāt rūpa ādi vat tat asti eva tat katham asya asatvam iti ced āha buddhi śabdāt ayopi vyākhyā tāḥ na ca sarvvaḥ ityādinā ādi śabdena tad bheda abheda upādānam yadi taiḥ vuddhi vyapadeśa ādibhiḥ tasya sādhana siddhiḥ iṣyate syāt etad pratibhāsamānam api dravyam lavaṇa rasa abhibhave khaṇḍa rasa vat na upalakṣyate tatas tad prasādhanāya liṅgam ucyate iti atas āha na ca pratyakṣasya arthasya rūpa anupalakṣaṇam yuktam dravya antareṇa anabhibhave sati abhibhave tu yuktam eva yathā khaṇḍa ādi rasasya na ca atra kenacid abhibhava usti 
VNṬ_38,1^2	 nīla ādibhiḥ asti iti ca iti na mahati aneka dravya vattāt rūpāt ca upaladdhiḥ tathā rūpa saṃskāra abhāva ādyāḥ vā anupalabdhiḥ iti uktam tasya ca anupalakṣaṇe teṣām api anupalakṣaṇa prasaṅgaḥ tatas ca sarvu apadārthānām anupalakṣaṇāt loka vyavahāra ucchedaḥ eva bhavet iti manyate yena anupalakṣaṇena tasya avayavinaḥ sādhanāya liṅgam ucyate tad bhāva sādhanañca liṅgam abhyupagamyeta tat bhāṣyate na tu tad gamakam liṅgam kiñcid api asti yathā uktam prāk tad pratipādaka pramāṇa abhāvepi tat asti eva iti ced āha apratyakṣa tvepya pramāṇasya satva upagamaḥ ayuktaḥ iti 
VNṬ_38,1^3	 apramāṇasya iti anena pratyakṣa vyatirikta tad prasādhaka pramāṇa abhāvam āha yasya sadbhāva sādhakam pramāṇam na asti na tat astī tyaṅgīkarttavyam yathā nabhastale kamalam na asti ca avayavinaḥ astitva sādhakam pramāṇam iti sat vyavahāra pratiṣedha phalām anupalabdhim manyate evam vistareṇa eka dravya abhāvam pra tipādya prakṛtam upasaṃharati tadi tyādinā mūlaprakaraṇam api nigamayati evantāva di tyādinā atas eva na teṣa ambuddhi ādīnām viparyayāt teṣām sattā ādīnām viparyayaḥ abhāvaḥ 
VNṬ_38,1^4	 yohi yasya bhāvam eva na sādhayati sa katham iva varttamānaḥ tad abhāvam sādhayati iti ākūtam yadi nāma buddhi ādayaḥ sattā ambheda abhedau vā na sādhayanti artha kriyā tu tān sādhayiṣyati iti atas āha arthaṃkriyātaḥ tu sattā vyavahāraḥ syāt iti tad lakṣaṇa tvāt sattvasya iti bhāvaḥ anena āvayoḥ atra sāmyam eva iti darśayati anyatra tu vivādaḥ iti āha na sattā bheda abheda vyavahāraḥ iti kutas ekasya api aneka artha kriyā darśanāt tatra na eka pratyaya janitam kiñcid asti tat katham evam ucyate satyam etat ekam tu bahavīṣu sāmagrīṣu varttate iti aneka artha kṛt iti ucyate yat āha 
VNṬ_39,1–39,2^1	 na kiñcadekam ekasmāt sāmagryā sarvu asambhavaḥ ekaṃsyāt api sāmagryoḥ iti uktam tat aneka kṛt iti kim vat yathā pradīpasya vijñānasya vartti vikārasya jvālā antarasya ca sva para santāna sambandhi kṣaṇa antarasya utpādanāni tat evam sattā bheda vyavahāra abhāve kāraṇam katham ekam anekam kāryam utpādayati iti ca iti ekasya eva īdṛśasya aneka kārya jananāt turya atiśaya kroḍīkṛtam rūpavataḥ sva hetubhyaḥ saṃjātattvāt iti bhāvaḥ nyāya tattva vidaḥ tathā anekasya api cakṣuḥ ādeḥ eka vijñāna kriyā darśanāt abheda vyavahāra abhāve kāraṇam etat kaṇabhu gmata viparyāsita dhiyaḥ tu āhuḥ na brūmaḥ ityādi kintarhi adṛṣṭa artha kriyā bhedena sattā bhedaḥ iti varttate 
VNṬ_39,2^2	 tat eva vyanakti yā artha kriyā madhu ādya āharaṇa ādi lakṣaṇā tasmin ghaṭa ādau= adṛṣṭā satī punar dṛśyate anyatra ghaṭa ādau sā evamvidhā sattā bhedam sādhayati teṣām ghaṭa ādīnām anena vyāptiḥ kathitāḥ kim iva yathā paṭe adṛṣṭā sati udaka dhāraṇa ādi artha kriyā ghaṭe dṛśyamānā sattā bhedam sādhayati iti prakṛtena abhisambandhaḥ dṛṣṭānta kathanam ca etat adṛṣṭā ca tantuṣu prāvaraṇa di artha kriyā paṭe dṛśyate iti pakṣa dharma upadarśanam iti tasmāt sattā bhedaḥ tantu paṭayoḥ siddhaḥ iti śeṣaḥ tat anena sādhana phalam saṅkīrtitam 
VNṬ_39,2^3	 svabhāva hetuḥ ca ayaṃyasmāt tad adṛṣṭa artha kriyā karaṇa mātra anubandhī sattā bhedaḥ iti tat etena tantubhyaḥ paṭasya anya tvam sādhayan= artha antara bhūta avayavi siddhim manyate ācāryaḥ t vāha sidhyati evam tantu paṭayoḥ sattā bhedaḥ iti prakṛtam vāṃchita artha siddhiḥ tu bhavataḥ na eva asti iti abhiprāyavāḥ na āha artha antarantathā api avayavī nasidhyati iti kutas etat yatas yathāpratyayam asyām saṃskāra saṃtatau svabhāva bheda utpatteḥ kāraṇāt artha kriyā bhedaḥ prāvaraṇa ādi lakṣaṇaḥ bhavati etat uktam bhavati piṇḍīkṛtebhyaḥ tantubhyaḥ upādāna kāraṇa bhūtebhyaḥ kuvinda ādi sahakāri pratyaya sannidhānāt ca viśiṣṭa sanniveśa avacchinnāḥ eva tantavaḥ jāyaṃte 
VNṬ_39,2^4	 ye prāvaraṇa ādi artha kriyāyām upayujyante tebhyaḥ ca pūrvvebhyaḥ paṭasya anya tvam iṣṭam eva asmābhiḥ api na tu viśiṣṭa saṃsthāna avacchinnebhyaḥ iti tyajyatām iyam artha antarāḥ vaya visiddhi pratyāśa iti tat etena evā viddha karṇṇaḥ ktam pūrvva uttara kāla bhāvi tvāt ityādi tad sādhanam apahastitam veditavyam asmābhiḥ tu vistareṇa prāk prayuktam eva iti na punar yojyate kimvat pratyaya vaśāt svabhāva viśoṣa utpatte rartha kiyā bhedaḥ iti āha araṇi nirmathanā dityādi su jñānam dṛṣṭāntam pradarśya dārṣṭa antikam āha 
VNṬ_39,2^5	 tathā yathā ityādi anena eva yathā pratyaya svabhāva bhedenayat eke codayanti nanu ca tantavaḥ paṭaḥ iti buddhi vyapadeśa bhedāt katham asya anya tvam na asti iti tad pratikṣiptam iti ākūtavān āha etena buddhi vyapadeśa bhedau vyākhyātau= iti tatra evam sthite yat uktam prāk tvayā artha kriyā ataḥ sat vyavahāra siddhiḥ bhavati viparyayāt ca artha kriyā nivṛtte viparyayaḥ asat vyavahāra eti satyam etat etāvat tubrūmaḥ saḥ eva viparyayaḥ artha kriyāyāḥ anupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpteṣu na sidhyati tathā hi yadi ayam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpta anupalambhaḥ na iṣyate tadā asya artha kriyā sāmarthyam na asti iti katham adhigatam bhavatā 
VNṬ_39,2^6	 na ca anupalabdhi mātrāt iti yuktam vaktum tasya vyabhicārāt tatra punar anicchata upyāyātam tava yasya idam artha kriyā sāmarthyam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam sanna upalabhyate saḥ asat vyavahāra viṣayaḥ iti kutas sāmarthya lakṣaṇa tvāt satvasya bhavatu evaṅkaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced āha tathā api kotiśayaḥ pūrvvakāt asmāt upavarṇitāt upalabhya anupalambhāt asya sāmarthya anupalambhasya bhavat parikalpitasya syāt matam sa svabhāvasya eva anupalambhaḥ ayam tu punar sāmarthyasya iti atas āha na hi ityādi 
VNṬ_39,2^7	 tathā ca tasya sāmarthyasya yonu palambhaḥ sa svabhāvasya eva iti tasmāt pūrvakā eva svabhāva anupalabdhiḥ eva iyam sāmarthya anupalabdhiḥ tasmāt dṛśya anupalabdhiḥ eva asat vyavahāra sādhana iti sthitam etat yasmāt ca evantasmāt anena vādinā kvacid śaśa viṣāṇa ādau= asat vyava vahāram abhyupagacchatā dṛśya anupalambhāt abhyupagantavyaḥ anyasya tad pratipatti upāyasya abhāvāt iti bhāvaḥ tatas sonupalambhaḥ anyatra api sāmānya viśeṣa saṃyoga avayavi dravya ādau tathāvidhe upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpte aviśeṣaḥ iti sa upi sāmānya viśeṣa ādiḥ tathā astu asat vyavahāra viṣayat tvena asti iti arthaḥ 
VNṬ_39,2^8	 syāt etat na eva sāmānya viśeṣa ādiḥ tathāvidha unupalabdhosya sat vyavahāra viṣayaḥ iti atas āha na vā kvacid śaśa viṣāṇa āt au= asat vyavahāraḥ abhyupagantavyaḥ kutas viśeṣa abhāvāt anupa lambhasya ayam atra arthaḥ dvyoḥ anupalambhe tad nimitte tulyepi yadi asat vyavahāraḥ sāmānya ādau na utpadyate anyatra api tarhi sa na abhyupeyaḥ viśeṣa hetu abhāvāt iti anena ca pūrvva uktam eva kasya cit asa tobhyupagame tad lakṣaṇa aviśeṣāt iti smārayati tasmai tsarvvaḥ evaṃvidhaḥ dṛśya anupalambhaḥ asat vyavahārasya viṣayaḥ iti vyāptiḥ anupalabdhau siddha iti śeṣaḥ 
VNṬ_42,1–42,2	 kāpilā stu āhuḥ sarvvam eva sarvu ātmakam anyathā yadi mṛd piṇḍa dugdha bīja ādiṣu ghaṭadadhi aṅkurādayaḥ na vidyante eva śakti ātmanā tadā katham punar tebhyaḥ teṣām utpattiḥ na hi śaśa viṣāṇam avidyam ānantatra udeti evañca sati dṛśyaḥ san= anupalabdhopi kaścid ghaṭa ādiḥ kvacid deśa ādau kathañcid ca saṃsthāna viśeṣa ādinā na eva abhāva vyavahāra viṣayaḥ bhavati iti teṣām matam āśaṅkate na eva ityādinā etat sāṅkhya paśoḥ konyaḥ sa lajjaḥ vaktum īhate adṛṣṭa pūrvvam asti iti tṛṇa agre kariṇām śatam 
VNṬ_42,3^1	 iti abhiprāyavān āha sarvu asya ityādi yadi adṛṣṭam api tatra asti tadā sarvvaḥ eva kṣīra ādayaḥ sarvve rghaṭa ādi rūpaiḥ ranu mata tvāt tad sādhyām artha kriyā aṅkuryuḥ iti arthaḥ kiñca idam aparam na syāt i dandadhi ādi kāryam atas kṣīra ādeḥ bhavati na anyatas jala ādeḥ yadi vā na atas kṣīra ādeḥ idam madhu ādikam tathā idaṅkuṅkuma ādikam iha kaśmīra ādi deśe na idam iha mālavaka ādi deśe yadi vā na idam candana ādikam iha tathā idaṅkunda ādikam idānīm śiśira samaye natu idam i dānīt nidāgha kāle athavā na idam kamala ādikam idānīn tathā idam khaṇḍa ādikam evam mādhurya ādi guṇa viśiṣṭam na idam evaṅkaṭuka ādi rūpam yat vā na idam nimvādikam evam iti vyākhyātavyam 
VNṬ_42,3^2	 kiṅkāraṇam evam etat iti atas āha kasyacid api ityādi idam evambidham adhunā asya rūpat na asti iti yoyam vivekaḥ abhāvaḥ tasya hetoḥ abhāvāt sarvu asya sarvu arūpāṇām sarvu ada anuvṛtteḥ iti matiḥ nanu idam anantaram eva vastutas abhihitam eva sarvva sarvu atra sarvvadā samupayujyeta iti atra taktim idam punar carvita carvvaṇam āsthīyate iti ced satyam pūrvam kāraṇa gataḥ vyāpāraḥ kathitaḥ adhunā tu kārya gataḥ iti viśeṣāt adoṣaḥ idañcā anyatara mukhena dūṣaṇa vacanam śiṣya vyutpādanāya tatas ca bheda abhāvāt na vidyete anvaya vyatirekau yasmim niti vigrahaḥ idam atra asti iti ādi anvayaḥ na asti iti vyatirekaḥ paraḥ prāha avasthā ityāḥ dinā etat uktam bhavati 
VNṬ_42,3^3	 yatra yat vyaktantat tatra asti ityādi vyavahirayate yatra tu yat na eva vyaktantatra tat na asti iti atas ayam adoṣaḥ iti natu iti ādi ācāryaḥ te eva avasthā nivṛtti pravṛtti bhedāḥ na sambhavanti tāvakīne darśane kutas sarvu aviṣayasya asat vyavahārasya abhāvāt atha api kvaci dviṣaye asat avyavahāraḥ iṣyate tadā tasya kāraṇam bhavadbhiḥ vaktavyam iti āha k vacit ityādi yadi vā avaśyam anena kvacid parikalpite vyatirikta avaya vyādau= asat vyavahāroṃgīkarttavyaḥ sa ca asya na yuktaḥ hetu abhāvāt iti āha kvacidi tyādi kutas yasmāt na hi anupalambhāt anyaḥ vyavacchedasya abhāvasya hetuḥ asti prasādhakaḥ iti śeṣaḥ sa ca tu ayā aneṣṭakaḥ iti bhāvaḥ 
VNṬ_42,3^4	 kasmāt evam yatas vidhinā svabhāva viruddha upalambha ādau pratiṣedhena vyāpaka anupalambha ādau vyavacchede sādhye anupalambhasya eva sarvvadā sādhaka tvāt atha aham api asmāt eva anupalambhāt vyavacchedam sādhayāmi iti brūṣe tat atra api brūmaḥ iti āha sonupalambhaḥ yatra eva asti sa sarvvaḥ asat vyavahāra viṣayaḥ iti vaktavyam kim iti viśeṣa abhāvāt tathā ca ghaṭa ādeḥ api kvacid pradeśa viśeṣa ādau= asat vyavahāra viṣaya tvam siddham tathāvidhasya anupalambhasya atra api bhāvāt tad kiṃbrūṣe na eva kvacid kaścid dṛṣṭa upyasat vyavahāra viṣayaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ anyathā atra api vyatirikta avayavi ādau mā bhūt asat vyavahāraḥ iti yāvat 
VNṬ_43,1	 sarvu apramāṇa nivṛttiḥ ityādi paraḥ tathā ca ayuktam uktam na hi anupalambhāt anyaḥ vyavaccheda hetuḥ asti iti evañca sati na ghaṭasya api kvacid asat vyava hāra viṣaya tvam āgama anumāna bhāvena sarvu apramāṇa nivṛtteḥ eva abhāvāt iti manyate kutas punar idam ati prajñā kauśalam āsāditam bhavatā iti āgūrya upahasati sukumāra prajñā etya ādinā na prasahate pramāṇa cintā parikleśam iti sukumāra prajña tve kāraṇam 
VNṬ_43,2^1	 nanu ca kim atra ayuktam uktam asmābhiḥ yena upahasasi iti āha na hi ityādi adiśa bdena āgama parigrahaḥ vyabhicāraḥ ca pūrvam eva pratipāditaḥ sarvu aprāṇi pratyakṣa nivṛttiḥ tarhi gamayiṣyati iti āha na sarvu apratyakṣa nivṛttiḥ iti kutas asiddheḥ ātma parayoḥ apratipatteḥ iti arthaḥ na hi atra sarveṣām pratyakṣat nivṛttam iti niścaye pramāṇam asti kiñcid ātma pratyakṣa nivṛttiḥ eva tarhi gamayati iti ced āha na ātma pratyakṣā viśeṣa nivṛttiḥ api iti na kevalam pūrva uktā iti api śabdaḥ aviśeṣeṇa nivṛttiḥ aviśeṣa nivṛttiḥ ātma pratyakṣasya aviśeṣa nivṛttiḥ ātma pratyakṣāḥ viśeṣa nivṛttariti vyutpatti kramaḥ sannihita sakala tad anya kāraṇasya tu ātma pratyakṣasya nivṛttiḥ trividha viprakarṣā viprakṛṣṭe a bhāvaṅgamayati eva iti kathanīyā viśeṣa viprakṛṣṭa vacanam yasmāt sarvu apramāṇa nivṛttiḥ nna asat vyavahāra hetuḥ tasmāt sa svabhāva viśeṣaḥ trividha vipra karṣā viprakṛṣṭa rūpaḥ bhāvaḥ yatas pramāṇāt saṃnihita samasta tad anyat kriyā ādi kāraṇāt pratyakṣāt niyamena sat vyavahāram pratipadyate samāsādayati 
VNṬ_43,2^2	 tasya eva yathā uktasya pramāṇasya nivṛttiḥ tasya svabhāva viśeṣasya asat vyavahāram prasādhayati avadhāraṇam anumāna avagama ādi nivṛtteḥ vyavacchedāya kiṅkāraṇantasya svabhāva viśeṣasya svabhāva sattāyāḥ tasya yathā uktasya pramāṇasya yā iyam sattā tayā vyāptaḥ kāraṇāt tathā hi yatra sa tādṛgvidhaḥ padārthaḥ tatra avaśyam tena api pramāṇena bhavitavyam samarthasya kāraṇasya kārya avyabhicārāt evañca etat pramāṇam tad vyāpaka tvāt nivarttamānam tām api vṛkṣa vat śiṃśapām nivarttayati anena ca yathā uktāt anupalambhāt ityādi uktam upasaṃharati syāt eta dupalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam api kṣīra ādiṣu dadhi ādikam na pratyakṣeṇa upalabhyate api tu anumānena aśaktāt anutpattiḥ iti atas na tad nivṛtya api asat vyavahāra viṣaya tvantasya iti atas āha na ca ityādi yena anya upalabdhi tvena anumānāt asya upalabdhiḥ syāt kimpunar anyā upalabdhiḥ na yujyate iti āha na cetyā di yasmāt arthecakāraḥ tasya rūpasya upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptasya anyathā bhāva pracyutiḥ nna tam antareṇa apratyakṣaḥ sa bhāvaḥ yuktaḥ iti śeṣaḥ 
VNṬ_43,2^3	 tat etena pratyakṣam eva tasya upalabdhiḥ apekṣaṇīyasya kasyacid hetoḥ abhāvāt iti prasādhayati prayogaḥ punar yat yat āsannihita sakala apratibaddha sāmarthya kāraṇantat tadā bhavati eva na ca ākṣepa kāri yathā samagra apratihata sāmarthya kāraṇa sāmagrī koṅkuraḥ tathā ca kṣīra ādi avasthāsu yathā upadiṣṭa pakṣa dharma vat dadhi ādi viṣayam jñānam iti svabhāva hetuḥ dvitīya sādhya apekṣayā vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhiḥ anyathā tu antasya bhavati eva atoyam hetuḥ asiddhaḥ iti ced āha anyathā bhāveca iṣyamāṇe tat evaḥ palabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptam dadhi ādi na syāt prācya rūpāt pracyuteḥ tathā ca tad rūpa tāyām niranvaya vināśa prasaṅgaḥ iti bhāvaḥ api ca ityādinā upacayam āha yat ayambhāvaḥ ajātaḥ anaṣṭaḥ ca rūpa atiśayosya iti vigrahaḥ nityam ekatva rūpa tvāt dravya antareṇa vyavadhāne dūra deśa sthitau ca bhaveyuḥ api pratyakṣa apratyakṣa tva ādayaḥ iti atas āha avyavadhāna dūra sthānaḥ iti na vidyate vyavadhāna duḥ rasthāne ca asya iti vigrahaḥ kvacid avyavadhāna adūra sthānaḥ iti paṭhyate 
VNṬ_43,2^4	 tatra vyavadhāna dūra sthāna śabdayoḥ pratyekam nañā samāsam kṛtvā paścāt viśeṣaṇa samāsaḥ kāryaḥ kañcid puruṣam apekṣya kopi pratyakṣaḥ anyañca apekṣya pratyakṣaḥ iti na virodhaḥ iti āha tasya eva tasya api unmīlita locana ādi avasthāyām pratyakṣaḥ anyadā ca apratyakṣaḥ iti nakācid kṣatiḥ iti āha tad avastha indriya ādeḥ eva tad avastham avikṛtam indriyam asya iti vigrahaḥ ādi grahaṇam manaskāra ādi ākṣepāya kadācid abhivyakta velāyāṃ pratyakṣaḥ bhavati kadācid ca anabhivyakta kṣīra ādi velāyām apratyakṣaḥ ca iti yena pratyakṣa apratyakṣa tvena kadācid anumānasya upalabdhiḥ aśaktāt anutpatteḥ iti kadācid tu vyakta avasthāyām pratyakṣam kim punar atra ayuktam yena evam brūṣaḥ iti ced āha ekasmin= eva anatiśaye dadhi ādau= amīṣām prakārāṇām pratyakṣā pratyakṣat tva ādīnām virodhāt iti ye paraspara viruddha rūpā na teṣām ekatra anatiśaye sambhavaḥ tat yathā śīta uṣṇa sparśa ādīnām paraspara viruddhāḥ ca pratyakṣa apratyakṣa tva ādayaḥ iti vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhim manyate 
VNṬ_45,1^1	 paraḥ prāha na anatiśayaḥ iti ekasya avyakta avasthā lakṣaṇasya atiśayasya nivṛtyā aparasya vyakta avasthā lakṣaṇasya utpatyā ca kṣīram dadhi iti vyavahārasya upagamāt anena ajātān aṣṭa rūpa atiśayaḥ iti ādeḥ asiddha tvam āha na tāvat ayam atiśayaḥ bhavadbhiḥ atiśaya vat bhāva vyatiriktaḥ abhyupagataḥ abhyupagame vā tad avasthaḥ anantara abhihitaḥ doṣaḥ syāt tasmāt avyatiriktaḥ eva ayam tatra ca āyan doṣaḥ iti āgūrya āha sotiśayaḥ vyavasthā lakṣaṇaḥ tasya atiśayavataḥ avasthātura ātma bhūtaḥ ananvayaḥ iti ekāntena nivarttamānaḥ vyāpaka svabhāvāt pravarttamānaḥ asan= ā iva kathat na svabhāva nānātvam sukha duḥkhayoḥ iva ākarṣati anvākarṣati eva iti arthaḥ prayogaḥ punar yaḥ yasyāḥ tma bhūtaḥ sa tad nivṛttau= ekāntena nivarttate pravṛttau ca āsan= eva pravarttate yathā tasya eva atiśayasya ātmā ātma bhūtaḥ ca atiśayasya atiśayavān iti svabhāva hetuḥ 
VNṬ_45,1^2	 tatas ca tayoḥ avasthayoḥ avasthāturnnānā tvam paraspara virodhi dharma adhyāsita tvāt sukha duḥkha vat iti svabhāva hetuḥ eva na eva asau= atiśayaḥ ananvayaḥ pravarttate nivarttate vā atas pūrvasmin pramāṇe sādhya vikala tvan dṛṣṭāntasya uttaratra tu asiddhiḥ hetoḥ iti ced āha sa anvaya tvecā tiśayasya nivṛtti pravṛtyoḥ aṃgīkriyamāṇe kā kasya nivṛttiḥ pravṛttiḥ vā iti na eva kācid kasyacid nivṛttiḥ pravṛtiḥ vā sarvu asya sarvvadā sattvāt tathā ca sarvvam sarvu atra samupayujyeta ityādinā puronukrāntaḥ doṣonupayujyate iti abhiprāyaḥ upacayam āha yadi ca kasyacid svabhāvasya atiśaya ākhyasya pravṛttiḥ nivṛttiḥ vā iti svayam abhyanujñāyatetvayā eka atiśaya nivṛtyā apara atiśaya utpatyā vyavahāra bheda upagama āditya vidhānāt tat etat eva paraḥ tathāgata vacaḥ abhyāsa upajāta avadāta matiḥ bruvāṇaḥ na anumanyate bhadra mukhena bhavet evam yadi yathā mayā pravṛtti nivṛttī abhyanujñāyete tathā tena api 
VNṬ_45,1^3	 yāvatā asya niranvaya upajanana vināśa upagamaḥ mama tu āvirbhāva tirobhāva mātran tat katham iva anumanyata iti kadācid brūyāt paraḥ iti tat matam āśaṅkate tasya ityādinā sadā eva bhavadbhiḥ śūnya hṛdayaiḥ ayam anvayaḥ ghoṣyate tatra vaktavī aṅkoyam anvayaḥ nāma bhāvasya janma vināśayoḥ iti sattyam eṣā paraḥ prāha kim atra abhidhānīyam yāvatā śaktiḥ anvayaḥ bhāvasya janma vināśayoḥ iti varttate kathampunar sa anvayaḥ iti āha yata usti eva prāk api janmanaḥ nirodhāt api ūrdhvam sā śaktiḥ avasthātṛ lakṣaṇāḥ yena etat evantena ayambhāvaḥ na apūrvaḥ san sarvathā jāyateapi tu śakti rūpeṇa pūrvvam vyavasthitaḥ eva kevalam āvirbhavati iti sarvu atha agrahaṇena jñāpayati tathā na pūrvvaḥ vinaśyati ekāntena api tu tirobhavati asataḥ na asti udayaḥ sataḥ ca na asti vināśaḥ iti yāvat ācāryaḥ āha yadi sā śaktiḥ sarvvadā ati robhau= a āvirbhāva kāle a natiśaya atiśaya rahitāḥ eka rūpe ti yāvat tadā kim idānīm atiśaya vat vidyate 
VNṬ_45,1^4	 yatas kutoyam vyavahāra vibhāgaḥ kṣīrandadhi takram ityādi sāṅkhyaḥ āha avasthāḥ atiśayavatyaḥ iti tāḥ ityādyā ca āryaḥ vikalpa dvayañca prakāra antara asambhavāt kṛtam na vā aharīka vādaḥ yujyate tat sva anya tvayoḥ paraspara parihāra sthiti lakṣaṇa tayā tṛtīya rāśi vyatirecaka tvāt eka tve kaḥ doṣaḥ iti ced āha ekaḥ ced tadā katham idam ekatra avibhaktā tmani avibhakta svarūpe yokṣyate vyapekṣayā bhavet api iti āha niṣparyāyam kimpunaḥ tad paraspara vyāhataḥ iti āha janma avasthānām ajanma śakteḥ tathā artha kriyāyām upayogaḥ avasthānām śaktaḥ tu anupayogaḥ i ti prayogāḥ punar śakteḥ api janma asti avasthābhyaḥ avyatirekāt avasthā svarūpa vat avasthānām vā na janma śakteḥ avyatirekāt śakti svarūpa vat svabhāva hetu viruddha vyāpta upalabdhiḥ etena eva prakāreṇa artha kriyā upayoga anupayoga nivṛtya nivṛti ādiṣu svabhāva hetu viruddha vyāpta upalabdhayaḥ yojyāḥ ādi grahaṇena patana āpatana poḥ api parigrahaḥ 
VNṬ_47,1^1	 punar api sāṅkhīya mmatam āśaṅkate astī tyāḥ dinā kenacid paryāyeṇa avasthā śaktyoḥ ananya tvamparama arthataḥ tu bhedaḥ eva tena janma ādīnām avirodhaḥ iti nūnambhavataḥ sva pakṣa rakṣaṇa ākula buddheḥ ātmā api vismṛtaḥ iti ākūtavān āha vismaraṇa śīlaḥ ityādi yatas ananya tva pakṣe ayan doṣa usmābhiḥ uktaḥ anyatva pakṣetu anyaḥ eva bhaviṣyati kaḥ punar asau= anyā eti tam evadarśayitum upakramate atha api anayoḥ śakti avasthayoḥ vibhāgaḥ anyatu antadā na kaścid virodhaḥ kevalam sa anvayaḥ bhāvasya janma vināśāt iti na syāt kiṃkāraṇam yasmāt yasya anvayaḥ śakti tvena abhimatasya na tasya janma vināśau nityam ekasmin= eva svabhāve vyavasthānāt yasya vā tāḥ uttpāda vināśau= avasthā tvena abhīṣṭasya na tasya anvayaḥ apara apara avasthā udaya astamayena avasthita rūpa abhāvāt tayoḥ śakti vyaktayoḥ abhedāt adoṣaḥ iti kāpilaḥ anuttara miti ādi ācāryaḥ 
VNṬ_47,1^2	 kim atrāyujyamānakam yena evam vadasi iti āha abhedaḥ hi nāma aikyam ucyate tau śakti vyakti bhedāḥ vityayañca bheda adhiṣṭhāna unyatva nibandhanaḥ vyavahāraḥ bhāvikaḥ iti kalpanā viracitasya apratikṣepāt kiñca nivṛtti prādurbhāvayoḥ sa tora nivṛtti prādurbhāvau tathā sthitau satya āmasthitiḥ ādi grahaṇāt gatau= agatiḥ ityādi yojyam etat bheda lakṣaṇaṅkatham yojyate bha vatā tathā hi avasthānivṛtti prādurbhāvābhyām anivṛtti prādurbhāvavatyāḥ śakteḥ abhedaḥ na iṣyate tvayā tathā śakteḥ avasthān epi na avasthānām avasthānam na ca śakteḥ tāsām anya tvam iṣṭam tasmāt evam rūpam nānātvam iti āha eṣa hi nivṛtti prādurbhāvayoḥ anivṛtti prādurbhāva etyādi bhedaḥ tathā hi yat nivṛtya ādinā na yasya nivṛtyādayaḥ tat tasmāt bhinnam yathā tālataruḥ tamālāt iti ati pratītam etat etat virahaḥ ca abhedaḥ iti yat nivṛtyā yasya nivṛttiḥ ityādi 
VNṬ_47,1^3	 nanu ca bhūta bhautika citta caitta ādīnām pratiniyata saha utpāda nirodha sthitīnām etat vidyate na ca teṣām abhedaḥ tat katham uktam etat virahaḥ ca abhedaḥ iti ced na teṣām bhinna utpāda ādima tvāt yathākramam udāharaṇa dvayam āha yathā ityādi anyathe ti yadi anantara ukta mbheda abheda lakṣaṇat na āśrīyate tadā bhedayoḥ lakṣaṇa abhāvāt kāraṇāt bheda abhedayoḥ avyavasthā syāt sarvu atra iti sukha ādīnāmparasparaṃcaitanyānāñca sukha ādibhyaḥ caitanyānām abhedaḥ sukha ādīnām pratyekambhedaḥ na bhavet iti yāvat tad ātmani ityādinā paraḥ sva samaya pratītambheda abhedayoḥ lakṣaṇam āha tena avirodhaḥ iti janma ajanma ādīnām anantara uktasya vā na vai mṛdā ātmani ityādinā mṛptiṇḍa ghaṭayoḥ ādhāra ādheya bhāvam pratikṣipati kintarhi mṛd ātmā eva kaścid viśiṣṭa grīvā ādi sanniveśa avacchinnaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti abhīdhīyate nanu ekam eva mṛd dravyam sarvu atra tat katham idam abhihitam iti atas āha 
VNṬ_47,1^4	 nahi ekaḥ trailokya mṛdā ātmā iti kutas prativijñapti pratibhāsa bhedan dravya svabhāva bhedāt iti sambandhaḥ anyonya bhinnānām eva dravyāṇām vijñāne pratibhāsanāt iti arthaḥ tathā pratyavasthā bheda bhinna avastha tvāt pratyartha kriyā bhedam ca āśritya dravya svabhāva bhedāt paraspara asambha vikārya kāraṇāt iti yāvat parasya api satva rajaḥ tamaḥ caitanyeṣu bheda abhyupagamaḥ idam eva kāraṇam yuktam iti kathayan na āha evam hi iti yadi prativijñapti pratibhāsa bheda ādinā bhedaḥ iṣyate caitanyeṣu ca iti bahuvacanam bahavaḥ pumāṃsaḥ iti siddhāntāt yadi evam iti prativijñapti pratibhāsa bheda ādinā punar api āha sati api etasmin prativijñapti pratibhāsa bheda ādau kasyaci dātmanaḥ iti śakteḥ anugamāt aikyam avasthānām iti ācāryaḥ āha yadi evam sukha ādiṣu api ayam eva abheda prasaṅ gaḥ caitanyeṣu ca 
VNṬ_47,1^5	 sukha ādiṣu api hi guṇa tvāt bhoktṛ tva karttṛ tva ādīnām anugamāt caitanyeṣu ca bhoktṛ tvā akarttṛ tva aguṇa tva ādīnān tathā sukha ādi caitanyeṣu satva jñeya tva ādīnām anvayāt iti abhiprāyaḥ prayogaḥ punar abhinnāḥ puruṣa sukha ādayaḥ parasparam anvaya anvaya bhāj tvāt śakti vyakti vat śakti vyaktī vā bhinne anvayonanvaya bhāktvāt eva sukha ādi caitanya vat iti svabhāva hetuḥ atha api syāt yatra sarvu ātmanā eva anvayaḥ tatra abhedaḥ na tu yatra kenacid rūpeṇa ghaṭa ādiṣu ca sarvu ātmanā anvayaḥ tatas yam a doṣaḥ iti atas āha na ca ghaṭa ādiṣu api sarvu ātmanā anvayaḥ pi tu kenacid rūpeṇa iti na kevalam sukha ādiṣu iti api śabdaḥ kutas avaiśva rūpya saha utpāda ādi prasaṅgāt tathā hi sarvu āsām avasthānām sarvu aprakāreṇa anvaye sati aikyam prāpnoti tatas ca viśiṣṭa rūpa rasa gandha śavīrya vipāka abhāvāt vaicitryan na bhavet evañca pañcabhūta abhāva prasaṅgaḥ adhyakṣa ādi vādhāprasam gaḥ ca iti bhāvaḥ 
VNṬ_47,1^6	 saha utpattiḥ ca sarvu āsām avasthānāmprasajyate ādi śabdena hi anirodha artha kriyā vyāpāra vikārādayā aupādīyante prayogāḥ punar yad viśiṣṭa rūpa rasa gandha śabda ādibhiḥ aneka prakāram na bhavati na tasya vaiśvarūpyam asti yathā ekasya sukha ādi ātmanaḥ tathā sati matānām api avasthānām anantara uktaḥ dharmaḥ na asti na ca asiddhaḥ hetuḥ yatas yadi asmāt na vyatiricyate na tad viśiṣṭa rūpa ādibhiḥ aneka prakāram yathā tasya eva ātmā na vyatiricyante ca avasthā abhīṣṭāḥ iti vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhī tathā yadi asmāt apṛthak bhūtam tad tad utpāda ādibhiḥ utpāda ādimat yathā tasya eva svarūpam apṛthak bhūtāḥ ca abhimatāḥ avasthāḥ tābhyaḥ anyasyāḥ iti svabhāva hetuḥ anyathā ghaṭoyam iti ananya tvam eva ayuktam nāma antaram vā artha bhedam abhyupagamya tathā abhidhānāt upacayam āha na ca ghaṭam mṛdātma ānañca kaścid a tyartha munmīlita locana upyayam ghaṭoyam ca mṛdā ātmā iti vivekena upalakṣayati 
VNṬ_47,1^7	 yena evam syāt idam iha prādurbhūtam iti tad anena abheda lakṣaṇam atyanta asambaddham eva iti āha nanu ca piṇḍa rūpa ātmṛd ātmanaḥ ghaṭasya vivekena upalakṣaṇam asti eva taktim evam uktam iti ced satyam asti na tu ghaṭāt bhinnantam parobhimanyate iti abhiprāyāt adoṣaḥ yadi nāma bhedena anupalakṣaṇantayoḥ tathā api kasmāt evam na syāt iti ced āha na hi adhiṣṭhāna adhiṣṭhā ninoḥ ādhāra ādheyayoḥ kuṇḍeva darayoḥ vivekena anunapa lakṣaṇe sati evam bhavati idam iha prādūrbhūtam iti tat anena ghaṭa mṛd ā ātmanoḥ ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ na asti vivekena anupalakṣaṇāt satva ādi tad svabhāvayoḥ eva iti vyāpaka anupalabdhim manyate adhunā yadi asmin prādurbhavati tat tatas abhinnam iti asya abheda lakṣaṇasya avyāpita āśā cikhyāsurāha na ca śakti ātmani prādurbhāvaḥ tasyāḥ nityam avasthāna abhyupagamāt anyathā avasthā eva sā syāt tathā ca tasyāḥ sva ātmanaḥ sakāśāt abhyupetaḥ abhedaḥ na syāt 
VNṬ_47,1^8	 abheda lakṣaṇa abhāvāt upalakṣaṇañca etat vyaktau sukha ādiṣu puruṣeṣu ca tulya doṣa tvāt anye tu sva darśana aparādha malīmasa dhiyaḥ kecid sāṃkhyāḥ evam āhuḥ yaḥ yasya pariṇāmassa tasmāt abhinnaḥ tat yathā hemnaḥ kuṇḍala ādi avasthā viśeṣaḥ iti tepi anena eva pūrvvasya abheda lakṣaṇasya avyāpita apradarśanena apahastitāḥ iti cetasya āropya āha etena eva ityādi yuṣmad darśana pariṇāma upi na yuktaḥ iti abhiprāyavān apakṣepaṅkaroti kiñca idam ityādinā pareṇa api kim atra vaktavyam yāvatā bhagavatā kapilena spaṣṭam idam uktam iti abhisandhāya āha avasthitasya dravyasya yathā kāñcanasya dharma antarasya keyūrasya nivṛttiḥ dharma antarasya ca kuṇḍala ādeḥ prādurbhāvaḥ pariṇāmaḥ iti ācāryaḥ tasya eva tāvat idam īdṛśaṃprajñā skhalitaṅkatham vṛttam iti sa vismaya anukaṃpat naḥ cetaḥ tat aparepi anuvadanti iti nirdaya ākrānta bhuvanam diś vyāpakantamaḥ kaḥ prāṇinaḥ hita icchā vipula tvasya aparādhaḥ iti manyamānaḥ prāha 
VNṬ_51,1^1	 nanu yadi nāma tena evam uktam bhavadbhiḥ tu nibhālanīyam etat yat tat dharma antaram kuṇḍa ādikam nivarttate prādurbhavati ca kim te deva avasthitam kāñcana dravyam syāt tatā ūrtha antaram vā iti kasmāt vikalpa dvayam eva kṛtam iti ced āha anya vikalpa abhāvāt nirgrantha vāda sya ayogāt iti abhisandhiḥ yadi ādyaḥ vikalpaḥ tadā kodoṣaḥ iti ced āha yadi tad dharma antaranta deva avasthitam dravyam tadā tasya ava sthānāt na nivṛtti prādurbhāvau= āvirbhāva tirobhāva lakṣaṇau= iti tasmāt kasya tau= iti vaktavyambhavadbhiḥ prayogaḥ punar yasya avasthānam na tasya nivṛtti prādurbhāvau yathā avasthātuḥ dravyasya tathā ca avasthā anantasya dharma antarasya iti vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhiḥ 
VNṬ_51,1^2	 na ca asiddhaḥ hetuḥ yatas yat avasthāturana nyat tasya avasthānam yathā tad svarūpasya eva ananyat ca etat dharma antaram tasmāt iti svabhāva hetuḥ kiñca yadi avasthitam eva dravyam tad dharma antaram tadā avasthitasya dravyasya dharma antaram iti vacanam sidhyati kiṅkāraṇam iti āha na hi tat eva tasya dharma antarambhavatī ti bhavati eva tat eva tasya dharma antaram yathā kṛtaka tvam śabdasya avyatiriktam api tasmāt iti ced āha anapāśrita vyapekṣā bhedam etat uktam bhavati atra hi saḥ eva śabdaḥ akṛtaka ādibhyaḥ vyāvṛt tattvāt tad vyāvṛtti apekṣayā tanmātra jijñāsāyām pratikṣipta bheda antareṇa śabdena dharma tvena vyapadiśyateiha tu punar vyapekṣā bheda upi na asti tat kathantadeva tasya dharma antaram bhaviṣyati iti 
VNṬ_51,2^1	 dharmasya dravyāt artha antara pakṣe tarhi kaḥ doṣaḥ iti āha atha ityādi kasmāt dharma nivṛtti prādurbhāvābhyām na dravyasya pariṇāmaḥ yasmāt na hi artha antara gatābhyām nivṛtti prādurbhāvābhyām artha antarasya pariṇatiḥ bhavati tat eva kutas ca eta nyepi pariṇateḥ prasaṅgāt na ca caitanyasya pariṇatiḥ iṣyate pradhāna puruṣayoḥ aikya āpatteḥ akartṛ tā ca iti vacanāt prayogaḥ punar yadyatortha antarat na tad gatābhyām nivṛtti prādurbhāvābhyām tasya pariṇatiḥ tat yathā caitanya bhinna svabhāvasya aṅkurasya nivṛtti prādurbhāvābhyām caitanyasya dharma antarañca dravyāt iti vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhiḥ bhavet etat na yasya kasyacid artha antarasya asambaddhasya api nivṛtti prādurbhāvābhyām anyasya pariṇatiḥ api kutas ca asambaddhasya eva yathā tasya eva aṅkurasya bīja sambaddhasya nivṛtti prādurbhāva abhyāmbījasya tena sāmānyena sādhane siddha sādhanam 
VNṬ_51,2^2	 dharmasya dravya sambandhāt tad viśeṣeṇa tu sādhana vikala tā nidarśanasya aṅkurasya caitanyena saha sambandha abhāvāditi ced āha dravyasya dharmaḥ iti vyapadeśaḥ na sidhyati kutas sambandha abhāvāt evam manyate dravya sambandhoyam dharmaḥ iti etat eva na vidyate tat kutas vyāvṛtti prasaṅgasya iti asti eva tarhi dravya dharmayoḥ ādhāra ādheya bhāva lakṣaṇa ssambandhaḥ tatas ca sa viśeṣaṇepi hetau asiddhiḥ iti atas āha na hi kārya kāraṇa bhāvāt anyaḥ vastu bhūtaḥ sambandhoḥ tī ti ādhāra ādheya bhāvaḥ api kārya kāraṇa bhāva viśeṣāt eva vyavasthāpyate yathā nirṇītam ādhāra tobhi nivṛtteḥ ātmanaḥ tādṛśaḥ nu yaḥ kāryantasya iti atra prakaraṇe pramāṇa viniścaya eti abhiprāyaḥ astu tarhi kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ tayoḥ iti ced āha na ca anayoḥ dravya dharmayoḥ kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ iti kutas svayam atad ātmanaḥ atad kāraṇa tvāt yat hi yat svabhāvam na bhavati na tad tad kāraṇa tayā bhavadbhiḥ abhyupeyam yathā rajaḥ tamasaḥ 
VNṬ_51,2^3	 tathā ca idam api dravya dharmassvabhāvaḥ bhavati tat katham iva tasya kāraṇa tvam upeyāt iti vyāpaka anupalabdhi prasaṅgam manyate na ca ayam asiddhaḥ hetuḥ iti mantavyam artha abhāva pakṣam samāśritya doṣa abhidhānasya prakṛtattvāt yat āha dharmasya dravyāt artha antara tvam syāt iti atha api asmad vaiphalye syāt pūrvvakān kāpilān atipatya sāṅkhyānām śaka mādhava vat dravyasya vyatirekepi dharma kāraṇa tvam iṣyate tadā api brūmaḥ iti āha artha antarat tvepi dravyasya dharma kāraṇa tve aṅgīkriya māṇe artha antarasya kāryasya utpādanāt kāraṇāt dravyasya pariṇāmaḥ iti iṣṭam syāḥ d bhavatā tatas kim syāt iti āha tad viruddhasya api tathāgatāḥ nusāriṇaḥ kiṅkāraṇantena api hetu phala saṃtānam mṛd dravya ākhye pūrvvakāt mṛptiṇḍāt kāraṇa bhūtāt uttarasya ghaṭa dravyasya kāryasya utpattau satyām mṛd dravyam pariṇatam iti vyavahāra bhedasya upagamāt kāraṇāt 
VNṬ_51,2^4	 syāt matam yadi nāma prakāra dvayena api pariṇāma ūna yujyate prakāra antareṇa tu bhaviṣyati iti etat āha na ca ityādi tasmāt ubhayathā api na pariṇāmaḥ iti upasaṃhāraḥ na nirvivekam nirviśeṣam dravyam eva paraḥ na api dravyāt artha antara mekāntena eva kintarhi dravya sanniveśaḥ avasthānta ranna anyaḥ yathā aṅgulīnām sanniveśaḥ avasthā antaram muṣṭiḥ yathā aṅgulīnām sanniveśaḥ avasthā antarantatva anyatvābhyām anirvacanīyam muṣṭiḥ kasmāt hetoḥ na hi aṅgulyaā iva nirvivekā muṣṭiḥ kutas prasāritānām amuṣṭi tvāt anyathā prasāritānām api viśeṣa abhāvāt muṣṭi avasthāyām iva muṣṭit tva prasaṅgaḥ iti abhāva hetu kāle rūpakaḥ na api artha antaram muṣṭiḥ aṅguli vyatirekeṇa apratihata kāraṇena prayatnavatā api muṣṭeḥ anupalabdheḥ iti kadāci tkāpilāḥ evam brūyuḥ iti tat matam śaṅkate na nirviveka mityādinā gata artham etat na hi muṣṭeḥ aṅguli viśeṣa tvāt iti pariharati 
VNṬ_51,2^5	 asakta aṅgulyaḥ eva ca nirvivekā muṣṭiḥ iti kathayan dṛṣṭānta ayogam āha atopi yat uta prasāritānām amuṣṭi tvāt iti tat api ayuktam eva kiṅkāraṇam yata uṅgu lyaḥ eva hi viśiṣṭa hetu pratyaya balena tathā utpannā kāścana muṣṭiḥ nna tu sarvāḥ tat eva kutas iti āha na prasāritāḥ aṅgulyaḥ nirviveka svabhāvāḥ muṣṭi aṅgulyaḥ ca iti ca śabdotra lupta nirdiṣṭaḥ jñeyaḥ athavā muṣṭi ātmikāḥ aṅgulyaḥ prasāritāḥ satyaḥ na hi nirviśiṣṭa rūpā iti vyākhyeyam kasmāt avasthā dūyepi prasārita aprasārita rūpe ubhayoḥ aprasārita prasārita avasthayoḥ yathākramam pratipatti prasaṅgāt prayogaḥ punar prasārita avasthā yāma prasārita avasthāyāḥ pratipattiḥ bhavet aṅgulīnām viveka abhāvāt aprasārita avasthāyām iva svabhāva hetuḥ evam aprasārita avasthāyām prasārita avasthāyām tad pratipattiḥ syāt iti aparaḥ yojyaḥ yat tu ubhayasya iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ yojyāḥ 
VNṬ_51,2^6	 athā api kathañcid kaścid vivekaḥ sthitayoḥ avasthayoḥ tadā sa vivekaḥ ca āsām aṅgulīnām svabhāva bhūtaḥ vā bhavet nava iti vikalpa dvayam prathame tāvat doṣam āha yaḥ eva khalu vivekaḥ svabhāva bhūtaḥ saḥ eva sva bheda lakṣaṇam sukha duḥkha vat iti dvitīyepi a āha para bhūte ca viveka utpāde aṅgulyaḥ prasāritāḥ eva upalabhyerat muṣṭi avasthāyām api iti śeṣaḥ kim iti yatas na hi svabhāvāt apracyutasya artha antara utpāde sati anyathā upalabdhiḥ bhavati atiprasaṅgāt uṣṭrasya api artha antarasya kalabhasya utpāde atyatha upalabdhiḥ syāḥ diti ati prasaṅgaḥ vaktavyaḥ prayogaḥ punar yatra svasya ātma bhāvāt apracyutam na tasya artha antara utpādepi anyathā upalabdhiḥ yathā uṣṭrasya kalabha prādurbhāve apracyutāḥ ca svasmāt svabhāvāt aṅgulyaḥ viveka utpādepī iti vidhi pratiṣedhābhyām hetu avakalpanāyām kāraṇa viruddha kāraṇa anupalabdhī nanu ityādi paraḥ tatvā anya tvābhyām anirvacanīyam tat uktam iti vākya arthaḥ 
VNṬ_51,2^7	 uktam etat na punar yuktam ityā ca āryaḥ katham ayuktam iti āha na hi sataḥ vastunaḥ tattva anya tve muktvā anyaḥ prakāraḥ sambhavati iti sat vastu grahaṇam kalpanā śilpa uparicatasya anya apoha ādeḥ sambhavati iti pratipādanāya kutas iti āha tayoḥ ityādi prayogaḥ punar yau paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇa autayoḥ eka tyāgaḥ apara upāda ānana āntarīyakaḥ eka upādānañca aparatyāganāntarīyakam tat yathā bhāva abhāvau yathā ukta dharmavantau ca tatvā anyatva prakārau= iti svabhāva hetuḥ nanu aṅgulībhyaḥ muṣṭeḥ tatva anyatva prakārau mukttvā api anyaḥ prakāraḥ saṃbhavati eva na hi aṅgulyaḥ eva muṣṭiḥ prasāritānām amuṣṭi tvāt na api artha antaram pṛthak svabhāva anupalabdheḥ iti ced āha aṅgulīṣu punar ityādi pratikṣaṇam vināśaḥ vidyate yāsām iti vigrahaḥ tāḥ eva kṣaṇika tvāt tathāvidhāḥ jāyante yena muṣṭi ādi vācyāḥ bhavanti iti arthaḥ 
VNṬ_51,2^8	 tat etat ca vastutas na muṣṭeḥ aṅguli viśeṣāt iti atra uktam api prasaṅgāt yuktam uktam iti avaseyam anyathā kim anena yadi evam kathantarhi muṣṭiḥ aṅgulī iti ca vyapadeśa bhedaḥ iti atas āha tatra muṣṭi ādi śabdāḥ viśiṣṭa viṣayāḥ viśiṣṭa avasthānām eva aṅgulīnām vācaka tvāt aṅgulī śabdaḥ tu sāmā nyaśabdaḥ sarvvā avasthānām tāsām abhidhāyaka tvāt yathākramam udāharaṇa dvayam āha vīja aṅkura ādi śabda vat brīhi ādi śabda vat ca iti evam śakalīkṛta sakala para pakṣaḥ kucodya śeṣam para upanyastam parijihīṣuḥ para mukhena codyam upasthāpayati tat yadītyā dinā idam asya ākūtam yathā hi tileṣu avidyamānam ghṛtam tathā tailam api tat yadi prāk asat eva kāraṇe kāryam utpadyate tathā ghṛtasya api tilebhyaḥ utpattiḥ syāt asatvāt taila vat na vā tailasya api tatas eva ghṛta vat na hi asatye kaścid viśeṣaḥ iti svabhāva hetu vyāpaka anupalabdhi tvena abhimatayoḥ vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva prasādhana prakāraḥ eṣaḥ 
VNṬ_55,1	 tat etat sarvammabhi avadhāya kṛtyā utthāpanambhavataḥ iti manyamānaḥ prāha nanu sarvu atra saru u asyā satvepyayan tulyaḥ doṣaḥ na hi satve kaścid viśeṣaḥ iti prayogaḥ punar tau= eva satvāt iti hetu viparyayaṃkṛtvā kāryau atha api kaścid viśeṣa usti tena satvepi na sarvvam sarvasmāt jāyate tena saṃdigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttika tvam pramāṇayoḥ iti ced āha viśeṣe cā abhyupagamya māne sa viśeṣaḥ traiguṇyāt satva rajaḥ tamaḥ rūpāt bhinnaḥ syāt kasmāt tasya traiguṇyasya bhāvepi viśeṣasya ananuvṛtteḥ kāraṇāt prayogaḥ punar yat bhāvepiyat na anuvarttate tat tasmāt atyantam bhinnam yathā śabda sparśa rūpa rasa gandhebhyaḥ caitanyat na anuvarttate ca viśeṣaḥ traiguṇya bhāvepi iti svabhāva hetuḥ etat ca abhyupagamya udgrāhitam adhunā satkārya vāde janma arthaḥ eva na yuktaḥ iti āha sataḥ ca ityādi na eva tasya ca asatvena abhimatasya janma asti satvāt niṣpanna avasthāyām iva iti viruddha vyāpta upalabdhiḥ asya manasi varttate anyathā punar jātasya api punar jātiḥ prasajyate iti anavasthā syāt yat āha sataḥ yadi bhavet janma jātasya api bhavet bhavaḥ iti 
VNṬ_56,1^1	 kiñca sādhanānām kāraṇānām bīja tejaḥ jala ādīnām vaiphalyam prasajyeta sādhyasya karttavyasya kasyacid rūpasya abhāvāt iti prayogaḥ yatra sādhyat na kiñcid api asti tatra sādhana sāphalyam vidyate yathā nabhasi anādheya atiśaye na ca sādhi aṅkiñcid api asti kāraṇe vyavasthite sati kāryam iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ na ca ayam asiddhaḥ hetuḥ iti mantavyam yasmāt yasya kasyacid atiśayasya tatra kāraṇe sthite kārye kathañcid utpattā viṣyamāṇāyām sotiśayaḥ tatra āsan kathañjāyeta na eva jāyeta asatvāt vyoma utpalam iva dugdhaḥ iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ asya cetasi sthitā atha āsan= api atiśayaḥ jāyate 
VNṬ_56,1^2	 tadā jātau vā tasya āsatopi sarvu otiśayaḥ sarvu asmāt jāyeta iti tulyaḥ paryanuyogaḥ iti bhavatā upi ghṛta atiśaya upi tilebhyaḥ utpadyeta asa tvāt tena atiśaya vat iti arthaḥ svabhāva hetu prasaṅgaḥ paramatamāśaṅkate na atiśayaḥ tatra ityādinā yathā na asti sa kathantatra āsan prakāraḥ jāyeta iti prakṣipati jātā uvā sarvvaḥ sarvu asmāt jāyeta iti tulyaḥ paryanuyogaḥ iti pūrva uktaḥ doṣaḥ na yujyate iti abhiprāyaḥ sarva prakāreṇa eva tarhi niṣpanna rūpa atiśaya usti iti ced āha na ca ityādi evantā vat sat asat kārya vādinoḥ sarvu asmāt sarvvasya utpatti doṣaḥ tulyaḥ iti pratipāditam 
VNṬ_56,2^1	 na ca tayoḥ api tulyañcodyan na tat ekaḥ vaktum arhati satkārya vāde ca nakaścid janma arthaḥ iti prasādhitam tena ayam asti iti adhikaḥ doṣaḥ tat evaṅkadācid paraḥ abhidadhyāt nanu bho yadi nāma mayā etat na parihṛtam bhavatā tu avaśyam sthiteḥ kiñcid sva pakṣasya rakṣaṇāyavācyam na hi parasya pakṣam dūṣayatā sva pakṣa sthitiḥ anavadyā labhyate na bhavati nityaḥ śabdaḥ mūrtta tvāt sukha ādibhiḥ vyabhicāreṇa iti ādau= anitya tva asiddha vat iti atas āha asatā upi kāryasya kāraṇāt utpāde yaḥ yat janana svabhāvaḥ tatas eva tasya janma janma na anyasmāt iti niyamaḥ iti api śabdaḥ sambhāvanāyām idam atra arthatatvam avidyamānam api tailam tilebhyaḥ eva utpadyate 
VNṬ_56,2^2	 tad utpādana śakti yukta tvāt tilānām na anyasmāt tad janana śakti vikala tvāt tasya śakti pratiniyamaḥ eva ca katham iti ca paryanuyoge vastu svabhāvaiḥ uttaram vācyam yaḥ evambhavanti yathā vā tathā eva pradhānāt mahān eva jāyate na ahaṅkāraḥ mahataḥ ahaṅkāraḥ na pañca tanmātrāṇi ityādi prakriyā tatra ca bhavataḥ śakti pratiniyama avalambanam eva śaraṇam anyasya parihāra upāyasya abhāvāt tat etat ca na mama api kākena bhakṣitam tenayat uktat nahi asatve kaścid viśeṣaḥ iti tat ayuktimat kāraṇa sāmarthya asāmarthya kṛta tvāt kārya utpati anutpatyoḥ tasmāt puronukrāntayoḥ pramāṇayoḥ sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttika tva sādhana kalaṅka aṅkitaḥ hetuḥ iti 
VNṬ_56,2^3	 bhavet etat tasya api hetoḥ ḥ tad janana svabhāva niyamaḥ kutas jātaḥ iti atas āha tasya api sa svabhāva niyamaḥ sva hetoḥ iti tasya api sa kutas iti ced āha iti evam anādi bhāva svabhāva niyamaḥ iti na vidyate ādiḥ asya iti vigrahaḥ anādi tva abhyupagamāt hetu phala prakṛti paraṃparāyāḥ na anavasthā doṣaḥ laghīyasīm api kṣatim āvahati anyathā adau kalpyamāne tasya ahetuka tva prasaṅgaḥ tena āsthānaḥ eva iyam āśaṅkā bhavataḥ iti bhāvaḥ athavā anyathā a yaṅgranthaḥ vyākhyāyate niṣparyāyeṇa āsan= eva tarhi atiśayaḥ jāyate na ca sarvvam sarvu asmāt jāyeta iti paryanuyojyam 
VNṬ_56,2^4–57,1	 yaḥ yat janana svabhāvaḥ tatas eva tasya atiśaya utpattiḥ iti śakti niyama samāśrayāt iti kadācid sva siddhāntam anādṛtya api parobhidadhāti āśaṅkāyām na mama api etat śakti pratiniyama ā= alam vanaṅkenacid daṇḍena nivāritam iti āgūrī āha asatā upi ityādi pada vibhāgaḥ tu pūrvavat prayogaḥ punar yasya yat jananāya samartham kāraṇam asti sosan= api jāyate eva yathā atiśaya viśeṣaḥ tat jananāya samarthaṅkāraṇam asti ca kārya viśeṣasya iti svabhāva hetuḥ tathā yaḥ yatra avidyamāna tad janana samartha kāraṇaḥ sa tatra āsatvepi na udeti yathā tileṣu ghṛta atiśayaḥ tathā ca avidyamāna tad janana samartha kāraṇaḥ kārya viśeṣaḥ kāraṇa viśeṣaḥ iti vyāpaka anupalabdhiḥ aparaḥ paryyāyaḥ sādhanasya liṅgasya sat akāraṇāt upādāna grahaṇāt sarvu asambhava abhāvāt śakyasya śakya karaṇāt kāraṇa bhāvāt ca satkā ryam 
VNṬ_57,2^1	 iti evamādeḥ vaiphalyam sādhyasya kartavyasya kasyacid saṃśaya viparyāsa vyavacchedasya niścaya pratyaya janmanaḥ ca abhāvāt sarvvam hisādhanam vivāda pade vastuni saṃśaya viparyāsau= apanayantat viṣayat niścaya pratyayam utpādayat vibhartti nāma anurūpam na dvayam api etat kāpila mate sambhavati sadā avasthitasya kāryasya hāni upajanana ayogāt atha san= api ayam niścayaḥ sādhana vacanāt anabhivyaktam pūrvvam abhivyaktim upayāti atas na vaiphalyam iti matam atas āha yasya kasyacid atiśayasyāḥ bhivyakti lakṣaṇasya tatra sādhye niścaya rūpe kathañcid asataḥ utpattau prāptāt sādhanāt saḥ atiśayaḥ tatra āsan kathan jāyate jātaḥ vā sarvvā atiśayaḥ samasta sādhya niścaya abhivyakti lakṣaṇaḥ sarvu asmāt anya sādhanāt sādhana ābhāsāt vā utpadyeta iti tulyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ pāvaka ādi pratipatti heta vodhūma ādayaḥ satkārya viniścaya ādi abhivyaktiṅkuryuḥ iti arthaḥ utpattya ca abhivyaktim etat ucyate na tu i yama vikṛta rūpeṣu kṛta āspadā sā hi tad svarūpa lakṣaṇā tad viṣaya jñāna lakṣaṇā 
VNṬ_57,2^2	 rūpa antara prādurbhāva lakṣaṇa abhāvāḥ bhavet svarūpam tāvat avikāryam iti na sādhanaiḥ anyaiḥ vā kartum śakyate vikāre vā pūrvvasvabhāvavān iva pūrvva rūpa prādurbhāvaḥ ca iti asatkārya vāda eva samarthitaḥ pūrva apara rūpa tyāga avāpti lakṣaṇa tvāt vikārasya caitanyasya eka tvāt aparaḥ tad viṣayaḥ pratyayaḥ na bhavati parasya iti tad rūpa abhivyaktiḥ anupapannāḥ rūpa antara prādurbhāve ca na anyasya kiṃcid api upajāyate vilakṣaṇa tvāt iti tṛtīyā api vyaktiḥ asambhavinī dvitīyāyām api ayam anivāritaḥ doṣaḥ tad viṣaya pratyaya udayepi artha antarasya ābhūta bhāva vaiparītyasya vyakteḥ ayogāt na ca anupakārakaḥ pratyayasya viṣayaḥ sambhavī tad upakāraka tve vā tasmāt eva asya utpattiḥ iti liṅga anapekṣāḥ svatas eva sādhya niścayosya abhivyaktiḥ iti prāptam sādhana apekṣāt eva sādhya niścayāt sva viṣaya jñāna utpādena eva apekṣā atiśaya utpatti lakṣaṇa asthireṣu labdhāspadā iti pratipāditam sarvvadā vā bhavet liṅgasya api sadā sannihita rūpa tvāt liṅga jñāna apekṣāyām api tulyaḥ tasya api satve vādinaḥ sarvu akāla astitvāt iti 
VNṬ_58,1^1	 api ca ityādinā satkārya vāda nirākaraṇe kāraṇa antaram āha tad avasthāyāḥ miti mṛd piṇḍa avasthāyām paścāt vat abhivyakta avasthāyām iva tad artha kriyā iti ghaṭa sādhya udaka dhāraṇa viśeṣa ādi artha kriyā vyakteḥ aviśiṣṭa saṃsthānāyāḥ aprādurbhāvāt iti ced parama tā śaṅkā tasyāḥ eva ityādi pratividhānam etat uktam bhavati grīvā ādi sanniveśa viśeṣa avacchinnaḥ eṣā urtha kriyā viśeṣa kārī kaścid mṛd vikāraḥ ghaṭaḥ iti ucyate na anyaḥ sa ced prāk api mṛptiṇḍa avasthāyām api tadā avyakta avasthāyām iva tad artha kriyā upalbdhau syātām na ca bhavataḥ tasmāt na asti eva asau= iti niścayaḥ samādhīyatām kim alīka nirbandhena iti avasthātuḥ bhāvāt asau= api asti iti ced āha na hi rūpa antarasya bhāve rūpa antaram asti pītaḥ iva nīlam iti viruddha vyāpta upalabdhiḥ ākūtāḥ na ca avasthā avasthātra urabhedāt asiddhaḥ hetuḥ iti garjitavyam 
VNṬ_58,1^2	 yasmāt na ca rūpa pratibhāsa bhedepi vastu bhedaḥ yuktaḥ atiprasaṅgāt rūpa pratibhāsa bheda grahaṇam upalakṣaṇa artham tena artha kriyā bheda upyabhyupagantavyaḥ evam manyate yadi bhinna pratibhāsi jñānam bhedam sādhayati tadā asukha duḥkha mohānām asaṅkīrṇā bheda vyavasthā bhavet na anyathā tathā ca mṛptiṇḍa ghaṭayoḥ api parasparam atyaṃtambhedaḥ iti pratijānīmahe bhinna ākāra jñāna paricchedya tvāt paraspara asambha vikārya kāri tvāt ca sukha ādi vat iti svabhāva hetū anyathā sukha ādīnām api parasparam abheda prasaṅgaḥ śakti vyakti vat viśeṣaḥ vā vācyaḥ iti tasmāt iti upasaṃhāraḥ na hi tasya ghaṭa ādeḥ tasmin= upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāpte svabhāve sthitau satyām anupalabdhiḥ yujyate atha api bhavati tadā asthitiḥ ca tasmin svabhāve ata tvam a tad svabhāva tvam upalabdhi lakṣaṇa prāptāt svabhāvāt ekāntena bhedaḥ iti yāvat 
VNṬ_59,1^1	 evam svabhāva anupalabdhau sādhana aṅga samarthanam prapañcena abhidhāya pariśiṣṭāsu anupalabdhiṣu āci khyāsuḥ āha vyāpaka anupalabdhau= ityādi dharmayoḥ yathā śiṃśapā tu avṛkṣa tvayoḥ vyāpyavyāpaka bhāvam kenacid pramāṇena prasādhya vyāpakasya vṛkṣa tva ādeḥ nnivṛtti prasādhanam samarthanam sādhana aṅgasya iti adhyāhāraḥ yathā na asti atra śiṃśapā vṛkṣa abhāvāt iti nanu tatra svabhāva anupalabdhyā eva tad abhāvaḥ sidhyati taktimanayā na hi niṣpādita kriye karmaṇā aṃviśeṣa ādhāyi sādhu sādhanam bhavati 
VNṬ_59,1^2	 sādhaka tam aṅkaraṇam iti vacanāt anadhigata artha adhigama rūpañca pramāṇam uktam ajñāta artha prakāśaḥ vā iti satyam etat tathā hi na iyam sarvu atra prayujyate kintarhi vyoma gata trapādi mātre yatra sālasarala pala arśā śaṃśapa ādi pādapa bheda avadhāraṇat na asti tatra sarvu athāḥ yatra eva vyāpya abhāvaḥ na niścīyate kvacid kutaścid bhrānti nimittāt tatra eva iyam prayujyate kāraṇa anupalabdhiḥ api yatra kārya abhāvaḥ na niścīyate tatra eva prayoktavyā na anyatra vaiyarthyāt yathā santamase dhūma abhāvā niścaye na asti atra dhūmaḥ agni abhāvāt iti kārya abhāve saṃśayāt kāraṇa abhāve ca niścayāt 
VNṬ_59,1^3	 svabhāva viruddha upalabdhiḥ api saṃga viṣaya bhāva avasthita gātra sparśa vālā kalāpa ākula anala ālīḍha eva vyoma ādi mātra varti nirdeśe prayoktavyā kāraṇa viruddha upalabdhiḥ ca api adṛśyamānakam āroma udgama danta vīṇā ādi bheda bhāva ābhā vākya śakya gānu samīpa avasthita puruṣa samākrānta bhū talaḥ eva prakṛtena anyatra vaiphalyāt anayā ādiśā anyāsām api anupalabdhīnām prayoga viṣayaḥ anusarttavyaḥ iti teṣām svabhāva vyāpaka kāraṇānām viruddhāḥ teṣām upalabdhayaḥ tāsu iti vigrahaḥ dvayoḥ virodhayoḥ madhye ekasya upadarśanam dvau punar virodhau= avikala kāraṇasya bhavatonyabhāve bhāvaḥ 
VNṬ_59,1^4–60,3	 paraspara parihāra sthita lakṣaṇaḥ ca anayā diśā svabhāva viruddha kārya upalabdhi ādiṣu api sādhana aṅga samarthanam su jñānam eva iti na uktam tathā api kiñcit mātra prayoga bhedāt ekādaśa anupalabdhi vyatiriktāsu api kāraṇa viruddha vyāpta upalabdhi kārya viruddha vyāpta upalabdhi vyāpaka viruddha kārya upalabdhi kārya viruddha kārya upalabdhi ādiṣu sādhana aṅga samarthanam uktam veditavyam tāsām punar udāharaṇāni yathākramam na atra dhūmaḥ tuṣāra sparśāt na iha aprativaddha sāmarthyāni agni kāraṇāni santi tuṣāra sparśāt na tuṣāra sparśaḥ atra dhūmāt na iha apratibaddha sāmarthyāni śīta kāraṇāni santi dhūmāt iti hetu kārya viruddha āpta bhāvaḥ vyāpaka kāryayoḥ viruddha kāryayoḥ anyaḥ pratiṣedhasya sādhakaḥ na iha dhūmaḥ hima sparśāt samarthanna agni kāraṇam na iha dhūmāt hima sparśaḥ na śakyam śīta kāraṇa miti saṅgraha ślokau 
VNṬ_60,4^1	 evam tāvat ekena prakāreṇa asādhana aṅga vacana tva ādinaḥ nigraha sthānam iti pratipāditam prakāra antareṇa api tat eva upapādayati athavā ityādi na ca iti samudāyaḥ ca ayam atra āvṛtyā pūrva udita artha parityāgena artha antara samuccaye varttate na tu dhava sthityā athavā khadiram iti ādau= iva pūrvva artha parityāgena vikalpa ādi vi dhasya api arthasya vivakṣita tvāt iha ca paryāye sādhana śabdaḥ karaṇa sādhanaḥ iha aṅga śabdaḥ avayava vacanaḥ pūrvasmin kāraṇa vacanaḥ iti viśeṣaḥ tri rūpa hetu vacana samudāya grahaṇena teṣu lakṣaṇa ādi vacanānām sādhana tvam tirayati syāt buddhiḥ sādharmyavati prayogena āsa pakṣe hetoḥ asatvam ucyate vaidharmyavati ca na sa pakṣa satvam anantaram eva niṣedhyamāna tvāt 
VNṬ_60,4^2	 tat kathantasya ekasya api avacanam asādhana aṅga vacanam iti etat na vakṣyamāṇe vyāhatam iti etat ca na evam eva hi vyākhyāyate trirūpaḥ hetuḥ artha ātmakaḥ parama artha tova sthitaḥ tasya vacane ye prakāśake pakṣa dharma vacanam sa pakṣa satva vacane pakṣa dharma vacanam vipakṣa satva vacane vā tayossamudāyaḥ tasya vacana dvaya samudāyasya aṅgampakṣa dharma ādi vacanam iti pakṣa dharma vat ananta avat avicalam itarayoḥ tu anyatara anyatarat kādācid kam tena vacana dvaya samudāya rūpasya aṅginā uṅgam dvividham eva sadā tasya idānīm aṅgasya ekasya api avacanam asādhana aṅgamvacanam na kevalam dvayoḥ prathama vyākhyā anusāreṇa iti api śabdāt dvayoḥ hi avacanam tūṣṇīmbhāvaḥ sa ca uktaḥ apratibhayā tūṣṇīṃbhāvāt iti paryāya antaram api āha 
VNṬ_61,1^1	 athavā ityādi tasya eva iti tri rūpa vacana samudāyasya yat na aṅgam na avayavaḥ katham punar pratijñā ādīnām asādhana aṅga tvam iti ced ucyate pratijñā vacana sādhanam sākṣāt pāraṃparyeṇa vā tasyāḥ siddheḥ anutpatteḥ tathā hi arthaḥ eva pratibandha arthaṅgamayati na abhidhānam artha pratibandha vikala tvāt tasmāt pratijñā vacanam hetu vacanam vā na sākṣāt sādhanam artha siddhau saṃśayaḥ ca pakṣa vacana ādaryem dṛṣṭaḥ na niścayaḥ tat ata upi na sākṣāt sādhanam syāt matam saṃśayaḥ eva asiddhaḥ pakṣa vacanāt vādi prativādinoḥ niścita tvāt atha anyeṣām bhavati evam sati kṛtaka tva ādi vacanepya vyutpannānām saṃśayaḥ bhavati iti anekāntaḥ tat etat asambaddham vādi prativādinaḥ rhi niścita tvam ekasmin vā dharme anitya tva ādike pratyāyayitum ārabdhe bhavet pratyanīka dharma dvaye vā na tāvat ekasmin vivāda abhāvataḥ sādhana prayoga anarthakya prasaṅgāt na api pratyanīka dharma dvaye vastunaḥ viruddha dharma dvaya adhyāsa prasaṅgāt yadāhi ekasmin vastuni pramāṇa balena viruddhau dharmau vādi prativādibhyām niścitau bhavataḥ tadā tat vastu dvi ātmakam prāptam 
VNṬ_61,1^2	 atha na pramāṇa sāmarthyāt tau niścitau= api tu svasmāt svasmāt āgamāt evam api tu dharmayoḥ pramāṇena niścayāt kathat na pakṣa vacanāt saṃśayaḥ bhavati iti vācyam tasmāt pakṣa vacanam na sākṣāt sādhanam na api pāramparyyeṇa sādhya abhidhāyaka tvena asiddhe hetu dṛṣṭānta ābhāsa ukti vat aśakya sūcaka tvāt hetu vacanantu śakya sūcaka tvāt śaktitas sādhana niṣṭam sadā ucyate sādhana aṅgampratijñā vacana tve sati sādhana upakāraka tvāt hetu vacana vat sādhana viṣaya prakāśana dvāreṇa ca pratijñā sādhanam anugṛhṇāti anyathā hya viṣayam tad sādhanam pravarttate jñāna ātma manaḥ sannikarṣa ādīnām api sādhana upakāraka tvam atas vacana tve sati iti viśeṣaṇam itas ca sādhana aṅga sādhya sādhana viṣaya prakāśanāt dṛṣṭānta vacana vat iti idam api atyartham asāram yasmāt anityam śabdam sādhaya iti abhyarthaṃnā vāhyam vacana tve sati sādhana upakārakam sādhya sādhaka viparyaya prakāśa kañca na ca tad antaraṅgam sādhya siddhāḥ vā aṅgam kaḥ vā viṣaya upadarśanasya upayogaḥ yadi hi anena vinā na sādhya siddhiḥ syāt 
VNṬ_61,1^3	 sarvu aśobheta yāvatā vinā api anena yāvat yaḥ kaścid kṛtakaḥ sa sarvaḥ anityaḥ yathā kumbha ādiḥ śabdaḥ ca kṛtakaḥ iti anuktepi pakṣa śabdaḥ anityaḥ iti artha aṅga mātraḥ eva tasmāt asya nirdeśaḥ nirarthakaḥ eva syāt ayam viparyāsaḥ yadi hetu vyāpāra viṣaya upadarśanāya pakṣa vat vacanat na eva prayujyate tadā kathampakṣa samāśraya labdha vyapadeśāḥ pakṣa dharma tva ādayaḥ sampadyante teṣu vā niśrita ātma su sambhūta sāmarthyāt pakṣa gatiḥ asambhāvyā eva sāmarthya labhya pakṣa balena pakṣa dharma tva ādayaḥ sampadyante iti api ayuktam teṣu asatsu sāmarthī alabhyasya eva pakṣasya asambhavāt anyonya āśrayam ced ampakṣa dharma tva ādi sāmarthyāya ātapakṣa vaśena pakṣa dharma tva ādayaḥ sampadyante pakṣa dharma tva ādi balena ca pakṣaḥ iti tat atra ucyate na khalu sādhana kāle pakṣa dharma tva ādi vikalpaḥ asti kevalam yatra eva jijñāsita viśeṣe dharmiṇi śabda ādau tu ca karīśa ādi sthagita tejasi vā kuṇḍādau yaḥ dharmaḥ kṛtaka tva dhūma tva ādi lakṣaṇa unumānataḥ pratyakṣatovā pratīyate pratyāyyate vā 
VNṬ_61,1^4	 tad viśeṣa yogi tayā vā niścite aparasmin ghaṭa mahānasāda avasthita tvena smaryate tad viśeṣa virahiṇi vā gagana sāgara ādau nāstitvena eva smaryate sa vastu dharma tayā eva vinā api pakṣa dharma tva ādi vyapadeśena tat dharmiṇam jijñāsita dharma viśiṣṭam sāmarthyāt eva pratipādayati sa ca asya sāmarthya viṣayaḥ pakṣa eti gīyate tatas paścāt tad samāśraya bhāvinyaḥ yatheṣṭa pakṣa dharma tva ādi saṃjñāḥ śāstreṣu saṃvyavahāra artham pratanyante yadi vā pratyālocana prakaraṇa balāt sādhanakāḥ lepi bhavantu pakṣa dharma tva ādi vikalpāḥ katham yohi vastunaḥ dharmaḥ vādinā vivāda āspadībhūta dharmi viśiṣṭa tayā sādhayitum iṣṭaḥ sa pakṣaḥ tasya yonyaḥ dharmaḥ sa pakṣa dharmaḥ prakṛta sādhya dharma sāmānyena ca samānorthaḥ sa pakṣaḥ tad virahī vāsapakṣaḥ iti yasya api hi sādhana kāle pakṣa prayoga usti tasya api na vādya kāṇḍam eva pakṣam jāte anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti kaḥ tu prastāva antareṇa api prakaraṇa balena eva pakṣa dharma tvāt ayopi vaktavyā ḥ tat ca pakṣa prayoga dūṣakasya api samānam tasmāt pratijñā vacanam na sādhana aṃgam 
VNṬ_63,1	 upanaya nigamana vacanantu yathā na sādhana aṅgantathā ucyate tatra tāvadu dāharaṇa apekṣaḥ tathā iti upasaṃhāraḥ na tathā iti vā sādhanasya upanayaḥ yathā tathā iti pratibimbana artham kimpunar atra pratibimbanan dṛṣṭānta gatasya dharmasya avyabhicārat tve siddhe tena sādhya gatasya tulya dharmatā evañcāyaṅkṛtakaḥ iti sādhyena saha sambhavaḥ upanaya arthaḥ nanu ca kṛtaka tvāt iti anena sambhavaḥ uktaḥ na uktaḥ sādhya sādhana dharma mātra nirdeśāt sādhya sādhana dharma mātra nirdeśaḥ kṛtaka tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ bhavati tat punar śabde kṛta kattvam asti na asti iti upanayena sambhavaḥ gamyate asti ca śabde kṛtaka tvam iti tathā ca hetu vacanāt bhinna artha pratipādaka tvam upanayasya abhinna rūpa tve prasiddha paryāya vyatirikta tve ca sati hetu vacana uttara kālam upādīyamāna tvāt dṛṣṭānta vacana vat iti śakyeta anumātum 
VNṬ_63,2^1	 hetu apadeśāt pratijñāyāḥ pūnarvacanat nigamanam pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam iti pratijñā viṣayasya arthasya aśeṣa pramāṇa upapattau viparīta prasaṅga pratiṣedha artham yat punar abhidhānam tat nigamanam na punar pratijñāyāḥ eva punarvacanam kiṅkāraṇam yasmāt pratijñā asādhya nirdeśaḥ siddha nirdeśaḥ nigamanam iti punar śabdaḥ ca nānātve dṛṣṭaḥ punar iyamacira prabhā niścarati punar idaṅgandharvvanagaram dṛśyate iti atra ca sāmarthyāt upanaya anantara bhāvī hetu apadeśaḥ gṛhyate na pratijñā anantara bhāvī asambhavāt 
VNṬ_63,2^2	 na hi kaścid pratijñā anantaram hetu apadeśāt nigamanam prayuṃkte anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt tasmāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti atas ca pratijñā artha vākyāt bhinna artham nigamana vacanam pratijñā vākyāt bhinna rūpa tve sati hetu vacana uttara kālam abhidhīyamāna tvāt dṛṣṭānta vacana vat na ca sādhya artha pratipāda kannigamanam śabda antara upāttasya avadhāraṇa rūpeṇa pravṛtta tvāt yoyam āgacchati ayam viṣāṇi iti kenacid ukte tasmāt anaśva ityādi vacana vat tasmāt śabda sahitam vākyam vicāra viṣayāya prasādhya artha pratipādakan na bhavati 
VNṬ_63,2^3	 kāraṇa upadeśa uttara kālam upāt tattvāt dṛṣṭāntaḥ pūrvavat tat etat pratiṣidhyate na khalu evam prayogaḥ kriyate anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt pratijñā prayogasya anantaram nirākṛta tvāt api tu kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ paḥ ca evam sa sarvaḥ anityaḥ yathā kalaśa ādiḥ yaḥ vā kṛtakaḥ sa sarvvaḥ anityaḥ yathā ghaṭa ādiḥ tathā ca kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ iti evam ubhayathā yatheṣṭam prayogaḥ kriyate sādhya siddheḥ ubha yathā api bhāvāt tatra yadi kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ yaḥ ca evam sa sarvvaḥ anityaḥ yathā ghaṭa ādiḥ iti abhidhāya tathā kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratibiṃbana artha mupanaya vacanam ucyate tat idam anarthakaṃvinā api anena pratibiṃbanena anantara ukta prayoga mātrāt pratīti bhāvāt sādhanañca yat anarthakam na tad sādhana vākye vidvadbhiḥ upādeyam tat yathā daśa dāḍima ādi vākyam tathā ca anarthakam pratibiṃbana artham upanaya vacanam iti vyāpaka viruddha upalabdheḥ sva artha anumitau= api ayam eva nyāyaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ na hi kaścid sa cetanaḥ kṛta kattvasya bhāvam śabde gṛhītvā tasya ca avinābhāvi tvam anusmṛtya tathā ca kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratibimbana artha karoti 
VNṬ_63,2^4	 atha api yaḥ kṛtakaḥ sa sarvvaḥ anityaḥ yathā ghaṭaḥ tathā ca kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ iti sambhava pradarśana artham upanaya vacanam ucyate tat etat dvayam api aṅgīkurmaḥ pratijñā anantara bhāvinaḥ tu sādhana mātra nirdeśam anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt iti evana pratipadyāmahe pratijñāyāḥ prayoga abhāvāt tatas ca upanayasya avayava antara tva pratipādanāya uktaḥ hetuḥ asiddhatā uraga daṣṭa tva aṅgatau= aśaktaḥ eva yat punar idam siddhārtha nirdeśa lakṣaṇam nigamanam paunarukti aparihārāya varṇyate tat na eva upapadyate vinā nigamanena artha siddheḥ eva pañca avayava sādhana vādinaḥ anupapatteḥ anyathā nigamanāt prāk eva arthasya siddha tvāt vyartha tayā na sādhana aṅgannigamanam prāpnoti tatas ca na idam upādeyam sādhana vākye siddham iti apratijñā bhavet vyāmohaḥ vipratipannasya pramāṇa antara vyapekṣā na asti iti siddham anitya tvam ucyate nigamanam tu prativiṣayasya arthasya aśeṣa pramāṇa upapattau= aśeṣa avayava parāmarśena avadhāraṇa arthama nityaḥ eva iti pravarttate iti yadi tarhi pramāṇa antara vyapekṣā na asti tat tarhi sādhyam sāmarthyāt avadhāryate eva 
VNṬ_63,2^5	 tathā hi yat akṛta kantat a nityam eva yathā kuṇḍa ādi śabdaḥ ca kṛta kaiti evam anitya tva avinā bhāvinaḥ kṛtaka tvasya śabde bhāva khyātau tad sāmarthyāt eva anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti niścayaḥ bhavati tat asya vacanam sāmarthyam pratīta artha pratyāyaka tvāt punaruktam anupādāna arhañca na ca atra viparyaya prasaṅgasya leśa upyāśaṅkyate yena tad vyavacchedāya saphalam etasya upādānam syāt anitya tvena eva kṛtaka tvasya vyāpti prasādhanāt prayogaḥ tu yat sāmarthyāt pratīyate na tasya vacanam prekṣāvatā karttavyam tat vacanampunaruktam vā tat yathā gehe na asti kumāraḥ jīvati ca iti etat sāmarthyāt pratīyaṃmānasya tat vahiḥ bhāvasya vacanam pakṣa dharma anvaya vyatireka tad vacana sāmarthyāt ca pratīyate tasmāt anityaḥ eva iti evamādinā punar sisādhayiṣitorthaḥ prathama sādhya apekṣayā vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhiḥ dvitīya sādhya apekṣayā ca svabhāva hetuḥ atas eva nigamanasya avayava antara tva pratipādanāya uktāḥ hetavaḥ asiddhāḥ tat api etena eva pratyuktam yat āha 
VNṬ_64,1–64,4	 pratyayekṣa pratijñā dīn vākya artha pratipattaye procyamānat nigamanam punar uktat na jāyate viprakīrṇauḥ ca vacanaiḥ na ekorthaḥ pratipādyate tena sambandha sidhi artham vācyat nigamanam pṛthak iti alamati prasāriṇyā kathayā anvaya vyatirekayoḥ vā iti paryyāya antara kathanam upādānam iti vartate dvitīyasya asāmarthyam jātāyāḥ siddheḥ punar ajanya tvāt pramāṇa samuccaya ṭīkākārāḥ tu āhuḥ nanvi tyādi ne tyādi uttaraḥ yadi ca iti upacaya hetuḥ sādhana avayavaḥ pratijñām prāpnoti niyamena sādhya pratītini mitta tvāt pakṣa dharma ādi vacana vat sandigdha vyatirekaḥ hetuḥ iti ced āha na hi pakṣa dharma vacanasya api iti tad tulyam iti viruddha anaikāntikayoḥ pakṣa dharma sadbhāvepya gamaka tvāt tatas eva saṃśaya utpatteḥ pakṣa dharma vacanan na sādhanam sādhāraṇa ādi vacana vat iti ced āha aitena tat tulyam ityādinā saṃśaya utpattiḥ pratyuktā iti etat eva vyanakti pakṣa dharma vacanāt api iti tad anena anantarasya hetoḥ vyabhicāraṅkathayati 
VNṬ_64,5	 nanu ca pakṣa dharmasya śrāvaṇa tva ādeḥ apradarśite sambandhena eva sādhana avayava tvam atas vipakṣa tva abhāvāt na vyabhicāraḥ pradarśite tu sambandhe sādhana avayava tvam tadā ca tasmāt saṃśayaḥ na asti iti sutarān na anekāntaḥ iti evam manyate pakṣa vacanepi tulyame tat iti tat api sādhanam syāt atha pratipadyethā satyam syāt yadi sādhyam syāt na ca asti anyatas sādhya siddhaḥ na ca niṣpādita kriye dāruṇi dātṛ ādayaḥ kañcana artham puṣyanti apradarśite tu saṃbandhe saṃśaya utpatti hetu tvāt idam uktantataḥ eva saṃśaya utpatteḥ iti yadi evam na tarhi tad prayogam antareṇa sādhya siddheḥ abhāvaḥ iti vyarthaḥ eva tad prayogaḥ syātanyathā kaḥ pakṣa vacanam sādhanāt apākarttum samarthaḥ tatas ca trirūpa liṅgā khyānam para artham anumānam iti ādi ācārya vacaḥ vyāhanyeta katham tarhi uktam 
VNṬ_66,1–66,6	 pakṣa dharma tva sambandha sādhya ukteḥ anya varjanam iti na asti virodhaḥ pakṣa dharma tva saṃbandhābhyām sādhyasya ukti prakāśanam ākṣepaḥ tasmāt anyeṣām pakṣa upanaya vacana ādīnām upādeya tvena sādhana vākya varjanami ti vyākhyānāt vivaraṇa ipi ayam arthaḥ yasmāt pakṣa dharma tva sambandha vacanam eva anvaya vyatirekābhyām vivakṣita artha siddhi kāraṇam yuktam na anyat tasmāt anumeyasya upadarśana artha siddhi artham pakṣa vacanam upādeyam na anyat iti upaskāraḥ pakṣaḥ ucyate ākṣipyate prakāśyate anena iti pakṣa vaca nantri rūpam liṅgam ākṣepaḥ hi abhidhāna tulyaḥ iti vacanam iti uktam vaceḥ aneka artha tvāt vā asmākam tu tatra anumeya nirdeśaḥ hetu artha viṣayaḥ mata iti api vacanam virudhyate yasmai tatra iti tarka śāstrasya sambandhotra abhidhīyate prayogasya tu sambandhe bahu syāt asamaṃjasam tasya eva prakṛteḥ uktam etat ca asya eva lakṣaṇe para vipratipattīnāt niṣedhāya viśeṣata iti alam prasaṅgena 
VNṬ_66,7^1	 tad bhāva rūpam sādhanam aṅgandharmaḥ viṣayi tvena yasya arthasyaprastutasya sa sādhana aṅgaḥ tasya eva abhivyaktiḥ uttareṇa pada dvayena ajijñāsitam prativādinā aśāstra āśraya vyāja ādibhiḥ iti ādipadena asambaddha prasaṅga parigrahaḥ prakṣepaḥ nāma mātreṇa ghoṣaṇam vistareṇa yathā buddhīndriya deha kalāpa vyatireka ātmā asti na asti iti etāvat mātre vubhuḥ tite naiyāyikāḥ pramāṇayanti sat ādyaviśeṣa viṣayāḥ viṣaya jñeya viṣayāḥ madīyāḥ pratyakṣa ādayaḥ pratyayā madīya śarīra ādi vyatirikta samvedaka samvedyāḥ sva kāraṇa āyatta janmavatu ādibhyaḥ puruṣa antara pratyaya vat iti tatas sat anityandravyavat kārya kāraṇam sāmānya viśeṣa vat iti dravya guṇa karmaṇā ām aviśeṣaḥ iti mahatā vyāsena sadādi aviśeṣāt vyācakṣate na hi atra sat ādi aviśeṣa viṣayāḥ viṣaya jñeya viṣaya tvan dharma viśeṣaṇam kathaṃcid api prakṛta sādhya sidhi upakāri para vyāmohana anubhāṣaṇa śakti vighāta ādi hetoḥ iti atra ādi śabdena uttara pratipatti śakti vighāta hetoḥ parigrahaḥ kriyamāṇaḥ prasaṅgaḥ yasya iti vigrahaḥ 
VNṬ_66,7^2	 nairātmya vādi udāharaṇena kim jñāpayati yatra nāma vihita pratiṣiddhaḥ vā didoṣa guṇa saugata dharma vinayasya api ahaṅkāra nimitta sakala uddha vādi mala kṣālanāya udyatam atra eva na ātma vādinaḥ tad sādhane nṛtya gīta ādeḥ prasaṅgaḥ tatra anyeṣām anyasya ca kā gaṇanā nanu ca vayam bauddhā brūmaḥ iti katham yāvatā sa viśeṣaṇasya pratiṣedha abhidhānāt ahambauddhaḥ bravīmi iti bhavitavyam yathā aham gārgyaḥ bravīmi aham paṭu bravīmi iti na ca bahuṣu evetat vahuvacanam iti śakyam abhidhātum kaścid iti vacanāt na eva yasmāt asau= ātmani parān sva yūthyān api anyān bahūn apekṣya tathā prayuktavān īdṛśyām eva ca vādinaḥ vivakṣāyām idam uktam udāharaṇam na anyasyām iti pratipattavyam athavā jaḍa śābdikā abhiniveśa nivāraṇāya idam evam uktam tathā ca vyartha tā śabda anuśāsanasya pratipādayiṣyati atas eva anyena mahā rathena api idam prayuktam tvam rājā vayam api upāsita guru prajñā abhimāna unnatā iti 
VNṬ_68,1^1	 sabhyaḥ sādhu saṃmatānām iti upahasati ahośabdaḥ ca iha adhyāhriyate dvādaśānāmpramāṇa ādi lakṣaṇānām yaḥ prapañcaḥ vistaraḥ tasya prakāśanāya yat śāstram mīmāṃsā ākhyam tasya praṇetā sa ca asau jaiminiḥ ca tena pratijñātam yatta tvam nityatā abhidhānam tasya adhikaraṇam yaḥ śabdaḥ sa ca ghaṭaḥ ca tayoḥ anyataraḥ tena sa dvitīyaḥ ghaṭaḥ iti ittham pratijñām uparacayya dvādaśa lakṣaṇa ādi vyākhyānaṅkaroti pramāṇa lakṣaṇam eva tāvat ekam mahatā kālena vyācaṣṭe codanā lakṣaṇaḥ dharma ścodanā iti kriyāyāḥ pravartakamvacanam āhuḥ codanā hi bhūtam bhavantam bhaviṣyantam sūkṣmam vyava hi tam viprakṛṣṭaḥ martham śaknoti avagamayitum na anyat kiñcana indriyam tathā hi sat saṃprayoge puruṣasya indriyāṇa ambuddhi janma tad pratyakṣam 
VNṬ_68,1^2	 animittam vidyamāna upalambhana tva ādi tyādinā saṃskāra duḥkha tā siddhim antareṇa na anitya tā siddhiḥ apratītya samutpannasya kṣaṇika tva ayogāt sa tarhi tādṛśaḥ dharmaḥ pṛthak vācyaḥ na iti āha tathāvidhaḥ tu ityādi evaṃvidhasya api prastuta sādhya dharmanāntarīyakasya prativādinā ajijñāsitasya tad vyatirekeṇa pratijñāyām anyatra ca ahetu dṛṣṭāntayoḥ kadā punar etat asādhana aṅga vacanam yathoktam nigraha sthānam iti āha prativādinā tathā abhāve asādhana aṅga tve pratipādite sati yadā tu na pratipādayati tadā dvayoḥ ekasya api na jaya parājayau bhavataḥ kutas sādhana anabhidhānāt na vādinaḥ jayaḥ prativādinā tathā abhāvasya apratipādita tvāt ca parājayopi na asti eva tasya pratipanna apekṣa tvāt atas eva prativādini api tayoḥ abhāvaḥ 
VNṬ_69,1	 samprati prativādinaḥ nigraha sthānam adhikṛtya āha adoṣa udūbhāvanam ityādi yatra viṣaye jijñāsite ajijñāsite punar doṣasya anudbhāvanepi na aparādhaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ ke punar te sādhanasya doṣāḥ iti āha nyūna tvam ṣaṣ prakāram ekaika dvi dvi rūpa anuktau syāt matiḥ sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ sat asat tvayoḥ yaugapadyena aprayoge kathañca prakārāt nyūna tā ucyate yadā sarvvā upasaṃhāreṇa vyāpti vyatireka abhyāntat ākṣepa upi na asti tadā iyam vyavasthāpyate atha ucyate tadā api apradarśita anvaya vyatireka ādi dṛṣṭānta doṣaḥ bhavati bhavatu ayam aparosya aparādhaḥ na hi eka doṣa ālīḍhāni eva sādhanāni bhavanti trayaḥ hetvābhāsā dṛṣṭāntāḥ bhāsāḥ ca aṣṭādaśa nyāyavindautṛtīye paricchede sa udāharaṇāḥ prapañcena draṣṭavyāḥ teṣām anudbhāvanam paryāya śabda dvayena vyācaṣṭe tat ca anudbhāvanam tribhiḥ kāraṇaiḥ iti āha tatas punar sādhanasya nirdoṣa tvāt ityādi 
VNṬ_70,1^1	 nanu ca yuktaḥ nirdoṣe sādhane prativādinaḥ doṣān udbhāvanāt nigrahaḥ sa doṣe tu ajñāna asāmarthyābhyām anudbhāvanepi doṣasya duṣṭa sādhana prayogāt vādinaḥ eva parājayaḥ yuktaḥ na prativādinaḥ iti atra āha na hi duṣṭa sādhana abhidhānepi iti yadi evam duṣṭena api sādhanena vādinā prativādinaḥ tiraskṛta tvāt kasmāt jayaḥ na bhavati tasya iti āha kevalam ityādi yadi evam kinna parājayaḥ tatva siddhi bhraṃśāt iti codyam na anirākaraṇāt itya ādi uttaram durjanānām vipratipattiḥ aśobhanaḥ vyavahāraḥ tasmāt na yoga vihitaḥ nyāyyaḥ kaścid vijagīṣuvādaḥ nāma yat chala ādibhiḥ kriyate iti adhyāhāraḥ 
VNṬ_70,1^2	 ukte sati nyāye tatvā arthī ced prativādī pratipadyeta tam artham nyāya upetam atha sva pakṣa rāgasya valīyaḥ tvāt uktepi nyāye na pratipadyeta tadā tena prativādinā tasya nyāyasya arthasya apratipattau= anya samīpa vartti ātma jñaḥ jana kāyaḥ na vipratipadyeta iti kṛtvā nyāya anusaraṇam eva satām vādaḥ iti varttate tatva rakṣaṇa artha m iti paraḥ yathā uktam tatvā adhyavasāya saṃrakṣaṇa arthan jalpa vitaṇḍe bīja praroha saṃrakṣaṇa artham kaṇṭaka śākhā āvaraṇa vat iti na ityādi ācāryaḥ evanta tvam sura kṣitam bhavati ekāntena pratidvandī unmūlanāt iti bhāvaḥ tad abhāvaḥ iti sādhana prakhyāpana sādhana ābhāsa dūṣaṇayoḥ abhāve anyathā api iti mithyā pralāpa ādi abhāvepi 
VNṬ_70,2^1	 katham asau na doṣaḥ sādhanasya iti āha tasya doṣa tvena abhimatasya bhāvepi siddheḥ vidhāta abhāvāt sādhayitum aniṣṭa upya ākāśa guṇa tva ādi kārya tvena anitya tva mātra sādhane dhvanau vivakṣite sati kāṇādāḥ kecid codayanti nyāya anabhijñāḥ śāstra upagamāt sarvvaḥ tat iṣṭaḥ sādhyaḥ tad pradhāne ca hetu pratijñayoḥ doṣaḥ iti tat ca ayujyamānam śāstra āśrayepi asti apagata mātrasya eva sādhya tvāt anyathā gandhe bhū guṇa tā viparyaya sādhanāt ayam eva hetuḥ asyām eva pratijñāyām viruddhaḥ prāpnoti tathā idam aparama doṣa udbhāvanam yathā āha bhāradvājaḥ na asti ātmā iti pratijñā padayoḥ paraspara virodhaḥ iti 
VNṬ_70,2^2–72,2	 yasmāt ātmā iti vastu abhidhīyate na asti iti tasya pratiṣedhaḥ idam api ayuktam anādi vāsanā udbhūta ātma vikalpa pariniṣṭhita pratibhāsa bhedasya śabda arthasya pareṣṭa anitya citta tva ādi viśeṣaṇa ātma lakṣaṇa bhāva upādāna tvasya nirācikīrṣita tvāt atra eva hi dharmiṇi vyavasthitāḥ sadasatvañcintayanti santaḥ kim ayam ātma vikalpa pratibhāsi arthaḥ yathā abhimata bhāva upādānaḥ na vā iti na tu punar atra ayam eva vikalpa pratibhāsi eva arthaḥ apahnūyate tasya eva buddhau= upasthāpanāya śabda prayogāt pratyātma vedya tvāt ca vikalpa pratibimba vyatiriktam tu bāhyam sva lakṣaṇam na eva śabda arthaḥ iti na tasya vidhiḥ na api pratiṣedhanam anyathā paramā ca ekatāna tve śabdānām anibandhanā na syāt pravṛti ratheṣu darśana antara bhediṣu atīta ajātayoḥ vā api na ca syāda nṛta artha tā vācaḥ kasyāścid iti eṣā bauddha artha viṣayā matā 
VNṬ_73,1^1	 sa ca ayam vikalpaḥ bhāva upādāna tvena nirācīkīrṣitaḥ deśa kāla pratiniyatim anapekṣya vikalpa pratibiṃba viṣaya tvāt eva ca ātma śabdasya na nirviṣaya tvam asti tatas ca yat uktam yat ca yatra pratiṣiddhyate tat tasmāt anyatra asti yathā na asti na asamāna adhikaraṇaḥ ghaṭa śabdaḥ na ghaṭa abhāvam pratipādayitum śaknoti api tu deśa kāla viśeṣāt pratiṣedha āga tiḥ na asti ghaṭaḥ iti deśa viśeṣe pratiṣedhaḥ gehe na asti iti kāla viśeṣe vā pratiṣedhaḥ idānīm na asti prāgnāsti ūrdhvam na asti sarvu asya ayam pratiṣedhaḥ na ananubhūta ghaṭa satvasya yuktaḥ tathā na asti ātmā iti kim ayan deśa viśeṣaḥ pratiṣidhyate uttara kāla viśeṣaḥ iti yadi tāvat deśa viśeṣa pratiṣedhaḥ saḥ ātmani na yuktaḥ adeśa tvāt ātmanaḥ na ca deśa viśeṣa pratiṣedhāt ātmā pratiṣiddhaḥ bhavati na ca ayambhavatām abhiprāyaḥ śarīram ātmā na bhavati iti ced kasya vā śarīram ātmā yam prati pratiṣedhaḥ śarīre na asti ātmā iti evam pratiṣedhaḥ iti ced 
VNṬ_73,1^2	 kasya śarīre ātmā yam prati pratiṣedhaḥ kva tarhi ātmā na kvacid ātmā kim ayam na asti eva na na asti viśeṣa pratiṣedhāt kā iyam vācaḥ yuktiḥ nna śarīre na anyatra na ca na asti eṣā eveṣā vācaḥ yuktiḥ yat yathā bhūtantat tathā nirdiśyate iti na ca ayam ātmā kvacid api iti tasmāt tathā eva nirdeśaḥ na ca kāla viśeṣepratiṣedhaḥ yuktaḥ ātmani traikālyasya anabhivyakteḥ ātma pratiṣedhan ca kurvāṇena ātma śabdasya viṣayaḥ vaktavyaḥ na hi ekam padam nirarthakam paśyāmaḥ atha api śarīra ādiṣu ātma śabdam pratipadyethāḥ evam api anivṛttau vyāghātaḥ katham iti na asti ātmā iti asya vākyasya tadānīmayam arthaḥ bhavati śarīra ādayaḥ na santi iti evamādi bahu asaṃbaddham tad apahastitambhavati pratijñā artha eka deśaḥ iti etat api asat sāmānya viśeṣasya abhāvāt yat vā na prayatna anantarīyaka tvasya pratijñā artha eka deśa tā dharmiṇam upalakṣya nivṛtta tvāt yasya hi yat upalakṣakam na tasya tat eka deśa tvam yathā na kākasya gṛddha eka deśa tvam iti 
VNṬ_75,1^1	 anyat tu na yuktam iti yat uktam akṣapādena dvāviṃśatividham nigraha sthānam pratijñāhāniḥ pratijñāntaram pratijñā virodhaḥ pratijñāsaṃnyāsaḥ hetu antaram artha antarat nirarthakam avijñāta artham apārthakam aprāpta kālam nyūna madhikam punaruktam ananubhāṣaṇam ajñānam apratibhā vikṣepaḥ mata anujñā paryanuyojya upekṣaṇat niranuyojya anuyoga upasiddhāntaḥ hetvābhāsāḥ ca nigraha sthānāni tāni imāni dvāviṃśatividhāni vibhajya vakṣyante pratidṛṣṭānta dharma anujñā sva dṛṣṭānte pratijñā hāniḥ tatra bhāṣya kāra matam dūṣayitvā vārttikakāroyam sthita pakṣam āha tam eva brūmaḥ iti bhāṣya kāra matasya bhāradvājena eva dūṣita tvāt asmākamarddhanta avadavasitam bhārasya iti bhāvaḥ tatra īdambhāṣya kārasya matam sādhya dharma pratyanīkena dharmeṇa pratyavasthitaḥ pratidṛṣṭānta dharma sva dṛṣṭa aṃtenujānan pratijñām jahāti iti pratijñā hāniḥ nidarśanam anityaḥ śabdaḥ aindriyaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti kṛte paraḥ āha dṛṣṭam aindriyakam sāmānyam nityaṅkasmātna tathā śabdaḥ iti pratyavasthita idam āha yadi aindriyakam sāmānyam kāmam ghaṭopi nityoḥ tu iti 
VNṬ_75,1^2	 sa khalu ayam sādhanasya dṛṣṭāntasya nitya tvam prasañjayat nigamana anantaram eva pakṣan jahāti pakṣan ca jahataḥ pratijñā ahāniḥ iti ucyate pratijña āśraya tvāt pakṣasya iti vārtikakāreṇa ca evam etat dūṣitam etat tu na buddhyāmahe katham atra pratijñā hīyate iti hetoḥ anaikāntika tvam sāmānya dṛṣṭāntena pareṇa codyate tasya anaikāntika doṣa uddhāram anuktvā sva dṛṣṭānte nityatām pratipadyate nitya tā pratipatteḥ ca asiddha tā dṛṣṭānta doṣaḥ bhavati iti soyam dṛṣṭānta doṣeṇa vā hetu doṣeṇa vā nigrahaḥ na pratijñāhāniḥ iti 
VNṬ_75,1^3	 dṛṣṭān tañca jahat pratijñān jahāti iti upacāreṇa nigraha sthānam na ca pradhāna asambhave upacāraḥ labhyate iti pratijñāhāneḥ mukhyaḥ viṣayaḥ vaktavyaḥ iti idānīm vārti kakāra matam svayam eva upanyasyati pratidṛṣṭāntasya ityādinā kaḥ punar atra dṛṣṭāntaḥ abhimataḥ yadi tāvat yatra laukika parīkṣakāṇām buddhi sāmyam sa duṣṭāntaḥ iti pāribhāṣikaḥ tadā bhāṣya kāra matāt aviṣeśaḥ tatra ca prativihitam atha anyaḥ sa na gamyate iti āha tatra dṛṣṭaḥ ca asau pañca avayavena sādhanena ante ca nigamanasya vyavasthitaḥ iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ pakṣaḥ 
VNṬ_75,1^4	 tatas sva śabdena saha viśeṣaṇa samāsaḥ tad viparītaḥ pratidṛṣṭāntaḥ yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ aindriyaka tvāt iti bruvanvādī pratipakṣa vādini sāmānya ādikam aindriyakam nityam ca tatas vipakṣepi vṛtteḥ vyabhicāryayam hetuḥ iti evam sāmānyena pratyavasthite satī āha yadi evam śabdopyevam astu iti eṣā pratijñāhāniḥ nāma nigraha sthānam kasmāt prāk pratijñātasya śabda anitya tvasya tyāgāt pratijñā śabdena dharmi viśeṣaṇa bhūtaḥ dharmaḥ ucyate samudāya avayava tvāt etat pratikṣipati atra bhāradvāja mate upagatāyāḥ pratijñāyāḥ tyāgāt kāraṇāt 
VNṬ_75,1^5	 yā iyam pratijñā hāniḥ vyavasthāpitā tasyām viśeṣa niyamaḥ kiṅkṛtaḥ kosau= anena prakāreṇa sva pakṣe pratipakṣa dharma anujñā svarūpeṇa pratijñāhāniḥ iti syāt mata mayam eva pratijñāhāniḥ prakāraḥ na anyosti tatas niyama artham ucyate iti sambhavati hi anyena apī ti atha matiḥ pradhānam etat nimittam tasyāḥ tatosmin pradarśite anyopi prakāśitaḥ eva bhavati iti tat atra api āha idam eva ca hetu doṣa udbhāvana ādi kaṅkāraṇam yasmāt evam hetu doṣa udbhāva nādinā pratipāditena prativādinā pratijñā hātavyā samyak dūṣaṇa abhidhānāt 
VNṬ_75,1^6	 yat ca idam abhyadhāyi sāmānyam nityam aindryikam iti ukte śabdopyevam astu iti atra pratividhatte idam punar asambaddham eva yasmāt kaḥ svastha ātmā sāmānya upadarśana mātreṇa sāmānyamastina ca aindriyakannityañca iti etat avicārya śabdam nityam pratipadyeta etāvat tu bhavet sāmanyasya api nityasya aindriyaka tve tasya aindriyaka tvasya anityepi ghaṭe darśanāt saṃśayitaḥ syāt api ca pratidṛṣṭānta dharma anujñā eva atra na yuktā iti āha na ca tat dhamam tasya sāmānyasya dharmat nitya tvam yatas anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti vadatā kasyacid nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti ayam añjasā iti pratyāsannaḥ pratipakṣaḥ syāt na sāmānyantasya dharmi antara tvāt tathā hi eka adhikaraṇayoḥ eva nitya tva anitya tvayoḥ virodhaḥ na nānā adhikaraṇayoḥ āñjasa grahaṇa mayam api viruddha dharma adhikaraṇa tvāt pratipakṣaḥ na tu ati nikaṭaḥ yathā nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti ayam iti paridīpana artham na anena prakāreṇa pratijñā hāneḥ nigraha arhaḥ iti vartate kena anena iti āha pratipakṣa dharma anujñayā athavā anena iti asādhana aṅga vacanena yathoktam idam eva pradhānam nimittam iti 
VNṬ_78,1^1	 pratijñāta artha pratiṣedhe dharma vikalpāt tad artha nirdeśaḥ pratijñāntaram iti dvitīya lakṣaṇa sūtram nigraha sthānam iti sarvu atra anuvartate asya arthaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ vipakṣe hetu sadbhāva kathanam tasmin sati sa pakṣa vipakṣaya ūrddharma bhedena karaṇa bhūtena pūrvva pratijñā artha pratipati artham pratijñā antaraṅkaroti yathā ghaṭaḥ asarva gataḥ evam śabda upyasarvvagataḥ ghaṭa vat eva anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti śeṣaḥ su jñānaḥ idam nirākaroti atra api ityādinā abiddhakarṇa stu bhāṣyaṭīkāyām idam āśaṅkya parijihīrṣati nanu ca asarvvagata tve sati iti he tuviśeṣaṇam uktam sa viśeṣaṇaḥ ca hetuḥ vipakṣe na asti iti na pratijñā antaram nigraha sthānam na hi tat evam asarvvagataḥ śabdaḥ iti pratijñā antara upādānāt hetu viśeṣaṇa upādāne hetu antaram nigraha sthānam iti etat ca ati sthūlam 
VNṬ_78,1^2	 sa hi evam pakṣa dharmam eva vidagdha buddhiḥ viśinaṣṭi na tu pratijñā antaram upādatte siddha tvāt yat api hetu viśeṣaṇa upādāne hetu antarat nigraha sthānam iti abhyadhāyi tat api ati pelavam yasmāt evam tat eva nāma astu pratijñā antara tva sambaddham udāharaṇa sādharmyādeḥ ca iti udāharaṇa sādharmyāt sādhya sādhanam hetu riti etasya pratijñā lakṣaṇasya sādhya nirdeśaḥ pratijñā iti etasya abhāvāt upādavatā ca anena pratijñām pratijñā sādhanāya pratijñā mātreṇa yukti rahitena siddhiḥ iṣṭā bhavati tatas ca prāk api prathama pratijñā anantaram api hetum aindriyaka tvat na brūyāt tasmāt evam prakārāṇa ambāla pralāpānām pratijñā sādhanāya pratijñā antaram ucyata iti evam rūpāṇām parisaṅkhyātum aśakya tvāt lakṣaṇa niyama upya sambaddhaḥ eva kosau pratijñāntara abhidhāne pratijñāntaram nāma nigraha sthānam iti 
VNṬ_79,1	 nanu na ayam īdṛśaḥ lakṣaṇa niyamaḥ pratijñāta artha pratiṣedhe dharma vikalpāt tad artha nirdeśaḥ iti evam kṛta tvāt na asti doṣaḥ tasya eva paryyāya antareṇa kathanāt atha ucyate yathā vidvāṃsaḥ na pratijñām pratijñāsā ādhānayāhuḥ tathā sādhya sidhi artham asiddha viruddha anaikāntaka ādīn api prayuñjate tatas ca asādhana aṅga vacanam ityādi tvayā api na vāci aṃbhavet atas prāha viduṣām apī ti anuddiśya apramāṇakam śāstra upagamam iti mām akīne tantre sāmānyam yathā bhūtam siddham iti eva na pradarśyataiti arthaḥ tathā hi vyutthita cetasaḥ na para samaya vyavasthā uparodham ādriyante tatva darśana adhyavasāya śūrāḥ sūrayaḥ apramāṇakamvacanam pramāṇa upetasya abhyupagamasya vidvadbhiḥ alaṅghanīya tvāt etat ca syāt pramāṇaiḥ asamarthita sādhana abhidhānāt vādi api jetā na bhavati pratipakṣasya nirākaraṇāt 
VNṬ_80,1^1	 pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ pratijñāvirodhaḥ nāma nigraha sthānam guṇa vyatiriktam dravyam iti pratijñā rūpa ādibhyortha antarasya anupalabdheḥ iti hetuḥ soyam pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ yadi guṇa vyatiriktam dravyam rūpa ādibhye artha antarasya anupalabdhiḥ na upapadyate atha rūpa ādibhyortha antarasya anupalabdhiḥ guṇa vyatiriktam dravyam iti na upapadyate etena eva pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhena pratijñā virodhaḥ sva vacanena vyākhyātaḥ sūtra kāreṇa asya upalakṣaṇa artham uktam etat śramaṇā prativirata puruṣa sambhogāḥ garbhaḥ ca na antareṇa puruṣa sambhogam iti sva vacana vyāhatiḥ hetu virodhaḥ etena ca uktaḥ iti vartate sarvva pṛthak nānā na asti ekaḥ bhāvaḥ iti yāvat samūhe bhāva śabda prayogāt samūha vācaka ghaṭa ādi bhāva śabda vācya tvāt iti arthaḥ yasmāt samūhaḥ iti bruvāṇena eka ubhi upagataḥ bhavati eka samuccayaḥ hi samūhaḥ iti
