VNṬ_80,1^2	 tathā hi gavā ādi dravyāṇi samuditāni pratipadyamānena samūha ubhyupeyaḥ sa ca ayam samūhayanti dravyāṇi etāni gavā ādi bhāvena vyavasthitāni iti na vyavatiṣṭhate bheda upyalpataratama tvena yat tatra parama alpam yat abhedyam tatas nivarttate yatas ca ayam bhedaḥ nivarttate tat ekam atha manyase yam tam abhedyam paramāṇum manyase sā upi rūpa ādīnām samudāyaḥ iti etasmin vai darśane ye rūpa ādayaḥ samuditāḥ te paramāṇuḥ iti paramāṇau rūpam sa kasya samudāyaḥ i ti vaktavyam evam śeṣeṣu guṇeṣu atha na tam samudāyam pratipadyase aṣṭau dravyāṇi samuditāni paramāṇuḥ iti śāstram vyāhatam kāme aṣṭa dravyakaḥ aśabdaḥ paramāṇuḥ iti tasmāt anupapattau= aneka upapattiḥ iti ati mauḍhyam asiddhaḥ ca ayam hetuḥ yasmāt anekavidha lakṣaṇaiḥ gandha ādibhiḥ guṇaiḥ budhna ādibhiḥ ca avayavaiḥ sambaddhaḥ ekaḥ bhāvaḥ upapadyate atas śabdāt ekārtha adhigatau śeṣa ūnu ṣakta ūrthaḥ gamyate iti 
VNṬ_81,1^1	 nanu ca ayam api pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ iti prathamāt asya aviśeṣaḥ mā evam ubhaya āśrita tvāt virodhasya vivakṣātaḥ anyatara nirdeśaḥ iti bhāradvāje na eva uktattvāt pratijñāyāḥ dṛṣṭānta virodhaḥ yathā vyaktam eka prakṛtikam parimita tvāt śarāva ādi vat iti śarāva ādiḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ eka prakṛti tvam bādhate dṛṣṭānta bhūtāyāḥ prakṛteḥ prakṛti aṃtara tvāt eka prakṛti tve vā śarāva ādiḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ ayuktaḥ hetoḥ ca dṛṣṭanta ādibhiḥ virodhaḥ yathā guṇa vyatiriktam dravyam artha antara tvena anupalabhyamānat tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat iti ghaṭa ādīnā ambhedena grahaṇāt hetum bādhate dṛṣṭāntaḥ 
VNṬ_81,1^2	 ādi grahaṇena hetoḥ upanaya nigamanaābhyām virodhaḥ gṛhyate anayoḥ udāharaṇam anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt yad kṛta kantat a nityam yathā ākāśan tathā ca kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ iti upanayena hetoḥ virodhaḥ tathā hi udāharaṇā pekṣaḥ tathā iti uyupasaṃhāraḥ na tathā iti ca iti sādhyasya upanayaḥ uktaḥ iha ca viparītam udāharaṇam iti etat apekṣā upanayena hetoḥ virodhaḥ īdṛśe ca prayoge tasmāt anityaḥ iti upasaṃhāre nigamanena pramāṇa virodhaḥ ca pratijñā hetoḥ yathā anuṣṇa ugniḥ dravya tvāt jala vat iti pratyakṣamba ādhate para pakṣaḥ ityādi etat ca yat ca sva pakṣāḥ napekṣan ca ityādi 
VNṬ_81,1^3	 etat api ubhayam pratijñā hetoḥ virodhaḥ iti anena eva saṅgṛhīta tvāt pṛthak nigraha sthāna tvena na eva vaktavyam iti darśayati para pakṣaḥ iti atra pareṇa pra māṇe kṛte kaṇā daḥ anaikāntikam udbhāvayati sva pakṣa an apekṣañcā iti atra tu vaiśeṣikaḥ eva pramāṇaṅkaroti parastam vyabhicārayati iti bhedaḥ yadi tarhi go tva ādinā vyabhicāre kṛte viruddham uttaram tathā sati anaikāntikaḥ nirviṣayaḥ iti āha ubhaya ityādi vādi prativādi prasiddhaḥ ubhaya pakṣa saṃpratipannaḥ saḥ anaikāntikaḥ tad viṣaya tvāt upacāreṇa tathā ca vṛttiḥ tena anaikāntika codanā iti atra api ityādi 
VNṬ_81,1^4	 na etat api pratikṣipati tad āśrayaḥ sā pratijñā aśrayaḥ yasya virodhasya sa tathā tad kṛtaḥ vā iti tayā pratijñayā kṛtaḥ pariśiṣṭam ati sphuṭam vyatiriktānām api kutaścid parvata ādeḥ sakāśāt viprakarṣiṇa ampiśāca ādīnām tatra idam eva nigraha adhikaraṇam yat uta pratijñāyāḥ prayogaḥ na virodhaḥ pratijñāyāḥ nigraha adhikaraṇam iti vartate kim iti tad adhikaraṇa tvāt pratijña āśraya tvāt iti arthaḥ yadi punar tad adhikaraṇaḥ na bhavet bhavet nigraha adhikaraṇam iti āha yadi ityādi prastāvasya vādasya upasaṃhāraḥ parisamāptiḥ tasya avasānat nimitam pratijñā prayogaḥ tanmātreṇa eva asādhana aṅga abhidhānāt vādinā ubhaṅgāt 
VNṬ_81,1^5	 kvacid prastāva upasaṃhāra avasara tvāt iti paṭhyate tatra api vāda parisamāpteḥ pratijñāpada prayoge satya vasaraḥ adhikāraḥ iti arthaḥ atha buddhiḥ yathā bhavadbhiḥ kasyacid arthasya kṣaṇika tva ādikam ekam eva sādhyam bahubhiḥ satva utpattimatva pratyaya bheda bhedi tva ādibhiḥ hetubhiḥ pratipādyate tathā eka mapi dūṣyampara upanyastam sādhana vākyam pratijñā upādāna dvāreṇa tad virodha dvāreṇa anyathā vā dūṣyate tathā ca na ayan doṣaḥ parājita parājaya abhāvāt iti tat atra āha ye tu hetavaḥucyante teṣām vikalpena pūrvvahetu anapekṣayā evam vā etat 
VNṬ_81,1^6	 athavā anyathā sādhayāmi iti etat sādhya sādhanāya vṛtteḥ kāraṇāt sāmarthyam asti kim punar kāraṇam na samuccaye na eva prayoga eti a āha anyathā yadi samuccaye na eva apara hetu antara prayoga ubhīṣṭaḥ tadā dvitīyasya vaiyarthyāt vikalpena sāmānyam iti vartate vaiyarthyam eva pratipādayati yadi hi tatra api eka prayogam antareṇa aparasya prayogaḥ na sambhavet ubhaya pratiṣedhena vidhi avasāyāt yadi ekasya prayoge aparasya samuccayena prayogaḥ sambhavet iti arthaḥ tadā na dvitīyasya kaścid sādhāna arthaḥ pratīta pratipādana abhāvāt 
VNṬ_81,1^7	 prathama hetu pratipāditaḥ eva arthe vyāpṛta tvāt niṣpādita kriye dāruṇi pravṛttasya eva dātṛ ādeḥ na kaścid sādhakatama tva arthaḥ iti yāvat nanu ca sādhana vat vikalpena eva dūṣaṇam api bhaviṣyati evam manyate na evam parobhyupagantuḥ mahati evam hi tena svayam eva pratijñāyāḥ asādhana aṅga tvam pratipad nam bhavet tatas ca etat vyāhanyate pratijñā hetu udāharaṇa upanaya nigamanāni avayavāḥ iti anyaiḥ eva hetubhiḥ iti avayavi dravya niṣedhakaiḥ pūrvva ukta prakāraiḥ kumbha ādi śabdasya eka ghaṭa ādi avayavi dravya lakṣaṇa viśeṣān abhidhānam anekasya ca arthasya rūpa ādeḥ yat sāmānyam eka artha kriyā sāmarthya ātma kantad abhidhānañca pratipādya sarvu asya śabda arthasya rūpa ādeḥ eka artha kriyā samarthasya nānā artha rūpa tayā karaṇa bhūtayā 
VNṬ_81,1^8–84,1	 ekaḥ ca asau vastu viśeṣa svabhāvaḥ ca avayavi dravya rūpaḥ te sya bhāvaḥ eka vastu viśeṣa svabhāva tā tasyāḥ abhāvam upadarśayat nāsti ekaḥ bhāvaḥ iti abhida dhyāt bauddhaḥ na tu rūpāṇi indriya arthān pratikṣipan syāt matiḥ rūpa ādi avyatirekāt sāmarthyam api anekam tat kathantat ekam iti ucyate katham vā tasya śabda artha tvam na hi sva lakṣaṇam śabda arthaḥ iti ucyate nānā bhūtam api sāmarthya bhinna vatsu a vyatirekāt eka artha kriyā kāritayā eka pratyavamarṣa hetu tvāt paramparayā ekam iti ākhyāyate yathā uktam eka pratyavamarṣasya hetu tvāt dhīra bhedinī ekadhā hetu bhāvena vyaktīnām api abhinnatā iti 
VNṬ_84,2	 puruṣa adhyavasāya anirodhena śabda artha tvam tasya vyavasthāpyate puruṣohyanādi mithyā abhyāsa vāsanā paripāka prabhāvāt antar mātrā viparivartinam ākāram bāhayeṣu eva āropya dṛśya vikalpayoḥ eka tvam pratipannaḥ paramārthataḥ tu nirviṣayāḥ eva dhvanayaḥ vyaktīnām vijñāna ākārasya ca artha antara anugama abhāvena abhilāpa agocara tvāt yathā adhyavasāyañca ākārasya satvāt yathā uktam sūtre yena yena hi nāmnā vai yaḥ yaḥ dharma ubhilapyate na sa samvidyate tatra dharmāṇām sā hi dharma tā iti tat ayam atra samadāya arthaḥ rūpa ādīna aṅghaṭasya ca yathā kramam aneka tvam eka tvañca vahu vacana eka vacana abhidhaya tvāt tat yathā nakṣatrāṇi śaśī iti evamādibhiḥ anumāna ābhāsaiḥ pareṇa ghaṭa ādi śabdasya viṣayoyoyam eka arthaḥ avayavi abhidhāna ubhyupagataḥ saḥ eva pratikṣipyate na tu rūpa rasa ādayaḥ paramāṇu svabhāvāḥ tathā hi teṣām pratyekam ekaika ātmaka tvam iṣṭam eva kevalāḥ tadā atisaphala bīja vat na samudāyam āsādayanti iti niyata saha utpāda tva paridīpanāya uktam kāma iṣṭa dravyakaḥ aśabdaḥ paramāṇuḥ atīndriyaḥ kāya indriyaḥ nava dravyaḥ daśa dravyaḥ apara indriyaḥ iti 
VNṬ_84,3^1	 yathā tu paramāṇūnāmaindriyaka tvam anitya tvañca tad vistareṇa uktam anyatra asmābhiḥ yat punar etat vahu vacana eka vacana abhidheya tvāt iti tat vyabhicāri tathā hi yadā ekasyām api yoṣiti jale sikatā dravye vā dārāḥ āpaḥ sikatā iti vyavahāraḥ tadā kintatra bāhulyam yena evam bhavati śakti bhedaḥ iti ced sarvu atra ucchinnam idānīm eka vacanam eka śakteḥ abhāvāt vastu abhedāt anyatra eka vacanam iti ced iha api astu tat ayat nirvastukaḥ niyamaḥ kriyamāṇaḥ svātantryam icchāyāḥ śabda prayoge khyāpayati etena tat api pratyuktam yat āha kumārilaḥ tatra vyaktau ca jātau ca dāra ādiḥ ced prayujyate vyakteḥ avayavānām vā saṃkhyām ādāya vartate iti 
VNṬ_84,3^2	 ṣaṇṇagarī iti ca katham vahuṣu eka vacanam na hi nagarāṇi eva kiñcid kutas teṣām samāhāraḥ prāsāda puruṣa ādīnām vijātīyānām anārambhāt kutas tad samudāyaḥ dravyam asaṃyogāt ca na api saṃyogaḥ prāsāda ādīnām paraspara saṃyogāt prāsādasya svayam saṃyoga ātmakasya nirguṇa tayā apareṇa asaṃyogāt ca tataa iva ca saṃkhyā bhāvaḥ tad saṃyoga puruṣa viśiṣṭā sattā nagaram iti ced kim asya aniratiśayāyāḥ viśeṣaṇam sattāyāḥ ca eka tvāt nagara bahutvā ipi nagarāṇi iti bahuvacanam syāt dvayasya paraspara sahita tā iti ced anupakārakayoḥ kaḥ sahāyībhāvaḥ puruṣa saṃyoga sattānām ca vahutvāt nagaram iti katham eka vacanam tathā bhūtānām kvacid abhinnā śaktiḥ sā nimittam iti ced na 
VNṬ_84,3^3	 śakteḥ vastu rūpa avyatirekāt vyatireke ca anupakāryasya pāratantrya ayogāt upakāre vā śakti upakāriṇyāḥ api śa kteḥ vyatirekaḥ iti avasthiteḥ apratipattiḥ tat avyatireke anyāsām api prasaṃgaḥ iti yat kiñcid etat prakāra antaram api āha dṛṣṭa upadarśanaḥ ca etat iti kim punar pañcamī anta nirdeśepi dṛṣṭāntaḥ bhavati iti āha kṛtaka anitya tva ādi ti yathā yena uktam hetoḥ sādhya anvayaḥ yatra ābhāvebhāvaḥ cakathyate pañcamyā tatra dṛṣṭāntaḥ hetuḥ tu upanayā atmakaḥ iti 
VNṬ_84,3^4	 kvacid arthe ghaṭa ādi dravye vipratipattau satyām rūpa ādi vyatiriktam asti na asti iti anekasya arthasya paraspara vyāvṛttasya nagara ādeḥ sāmānyam ṣaṇṇagarīti ādiyat budhya āropitam tatra prasiddham śabda prayogam ādarśya paraspara vyāvṛttānām ekārthān anugatānām buddhi samākṛte samūhe bhāva śabda prayogāt iti anena paścāt upanayena pakṣa dharma upasaṃhāram āgūrya pratipādita vipratipatti sthānaḥ san sāmānyena upasaṃharati sarvvam pṛthak iti pratipāditam pratipatti sthānam anena iti vigrahaḥ etat uktam bhavati kapāla ādi vyatirekeṇa avayavi asti na asti iti vivāde sati ayam tri lakṣaṇa hetu sūcana paraḥ dṛṣṭānte upanyastaḥ na hetuḥ prayogaḥ tu atra evam kriyate ye paraspara vyāvṛttāḥ na te vyatiriktā eka avaya vi dravya anugata mūrttayaḥ tat yathā ṣaṇṇagarya ādayaḥ tathā ca paraspara vyāvṛttāḥ kapāla ādayaḥ iti 
VNṬ_86,1	 nanu ca yadi ayam dṛṣṭānta prayogaḥ taktim ṛjunā eva tad prayoga krameṇa na prayuktaḥ yathā yat sat tad kṣaṇikam yathā ghaṭaḥ ityādau kimpañcamī anta nirdeśena vipratipatti viṣayaḥ ca kinna darśitaḥ kapāla ādeḥ avayavi pratiṣedha viśiṣṭaḥ yathā anyatra anityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka anitya tvāt iti cakārāt spaṣṭaḥ ca kasmāt hetuḥ sādhya anugataḥ na prada rśitaḥ tathā hi atra paraspara vyāvṛttānām ekārthān anugatānām buddhyā samāhite samūha bhāva śabda prayogāt iti abhyūhya vākya parisamāptiḥ kriyate atra uttaram na samāsa nirdeśāt saṃkṣepa abhidhānāt iti arthaḥ evam api prayoga darśanāt kṛtaka anitya tvāt ityādau asādhanam vākya tvāt ca sādhana prayoga utprekṣā sūcakam vākyam etat na tu idam sādhana vākyam iti arthaḥ atas eva iti dṛṣṭānta vākya tvāt eva iti yaḥ ca ayam hetuḥ tantu paṭa rūpe bhinna kāraṇe viśeṣava tvāt rūpa sparśa vat iti ayam api tantu paṭayoḥ bheda asiddhau tad āśritasya api guṇasya vibhāga asiddheḥ asiddha āśrayaḥ iti na alam iṣṭa siddhaye tathā hi sūkṣma sthūla dravya samavāyaḥ viśeṣava tvam bhinna kāla utpanna dravya saṃvāyauva iti vyācakṣate 
VNṬ_86,2	 pare nanu vicitra abhisandhayaḥ yoktāraḥ tatra ye kecid hetu abhiprāyeṇa eva vācaḥ prayuñjate tān pratyasmābhiḥ pratijñayā hetoḥ bādhanam ucyate na tu ye dṛṣṭānta abhimāninaḥ iti atra āha nace tyādi bhagava ttathāgata mata avalambinām upari ayam upakṣiptaḥ virodhaḥ bhavadbhi rākṣapādaiḥ rna ca naḥ sva pnavye tādṛśosti iti piṇḍa arthaḥ syāt matam asti eva yoga ācāraḥ yaḥ 
VNṬ_86,3^1	 paṅkena yugapad yogāt paramāṇoḥ pataṅga tām ṣaṇṇām samāna deśa tvāt piṇḍaḥ syāt aṇu mātrakaḥ ḥ ityādinā paramāṇoḥ eka tvam anabhyupagacchan= api piṇḍam samūha apara paryāyam icchati iti etat ucyate yopī tyādi kintarhi abhāvaḥ eva aṇoḥ anena prakāreṇa sādhayitum iṣṭaḥ katham eka aneka pratiṣedhāt paṅkā yoga ādinā tāvat eka tvam pratiṣiddham tad samudāya rūpam aneka tvam api tad abhāvāt eva na vidyate yathā uktan nanu tasya tasyai katā na asti yaḥ yaḥ bhāvaḥ parīkṣyate na santi tena anekepi yena ekopi na vidyate iti nanupaṅka yoga ādinā katham eka tvam apoditam yāvatā tatra tasya sāvayava tvam āpāditam te eva ca avayavāḥ tasya alpīyāṃsaḥ paramāṇavaḥ vibhāga paryavasāna lakṣaṇa tvāt paramāṇūnām atha teṣām api aṅgānām anena eva vidhānena sāvayava tvam āpādyate 
VNṬ_86,3^2	 tathā sati tatra api etat eva uttaram iti anena eva prakāreṇa na śakyate paramāṇoḥ ekatva niṣedham karttu vibhāgasya vibhajyamāna tantrattvāt kathañca anabhyupagatāṇuḥ tasya paṅka yoga ādikam abhyupagacchati iti tad asatva pratipādane sarve hetavaḥ svatas eva āśraya asiddhāḥ iti etat ca na evam yasmāt samarthāḥ vādinaḥ apagata avayava vibhāgam āsādita apakarṣayantam bhāvam aṇuḥ iti ācakṣate tasya tena paṅkā yoga ādinā eka tvam apākriyate te ca yadi evam nirākṛtāḥ santaḥ yathā upagatasya sāvayava tvam pratipadyante tadā sva pratijñāyāḥ cyaveran na hi anaṅgīkṛta sāvayava tvāḥ tathā pratyavasthānam arhanti te eva avayavāḥ santu paramāṇavaḥ iti taiḥ eva ca tad lakṣaṇam vyavasthāpanīyam yoga ācāre ṇa ca niṣedhyam iti nigṛhyante 
VNṬ_86,3^3	 atas eva na anavasthā prasaṅga sādhana tvāt ca asiddha tā doṣa upi na asti iti alam etena atha ucyate na vayam bhavantam prati idam brūmaḥ yaḥ tu kaścid adhauta pādaḥ vādī evam prāha tamprati iti tat ca asat sarvvam pṛthak bhāva lakṣaṇa pṛthak tvāt na aneka lakṣaṇena eka bhāva niṣpatteḥ iti atra prastāve bhāradvāje na asmān pratyeva kāma iṣṭa dravya kaḥ ityādinā siddhāntam asmākīnam upakṣipya api abhidhānāt tathā api abhyupagamya doṣa antaram āha na ca ayam pūrvakāt guṇa vyatiriktam iti ādi pada sūcitāt paraspara artham ādhāya bhidyate hetu pratijñayoḥ sambandhinyoḥ bādhayoḥ udāharaṇa upetayoḥ pṛthak bādha udāharaṇayoḥ na kaścid artha bhedaḥ śabda bhedaḥ tu kevalaḥ tathāvidhasya ca pṛthak udāharaṇe atiprasaṅgaḥ akṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tvāt ityādi api udāha rttavyam bhaveta 
VNṬ_86,3^4	 saha pṛthak vā iti kvacid pāṭhaḥ tatra ayam arthaḥ saha yaugapadyena yathā prathame pṛthak pratyekam yathā iha athavā virodha cintā api atra ayuktā iti āha apicā ityādi sarvvam pṛthak samūhe bhāva śabda prayogāt iti ayam hetuḥ sarvu asya dharmiṇaḥ dharmaḥ eva na bhavati śabda dharma tva āditya siddhaḥ tathā ca vyadhikaraṇa tvāt asiddha tā eva doṣaḥ guḍaḥ madhuraḥ kākasya kārṣṇyāt iti yathā tatra na virodhaḥ bhinna adhikaraṇa tvāt hetu pratijñā arthayoḥ syāt buddhiḥ samūha vācaka śabda vācya tvāt iti evam bhāvi viktena bhāṣyaṭīkāyām prayogāt vyadhikaraṇa tvam na asti evam manyate na tāvadaya mudyota kare ṇa evam prayuktasya vā ayam asmābhiḥ doṣobhidhātum ārabdhaḥ yepi samprati anyathā prayuñjate teṣām api yadi ayam doṣaḥ na bhavati 
VNṬ_86,3^5	 bhavatu anantara uktaḥ tu doṣaḥ vakṣyamāṇaḥ ca brahmaṇā api na śakyate parihartum iti pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhasya ca nigraha sthāna antara tvam aṅgīkṛtya mayā idam abhyadhāyi na tu asya tat yuktam hetvābhāsāḥ ca nigraha sthānānī ti anena eva saṅgṛhīta tvāt iti etat vibhaṇiṣuḥ āha apicā ityādi dvau= avayavau yasyāḥ doṣa jāteḥ daḥ ṣa prakārasya sā dvayī kām iti a āha viruddha tām asiddha tāñca kathampunar viruddha tā iti āha viruddha tā ityādi ayam atra saṃkṣepa arthaḥ pratijñā hetvoḥ yatra prayogeṃvirodhaḥ codyate tatra avaśyam siddhena dharmiṇā bhāvyam siddhe ca tasmin dharmiṇi hetoḥ vā satvam bhavet sādhya dharmasya dvayoḥ vā tatra na tāvat dvayoḥ api satvam paraspara virodhi tvena śīta uṣṇayoḥ iva eka adhikaraṇa tva abhāvāt 
VNṬ_86,3^6	 anyathā saha ekatra avasthānāt rasa rūpavat avirodhaḥ eva bhavet iti pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhaḥ dūrataraḥ eva prasajyate tat vakṣyati viruddhayoḥ svabhāvayoḥ ekatra asambhavān na ca anyathā virodhaḥ iti atha hetoḥ tatra satvam evam api yatra hetuḥ tatra na sādhya dharmaḥ tad viparyayaḥ tu vidyate iti vyaktam asya viruddha tvam nityaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtaka tva ādi vat tat āha viruddha tā siddheḥ hetvoḥ dharmiṇi bhāvaḥ iti yadā punar tasmin dharmiṇi pramāṇa antareṇa sādhya dharmasya satvam niścitam tadā tatra hetoḥ avṛttiḥ virodhinā kroḍīkṛtattvāt atas ca asiddhatvam hetoḥ kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ akārya tvāt iti yathā tad jāte asiddha tā punar ddharmiṇī ityādi atham anyase 
VNṬ_86,3^7	 pramāṇena siddhaḥ eva guṇa vyatirikte dravya ādau dharmiṇi pratijñā hetoḥ virodhaḥ vyavasthāpyate tatas na ayam doṣaḥ iti atas idam āśaṅkate asiddhaḥ ityādinā evam api yadi nāma dharmya bhāvena pakṣa dharmasya asambhavāt viruddha tvam parihṛtam asiddha tvam punar tad avastham eva iti manasi ādhāya āha pramāṇa yoge tu ubhayoḥ vādi prativādinoḥ dharmiṇi hetoḥ vṛtti saṃśayaḥ pramāṇa nivṛttau= api artha abhāva asiddheḥ atas ca asidh dha tā eva sandigdha āśraya tvāt iha ni kuñje mayūraḥ kekāyi tattvāt itya ādi vat tu śabdaḥ pratipādaka pramāṇā yoge dharmiṇaḥ sandigdha āśraya tā hetoḥ dharmi bādhaka pramāṇa vṛttau sphuṭam eva āśraya asiddhatatvam sarvvagataḥ ātmani sādhye sarvatra upalabhyamāna guṇa tva vaditi asya samuccaya arthaḥ 
VNṬ_86,3^8	 tathā hi asiddheḥ dharmi svabhāvaḥ iti atra pratipādaka pramāṇa āvṛtteḥ asiddhaḥ dharmī vivakṣitaḥ syāt bādhaka pramāṇa vṛtteḥ vā pūrvasmin pakṣe kaṇṭhena eva uktaḥ doṣaḥ uttaratra śabdena samuccitaḥ atra audyota karam uttaram āśaṅkate ubhaya āśraya tvā diti ādinā gata artha tvāt su jñānaṃsarvvam etat na sarvu atra ityādinā nirākaroti yathā uktam prāk na dvayīm doṣa jātim iti atra atha pratijñā mātra bhāvyā iva hetu anapekṣaḥ pratijñā virodhaḥ vyavasthāpyate yathā na asti ātmā śramaṇā garbhiṇī iti atra iti atas āha anapekṣe ca hetu grahaṇam asamvaddham anupakāraka tvāt yat api idam hetu virodhasya udāharaṇam dattam nityaḥ śabdaḥ ityādinā tad pratijñā virodhasya hetunā yuktam iti kathanāya āha na cedi tyādi syāt matam ubhaya āśraya tvāt virodhasya evam api na hetutaā iva iti atas ucyate ubhaya āśrayepī tyādi 
VNṬ_86,3^9	 evam upadarśitāni udāharaṇāni prakṣipya atidiṣṭa dūṣaṇāya āha yat ca uktam etena pratijñāyāḥ dṛṣṭānta virodha ādayā upi vaktavyā bhaṇḍa ālekhī anyāḥ yene ti iti śabdaḥ vaktavyaḥ iti atra pratipattavyaḥ anyathā pareṇa uttarasya aprayuktattvāt duḥśliṣṭaḥ bhaveta bhaṇḍa grahaṇat nitya puruṣa upalakṣaṇa artham yathā hi bhaṇḍā prākṛtān vismāpayantaḥ citra lakṣaṇa upetakapi śāla bhañjikā ādi praticchandakam ālikhya vicitra śilpa kalā kauśala śālinaḥ atidi śaṃti evam prakārāṇi api asmad kauśala nirmitāni eka tāla mātreṇa hasti ādi rūpaka sthānāni pratipattavyāni iti tathā jātīyakam etadu dyota karasya tathā hi etat eva bhāvaḥ upadarśita hetu virodha ādikam hetvābhāsa vyatirikta lakṣaṇa upetam tat atidiṣṭe punar kā eva cintā tām eva ca atidiṣṭasya dṛṣṭānta virodha ādeḥ hetvābhāsa vyatirikta lakṣaṇa apetatām abhidhātum upakramate 
VNṬ_86,3^10	 tatra api ityādinā yatra pratijñāyāḥ dṛṣṭānta virodhaḥ tatra api pakṣīkṛta dharma viparyayavati dṛṣṭānte sati virodhaḥ syāt pratijñāyāḥ dṛṣṭāntena iti śeṣaḥ pakṣīkṛtaḥ ca asau dharmaḥ ca tasya viparyayaḥ sa vidyate yasmin= iti vigrahaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ iti ca sādharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ abhipretaḥ yasmāt vaidharmya dṛṣṭāntaḥ sādhya dharma viparyayavān eva tatra kaḥ virodhaḥ tatra udāharaṇam nityaḥ śabdaḥ ghaṭa vat iti viruddhe ca dṛṣṭānte sati yadi pakṣa dharmasya vṛttiḥ ananya sādhāraṇā prasādhyate pramāṇena viruddhaḥ tadā hetvābhāsaḥ na anya sādhāraṇa iti ananya sādhāraṇāḥ anya śabdena pakṣīkṛta dharma viparyayavataḥ pṛthak bhūtaḥ pakṣīkṛta dharmavān abhipretaḥ pakṣīkṛta dharma viparyayavatī evavartate iti evam yadi sādhyate iti arthaḥ 
VNṬ_86,3^11	 yathā anayoḥ eva sādhya dṛṣṭāntayoḥ kāryatvāt iti tad vipakṣīkṛta dharma bahis vyoma ādau na vartate tad viparīte punar ghaṭe vartate iti sādhāraṇāyām vṛttau sādhitāyām sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ iti śeṣaḥ anaikāntikaḥ sādhāraṇa ākhyaḥ yathā anayoḥ eva sādhya udāharaṇayoḥ prameya tvāt iti aprasādhite ca ātad vṛtti niyame tayoḥ sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ vṛtti niyame sa pakṣaḥ eva varttate vi pakṣaḥ eva iti anaikāntikaḥ eva sandigdha anvayaḥ sandigdha vyatirekaḥ vā yathā sarvu avidvīta rāgaḥ vā vivakṣitaḥ puruṣaḥ na vā tathā vaktṛ tvāt rathyā nara vat iti tayoḥ eva sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ avṛttau vā satyāmasādhāraṇaḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ śrāvaṇa tvāt iti yathā 
VNṬ_86,3^12	 paraḥ prāha viruddha dṛṣṭānta āvṛttau hetoḥ viparyaya vṛttau ca satyāt na kaścid hetu doṣaḥ tat yathā anityaḥ śabdaḥ pratyaya bheda bhedi tvāt nabhaḥ vat iti sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa ca ghaṭa vat iti atra na asiddha tvam dhirmaṇi hetoḥ sadbhāvāt na api anaikāntika tvam ubhayatra āvṛtteḥ pratibandha sadbhāvāt ca na ca viruddha tvam sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ vaiparītyena vṛtya bhāvāt dṛṣṭāntena tu virodhaḥ pratijñāyāḥ iti ayam hetu doṣān atikrāntaḥ viṣayaḥ pratijñāyāḥ dṛṣṭāntena ca virodhasya iti idam apanudati na tadā api saṃśaya hetu tva anativṛtteḥ yasmāt dṛṣṭānte na pratijñāyāḥ virodhaḥ sādharmye dṛṣṭānte doṣaḥ na vaidharmye kasmāt abhimata tvāt virodhasya pakṣīkṛta dharma viparyayavān eva hi vaidharmyaṃdṛṣṭāntaḥ ucyate iti abhiprāyaḥ 
VNṬ_86,3^13	 yadi nāma evam tathā api katham hetvābhāsān ativṛttiḥ iti āha sādharmya dṛṣṭānte ca viparīta dharmavati nabhasi nā avyabhicāra dharma tā śakyāḥ darśayitum tad arthaḥ ca dṛṣṭāntaḥ pradarśate yat āha tri rūpaḥ hetuḥ iti uktam pakṣa dharme ca saṃsthitaḥ rūḍhe rūpa dvayam śeṣam dṛṣṭāntena pradarśyate iti nanu ca katham aśakyā yāvatā pratyaya bheda bhedi tvam anitya tva avyabhicāryā iva tatvataḥ iti atas āha vastutas sādhya avyabhicārepī ti vidyamānopya vyabhicāraḥ pramāṇena apratipādita tvāt asat kalpaḥ iti bhāvaḥ tat etat na apradarśitāvi na abhā= a sambaddhāt hetoḥ sādhya niścayaḥ tat tasmāt na pratijñāyāḥ dṛṣṭānta virodhopi hetvābhāsān ativartate asya api tadānīm saṃdigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttika tva ādi tyāgūritam na kevala hetu virodhaḥ iti api śabdaḥ paramatamāśaṅkate 
VNṬ_86,3^14	 ubhayathā api hetu dvāreṇa dṛṣṭānta dvāreṇa ca na hetu dvāreṇa prāk dṛṣṭānta doṣāt prasaṅgena parājitasya vādinaḥ doṣa antarasya dṛṣṭānta virodhasya vācyasya vā anapekṣaṇāt parājita parājaya abhāvāt ityākūtam viśeṣeṇa sādhana avayava anukrama vādinaḥ naiyāyikasya sa hi pratijñā hetu udāharaṇa upanaya nigamanānām ānupūrvīm pratipannaḥ kaḥ punar tasya atiśayaḥ iti āha udāharaṇa sādharmyam ityādi aṅgīkṛtya ca idam avādina tu dṛṣṭānta virodhaḥ hetvābhāsa rūpa asaṃsparśi asti yathoktam anantaram iti etena vikalpataḥ doṣa vidhānam pratyuktam evantā vat vyavasthitam etat yathā pratijñāyāḥ dṛṣṭānta virodhaḥ hetvābhāsāt na ativartate iti yat punar udāhṛtam aviddha karaṇena bhāṣyaṭīkāyām vyaktam eka prakṛtikam parimita tvāt śarāva ādi vat iti 
VNṬ_86,3^15	 tatra api viruddhaḥ hetuḥ parimitattvasya hetoḥ sa pakṣe abhāve vā vṛtteḥ vipakṣe ca aneka prakṛtike śarāva ādau vṛtteḥ mṛdaḥ pratikṣaṇam pratyavayavañca bhidyamāna tvāt saṃprati hetoḥ api dṛṣṭāntena virodhaḥ hetvābhāsa antargataḥ iti kathayati hetoḥ api dṛṣṭānta virodhe satya sādhāraṇa tvam ubhayatra āvṛtteḥ viruddha tvam vā kadāviruddhattvam iti āha vaidharmye yadi syāt api atra udāharaṇam uktam tena eva guṇa vyatiriktam dravyam artha antara tvena anupalabhyamāna tvāt ghaṭa vat iti atra api dṛśya tve sati iti hetu viśeṣaṇe viruddhaḥ sa pakṣe avartamāna tvāt vipakṣe ca rūpa ādīnām svarūpe vartam āgattvāt viśeṣaṇa anupādāne tu vyabhicārortha antarattvena anupalabdhānām api piśāca ādīnām paraspara vyatireki tvāt 
VNṬ_86,3^16–93,3	 na ca atra ghaṭa vat iti dṛṣṭāntaḥ yuktaḥ tasya eva dravya antara tvena pakṣīkṛta tvāt tasya rūpa ādibhyaḥ bhedena grahaṇam pūrvvam eva pratiṣid dhaṃgrahaṇe ca asiddhaḥ hetvābhāse iti asmat matam eva sthitam atha hetoḥ pramāṇa virodhe kaḥ hetvābhāse iti āha asiddha ugneḥ śaityasya avidyamāna tvāt yat punar atra udāharaṇam anyat anuṣṇa ugniḥ dravya tvāt jala vat iti tat ayuktam na hi pratyakṣam dravyam hetum bādhate tasya dharmiṇi siddha tvāt kintu pratijñā artham anuṣṇa tvam atha pratijñā arthasya pratyakṣeṇa bādhita tvāt hetoḥ tena vyāptiḥ nna asti iti hetoḥ pramāṇa virodhaḥ ucyate evantarhi viruddhena sādhya dharmeṇa avyāpteḥ sandigdha vyatirekaḥ hetvābhāse iti asmad pakṣaḥ eva samarthitaḥ hetoḥ pramāna viroghasya hetvābhāsa anatikramāt tat uktam pratyakṣa ādi virodhāḥ ye vyāpta kāla upapātinaḥ te sarve na viruddhena vyāpti dharmeṇa yuñjate iti 
VNṬ_93,4^1	 syāt matam pratijñāyāḥ pramāṇa virodhaḥ tanmātra bhāvi tvāt hetvābhāse antargamayitum na pāryate iti atas āha pratijñāyāḥ pramāṇa virodhaḥ sva vacana virodhena vyākhyātaḥ kṛta pratikriyaḥ tatra idam eva nigraha adhikaraṇam asādhana aṅga bhūtāyāḥ pratijñāyāḥ sādhana vākye prayogaḥ ityādinā iti tasmāt sarvvaḥ eva iti upasaṃharati yat tu viruddham uttaram iti pūrvva pakṣa uktam aparam upakṣipati tad asambaddham eva yasmāt yadi hī tyadi ani tyaḥ śabdaḥ aindriyaka tvāt ghaṭa vat iti ekam bauddhena anyena vā kṛte mīmāṃsakaḥ kāṇādonyaḥ vā sva pakṣa siddhena go tva ādinā sāmānyena parasya sādhana vādinaḥ bauddhasya hetoḥ vyabhicāra siddhim ākāṃkṣeta go tvam api aindriyakam tat api bhavataḥ anityam prasajyate iti eva yadi param pratyeva adhyāropya abhidadhyāt vyabhicāram tadā tasya bauddha sya tad sāmānyam aindriyakam nityañca sva pakṣa viruddham nitya padārtha an abhyupagāmāt na abhimatam atas ca katham vyabhicāraḥ iti virodhaḥ vyāhatiḥ ayuktattvam itiyāvat yujyate uttarasya iti adhyāhartavyam 
VNṬ_93,4^2	 na tu punar evam asau parasya iva upari bhāram upakṣipya vyabhicāram udbhāvayati tat katham uttarasya virodhaḥ yatas sahyuttara vādī svayam pratipanne nitya tvena go tve hetoḥ aindriyaka tvasya vṛtteḥ saṃśayānaḥ san kiṅghaṭa vat aindriyaka tvāt anityaḥ śabdaḥ bhavatu kimvā go tva āt i vat nityaḥ iti apratipattim aniścayam ātmanaḥ tathā bruvāṇaḥ khyāpayati sat pakṣe khalva indriyakam api go tvam nityam tasmāt ayam sāṃprati anaikāntikaḥ iti ittham ātmīyam eva abhyupagamam puraskṛtya anekān tañcodayati tatas sādhu iva uttaram iti samudāya arthaḥ syāt matambauddhasya na asti eva go tvam nityam tatas vyāhatam eva uttaram iti atas āha sa ca hetu raindriyaka tvāt iti satyasati vā go tve paramārthataḥ 
VNṬ_93,4^3	 aprasādhita sādhana sāmarthyaḥ san viparyaye bādhaka pramāṇa āvṛtyā saṃśaya hetu tvāt anaikāntikaḥ eva aprasādhitam sādhanāya sāmarthyam sādhyāḥ vinā abhau= i tva lakṣaṇam asya iti vigrahaḥ sādhana śabdaḥ bhāva sādhanaḥ yadā tu bādhaka pramāṇa balena hetoḥ avi na abhāvam sarvvā upasaṃhāreṇa sādhayati yat kiñcit indriya jñāna grāhyam sva nirbhāsa jñāna janaka tvāt tatra sarvvam anityam nitya tve sarvvadā tad viṣayam jñānam prasañjate na vā kadācid apitathā hi sva ātmani jñāna janane yat śaktam śaktam eva tat athavā aśaktam kadācid ced aśaktam sarvadā eva tat tasya śaktiḥ aśaktiḥ vā yā svabhāvena saṃsthitā nitya tvāt acikitsyasya kaḥ tām kṣapayitum kṣamaḥ iti 
VNṬ_94,1^1	 tadānīm go tva ādīnām api nityānām eka praghaṭena iva pāṭita tvāt go tve hetoḥ avṛtteḥ na saṃśayaḥ eva bhavati etene tyādi su jñānam tatra api anaikāntika hetvā abhāsa tvānativṛttiḥ iti saṃkṣepaḥ tad saṃśaya hetu tva mukhena anaikāntika tvam asamarthite sati hetau anyatra apī ti eka pakṣa pratipad nepi vastuni tulyam iti na ubhaya siddha itarayoḥ vastunoḥ anaikāntika tva viśeṣaḥ yathā kathitam anantaram eva sa ca hetuḥ sati asati vā ityādinā itarat eka pakṣa pratipannam anaikāntika viṣaya tvāt ca anaikāntikam iti vyākhyātam syāt cittannā niṣṭeḥ dūṣaṇam sarvu aprasiddhaḥ tu dvayoḥ api sādhanam 
VNṬ_94,1^2	 dūṣaṇam va iti etat katham evannavya ahanyate iti tat ca na evam niścita dūṣaṇa abhisandhi vacanāt tatas eva tad anantaram āhānyaḥ punar sādhya tvam īkṣate iti etat tu syāt tadā dvayoḥ ekasya api na jaya parājayau yat api ukta mudya uta kareṇa pratijñā virodha sūtram eva vivṛṇvatā dṛṣṭānta ābhāsāḥ ityādi tat api avayava antara vādinaḥ naiyāyikasya ayuktam bauddhaḥ eva evam bruvāṇaḥ śobhate iti abhipretam tad vacanena hetvābhāsa vacanena gamyamānasya dṛṣṭānta ābhāsasya tasmāt hetoḥ sakāśāt sā dhana antara tva abhāva prasaṅgāt dṛṣṭāntasya iti śeṣaḥ 
VNṬ_95,1^1	 nanu ca dṛṣṭānta ābhāsānām hetvābhāseṣu antarbhāve atidiṣṭe hetoḥ dṛṣṭānte a vayava antaram na prāpnoti iti vacanam asambaddham eva iti atas āha dṛṣṭānta ābhāsānā mi tyādi ayam asya prayogaḥ manasi vijṛmbhate yadi atas artha antara bhūtam na tad ābhāsa vacanena tad ābhāsa vacanam nyāyyaṃna ca tad ābhāseṣu tad ābhāsānām antarbhāvaḥ tat yathā pratyakṣa ābhāsānām anumāna ābhāseṣu tathā ca bhavataḥ hetoḥ dṛṣṭānta ūrtha antara bhūtaḥ iti vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhiḥ atas avaśyam dṛṣṭāntasya hetau= antarbhāvaḥ eṣṭavyaḥ tatra ca na dṛṣṭāntaḥ pṛthak sādhana avayavaḥ syāt apṛthak vṛtteḥ eka vyāpārat tvāt iti arthaḥ etat eva vyācaṣṭe yaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ ityādinā 
VNṬ_95,1^2	 evam pratijñā hetvoḥ virodhasya prapañcasya hetvābhāsaiḥ saṅgṛhīta tvāt na pṛthak vacanam karttavyam iti abhidhāya adhunā pratigha hāni ādīnām api iyam eva gatiḥ iti āvedanāya āha api ca ityādi pūrvva pakṣa vādi grahaṇam uttara pakṣa vādinaḥ ajñāna ādīni hetvābhāsa sparśāni saṃtīti kathana artham tad sambandhīni iti hetvābhāsa pūrvva pakṣa vādi sambandhīni vā atha ucyate artha antara gamana ādīnām hetvābhāsā saṃsparśittvā nnateṣu antarbhāvaḥ iti tat ca asat artha antara gamana ādeḥ api hetoḥ asamarthaḥ evam ati sambhavāt kutas asamarthasya nyāya balena sādhya pratipādane vādinaḥ iti śeṣaḥ mithyā pravṛtteḥ artha antara gamana ādinā iti abhiprāyaḥ 
VNṬ_96,1^1	 uttaraḥ paścāt phala bhāvī sa ca asau pratijñāsanyāsaḥ ca tasya apekṣayā kinna kiñcid iti arthaḥ aśaktaḥ paricchedaḥ sam khye yeṣām klīva pralāpa ceṣṭitānām tāni tathā klīva ādīnām pralāpāḥ yeṣām vādinā anteṣām ceṣṭitāni pratijñā saṃnyāsa ādīni vai kim upanyastaiḥ kaḥ punar evam sati doṣaḥ iti āha evam hi ati prasaṅgaḥ syāt evamādyapi iti mūrcchā vepathutra sattva ādīnām ādi śabdena avarodhaḥ tasmāt etat api asambaddham vidvat sadasi evam prakārasya sthūla tvāt ittya abhiprāyaḥ tat atra bhāvi viktaḥ svayam āśaṃkya kila pratividhatte sthūla tvena idam nigraha sthānam iti ced prāśnika prativādi sannidhau pratijñāta artha apahnavaṅkaroti iti asambaddham ucyate tat nābhi prāya aparijñānāt 
VNṬ_96,1^2	 na brūmaḥ dhvaṃsī śabdaḥ iti kintu saṃyoga vibhāgābhyām na vyaktaḥ iti ayam pratijñāta arthaḥ iti āha sāmānyasya ca sva āśraya vyaṅgya tvāt vivāda abhāvaḥ iti nigraha sthānantu pūrvam apratijñāta artha tvāt anaikāntika doṣeṇa pratiṣedhe hetau pratijñāta artha apahnavaṅkaroti iti nigṛhyate iti tatra vācyam yadi vādī sā akāṃkṣa eva antarāle kenacid durvvidagdhena anaikāntika doṣeṇa coditaḥ san pratijñāta artha phalīkaraṇena sva abhiprāyam āviṣkaroti tadā anyopi na kaścid doṣaḥ kim aṅga punar pratijñāsaṃnyāsaḥ atha nirāka aṃkṣaḥ san paścāt coditaḥ pratijñām viśinaṣṭi tat api anaikāntika doṣeṇa eva nigṛhyate iti kim uttara pratijñā saṃnyāsa apekṣayā iti na kiñcid parihṛtam kiñca sphuṭam idam pratijñā antarentarbhavati iti naḥ pṛthak vācyam iti 
VNṬ_97,1^1	 aviśeṣa ukte hetāvi tyādi sūtraṃatra nidarśanam udāharaṇam iti arthaḥ kāpilaḥ pramāṇayati pradhāna siddhi pratyāśayā eka prakṛti idam vyaktam vyakta ādi parimita tvāt ghaṭa śarāva ādi vat iti ekā pra kṛtiḥ asya iti vigrahaḥ prakṛtiḥ upādāna kāraṇam yā ca kila sā prakṛtiḥ vikāra grāmasya tad pradhāna miti iyam alīka pratyāśāsāṅkhyasya aparimāṇañcatura sramparimaṇḍalam ityādi mṛd pūrvvakāṇām iti anvayam āha asya hetoḥ vyabhicāreṇa pratyavasthānam prativādinā kriyate nānā prakṛtīna aṅga vāśu ādīnām eka prakṛtīnāñca kumbha udañcana ādīnān dṛṣṭam parimāṇam iti evam pratyavasthite sati prativādini yadi vā pratyavasthitaḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ pradhāna vādī āha 
VNṬ_97,1^2	 eka prakṛti samanvaye sati parimāṇa darśanāt iti sa viśeṣaṇa tvāt hetoḥ vyabhicāra abhāvaḥ iti matiḥ katham punar eka prakṛti samanvayaḥ iti āha sukha duḥkha moha samanvitam hi idam vyaktam parimitam gṛhyate sarvu atra tad kārya darśanāt ityākūtam tathā hi sukha bahulānāmprasāda lāghava prasava abhiṣu aṅgāt harṣa prītayaḥ kāryam rajaḥ bahulānām śoṣa tāpa bheda staṃbha udvega āpad veṣāḥ tamaḥ bahulānām sa āvaraṇam ādanāya dhvaṃsa vībhatsa dainya gauravāṇi etāni ca sarvvāṇi sarvu atra eva yathā utkarṣa apakarṣa bhedam upalabhyante tasmāt traiguṇya prakṛti idam viśvam tat idam ityādinā nigraha sthāna tve kāraṇam āha atra apī tyādyasya pratiṣedhaḥ su jñānaḥ avirāmāt acchedāt apari samāpta tvāt sādhana abhidhānasya iti arthaḥ 
VNṬ_98,1	 yathā ukta lakṣaṇaḥ iti eka adhikaraṇau viruddhau dharmau= iti pakṣa pratipakṣa lakṣaṇam smarayati parigrahe vādi prativādibhyām kṛte sati hetutaḥ sādhya siddhau prakṛtāyām hetu vaśāt sādhya siddhiḥ iti etasmin prakaraṇe sati prakṛtorthaḥ śabda nitya tvam tena asaṅgata tvāt tad asambaddhattvāt tad anupakāraka tvāt iti arthaḥ tathā hi vinā api rūpa siddhyā prātipadikā ādi vyākhyānam yathā kathañcid pratipāditāt arthāt eva arthaḥ sidhyati nyāyyam etat iti sva matena aviruddha tvāt abhyanujānāti kadā ca pūrva uttara pakṣa vādinoḥ nyāyyam nigraha sthānam iti āha pratipādite doṣe sati vādi prativādibhyām anyonyam asādhana aṅga vacanam etat adoṣadbhāvanañca bhavet iti anyathā na hi anayoḥ ekasya api jaya parājayau= iti uktam prakṛtam parityajya iti nyāyyatām eva asya pratipādayati prakṛtam atra sādhya sādhana hetu abhidhānam tat akṛtvā iti upanyaste doṣena samarthanam aparasya rūpa sidhyādeḥ atanna āntarīyakasya api iti upanyasta sāvana samarthana aṅgasya iti arthaḥ aparasya nāma ādivyākhyāna ādeḥ upakṣepaḥ parājaya sthānam iti varttate 
VNṬ_99,1^1	 varṇa krama nideśa vat nirarthakam yatra varṇāḥ eva kevalam krameṇa nirdiśyante na padat na api vākyam artha antare kila aprakṛta artha kathanam iha varṇa mātra uccāraṇam iti śeṣaḥ asamvaddhatām eva āha na hi varṇṇa krama nirdeśāt eva kevalāt ānarthakyam api tu yat eva kiñcid asādhana aṅgasya asiddha viruddha ādeḥ śabda rūpa sidhya ādeḥ ca vacananta deva anarthakam kim kāraṇam sādhya siddhi upayoginaḥ abhidheyasya abhāvāt sādhya siddhi upayoginaḥ abhāvepi kasya anyat prayojanam asti iti api na mantavyam iti kathayati niṣprayojana tvāt ca iti sādhya siddheḥ eva prastuta tvāt anya prayojanavatu epi ānarthakyam eva tatra prastāvaḥ iti abhiprāyaḥ tasmāt prakāra viśeṣa upādāna varṇa krama nirdeśa vat iti asambaddham paraḥ prāha na sādhya siddhau yat anarthakam anaṅgantat nirarthakam abhipretam api tu yasya vacanasya kāka vāsita ādeḥ iva na eva kaścid arthaḥ 
VNṬ_99,1^2	 tathā ca na artha antara apārthaka ādīnām anena eva saṃgrahaḥ tatrakasyacid artha leśasya sadbhāvāt ācāryaḥ āha yasya kasya cida pyādinopi nirarthaka abhidhāne vāhitaḥ iva kin na nigrahaḥ bhavati katham syāt iti āha nigraha nimitta ttasya nirarthaka abhidhānasya vādya vādinoḥ aviśeṣāt na iti parantasya vādinaḥ iha vāda prakaraṇe āyātam iti ācāryaḥ tasya tena eva nirarthaka abhidhānena tatra evam sthite vāde tulyam sarvasya asādhana aṅga vādinaḥ nirarthaka abhidhāyi tvam iti adhyāha rttavyam kvacid tava iti pāṭhaḥ tatra na upaskāreṇa kiñcid anena eva nirarthaka abhidhānena pratyucyate yasya na evakaścid arthaḥ iti etat api asambaddham yasmāt na ca varṇa krama nirdeśa upi nirarthakaḥ kvacid prakaraṇe pratyāhārāt au= arthava tvāt ca tasmāt atra eva vādesya varṇṇa kramasya ānarthakyam tat ca artha antara ādeḥ api tulyam iti cittam kakkaṅpiṅgitam iti atra ādi śabdena utplutya gamanam tāla dāna nṛtya ādīn āṅga haṇam 
VNṬ_100,1	 tris abhihitam iti tri vacanaṅkāryam iti nyāya tvam darśayati sakṛt uktam spaṣṭa artham api kadācid na jñāyate iti tris uccāraṇaṅkāryam kasmāt punar pada vākya pramāṇa vidbhiḥ vākyat na jñāyate iti āha kliṣṭa śabdam ityādi kliṣṭa śabdam manāk uccārita tvāt apaśabda tvāt iti apare kasmāt evam prayuktam iti āha asāmarthya samvaraṇāye ti spaṣṭa arthasya prayoge dūṣaṇam vakṣyati iti bhayāt prayuṃkte idañca sādhana dūṣaṇa vādinoḥ samānam dūṣaṇa vākyam api hi evaṃbhūta nigraha prāpti kāraṇam na idam nirarthakāt bhidyate tathā hi śliṣṭa śabda ādibhiḥ prakṛta artha sambaddhaṅgamakam eva brūyāt etat viparītam vā prāktane prakāre na asya āsāmarthī antatra tu pariṣad ādayaḥ jāḍyāt tat uktat na pratipadyaṃte iti neyatā vidvān vādī nigraham arhati 
VNṬ_101,1–101,2	 vaktuḥ eva hi tat jāḍyam yat śrotrā na avabuddhyatem tatosau nigraha arhaḥ eva iti ākūtavān āha paraḥ pariṣad prajñām iti nyāya vādinaḥ iti pariharati nyāya vādinaḥ uktam iti sambandhaḥ vādī tu jāḍyāt pariṣad ādeḥ avijñāta sādhana sāmarthyaḥ iti kṛtvā vijetā na syāt pariṣad prativādi pratyāyanena jaya vyavasthāpanāt avijñātam pratipādana sāmarthyam pariṣad prativādibhyām yasya iti kāryam dvitīyantu vikalpam adhikṛtya āha asambaddha abhidhāne nirarthakam eva iti 
VNṬ_101,3^1	 anekasya padasya iti yat ānīm asambaddha artha pratipādakattve vākya artha pratipādaka tvam nirākaroti vākyasya asambaddha artha pratipādaka tve prakaraṇa adhyāya pratipatya bhāvaḥ samudāya pratipatya bhāvāt ca nigraha sthānam udāharaṇam daśa dāḍimāḥ ṣaṣ apūpāḥ kuṇḍamaja ajinam palala piṇḍam atha raurukam etat kumāryaḥ sphaiya kṛtasya pitā pratiśīnaḥ iti atra ca bhāradvājena nirarthaka apārthakayoḥ abhedaḥ iti āśaṅkaya prativihitam tatra hi varṇṇa mātram iha yadā anya sambaddhāni iti tat eva ācārya upyupakṣipati idam kila ityādinā asambaddhā varṇṇāḥ yasmin nirarthakaḥ iti vigrahaḥ kila śabdaḥ anabhimata tva pradarśana arthaḥ anabhimata tvam eva āha nanu ayam padānām asambandhāt apārthaka vat asambandha vākyam api nirarthakāt pṛthak vācyam syāt sya ātmatam apārthakam na eva asambaddha padārtha asambaddha vākya arthayoḥ saṅgṛhīta tvāt pṛthak na vācyam iti atas ucyate 
VNṬ_101,3^2	 na ubhaya saṅgrahāda pārthakam yuktam kasmāt asambaddha padārthena apārthakena eva asambaddha vākyasya iva nirarthakasya api varṇṇa krama mātra lakṣaṇasya saṅgraha prasaṅgāt atha ucyate nirarthakam kim ucyate yasya arthaḥ eva na asti kevalam varṇṇa krama mātram asambaddha pada vākyayoḥ tu sādhya siddhi anupayogepi na sarvathā nairarthakyam atas artha tatve sāmyāt dvayoḥ eva ekīkaraṇam iti atas āha evam vidhāt ca ityādi kapola vādita ādīnām api pṛthak abhidhāna prasaṅgaḥ iti atra atiprasaṅgaḥ uktaḥ nahi kiñcitmātreṇa viśeṣaḥ na śakyate kvacid pradarśayitum iti abhisandhiḥ atha nirarthaka apārthakayoḥ saṅgraha nirdeśa doṣam bheda nirdeśe ca guṇampaśyatā a kṣapādena na saṅgraha nirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ iti manyase na sādhu manyasaḥ iti āha na ca saṅgrahaḥ ityādi 
VNṬ_102,1^1	 yathā lakṣaṇam artha vaśāt iti arthaḥ sāmarthyam anupadarśite hi viṣaye nirviṣayā sādhana pravṛttiḥ mā bhūt iti sādhya nirdeśa lakṣaṇā pratijñā pūrvvam ucyate tad anantara mudā āharaṇa sādharmyān= sādhya sādhanam hetu riti evam lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ tad sādhanāya ucyate tatas hetoḥ vahiḥ vyāpti pradarśana arthaṃsādhya sādharmyāt tad dharma bhāvi dṛṣṭāntaḥ udāharaṇami ti evam lakṣaṇam udāharaṇam tatas pratibiṃbana artham sādhya dharmiṇi sambhava pradarśana artham vāudāharaṇa apekṣaḥ tathā iti upasaṃhāraḥ na tathā iti veti sādhanasya upanayaḥ iti evaṃlakṣaṇaḥ upanayaḥ 
VNṬ_102,1^2–103,1	 tatas uttara kālam sarvvā avayava parāmarśena viparīta prasaṅga nivṛti artham hetu apadeśāt pratijñāyāḥ punarvacanam niga manami ti evam lakṣaṇam nigamanam iti ayam asau yathālakṣaṇam artha vaśāt kramaḥ tathā hi lokepi pūrvvaṅkāryam mṛd piṇḍa ādi upādīyate paścāt tu karaṇañcakra daṇḍa ādikam iti nyāyaḥ tatra etasmin kramenyāyataḥ sthite avayavānām pratijñā ādīnām viparyayeṇa abhidhānam nigraha sthānam yathā ghaṭa vat kṛtaka tvāt anityaḥ iti na evam api siddheḥ iti bhāradvājaḥ svayam eva āśaṅkya pariharati na prayoga apeta śabda vat etat syāt iti anena iti goṇīpadena yathā ambambiti yathā vālaḥ śikṣyamāṇaḥ prabhāṣate avyaktaṃtad vidāntena vyakte bhavati niścayaḥ 
VNṬ_103,2^1	 tathā kila goṇya ādayaḥ śabdāḥ te sādhuṣu anumānena pratyaya utpatti hetavaḥ iti tat etat unmattakasya vaiyākaraṇasya unmattaka saṃvarṇṇanam unmattakenaḥ dyota kareṇa saṃvarṇṇanam yathā hi ekaḥ unmattaḥ dvitīyam unmattakam samvarṇṇayati tathā bhūtam etat api iti yāvat yadi ca unmattakasyaḥ dyota kara sya unmattakasya vaiyākaraṇasya samvarṇṇanam tathā hi śābdikaḥ eva tāvat unmattaḥ pramāṇa viruddhavat tva abhidhāyi tvāt tatas kutas tad prakriyāyāḥ pramāṇa cintāyāḥ jñāpaka tvam iti abhipretam kathampunar śābdikasya ayukta abhidhāyi tvam iti āha yadi tyādi su bodham strī śūdra śabdaḥ mūrkha vacanaḥ yaḥ tu nakka śabdam mukka śabdam eva nāsā aparyāyam vetti sa katham apaśabdāt śabdam sādhum pratipadyātaḥ sādhoḥ śabdāt artham pratipadyeta kim ucyate na eva asau tathā vivodham pratipadyate iti āha 
VNṬ_103,2^2	 dṛṣṭāca anubhaya vedinopi sanakāḥ deḥ pratītiḥ iti tasmāt na paramparayā pratītiḥ arthasya ayam atra saṃkṣepaḥ syāt evam asādhūnām sādhu anumāpaka tvam yaḥ dyeṣān dhūma ādīnām iva trairūpī ambhave nniścitam tat ca na sambhavati yasmāt etāvat anubhaya vedinaḥ sanakāḥ dayaḥ te santam api vyāpya vyāpaka bhāvan na pratipadyante na ca asau= ajñātaḥ gamakaḥ jñāpaka tvāt yepi śabda apaśabda pravibhāga kuśalāḥ tepya vidyamāna tvāt eva bhāvayanti tathā hi asādhūnām sādhubhiḥ sambandhaḥ tādātmyam kārya kāraṇa bhāvaḥ vā abhaveta tad ubhaya vikalasya avyabhicāra niyama abhāvāt tatra ca tāvat na tādātmyam abhyupeyam pāramārthikasya eva bhedasya sphuṭam pratyakṣatas pratīteḥ śabdavat asādhoḥ api avyatirekataḥ vācaka tva prasaṅgāt ca tad utpattiḥ api dūra utsāritā iva yatas na asādhavaḥ sādhubhyaḥ jāyante 
VNṬ_103,2^3	 kāraṇa guṇa vaktu kāma tā mātra hetutvāt teṣām na ca teṣān nitya tu aṅkādācid kopalambhataḥ tatve vā sutarā an tad utpatteḥ abhāvaḥ sati api vā vyāpya vyāpaka bhāve tad parijñāne ca pakṣa dharma tva vaikalyāt cākṣuṣa tva ādeḥ iva asādhubhyaḥ na anumānam na hi atra dharme vidyate yatas pakṣa dharma tvam niṣpadyate na hi sādhūnām eva dharmitu anteṣām eva anumīyamāna tvāt na ca dharmi sādhanam yuktimataḥ bhāva abhāva ubhaya dharmasya asiddha viruddha anaikāntika doṣa duṣṭa tvataḥ katham vā sādhūnām tad dharma tvam na hi tad kāle te santi asatāñca dharmi tvam vācaka tvaṃca iti su bhāṣitam kim ucyate puruṣaḥ dharmī sādhu śabda vivakṣā sādhya dharmaḥ pakṣa dharmaḥ ca asādhuḥ iti tat api asambaddham vyāpya vyāpaka bhāva abhāvāt eva yasmāt na ca goṇī śabda prayoga kāle go śabda vivakṣām upalabhāmahe atha pratyavasthīyate 
VNṬ_103,2^4–104,1	 yathā pakṣa dharma tva ādi vaikalyepi avyaktam bāla vacaḥ vyaktam anumāpayati tathā eva asādhava upisādhūn iti tat ayuktam tatra api tulya paryanuyoga tvāt vayantu pratipadyāmahe sākṣāt eva tasmāt api avyaktān mātra ādi arthaḥ pratīyate iti tatra saṃjñā saṃjñi sambandhasya ananubhūta tvāt ayukta apratītau= iti api na mantavyam anādimati saṃsāre vyavahāra paramparāyāḥ tathā bhūtāyāḥ sambandhasya ulliṅgita tvāt tathā hi na gavā ādi śabdānām api prāyas śṛṅgaṅgrāhikayā artha niyamaḥ saṅketyatepi tu vyavahāra pāramparyataḥ vidagdhāḥ niścinvanti tat ca iha api samānam eva tasmāt etat araṇya ruditam ambam u iti yathā bālaḥ śikṣyamāṇaḥ prabhāsate avyaktanta dvidāntena vyaktena bhavati niścayaḥ evam sādhau prayoktavye yaḥ yat bhraṃśaḥ prayujyate tena sādhu vyavahitaḥ kaścid artha uvasīyate iti yat api abhyadhāyi kumārilena go śabde avasthitesmākantada śakti ja kāritā gāvi ādeḥ api go buddhiḥ mūla śabda anusāriṇī ti 
VNṬ_105,1^1	 tasya api idam eva pratividhānam idañca sarvam āgūryya nigamayati na paramparayā prati iti riti atra eva upacayam āha arthe pratipādana āya asamarthasya asādhoḥ śabdepi sādhau pratīti janana asāmarthyāt ca tatra etat syāt na vayam asādhūnām artheṣu pratīti janaka tvam nirākurmaḥ kintu vācaka tvam śabde ca asādhuḥ pratīti janakaḥ eva na vācakaḥ eva iti atas āha na hya rthepi śabdasya vācaka tvam anya deve tyādi yadi asā adhoḥ arthe pratīti janaka tvam iṣyate tadā etāvatā vayam āhita paritoṣāḥ kim asmākam abhidhāna antara kalpitena vācaka tvena iti ākūtam na eva tarhi asau= artha pratītim janayitum kṣamaḥ api tu śabdaḥ eva iti ced āha apaśabdaḥ ced iti atha ucyate śabdena tasya svābhāvikaḥ sambandhaḥ na arthena tatas tam eva pratipādayati na arthantat yathā svabhāvataḥ cakṣū rūpam prakāśayati na śabda ādīn atas āha akṛta samayasye tyādi adarśanāt iti na hi apratīta sambandhāḥ siṃhala śabdāḥ ārya jana vyavahārāya varttante samayaḥ eva tu janayet pratītim sāmayike ca tatra sambandhe sorthepya nivāryaḥ 
VNṬ_105,1^2	 samaya vaśāt asādhuḥ sādhau varttamāna ūrthaḥ eva gavādaukin na pravartate na hi kiñcid tathā doṣaḥ guṇaḥ tu kevalaḥ iti āha evam hī tyāḥ di etat uktam bhavati ye svabhāvataḥ prakāśakāḥ na te samayam apekṣante yathā cakṣuḥ dīpa ādayaḥ rūpa ādīnām svabhāvataḥ ca apa śabdaḥ yadi śabdasya prakāśakaḥ bhavet tatas tena api sambandha ūna apekṣaḥ syāt apekṣyate ca tatas na asya śabde svābhāvikam sāmarthyam tathā ca idam api śakyam anumātum ye samaya apekṣa pravṛttayaḥ te sarvatra yathā samayam anivārita prasarāḥ sākṣāt eva pratipādakāḥ bhavanti 
VNṬ_105,1^3	 yathā kāya vijñapti ādayaḥ tathā cāpa śabdāḥ api samaya apekṣa pravṛttayaḥ iti siddham eṣām avyavadhānataḥ eva artha pratipādaka tvam iti viparyaya darśanāt ca iti upacaya antaram tathā hi vṛkṣa ugniḥ utpalam iti ukte avyutpanna dhiyaḥ vālāḥ praśna upakramam santiṣṭhante koyam vṛkṣaḥ ityādinā te ca anyasya vyutpādana upāyasya abhāvāt apa śabdaiḥ eva vyutpādyante rukkhaḥ aggī uppalam iti te devam atra asādhavaḥ eva vācakāḥ na sādhavaḥ santopī iti viparyayaḥ dṛśyate atha pratipadyase dharma sādhana tā śabda saṃskāraḥ yathovatam 
VNṬ_106,1–106,2	 śiṣṭebhyaḥ āgamāt siddham sādhanaḥ dharma sādhanaṃartha pratyāya nābhede viparītāḥ tu asādhavaḥ iti tathā mantraḥ hīnaḥ svarataḥ varṇa tova āmithyā prayuktaḥ na tam artham āha sa vāc vajraḥ yajamānam hinasti yathā indra śatruḥ svarata uparādhāt te surāḥ he alayohe alayaḥ iti uktavaṃtaḥ parau= abhūvuḥ ekopi śabdaḥ samyak prayuktaḥ sukṛtinām lokaṅgamayati āhitāgniḥ apa śabdam abhidhāya prāyaścittīyām iṣṭim nirvapet ityādi 
VNṬ_106,3	 idam apasārayati na dharma sādhana tā śabdānām saṃskāraḥ iti vartate kiṅkāraṇam iti āha mithyā vṛtti codanebhyaityādi mithyā vṛttiḥ codyate yaiḥ iti kāryam yathā hi asya abhinava vidruma aṅkura prakara abhirāma ki śalaya mañju mañjarī rājī virājita taroḥ aśoka vanaspateḥ adhas śayitasya dvijanmanaḥ nīla nīraja nīla tā atiśāyinā maṇḍalāgreṇa śiraḥ chittvā iti uktā ipi bhavati eva brahmahatyayā sambandhaḥ prayojakasya anyebhyaḥ iti asambhūtebhyaḥ viparyayeṇa samyaktva vṛtti codanena yathā assa bambhaṇassa gāvī dīadi sarvañcedam a pramāṇa tvāt vacana mātram bhavatauvimatya akūtavān upacayam āha śabdasya su prayogāt eva ityādi evam vidha anityapramāṇakān 
VNṬ_106,4	 nanu ca pratiṣṭhite bhū pradeśe ca eti aṅkārayati brāhmyam puṇyam prasavati kalpam sva gaṣu modate iti ādau= api pramāṇa abhāvāt ayam tulyaḥ prasaṅgaḥ bhavatām api na tulya uyasmāt atra viṣaya dvaya pariśuddhiḥ parinārthāḥ visamvādaḥ ca asti iti tṛtīyepi rāśau= āhita paritoṣāḥ prekṣāvantaḥ pravarttante na tu evam bhavat mate anantara udita dvayam api pramāṇa vyāhata tvāt pramāṇa vyāhatiḥ ca anantaram eva āveditā tasmāt daridra īśvara spardhā samānam etat 
VNṬ_107,1	 vidita vedya ādi guṇa prayuktāḥ iti antar bhāvita bhāva pratyayaya nirdeśaḥ viditam vedyam heya upādeya tvam yaiḥ te tathā uktāḥ ādi grahaṇāt karuṇā ādi parigrahaḥ amūne va saṃskṛtān aparāna saṃskṛtān etat uktam bhavati śabdaḥ hi vyavahārortha pratyāyana phalaḥ tat ca yathā saṃskṛtebhyaḥ saṅketa vaśāt sampadyate tathā asaṃskṛtebhyopīti kimasthānebhi niviṣṭāḥ śiṣṭāḥ atas eva ca manye prekṣā vadbhyonya tvāt anugata artham evam nāma āmīṣām iti athavā kim asmākam arhaṣitiḥ pratyākhyānaiḥ te amūt na eva prayuñjate na aparān iti atra eva niścaya abhāvāt yat āha na ca atra śabde parokṣaḥ sākṣī yatas sākṣiṇaḥ idam eva amūnā iva prayuñjate na aparān iti niścinumaḥ 
VNṬ_107,2–108,1	 nanu ca uktantadanva ākhyānasya prayojanam rakṣoha āgama laghva sandehāḥ mahā bhāṣya ia āhnike iti tat katham guṇa atiśaya abhāvāt iti ucyate iti āha veda rakṣā ādi kañcā prayojanam eva atad samaya sthāyinaḥ stāthāgatasya nyāya anupāyi tvāt tad svabhāvasya sādhu śabda rūpasya anyatopi iti bṛddha pravāda pāramparyāt etat eva dṛṣṭānta uprakramam vyanakti prākṛta ityādinā ittham śāibdakasya unmattaka tām upadarśya adhunā bhāradvāja sya āha 
VNṬ_108,2^1	 avayava viparyaya ipi ityādi samvandha pratītiḥ iti sambandhaḥ parasparam upakārya upakāraka bhāvaḥ sāmarthyāt vivakṣita pratipādanaḥ iti śeṣaḥ atha syāḥ dakṣa pāda siddhāntanīti pālanāya na pratijña ādīnām krama vyatyayaḥ kriyate iti atra āha na hi atra kaścid sa mayaḥ siddhāntaḥ niyamaḥ vā pramāṇa upetaḥ iti api āha na paraḥ āha na viparyayāt pratītiḥ sādhyasya kintu tatas viparyayāt ānupūrvyā pratītiḥ iti asya pratiṣedhaḥ na apratīyamāna sambandhebhyaḥ ānupūrvī pratītiḥ iti yeṣām ityādi nai tat eva vyācaṣṭe api ca pratijñā upanaya nigamanānām pūrvam eva asmābhiḥ sādhana vākye prayogaḥ pratikṣiptaḥ 
VNṬ_108,2^2	 tad kutas tad kṛtaḥ viparyayaḥ iti etat kathayati pratipāditam ityādinā pratijñā grahaṇam upalakṣaṇa artham atha sāmarthī alabhya api prayujyate tadā atiprasaṅgaḥ iti etat āha pratīyamāna arthasya ca prayoga iti prasaṅgaḥ sādharmyavati prayoge vaidharmyasya api prayoga prasaṅgaḥ na ca iṣyate arthāt āpannasya sva śabdena punarvacanañca iti nigraha sthāna vacanāt pakṣa dharma anvaya vyatirekeṣu tarhi pratijña ādi abhāvepi krama niyama ubhaviṣyati iti atas āha pariśiṣṭe ṣu ityādi apratīyamāna sambandha pakṣe doṣa antaram brūte na idam apārthakāt bhidyate iti na pṛthak vācyam syāt iti 
VNṬ_109,1^1	 yasmin vākye pratijñā ādīnāt nigamana paryantānām anyatamaḥ avayavaḥ na bhavati tat vākyam hīnam nigraha sthāna tve kāraṇam āha sādhana abhāve sādhya āsiddheḥ iti idat nirākaroti na pratijñā ādīnām ityādinā pratijñā grahaṇam upalakṣaṇa artham tena upanaya nigamanayoḥ api parigrahaḥ udyota karasya matam upanyasyati hīnam eva tat pratijñānyūnam tasyāḥ pratijñāyāḥ nyūna tāyām api nigrahāt iti asya ayukta tām āha yaḥ sādhana sāmarthyā tpratīyamāna artham anarthakam śabdaṃsādhya abhidhāyinam sādhane prayuṅkte sa nigraham arhet 
VNṬ_109,1^2	 tathā hi śabdasya anityat tva vicāre prastute yadā bravīti kṛtakānām anitya tvam dṛṣṭaṅkṛtakaḥ ca śabdaḥ iti tadā vacana dvayāḥ deva sādhya arthaḥ pratīyate iti nirartha kampratijñā vacanam na artha upasaṃhitasya yukti yuktasya pakṣa dharma sambandha mātrasya abhidhānā itya samīkṣita abhidhānam etat vārtikakārasya atas eva ca iti yatas pratīyamāna arthem śabde prayuktenigraham arhati tada trābiddhakarṇaḥ pratibandhaka nyāyena pratyavatiṣṭhate yadi evaṅkṛtakaḥ ca śabdaḥ iti etat api na vaktavyam kiṃnimittam anitya tvam iti etena eva śabdepi kṛtaka tvam anitya tvañca ubhayam pratipadyate 
VNṬ_109,1^3	 yasmāt pūrvam api śabde kṛtaka tvampareṇa pratipannam eva karaṇāt śabdopi buddhau vyavasthitaḥ atas nvaya vākyena smṛti mātrakam utpādyate apratipanna kṛta kattvasya punar kṛtakaḥ ca śabdaḥ iti etasmāt api na eva bhavati yat vā kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ iti etāvat vaktavyam kṛtaka tvasya tu anitya tvena avinābhāvi tvam parasya prasiddham iti śabdepya nitya tvam pratipadyate iti tena anukūlam eva ācaritam tathā hi yadi vādinā kathañcid niścitam bhavati pratipannam anena vādinā kṛtaka tvam śabdaḥ iti tadā na eva tena pakṣa dharma upasaṃhāraḥ kartavyaḥ niṣphala tvāt 
VNṬ_109,1^4–110,1	 pratibandha m ātrantu pradarśanīyam atha tathā na niścitam tathā api yadi ayam paraḥ pakṣa dharma upasaṃhāre mayā kṛte tasya asiddhiñcodayiṣyati tat āhantām pratyaya bheda bhedi tva ādibhiḥ upāyaiḥ pratinivārayiṣyāmi svayam eva vā acodita eva āśaṅkyā etat cetasi ādhāya pakṣa dharma tvam upasaṃhartavyam eva kṛtakaḥ ca śabdaḥ iti yadā api evam vādī niścitavān kṛtaka tvasya anitya tvena avinābhā vitvam parasya prasiddham iti tasyām api avasthāyām kṛtakaḥ śabdaḥ iti etā= edava vaktavyam yathā uktan tad bhāna hetu bhāvau hi dṛṣṭānte tad avedinaḥ khyāpyate viduṣām vācyaḥ hetuḥ eva hi kevalaḥ iti tad etat niyama abhyupagamaḥ iti adhikam nigraha sthānam viśiṣṭe viṣaye sthāpayati tañca viśiṣṭam viṣayam āha yatra ityādinā nanu ca idam niyama abhyupagame veditavyam iti bhāṣya kāreṇa eva uktam tat kim atra dūṣaṇam ācāryeṇa uktam satyan na kiñcid uktam ācāryeṇa tu pakṣilaḥ ktam evanūdyate abhyanujñāna artham 
VNṬ_110,2^1	 śabda arthayoḥ punarvacanam punarukta miti asya apavādam āha anyatra anuvādāt iti anuvādaḥ nigamanam anuvādaḥ hi na punar ukta vyapadeśam labhate śabdābhyām artha viśeṣa utpattiḥ yasmāt sādhya nirdeśaḥ pratijñā asiddha nirdeśaḥ nigamanam iti uktam punar śabdaḥ ca nānātve dṛṣṭaḥ punar iyamacira prabhā niścarati iti api āveditam eva yadi evantatra tarhi punarukta tāyāḥ prāptiḥ eva na asti iti kimartha mayam apavādaḥ prārabhyate satyam evam etat te eva tu prakṛṣṭa tārkikāḥ praṣṭavyāḥ katham etat iti asmākantu kim parakīyābhiḥ gṛha cintābhiḥ cintitābhiḥ iti alamprasaṅgena atra ca idam api dvitīya sūtram asti arthāt āpannasya sva śabdena punarvacanam iti tad ācāryeṇa na upanyastam upalakṣaṇa artha tvāt tad bhāṣyam apakṣipya nirākariṣyati gamyamāna artham punarvacanam api ityādinā atra ityādinā dūṣaṇam ārabhate etat uktam bhavati 
VNṬ_110,2^2	 yatra śabda sāmya īpi arthaḥ na bhidyate tatra artha punarukte na gatam yatra tu śabda sāmya īpi artha bhedaḥ tatra śabda punarukta tāyām api na kiñcid kṛtam kim asti ayam īdṛśaḥ sambhavaḥ yat śabda punarukta tāyām api artha bhedoḥ ti iti atas āha yathā hasati hasati ityādi atra hi pūrvaḥ hasati śabdaḥ saptamī antaḥ dvitīyaḥ ca tiṅntaḥ iti artha bhedaḥ evam uttaratra api kāvyaḥ īdṛśaḥ sambhavaḥ na tu vādaḥ iti āśaṅkāyām udāharati yathā ca ityādi nanu ca iha api artha bheda vat śabda bheda upyasti subantatiṅanta tayā sattyan na kevalam atra api atra api anittyaḥ śabdaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti atra asti eva śabda bhedaḥ sva lakṣaṇa bhedāt anyathā na krama bhāvi śravaṇam syāt samāna śruti samāśrayam iha paunaruktyam yadi vyavasthāpyate tat atra api tulyam eva artha bhedaḥ eva ayam kriyā bheda ādi vācya bhedāt tad vala kalpitaḥ eva hi pada bhedaḥ 
VNṬ_110,2^3	 gamyamāna artham punarvacanam api punaruktam iti dvitīyampunarukta lakṣaṇa sūtram upalakṣayati asya codāharaṇam vātsyāyanena nyāya bhāṣya uktam sādharmyavati prayoge vaidharmyasya ācāryaḥ tu pratijñāyām api etat samānam iti āgūrya pratijñāyāḥ sādhana vākye anupanyāsam pratipādayitu kāmaḥ vakra uktyā pratijñā vacanam eva udāharaṇa tvena upanyasyati niyata pada prayoge sādhana vākye yathā pratijñā vacanam iti niyatānāṃpadānām prayogaḥ yasmin= iti kāryam idam pratikṣipati artha punaruktena eva gata artha tvāt na pṛthak vācyam iti yathā hi eka śabda pratipāditerthe tad pratipādanāya paryā yaśabda antaram upādīyamānam anartha kantathā sāmarthya gamya īpi arthaḥ iti artha punaruktena eva asya saṅgrahaḥ iti samudāya arthaḥ kva punar etat pratijña ādi vacanam arthāpatti labhyam punar uktam sannigraha sthānam bhavati iti praśne niyata prayoge sādhana vākye iti etat evampakṣeṇa vivṛṇoti 
VNṬ_110,2^4	 ayam api doṣaḥ gamyamāna artha punarvacana kṛtaḥ sādhana vākyaḥ eva niyata pada prayogaḥ iti vartate idam uktam bhavati yadā prāśnikāḥ śabda artha pramāṇa pravicaya nipuṇāḥ prekṣāvanta uti aṃtam avahita manasaḥ ca bhavanti prativādi api tathābhūtaḥ eva iti vadanti yad antareṇa na sādhya siddhiḥ tat eva prayoktavyam na abhyadhikam iti tadāyan doṣaḥ na anyathā yasmāt karuṇā paratantra cetasaḥ anibandhana vatsalāḥ prativādinam ati durllabham iva śiṣyam nyāya vartma avatārayitum yatante tatra punarvacanam api na doṣāya etat eva āha vyācakṣāṇaḥ hi vādī sākṣī prabhṛtīnām asamyak śravaṇa pratipatti śaṅkayā karaṇa bhūtayā samyak śravaṇa pratipati arthampunar punar brūyāt api iti nā viṣaya tvāt iti paraḥ idam eva vyācaṣṭe na ayam vādī guruḥ prativādinaḥ na śiṣyaḥ prativādi api vādinaḥ dvayoḥ api paraspara jigīṣayā vyavasthānāt iti tasmāt na vādinā prativādī yatnatas pratipādanīyaḥ 
VNṬ_110,2^5	 na ityādi ācāryaḥ yadi nāma prativādī na pratipādyate yatnena sākṣiṇaḥ tu avaśyam yatnena pratipādyāḥ tad bodhanā deva hi vādinaḥ jayonyathā ca parājaya iti katham sākṣiṇaḥ eva na pratipādayet kiñca avaśyam sākṣi vat prativādi api pratipādyaḥ kasmāt tad apratipādane doṣa abhidhānāt tad chalena sākṣi prabhṛtayaḥ pratyavamṛśyante yadi sākṣi prabhṛtayaḥ na pratipādyāḥ bhaveyuḥ tatas yat bhavadbhiḥ pariṣad prativādibhyān triḥ abhihitam avijñātam avijñāta artha nigraha sthānam uktam tat viruddhi atas iti arthaḥ yat ca ucyate na ayam śiṣyaḥ iti tat asiddham pratipādyasya śiṣya tvāt tatva jñāna artha tayā pratipādya eva śiṣya unyasya tad lakṣaṇasya abhāvāt prativādī ca tathābhūtaḥ katham na śiṣyaḥ kim ucyate na eva asau prativādī tatva jñāna artha aspardhayā vyutthita tvāt iti tat ayuktam pūrvvañjigīṣu vāda pratiṣedhāt 
VNṬ_110,2^6	 evam api na eva asau yatna pratipādyaḥ tris abhidhāna niyamasya mahā ṛṣiṇā kṛta tvāt iti atas āha tris abhidhāna vacanāt ityādi anena etat darśayati yat vakṣyati yadi tāvat para pratipādana arthā pravṛttiḥ kintriḥ abhidhīyate tathā tathā sa grāhiṇīyoyatha asya pratipattiḥ bhavati atha para upatāpana arthā tathā api kim tris abhidhīyate sākṣiṇā aṅkarṇe nivedya prativādī kaṣṭā pratīta druta saṃkṣipta ādibhiḥ upadrotavyaḥ yathā uttara pratipatti vimūḍhaḥ tūṣṇīm bhavatī iti na ca idam iti śabda arthayoḥ punarvacanam gamyamāna artha punarvacanam ca abhedam eva sādhayati viniyata ityādinā ādhikyam hetu udāharaṇayoḥ doṣaḥ ekena kṛta tvāt itarasya ānarthakyam iti vacanāt punarvacanepi gataḥ jñātaḥ pūrveṇa eva śabdena arthaḥ yasyaḥ ttarasya padasya tat evam uktam tasya ādhikyam eva doṣaḥ iti adhikṛtam kimpunar niyata pada prayoge ayan doṣaḥ iti uktam iti ced āha 
VNṬ_110,2^7	 prapañca kathā āyāma doṣaḥ iti abhisambandhaḥ kasya hetu ādi bāhulyasya punarvacanasya ca ādi śabdena udāharaṇa bāhulya grahaṇam kīdṛśyāmanirūpita eka artha sādhana adhikaraṇāyām arthaḥ sādhyaḥ arthyate iti kṛtvā sādhanam hetuḥ adhikaraṇandharmī artha sahitam sādhanam artha sādhanam madhya pada lopāt ekañca tad artha sādhanañca tathā uktam tasya adhikaraṇantada nirūpitam ekārtha sādhana adhikaraṇam yasyām prapañca kathāyām prativādinā dharmiṇaḥ jīva śarīra ādeḥ na ekaḥ dharmaḥ nairātmya ādiṣu pramātum iṣṭaḥ api tva nekaḥ kṣaṇika tvānātma tvānīśvara karttṛ tva ādiḥ tathā na ekena eva hetunā kintu anekena api tasyām iti arthaḥ etat eva yathākramam brūte nānā artha sādhana īpsāyām nānā sādhana īpsāyām vā śrotuḥ iti pūrvvakaḥ sādhana śabdaḥ bhāva sādhana tvāt siddhi vacanaḥ uttaraḥ tu karaṇa sādhana tvāt hetu vacanaḥ 
VNṬ_110,2^8	 tasmāt hetu ādi bāhulyam vacana bāhulyam sādhanena viniyata pade doṣaḥ kasmāt pratīta āyya abhāvāt pratya tulyaḥ doṣaḥ iti kṛtvā saṅgrahaḥ eva nyāyyaḥ adhikam eva vā vaktavyam punar uktam eva ca iti arthaḥ anayoḥ ekasmin dvitīyasya antar bhāvāt katham punar śabda punar ukte adhikasya antarbhāvaḥ iti āha paryyāya śabda kalpaḥ hi aparaḥ dvitīyaḥ hetuḥ eka hetu pratipādite viṣaye pravarttamānaḥ kim kāraṇam pratipādyasya viśeṣa abhāvāt arthasya punar uktantarhi katham adhikentarbhavati iti āha arthaḥ punar pratipādanāḥ nna bhidyate iti artha śabdena artha punaruktam upalakṣayati punar pratipādyate anena iti punar pratipādanam hetu udāharaṇa adhikam eva idam uktam bhavati sphuṭam eva asya udāharaṇa adhikentarbhāvaḥ tathā hi sādharmyavati prayoge vaidharmya udāharaṇasya aprayogaḥ artha punaruktasya udāharaṇam uktam yat punaruktam eva ādya pavāda pratiṣedhaḥ su jñānaḥ 
VNṬ_114,1^1	 vijñātaḥ vākya arthaḥ yasya tris abhihitasya tat tathā viśeṣaṇa samāsaḥ vā vijñātaḥ ca asau vākya arthaḥ ca iti tris abhihitasya vādinā iti pratipattavyam prativādinā pada pratyuccāraṇam iti sambandhanīyam trivacanam sakṛt abhihitasya ananubhāṣaṇepi na nigrahaḥ iti jñāpana artham apratyuccāraṇañca śabda dvāreṇa artha dvāreṇavā nigraha sthāna tve kāraṇam āha apratyuccārayan kim āśrayampara pakṣe pratiṣedham brūyāt iti na viṣayan dūṣaṇa abhidhānat na asti iti arthaḥ idantvayā uktaṃmati ṅkṛttvā dūṣaṇam vācyam evandūṣaṇa vākya mapi sādhana vādinā pratyanubhāṣya parihartavyam atas dvayoḥ api idam nigraha sthānam atra bhāradvājaḥ nyakṣeṇa ākṣepantāvat karoti uttareṇa avasānāt parijñānāt na idat nigraha sthānami ti ced iti 
VNṬ_114,1^2	 idam vākyam vyācaṣṭe svāt etat ityādinā na uttara viṣaya parijñānāt iti saḥ eva pratividhatte yadi ayam iti ādyasya eva vibhāgaḥ apratijñānāt ca iti saḥ eva uttarañca āśraya abhāve para pakṣa upakṣepa abhāve satya yuktam iti yuktam apratyuccāraṇenigraha sthānam itye tāvān parakīyaḥ granthaḥ atra ācāryaḥ dūṣaṇam vaktum ārabhate yadi nāma vādī sva sādhana arthasya vivaraṇa vyājena prasaṅgāt apara aparam ghoṣaye t yathā udāhṛtam prāk tatra karaṇa bhuvanāni buddhi sat kāraṇa pūrvvakāṇi iti pratijñā śarīra ādi vyākhyāna= chadmanā sakalam vaiśeṣika tantram ghoṣayet iti tathā jijñāsitam artha mātram uktvā kathām vistārayet yadi nāma vādī iti vartate kiṅkṛtvā vistārayet iti āha 
VNṬ_114,1^3	 pratijña ādiṣu artha viśeṣaṇa paramparayā aparān sidhī anupayoginā urthān upakṣipya yathā nidarśitam pūrvvat nityaḥ śabdaḥ anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti vivāde jaiminīyaḥ pramāṇayati dvādaśa lakṣaṇe tyādinā vyācaṣṭe ca dvādaśa lakṣaṇāni yathā vā akṣapādāḥ evaṅkurvanti kim amī sarve saṃskārāḥ kṣaṇikāḥ naḥ vā iti vivāde rūpa tva ādi sāmānya āśrayat tvāt tad āśrayāḥ tad viṣayāḥ ca pratyakṣa ādayaḥ pratyayāḥ sva ātma lābha anantara pradhvaṃsinaḥ na bhavanti samānānām asamāna jātīya dravya saṃyoga vibhāga janita śabda kārya śabda abhidheya tvāt prāgabhāva ādi vat iti nanu ca pratijñā ādīṣu iti atra ādi śabdena kim gṛhyate na tāvat hetu udāharaṇe tanmātram uktvā iti vacanāt na ca aparaḥ kaścid prastutaḥ atra iti 
VNṬ_114,1^4	 na eṣa doṣaḥ yatas hetu ādi mātram api uktvā iti draṣṭavyam tena hetu ādīnām eva ādi grahaṇena ākṣepaḥ iti kecid apare punar āhuḥ asthānam eva idam āśaṅkitam ktvā apratyaya nirdeśetra yasmāt ayam atra arthaḥ yatra prativādinā jijñāsitam artha mātram anya viśeṣaṇa rahita makṣaṇika tva ādikam tad uktvā vādi aham etat sādhayāmi iti uttara kāla pramāṇa māracayan pratijña ādiṣu artha viśeṣaṇa paramparayā aparān arthān upakṣipya kathāmvistārayet iti tat ca iti pratijña ādi viśeṣaṇa paramparayā yat aprastutam eva nāṭakā khyāyikā ghoṣaṇa kalpam vādinā udgrāḥ hitam tadā kaḥ tasya vivāda āśrayaḥ ca asau= artha mātraḥ ca akṣaṇika tva ādi kantasya uttara vacane sāmarthya vighātaḥ na eva iti arthaḥ tasmāt na vādi kathām ananu bhāṣamāṇaḥ prativādi uttara vādyena samarthaḥ 
VNṬ_114,1^5	 kintu yat vacanana antarīyikā jijñāsita artha siddhiḥ tat avaśyam upadarśyate eva iti sambandhaḥ kasmāt sādhana aṅga viṣaya tvāt dūṣaṇasya para upanīte hi sādhane dūṣaṇam pravartate iti sambandhaḥ kinna antarīyikā punar jijñāsita artha siddhiḥ iti āha yathā pakṣa dharma tā vyāpti prasādhana mātra mi ti vyāptiḥ prasādhyatenena iti vyāpti prasādhanam bādhaka pramāṇa upadarśanam kim iyam iti api sādhana prayoge artha antara upakṣepaḥ kartavyaḥ na iti āha na tatra api prasaṅga antara upa kṣepaḥ iti nairarthakyāt iti matiḥ tāvat mātram upadarśyate kim prāc anukrameṇa paścāt tu dūṣyate na iti āha tatra api dūṣaṇa viṣaya upadarśana arthe anubhāṣaṇe na sarvvam yāvat upanyastam vādinā tad dūṣaṇa abhidhānāt 
VNṬ_114,1^6	 prāc anukrameṇa uccārayitavyam kasmāt tris uccāraṇa prasaṅgāt dvis uccāraṇa prasaṅgam eva pratipādayitum ādi prasthānam ācarati dūṣaṇā ityāḥ dinā yadi vacana anukrama ghoṣaṇam na karoti nirviṣayam idānīm dūṣaṇam prasaktam iti āha na antarīyaka tvāt dūṣayatā viṣaya upadarśanam kriyate eva katham pratidoṣa vacanam doṣa vacanam doṣa vacanam prati yaḥ yaḥ doṣaḥ bhaṇyate tasya tasya viṣayaḥ kathyate iti arthaḥ idam eva āha asya vādi uktasya āyan doṣaḥ iti kimpunaḥ kāraṇam sarvu apratyuccārya yugapad dūṣaṇannocyate iti ced āha na hi ityādi kutas pratyartham daḥ ṣabhedāt viṣaya vat bhidyate doṣaḥ iti yāvat evam āracita ādi prasthānaḥ dvis uccāraṇa prasaṅgam pradarśayati sakṛt eva apraghuṣṭaḥ na 
VNṬ_114,1^7	 sarvva anubhāṣaṇesya pradarśite viṣaya doṣasya vaktum aśakyatvāt kevalam idam niḥprayojana parājaya adhikaraṇam ca iti āha dūṣaṇa vādinā dūṣaṇe vaktavye sati yatra sarvva anukrama bhāṣaṇam tatrapara pakṣa kṣobhena upayujyate tasya abhidhānam idandvirukta pada udbhāvanañcā iti evam vyatyāsena pada vinyāsaḥ kāryaḥ iti tasmāt sarvva anukrama bhāṣaṇamparājaya adhikaraṇam vācyam atra idānī mākṣapādaḥ sarvvam idam dūṣaṇam anabhyupagamena eva pūrvva pakṣasya asmābhiḥ prativyūḍham iti manyamānaḥ abhyanujānāti tathā astu iti syāt etat iti etat eva vyācaṣṭe yatas kutaścid iti sādhana artha vivaraṇasya vyājena pratijña ādiṣu artha viśeṣaṇa parampara upakṣepeṇa ca aprasaṅgāt anaṃtarīyaka abhidhānam rūpa siddhi nāma ādi vyākhyāna kalpattvāt vādinaḥ artha antara gamanam eva iti sa tena nigraha arhaḥ 
VNṬ_114,1^8	 prāsaṅgikam bruvāṇaḥ kim iti nigṛhyate iti ced āha na hi kaścid kvacid kriyamāṇa prasaṅgaḥ na prayujyate yathā uktamprāk nairātmya vādinaḥ tad sādhane nṛtya gīta ādeḥ api prasaṅgaḥ iti na api tat yad vādinā prasaṅga tvena āhitam tasya prativādinaḥ anubhāṣaṇīyam anupayujyamāna tvat na eva anubhāṣaṇam arhati iti arthaḥ tat etena yat pūrvam uktam yadi nāma vādī svasādhana artha vivaraṇa vyājena ityādi tad abhyanujñātam saṃprati yat uktam tatra api na sarvvam krameṇa uccārayitavyam paścāt dūṣaṇam vācyam dvis uccāraṇa prasaṅgāt iti tadanu jānāti na ca idam api asmābhiri tyāḥ dinā 
VNṬ_118,1^1	 ācāryaḥ āha yadi bhavadbhiḥ apīda meva iṣṭam evantarhi na ananubhāṣaṇam pṛthak vācyam kasmāt pratibhayāga tvāt gatattvam eva pratipādayati uttarasya hi apratipatteḥ apratibhā tatas kathaṅgatam iti āha na ca uttara viṣayam apradarśayan prativādi uttaram pratipattum jñātum abhidhātum vā samarthaḥ kim iti na śaktaḥ iti āha na hi ityādi ca uttara pratipattiḥ uttarā pratipattiḥ iti arthaḥ sā na ākṣiptā yena ananubhāṣaṇena tat tathā pratiṣedha dvayāt vidhi avasīyaa ākṣipta uttarā pratipattikam eva iti etat uktam bhavati yaḥ hi nāma uttaram pratipadyate atas vaśyam tat viṣayam api avetyasya idam dūṣaṇam iti parijñānāt parijñāta viṣayaḥ ca katham sa cetanaḥ na tam anubhāṣate tasmāt yatra ananubhāṣaṇantatra apratibhayā bhāvyam iti sā tasya vyāpikā taru ūri va khadirasyatasyāḥ ca vihitam nigraha sthāna tvam vyāpye ananubhāṣaṇe tadā kṣipati iti etat nigamana vyājena āha tena ityādi 
VNṬ_118,1^2	 atra eva dṛṣṭāntam brūte gavya parāmṛṣṭa tad bhedāyām sāmānya bhūtāyām vihitam iva sāsnā ādimattvat tad vyāpta bāhuleye apilabdham iti varttate prayogaḥ punar yat eka vidhāna sāmarthyāt anuktam api labhyate nanubhūyas prekṣā pūrva kāriṇā vidhātavyam tat yathā go jātausāsna ādima tva vidhāna sāmarthyāt pratilabdham tarhya iṣu sāsnā ādima tvam apratibhā nigraha sthāna tva vidhāna sāmarthyāt pratibaddhaḥ ca ananubhāṣaṇa nigraha sthāna tvam iti vyāpaka viruddha upalabdhiḥ nanu ca viṣayam viṣayaḥ ca prapañca uttaram pratipadyamāna upyati bhaya kampa ādibhiḥ vyākulīkṛta cetāḥ prativādīna anubhāṣate sa viṣayaḥ ananubhāṣaṇasya apratibhayā anālīḍhaḥ tat katham sā tasya vyāpikāḥ yatas ayam hetuḥ siddhaḥ bhaviṣyatinā eva sambhavāt na hi viṣayam viṣaya viṣayañca uttaram pratipadyamānaḥ kutaścid vibheti vepate vā tad ajñāna kṛta tvāt bhaya vepathu sveda ādīnām atha tathābhūtaḥ api bhaya ādibhiḥ ākulīkriyate sa tarhi ādau= eva tathābhūtaḥ vādam api kartunna eva dhāvati 
VNṬ_118,1^3	 api ca yadi param bālāḥ eva evam bhūtāḥ bhavanti na ca bāla vyavahāra an adhikṛtya nyāya śāstrāṇi praṇīyante yat vā evam api apratibhāyām antarbhāvaḥ na eva vyāhanyate yasmāt vividha uttarā pratipattiḥ uttara ajñāna rūpa uttara anabhidhāna rūpāca tasmāt yat kiñcid etat atha para upatāpana arthā tathā api kintriḥ abhidhīyate kintarhi kāryyam iti āha sākṣiṇā mutkaḥ ca upasaṅkramam karṇem nivedya ayam atra arthaḥ mayā vivakṣitaḥ iti uttara kālam prativādya nāthaḥ varākaḥ kaṣṭā apratīta druta saṃkṣipta ādibhiḥ śabdaiḥ iti śeṣaḥ upadrotavyaḥ kasmāt durbhaṇāḥ apratītāḥ siṃhala bhāṣā ādi vadasam ketikāḥ drutāḥ śīdhram uccāritāḥ saṃkṣiptā sūtra vāṇṭa ādi vat varttulīkṛta arthāḥ ādi grahaṇena gopita arthānāṅgrahaṇam yathā satva at urvāyuḥ te diśyāyotāya añca arātyasvantam pakṣe na ulaṃvam vijñāyaiḥ veṣṭā toya aspṛṣṭa īśaḥ śam iti yathā saṃprati vādī uttara pratipattauvimūḍhaḥ tūṣṇīm bhavati 
VNṬ_118,1^4	 parṣad prativādibhyām tris abhihitam avijñātam avijñāta artha miti atra śliṣṭa kaṣṭa ādi śabda prayogasya muninā anivārita tvāt na evam anyāyam katum labha te iti ced āha na hi para upatāpa kramaḥ iti ādikiñca na para upatāpanāya santaḥ pravartante śāstrāṇi vā praṇīyante taiḥ iti uktam durjana vipratipati adhikaraṇe satāṃśa astra apravṛteḥ iti atra yatas ca parān upatāpayitum na santaḥ pravartante tasmāt tāvat vaktavyam yāvat anena na gṛhītam na tris eva vaktavyam iti adhikṛtam athavā ādinā śatadhā punar puna rabhidhāne prativādi ati jaḍa tvāt gṛhītum na śaknoti iti niścitanta dā agrahaṇa sāmarthye kathañcid niścite sādhana prayogāt prāk eva parihartavyaḥ na anena saha udgrāhayāmi iti paricchinnam asāmarthyam grahaṇe ati jāḍyā para nāmaka prativādi sambandhiyena vādinā sa tathā kathaṃtathā pariharanna aśaktaḥ śaṃkyate iti āha parāṇan sākṣiṇaḥ prabodhya na ayam śaktaḥ vākya artham boddhum vastu tu evam vyavasthitam iti 
VNṬ_120,1^1	 avijñā tañca ajñāna miti bhāve niṣṭhā vidhānāt sādhana vākya artha aparijñānam nigraha sthānam tatas eva bhāṣye ṭīkā kṛtaḥ vivṛṇvanti vākya artha viṣayasya vijñānasya anutpattiḥ ajñānam iti astu vā karmaṇi eva niṣṭhā vidhānam tathā api vākya artha viṣaya jñāna anutpatyā viśeṣi tam vādi prayuktam vākyam eva prativādinaḥ nigraha sthānam iti na kiñcid vyāhanyate anye punar vivaraṇertha grahaṇam paśyantaḥ sūtrepi artha grahaṇam bhrāntyā paṭhanti avijñāta arthañcā jñānam iti saḥ anyeṣām pāṭhaḥ vijñāta arthaṃsā dhana vākyam pariṣadā tasya prativādinā yat avijñātam anavabodhaḥ tat ajñānam iti evam bhāva pakṣe akṣara vinyāsaḥ karma pakṣe tu tasya iti na adhyāhartavyam ekavā kyatayā eva tu vyākhyātam 
VNṬ_120,1^2	 vijñātam parṣadā iti kim artham parṣadā api avijñāte vādinaḥ eva avijñāta artha nigraha sthānam bhavati iti jñāpanāya nigraha sthāna tve kāraṇam āha arthe khalvavijñāte prativādī na tasya pratiṣedham brūyāt iti apare tu uttareṇa dūṣaṇa granthena saha etat sambadhnanti tat ca ayuktam bhāṣya vārtika grantha tvāt asya gamya tvam eva sādhayati yathā ananubhāṣaṇe anuttara pratipatya eva nigraha sthāna tvam katham uttara apratipattiḥ iti āha apradarśita viṣaya tvāt prativādinā uttara pratipattiḥ aśakyā itikṛtvā apradarśitaḥ viṣayaḥ yena iti vijñeyam viśeṣaṇa samāsaḥ vā tathā hi dūṣaṇasya viṣaya khyāpana artham anubhāṣate tañca parityajya yat yat eva vādinā anudgrāhita māla jālam anubhāṣate 
VNṬ_120,1^3	 tadānīm uttara viṣaya pradarśana prasaṅgam antareṇa tathābhūtasya anubhāṣaṇasya vaiyarthyāt aśakyā itivartate anugraha pratipatya eva nigraha sthāna tvam iti vā dārṣṭa antikam upasaṃharati tathā jñāne api utarā pratipatya eva nigraha sthāna tvam iti yasmāt ajānan prativādi dūṣaṇa tad viṣayau katham uttara viṣayañca brūyāt uttara viṣayaḥ dūṣyaḥ kvacid tu pāṭhaḥ katham uttaram uttaraviṣayañcotaram iti atra evam yat asambandhaḥ ajānannuttara viṣayañca katham uttarambrūyāt iti tasmāt viṣaya ajñāna mutarājñānañca nigraha sthānam apratibhayā eva gamya tvāt avācyam iti vartate kiṃkāraṇam anyathā evam aniṣpramāṇe satya pratibhāyāḥ nirviṣaya tvāt 
VNṬ_120,1^4	 katham nirvviṣaya tvam iti āha anavadhārita arthaḥ hi ityādi anavadhāri tortha pūrva pakṣasya uttarasya ca yena prativādinā sa na anubhāṣet ananubhāṣyamāṇaḥ ca asau viṣayam apradarśya uttaram pratipattut na śaknuyāt iti atas utarat na pratipadyeta na jānīyāt na abhidadhyāt vā kasmāt uttara viṣayayoḥ ajñāne sati uttara apratipattiḥ iti atas āha jñāna uttara tad viṣayasya uttara apratipatteḥ asaṃbhavāt iti jñātā uttara tad viṣayaḥ yena iti vṛttaḥ tasmāt ubhayam etat uttara ajñānam viṣaya ājñānañca pratipatteḥ apratibhā para paryyāyāyāḥ kāraṇam nanu ca uttara ajñānam eva apratibhā tat katham sā eva ātmanaḥ kāraṇa tvena upadiśyate 
VNṬ_120,1^5	 na uttara anabhidhāna lakṣaṇāyāḥ apratibhāsāyāḥ vivakṣita tvāt tad abhāvaḥ iti tayoḥ uttara viṣaya ājñānayoḥ abhāve sati pratipattiḥ abhidhānam uttarasya bhavati eva iti tasmāt tayoḥ viṣaya ajñāna uttara jñānayoḥ ajñāna saṃjñitena nigraha sthānena apratibhā nigraha sthānāt pṛthakvacane satya pratibhāyāḥ kaḥ viṣayaḥ iti vaktavyam na ced viṣayaḥ bhaṇyate tadā nirviṣaya tvāt avācyā eva syāt apratibhā tayoḥ ajñāna anubhāṣaṇayoḥ pṛthak vacanaḥ iti anye vyācakṣate ajñāna apratibhayoḥ viṣaya bheda vyavasthāpanāya paraḥ prāha na uttara jñānam ajñānam ucyate yatas apratibhā nirviṣaya tvāt avācī ambhavet kintarhi ajñānam iti āha viṣaya ajñānam 
VNṬ_120,1^6	 evam api katham apratibhā viṣayavatī bhavati iti āha jñāte viṣaye sati uttara kālam uttara ajñānāt prativādī tat utarat na pratipadyeta na brūyāt atas asti viṣayaḥ apratibhāyāḥ ajñāna ākrāntaḥ evam api avācya tvā annam ucyasaḥ iti āha evantarhi iti ajñānena anubhāṣaṇasya ākṣepam eva sādhayati na hi viṣayam samyak pratipadyamānaḥ kaścid sa cetanaḥ na anubhāṣeta iti na anubhāṣaṇam ajñānāt pṛthak vācyam api caivam apratibhā api ananubhāṣaṇa vat ajñānāt pṛthagna vācyā iti āha uttara ajñānasya cākṣepāt iti idam vyācaṣṭe viṣaye tyādinā jñāte viṣaya etya ādi paraḥ idam uktam bhavati dvidhā uttara ajñāna viṣaya ajñāna sahacarañca viṣaya jñāna sahacarañca 
VNṬ_120,1^7	 tatra ādyasya viṣaya ajñāne na ākṣepe api uttaram anākṣiptam evatataḥ dvitīya apekṣayā apratibhāyāḥ pṛthak upādānam iti anavasthā eva nigraha sthānānām prasajyate iti āha evantarhi ityādi yathā iti ādyasya eva vibhāgaḥ tathā jñānayoḥ api iti viṣaya uttara ajñānayoḥ api sarvu asya uttarasya viṣayasya ca ajñānam ādi grahaṇena dvi tri catur bhāga ādi avarodhaḥ viṣaya uttara ajñānayoḥ saṅgraha vacane doṣaḥ iti ced āha na ca iti yathā na doṣaḥ tathā aguṇopi na asti iti ced āha gu ṇaḥ ca lāghava saṃjñaḥ syāt iti saṃgraha vacanam nyāyyam apratibhā viṣaya tvāt na pṛthak vacanam apratibhā vacanena eva anayoḥ saṅgrahaḥ iti arthaḥ na kevala m anayoḥ eva apṛthak vacanam 
VNṬ_120,1^8	 nyāyyam api tu anyeṣām api iti āha api ca ityādi tad ubhaya vacanena eva iti hetvābhāsā apratibhayoḥ eva vacanena sarva pratijñā ahāni ananubhāṣaṇa ādi uktam na hi kaścid hi anya ssādhanavādī pratipakṣa dharmam abhyunujānāti pratijñām vā pratijñā sādhanāya upādattaḥ ityādi vācyam tadā na kañcid dūṣaṇam vyaktam eva yat na anubhāṣate kathām vikṣipati parama tañca anujānāti iti vaktavyam tad ubhaya ākṣepa ipi prapañcaḥ guṇavān atas tat avacanāt araḥ muneḥ iti ced āha tad ubhaya ākṣipteṣu prabhedeṣu guṇa atiśayam antareṇa anupalabhyamāna tvāt guṇasya prapañca vacana ādare ati prasaṅgāt kakṣa piṭṭita ādīnām abhidhāna prasaṅgāt atas vyarthaḥ prapañcaḥ mahā muninā akriyata 
VNṬ_123,1	 para pakṣa pratiṣedhe kartavye uttaram dūṣaṇam yadā na pratipadyate na vetti na abhidadhāti tadā nigṛhītaḥ veditavyaḥ iti iyān para granthaḥ sādhu etat nigraha sthānam ataa iva asmābhiḥ api īdama doṣa udbhāvanam iti atra uktam iti etat matvā abhyanujānāti sādhana ityādi sādhana vacana anantaram prativādinā dūṣaṇam vaktavyam sa yadā sarvvam tat akṛtvā sarvva anukrama anubhāṣaṇena śloka pāṭhena sabhā samvarṇṇanena anyena kālan nayati tadā asau vyartham niṣprayojar na kālaṅga mayan karttavyasya dūṣaṇa abhidhānasya pratipattyā ananuṣṭhānena nigṛhyate vyarthasya idam kriyāyāḥ kālasya viśeṣaṇam 
VNṬ_123,2^1	 kārya vyāsaṅgaḥ karṇīya upanyāsaḥ kathā vicchedaḥ kathā nivṛttiḥ yathā jīrṇṇa kalā me bādhate samprati vaktum na śaknomi paścāt kathayiṣyāmi iti evamādinā prakāreṇa kathām udgrāhaṇe kācid śinattiḥ nigraha sthānekāraṇam āha ekatarasya vādinaḥ prativādinaḥ vā asādhana aṅga vacanena adoṣa udbhāvanena ca nigṛhaṇantī nigraha paryavasānā kathā tasya añca tathābhūtāyām prastutāyām sa svayam eva kathā aṃtam kathā paryavasānam pratipadyate iti nigraha sthānam etat atra ācārya ubrūta 
VNṬ_123,2^2	 idam api kārya vyāsañjanam yadi tāvat pūrva pakṣa vādī kuryāt sādhana abhidhāna śakti vikala tvāt vyāja upakṣepa mātreṇa yena kenacid chalena iti arthaḥ na punar bhūtasya tathāvidha kathā uparodhinaḥ kāryasya bhāve sati kuryāt iti varttate tathā vidhām udgrāhaṇikā rūpāṅkathām uparoddhum śīlam yasya kāryasya ajīrṇṇa kalā kukṣi śūla gehu dāha ādyaiḥ tat tathā yadi sadbhāvena eva tasya tasyām velāyām kukṣi gala śūla gehu dāha ādayaḥ bhavanti tathā sati na eva nigraha sthānam iti arthaḥ yadā punar vyāja mātreṇa eva karoti tadā tasya pūrvva pakṣa vādinaḥ sva sādhana āsāmarthya paricchedāt eva vikṣepaḥ syāt tatas kim iti āha 
VNṬ_123,2^3	 tathā ca idam vikṣepa sañjñi tat nigraha sthānam artha antaraḥ eva antar bhavet rūpa siddhi nāma ādi vyākhyāna samānat tvāt karaṇīya upanyāsasya hetvābhāseṣu eva antar bhavet iti adhikṛtam kasmāt asamarthañca tad sādhanañca tasya abhidhānāt kiñca idam nirarthaka apārthakābhyām sakāśāt na bhidyate kiṃkāraṇam prakṛtañca tad sādhanañca tena asambaddhā ca sā pratipattiḥ ca tatas sādhana vākyena saha asya daśa dāḍima ādi vacanasya iva jabagaḍa ādi varṇṇa kramasya iva casambaddha anupalambhāt iti arthaḥ kiñcid mātra bhedāt nimitta leśena pṛthak uktam iti ced āha ati prasaṅgaḥ ce tyādi 
VNṬ_123,2^4	 asambaddha asā dhana vākyena pratipattiḥ yeṣāṃpratibhedānānte asambaddha sādhana vākya pratipattayaḥ te ca te prabhedāḥ ca teṣām iti kāryam evantā vat pūrva pakṣa vādi sambandhena vikṣepasya pṛthak anabhidhānam uktam adhunā prativādi sambandhena api āha atha uttara pakṣa vādī evam balāsakala ātma kaṇṭham kṣiṇoti ityādinā prakrameṇa kathām vikṣipet tad ānīntasya apyu ttara pakṣa vādinaḥ sādhana anantaram uttare pratipattavye sati tad apratipattyā tasya uttarasya anabhidhānena vikṣepa pratipattiḥ yāsā a pratibhāyām artha antare vā antarbhavati iti paraḥ tu yathoktam antar bhāvam asahamānaḥ codayati 
VNṬ_124,1^1	 nanu na avaśya miti tat eva draḍhayati bhavati hi anibaddhena api sādhana vākyena asambaddhe na api kathā prabandhena para pratibhā haraṇāya antaśas jananī vyabhicāra codanena api vivādaḥ iti ācāryaḥ āha na asambhavāt evaṃvidhasya vivādasya yasmāt ekatra śabda ādau= adhikaraṇe nitya tva anitya tva ādi pratijñāna aviruddhau= abhyupagamau yayoḥ vādi prati vādinoḥ tayoḥ vivādaḥ syāt kutas etat iti āha aviruddhau= abhyupagamau yayoḥ tau tathā na vidyete viruddha aviruddhayoḥ abhyupagamau yayoḥ puruṣayoḥ tau= abhyupagamau tayoḥ vivāda abhāvāt tatra etasmin vyavasthite nyāya nirdhāraṇe vā tatra śabdaḥ ekasya vādinaḥ prativādinā uvaśyam prāc vacana pravṛttiḥ yaugapadyena kin na brūte iti āha yugapad pravṛttau svastha ātmanām apravṛtteḥ iti sambandhaḥ etat eva kutas iti āha 
VNṬ_124,1^2	 paraspara vacana śravaṇa avadhāraṇa uttarāṇām asambhavena karaṇa bhūtena pravṛtti vaiphalyāt yadi hi paraspara vacanasya asaṅkareṇa śravaṇam bhavet tatas tad artham avadhārayati uttarañca yugapad pravṛttau ca digambara pāṭha kalakalaḥ iva sarvvam etat na saṃbhavati tasmāt avaśyam ekasya prāc vacana pravṛttiḥ atas tena ca svastha ātmanā pūrvva pakṣa vādinā anityam śabdam sādhayāmi ityādinā sva upagama upanyāse kṛte sati a vaśyam sādhanam vaktavyam anyathā iti hetu anabhidhā ne pareṣa aṃsa akṣi prabhṛtīnām apratipatteḥ apareṇa ca iti uttara pakṣa vādinā tad sambandhi vādi prokta sādhana sambandhi dūṣaṇam vaktavyam iti varttate tasmāt ubhayoḥ vādi prati vādinoḥ asamyak pravṛttau satyām hetvābhāsā pratibhayoḥ saṃgrahaḥ iti sarvvaḥ nyāya pravṛttaḥ pūrvva uttara pakṣa upanyāsaḥ dvayam hetvābhāsa apratibhāñca na atipatati 
VNṬ_125,1^1	 nanu ca yadi nyāyaḥ pravṛttaḥ kathantatra asya dvayasya adhikāraḥ kathañca ekatra dharmiṇi viruddhau= upanyāsau nyāya pravṛttau= avaśyam hi tatra ekena upanyāsena nyāyam pravṛttena bhāvyam anyathā dharmīdvyātmakaḥ bhavet nābhi prāya aparijñānāt na idambhavatā nyāya pravṛtta tvam ācāryeṇa vivakṣitam paryajñāyi nyāya pravṛttau hi pūrvva uttara pakṣa upanyāsasya yugapad pravṛtya bhāvena jananī vyabhicāra vedanā ādi abhāvena ca abhipretam etena ekatra hi adhikaraṇe viruddha abhyupagamayoḥ vivādaḥ syāt ityādinā vitaṇḍā pratyuktāḥ katham pratyuktā iti āha abhyupagama abhāve vivāda abhāvāt idam uktam bhavati sva pakṣa sthāpanā hīnaḥ vākya samūhaḥ vitaṇḍe ti ucyate yadi ca vaitaṇḍikrasya sva pakṣaḥ na asti vivādaḥ tarhi katham iti vaktavyam 
VNṬ_125,1^2	 para pakṣa pratiṣedha artham vaitaṇḍikaḥ pravarttate iti ced para pakṣa pratiṣedhaḥ eva tarhi asya sva pakṣa sthāpanā iti vitaṇḍā lakṣaṇam viśīryate tathā hi yaḥ yena abhyupagataḥ sa tasya sva pakṣaḥ para pakṣa pratiṣedhaḥ ca tena abhyupagataḥ sva pakṣa tām na ativartate iti yadā tarhi upagamya vādam pratijñā mātreṇa viphala tayā pariṣad śāradyena vyākulīkṛtattvāt iti arthaḥ na kiñcid sādhanam tat āyāsam vā vakti anyat vā kiñcid pralapa ti sādhana tad ābhāsa vyatiriktam kākaḥ virūpam virauti nūnam ayam me gehe vipadam sūcayati tat alam anena vivādena yāmi tāvat gehe kinnu me pituḥ maraṇam anyat vā varttate ityādi tathā katham hetvābhāsa antarbhāvaḥ sādhana abhāvāt hetvābhāsā sambhavam manyate uttara apratipattiḥ api na asti eva pūrvva pakṣa vādi tvāt iti abhiprāyaḥ 
VNṬ_125,1^3	 tat anena dvayat = ātipatati iti etat vighaṭayitum icchati paraḥ ācāryaḥ āha asamarthita sāghana abhidhānaḥ evam uktam dvayam na atipatati iti prokta sādhanaḥ etat uktam iti yāvat aprokte tu katham pratipattavyam iti āha anabhidhānāni abhidhānayoḥ api satoḥ parājayaḥ eva iti uktam prakaraṇa avatāraḥ eva tat eva smarayati abhyupagamya vādam asādhana aṅga vacanāt iti tathā hi tatra vyākhyātam sādhana aṅgasya anuccāraṇam sādhana aṅgāt vā yat anyasya abhidhānam tat saru vama sādhana aṅga vacanam iti etena iti anya abhidhānena parājaya vacanena adhikasya punar uktasya ca pratijñādeḥ vacanasya ca nigraha sthāna tvam vyākhyātam katham iti āha tat api hi ityādi anena etat āha 
VNṬ_125,1^4	 yat yukti yukta makṣa pādena kiñcid nigraha sthānam uktantat asmābhiḥ asādhana aṅga vacana padena eva saṃgṛhītam iti yadi evam pratijñādeḥ vacanasya ca iti kim artha yuktat = ahi pratijñā upanaya nigamanānām vacanat nigraha sthāna makṣa pāde na uktam pratyuta tat avacanam eva nigraha sthāna tayā yat iṣṭam hīnam anyatamena api avayavena nyūna miti evam tarhi dṛṣṭānta artham etat yathā tasya apratīta pratyāyana śakti vikala tvāt asādhana aṅga vacana padena abhidhānam tathā adhika punarvacanayoḥ api iti tatas eva ca dvitīyaḥ cakāraḥ iva śabda arthe varttate anyathā punaru ktasya ca iti ayam bodhi arthaḥ syāt kecid tu uttarañcakāran na paṭhanti taiḥ punarukta vyākhyānam eva pratijñādeḥ vacanasya ca iti etat vyākhyeyam evam api na yuktam akṣapādena evamvidhasya punar uktasya aniṣṭa tvāt na asti doṣaḥ pūrvva tulya dharma tayā asya api punar ukte antar bhāvita tvāt
