VNṬ_127,1^1	 sva pakṣa doṣa abhyupagamāt para pakṣa doṣa prasaṅgaḥ mata anujñā doṣa parihāre vaktavye doṣasya aparijñānāt para matam anujānātyataḥ nigṛhyate tat āha pareṇa vādinā coditam paryanuyuktam doṣam anuvṛtyā parihṛtya bhavatā upyayam doṣaḥ iti bravīti yathā bhavān= cauraḥ puruṣatvā cchavara ādi vadi tyukte vādinā sa prativādī tam vādinam pratibrūyāt bhavān api cauraḥ iti sa upi śabda prayogāt ātmanaḥ caura tvam abhyupagamya para pakṣe tandoṣam āsañjayan= āpādayati apareṇa vādinā yat matam prativādinaḥ caurat tvam tad anujānāti tathā hi te na mukta saṃśayantā vat ātmanaḥ caurattvam pratipattum anyathā na api tam abhidadhyāt vādini tu tat astinā asti iti cintyam atas mata anujñā nigraha sthānam 
VNṬ_127,1^2	 idam ācāryaḥ nirākaroti atra api yadi ayam abhiprāyaḥ uttara vādinaḥ puruṣa tvāt cauṃraḥ bhavān api syāt aham iva na ca bhavatā ātmā evam caura tvena iṣṭaḥ tat na ayam puruṣa tvāt iti caurye sādhye hetuḥ acaurepi bhavati vipakṣa bhūte vṛtteḥ anaikāntika doṣa duṣṭa tvāt iti tat asmin prativādinaḥ abhiprāye na kaścid tasya doṣaḥ mata anujñā lakṣaṇaḥ anyaḥ vā kasmāt anabhimate caurat tve na rūpeṇa tasya vādinaḥ ātmani vipakṣa bhūte hetoḥ satva pradarśanena prakāreṇa dūṣaṇāt vidagdha bhaṅga avyabhicāra udbhāvanāt iti yāvat audyota karaṃcodyamā śaṅkateprasaṅgam antareṇa bhavān api syāt iti evam āñjasena eva mṛjunā eva krameṇa kin na vyabhicāritaḥ hetuḥ tvayi api acaure varttate puruṣa tvam atas anaikāntika tvam iti 
VNṬ_127,1^3	 tasmāt yataeva asau= akauṭilye kartavye kauṭilyam ācarati tatas eva nigṛhyate iti ācāryaḥ āha yat kiñcid etada audyota karam vacaḥ yasmāt santi hi evam prakārāḥ vaidagdhya pravartitā vyavahārāḥ loke tathā hi mātaraḥ bhāvatkyaḥ bandhakyaḥ strī tvāditarabandhakī vat iti uktāḥ paśupālādayopi jaḍa janaṅgama ādi jana sādhāraṇam vaidagdhyam anu saraṃtaḥ pratyavatiṣṭhante tāvakīnā api mātā tathā syāt iti na ca te anena prakāreṇa svasyāḥ svasyāḥ mātuḥ bandhakī tvam pratipadyante api tu bhaṅgyāḥ hetu vyabhicāra codanayā param prativadanti tasmāt evam bāla hālikā ādi loka prakaṭam api vyavahāra ālokam apasārayatā yadi param udyota kara tvam evaḥ dyota kareṇa udyotitam ātmanaḥ 
VNṬ_127,1^4	 atha ucyate na eva asau bhaṃgyā vyabhicāram ādarśayati api tu tasya sādhanasya samyak tvam abhyupagamya eva tena doṣeṇa param apikalaṅkayati iti atas āha atha tad upakṣepaḥ puruṣa tvāt bhavān= cauraḥ iti enam abhyupagacchati eva tadā api asau tad sādhana uttara apratipatya eva nigraha arhaḥ na aparatra vādi nisva doṣasya caura tvasya upakṣepāt nigraha arhaḥ iti varttate idam eva upodbalayati tad sādhana nirdoṣa tāyām hi aṃgīkṛtāyām iti śeṣaḥ tasya upakṣepasya abhyupagamaḥ eva yaḥ saḥ eva uttara apratipattiḥ iti tāvatā eva uttara apratipatti mātreṇa eva aparatra doṣa prasañjanāt pūrva sādhana nigrahasya sataḥ prativādi naḥ āpannaḥ prāptaḥ nigrahaḥ yena tasya iti ca iti vigrahaḥ para doṣa upakṣepasya mata anujñā lakṣaṇasya anapekṣaṇīya tvāt parājita parājaya abhāvāt iti bhāvaḥ 
VNṬ_128,1^1	 nigraha prāptasya anigrahaḥ paryanuyojya upekṣaṇam paryanuyojyaḥ nāma nigraha prāptasya upekṣaṇat nigraha prāptosi iti anabhidhānam kaḥ punar idam paryanuyojya upekṣaṇam nigraha sthānaṃcodayati na tāvat paryanuyojyaḥ iti yuktam asambhavāt na hi asti sambhavaḥ yat para doṣa pratipādana artham ātmanaḥ doṣava tvam asau= abhyupeti nigraha prāptaḥ sat na hamanena upekṣitaḥ nigraha sthānasya aparijñānāt tasmāt ayan doṣavān iti na api upekṣaḥ iti yuktam yasmāt asauni jānāti eva ayam nigraha prāptaḥ iti tathā hi aparijñānāt eva asau na anuyuṃkte nigraham prāpta ūsi iti parijñāne vā katham upekṣeta upekṣaṇe vā sama cittaḥ katham evam prakaṭayet ayam mayā upekṣitaḥsa doṣaḥ tatas mama paryanuyojya upekṣaṇam nigraha sthānam iti 
VNṬ_128,1^2	 na ca anyaḥ tṛtīyaḥ kaścid iha anuṣaṅgī tat kena idam codanīyam iti etat sarvvam āśaṅkya pakṣila svāmī brūte etat ca paryanuyojya upekṣaṇam vakta vyañcodanīyaṅkasya parājaya iti evam vādi prativādibhyām praguṇā tad anyaiḥ vā paryanuyuktayā pṛṣṭayā satyā pariṣadā prāśnikaiḥ vaktavyam iti arthaḥ ca śabdaḥ avadhāraṇa arthaḥ evam eva anyāni nigraha sthānāni vādi prativādibhyām eva udbhāvyante etat punar prāśnikaiḥ eva kim punar kāraṇam tābhyām eva na ucyate iti āha na khalu nigraha prāptaḥ sva kaupīnam sva doṣam vivṛṇuyāt prakāśayet atra api ityādi ācāryaḥ yadi tu nyāyaḥ cintyate tadāna ekasya api jaya parājayau nyāyyau katham vādinaḥ jayaḥ iti āha sādhana ābhāsena jijñāsitasya arthasya apratipādanāt 
VNṬ_128,1^3	 atas eva na prativādinā upi parājayaḥ vādi vivakṣita artha siddhi apekṣayā prativādinaḥ parājaya vyavasthāpanāt prativādinaḥ tarhi kim jayaḥ iti āha bhūte doṣān abhidhānāt ca ataeva ca na vādinaḥ parājayaḥ tad dūṣaṇa apekṣayā tad vyavasthiteḥ atha uttara pakṣa vādi aneka doṣa sadbhāvepi vādi proktasya sādhanasya kañcid doṣam udbhāvayati kañcid naḥ na tadā asaunigraham arhati kiṅkāraṇam uttarasya pratipatteḥ abhidhānāt iti arthaḥ paraḥ āha arhati eva nigraham sarvu eṣān doṣāṇām anudbhāvanāt ācāryaḥ āha na khalubhoḥ santaḥ iti kṛtvā sarvve doṣāḥ avaśyam vaktavyāḥ prativādinā avacane vā doṣa antarasya nigrahaḥ bhavati na iti varttate kasmāt sarvve doṣāḥ na udbhāvi aṃte iti āha 
VNṬ_128,1^4	 ekena api doṣeṇa asiddha tva ādinā udbhāvitena na tasya vādi prayuktasya sādhanasya vighātāt sādhya siddhim pratyasamartha tva pratipādanāt iti arthaḥ bhāva sādhanaḥ vā sādhana śabdaḥ atra eva dṛṣṭāntam āha eka sādhana vacana vat iti yathā iti ādyasya eva vibhāgaḥ ekasya arthasya kṣaṇika tva ādeḥ pratipādanāya anekasya sādhanasya satva kārya tva prayatna uttha tva ādeḥ sadbhāvepi sati ekena eva satva ādīnām anyatamena upāttena tasya kṣaṇika tva ādeḥ arthasya siddheḥ niścayāt na sarvu eṣām sādhanāḥ nām upādānam tathā ekena api doṣeṇa tad sādhana vighātāt na sarvvā upādānam iti īdan dṛṣṭāntena sāmyam iti tasmāt na uttara pakṣa vādī pūrvvam ekam doṣam udbhāvayan= eva aparasya doṣa antarasya anudbhāvanāt nigraha arhaḥ pūrvva vat iti sādhana ābhāsena apratipādanāt bhūta doṣān abhidhānāt ca 
VNṬ_130,1	 nanu ca kathat na vādinaḥ jayaḥ yāvatā na tena sādhana ābhāsaḥ prayuktaḥ prativādī tu asantam doṣam udbhāvayati iti atas āha doṣa ābhāsam bruvāṇam uttara pakṣa vādinam sva sādhanāt sakāśāt anusārayataḥ a nivarttayataḥ tad ukta dūṣaṇa ābhāsa tvena apratipādayate iti yāvat vādinaḥ na jayaḥ kasmāt asamanvita sādhana aṅga tvāt asamanvita sādhana aṅgam yena tasya bhāvaḥ tatvam etat eva kutas iti āha sarvva doṣa abhāva pradarśanena sādhana aṅga samarthanāt itttham bhūta lakṣaṇe karaṇe vā tṛtīyā asamarthi tattvāt sādhana ābhāsaḥ eva tena prayuktaḥ iti saṃkṣepa arthaḥ na api uttara pakṣa vādinaḥ jayaḥ iti varttate tasmāt evam api iti yadi pūrva pakṣa vādi uttara pakṣa vādi naṃna nigraha prāptam nigṛhṇāti na kevalam uttara vādi sambandhena iti api śabdaḥ 
VNṬ_130,2^1	 niranuyojyasya anuyogaḥ anigraha prāpte nigṛhīta usi iti abhidhānam kiṃpunar evam brūtaḥ iti āha nigraha sthāna lakṣaṇasya mithyā vyavasāya adya tha uktasya nigraha sthāna lakṣaṇasya samyak aparijñānāt iti arthaḥ evañcā pratipattitaḥ nigṛhyate atra api ityādi ācāryaḥ yadi tasya sādhanasya vādinam abhūtaiḥ alīkaiḥ doṣaiḥ savyabhicāra ādi doṣa duṣṭam tvayā sādhanam prayuktam tatas nigṛhīta usi iti evam abhiyuñjīta tadā saḥ asthāne asya vyākhyānam nirdoṣa nigraha sthānasya asya vibhāgāt eva asya iti abhiyoktā iti asya vivṛtiḥ udbhāvayitā iti tathā ca alīka doṣasya abhidhāyi tve sati doṣa udbhāva lakṣaṇasya uttarasya apratipatteḥ abhidhānāt apratibhayā eva karaṇa bhūtayā uttara vādī nigṛhītaḥ iti kṛtvā na idat niranuyojya anuyoga abhidhānat nigraha sthānam atas apratibhā nigraha sthānāt sakāśāt na nigraha sthāna antaram kadā ca ayam apratibhayā nigṛhyate iti āha itareṇa vādinā tad uktasya uttara ābhāsa tve pratipādite anyathā na dvayoḥ ekasya api pūrvavat jaya parājayau= iti ākūtam evam prativādi sambandhena asya apṛthak vacanam pratipādya vādi sambandhena api āha 
VNṬ_130,2^2	 atha uttara vādinam bhūtam satyam sādhana doṣam sa vyabhicāra ādikam udbhāvayantam aparaḥ iti pūrva pakṣa vādī doṣa ābhāsa vacanena abhiyuñjīta jāti uttaram anaikāntika ādi ābhāsam tvayā prayuktam tasmāt nigṛhītosi iti evam yadi abhiyuñjīta iti arthaḥ tadā tasya udbhāvitasya doṣasya vyabhicāra ādeḥ tena uttara vādinā bhūta doṣa tve pratipādite jāti uttarava tve parihṛtaḥ iti yāvat sādhana ābhāsa vacanena eva vādī nigṛhyate iti tasmāt evam api prativādi sambandhena api na idam hetvābhāsebhyaḥ bhidyate iti pṛthak vācyam asya eva upodvalanam avaśyam hi dvāviṃśati nigraha sthāna vādinā hetvābhāsāḥ pṛthak nigraha sthāna tvena vaktavyāḥ kimartham iti āha viṣaya antara prāpti artham niranuyojya anuyoga ādibhiḥ nnigraha sthānaiḥ anākrānta saṅgraham api iti anyathā dvāviṃśati tvam nigraha sthā nānām abhyupagamam viruddhi atas iti abhiprāyaḥ tathā ca tad uktau teṣām hetvābhāsānām nigraha sthānena uktau satyām aparoktiḥ aparasya niranuyojya anuyogasya uktiḥ nirirthakā hetvābhāsa vacanena eva saṃgṛhīta tvāt 
VNṬ_132,1^1	 siddhāntam abhyupetya aniyamāt kathā prasaṅgaḥ apasiddhāntaḥ iti sūtram siddhāntam abhyupetya pakṣa parigraham kṛtvā aniyamāt pūrva prakṛta artha uparodhena śāstra vyavasthām anādṛtya iti yāvat kathā prasaṅgaḥ artha antara upavarṇanam kasyacid arthasya iti dharmiṇaḥ dharma antaram pratijñāya pratijñāta artha viparyayaḥ virodhaḥ idam udāharaṇena spaṣṭayati yathā na sataḥ vastunaḥ vināśaḥ niranvayaḥ kevalam tirobhāva mātram bhavati na asat khara viṣāṇa tulyam utpadyate kintarhi āvirbhāvataḥ sadeva utpadyate iti evam kāpilaḥ siddhānta vyavasthām ādarśya pakṣaṅkaroti ekā prakṛtiḥ vyaktasya avyakta lakṣaṇā vyaktasya iti mahat ādeḥ atra hetum āha vikārāṇām śabda ādīnām anvaya darśanāt 
VNṬ_132,1^2	 mṛd anvayānām ityādi dṛṣṭāntaḥ tathā ca ayam iti upanapanayaḥ sukha duḥkha moha samanvitā eti sukha ādi maya tvam darśayati darśi tañca sukha ādi maya tvam vyaktasya pūrvam yathā sāṃkhyena abhimatam tat tasmāt sukha ādibhiḥ eka prakṛtiḥ iti ayam vyakta bhedaḥ iti nigamanaṃsukha ādibhiḥ iti ittthaṃbhūta lakṣaṇe tṛtīyā sukha ādi prakārā sukha ādi lakṣaṇā ekā prakṛtiḥ asya iti arthaḥ anye paṭhanti ekā prakṛtiḥ vyaktāḥ vyakta vikārāṇām anvayada rśanāt iti evañca vyācakṣate ekā prakṛtiḥ abhinnā sarvu ātma svabhāvāḥ vyakta avyakta vikārāṇām anvaya darśanāt ye vyaktāḥ vikārāḥ mahat ādayaḥ ye ca avyaktāḥ pradhāna ātmani vyavasthitāḥ teṣām api anvaya darśanāt iti 
VNṬ_132,1^3	 apare tu paṭhanti ekā prakṛtiḥ avyaktāḥ vyakta vikārāṇām iti vyakta rūpāṇām vikārāṇām iti ca āhuḥ prakṛta artha viparyayeṇa iyam yathā pravṛttā iti pradarśanā artham āha sa kāpilaḥ evam uktavān paryanuyujyate atha prakṛtiḥ vikāraḥ iti etat ubhayaṅkatham lakṣayitavyam pratipattavyam iti saḥ evam anuyuktaḥ prāha yasya avasthitasya dharma antara nivṛttau dharma antarampravarttate sā prakṛtiḥ avasthita rūpāḥ yat tad pravṛtti nivṛtti sat dharma antaram sa vikāraḥ iti lakṣayitavyam param uktavān sāṅkhyaḥ prakṛta artha parityāga doṣeṇa upapādyate soyam vādī prakṛta artha viparyayāt aniyamāt kathāmprasañjayati pūrvva prakṛtam parityajati iti arthaḥ katham iti āha 
VNṬ_132,1^4	 pratijñātam khalu anena iti pūrva uktam smarayati yadi evaṅkaḥ doṣaḥ iti āha sat asataḥ riti ādi sataḥ tirobhāvam ekāntena vināśam antareṇa na kasyacid dharmasya pravṛti uparamaḥ sidhyati kena cit virūpeṇa avasthāne sati sa tirohitaḥ aṅgaḥ tasya avasthitasya ātma bhūtaḥ para bhūtaḥ vā bhavet ātma bhūta tve tirohitāt avyatirekāt tirohita vat avasthitasya api anavasthānaṃavasthita vat ca tat avyatirekataḥ tirohitasya api avasthānam āśaṃkyate para bhūta tvepi katham ananvayaḥ na vināśaḥ na hi anyasya avasthāne anyat avatiṣṭhate anyaḥ vā anyasya anvayaḥ caitanyasyā api ghaṭa anvaya prasaṅgāt tathā na asataḥ āvirbhāvam utpādam antareṇa kasyacid dharmasya pravṛttiḥ vā sidhyati 
VNṬ_133,1^1	 nanu ca vidyamānam eva dharma antaram āvirbhāvyate grahaṇa viṣaya bhā vam āpādyate na vidyamānasya kriyāḥ ti upādānam iti upalabdhiḥ vā vidyamāna tvāt na kāraka janya tvam iti evam pratyavasthitaḥ pratiṣiddhaḥ sāṅkhyaḥ kvacid saptamī āpadyate tatra pratyavasthite prativādini satī iti vyākhyeyam yadi sa kāpilaḥ sataḥ dharmasya ātmahānam asataḥ ca ātma lābham abhyupaiti tadānīm apasiddhāntaḥ bhavati abhyupagama viruddhasya pratijñānāt apasiddhānta saṃjñakam nigraha sthānam asya bhavati iti arthaḥ atha sataḥ ātma hānam asataḥ ca ātma lābhat na abhyupaiti evam api eka prakṛtiḥ vikārāṇām iti yoyam pakṣaḥ pūrvva pratijñātaḥ sosyana sidhyati prakṛti vikāra lakṣaṇasya anavasthita tvāt 
VNṬ_133,1^2	 tathā hi tayoḥ lakṣaṇam yasya avasthitasya ityādinā uktam tasya ca ayogaḥ sat asatoḥ ce tyādinā pratipāidate iti etāvān paragranthaḥ atra samprati ācāryaḥ pratividhatte ita upi pratividadhmahe iti śeṣaḥ na kaścid aniyamāt siddhānta nīti virodhāt sāṅkhya sya prasaṅgaḥ tasmāt yat tena upagatam na asat utpadyate na sattirobhavati iti tasya samarthanāya it am uktam kim uktam iti āha eka prakṛtikam idam vyaktam anvaya darśanāt iti tatra ekā iti etat eva vibhajati tat avibhaktayonikam idam vyaktam te sukha ādayaḥ avibhaktāḥ apṛthak bhūtā yoniḥ sthānam adhikaraṇam yasya vyavatasya tad tat avibhaktayonikam kiṅkāraṇam tad anvaya darśanāt 
VNṬ_133,1^3	 taiḥ sukha ādibhiḥ anvaya darśanāt tādātmya upalambhāt tatas kim siddham iti āha vyaktasya tad svabhāva tā sukha ādi svabhāva tā tatra svabhāva tā eva kathat niścitā iti āha abheda upalabdhe riti sukha ādibhiḥ śabda ādīnām anānāt tva darśanāt iti yāvat evam api kim siddhambhavati iti āha sarvu asya śabda ādeḥ vikāra grāmasya sukha ādi ātmakasya na utpatti vināśau= iti sambhavati kasma ādi tyāha sukha ādīnām utpatti vināśa abhāvāt sukha ādi a vyatirekāt tad ātma vat śabdādayopi nityāḥ siddhāḥ bhavanti tathā ca yat pūrvvam abhyupagatam nasatas vināśaḥ na asat utpadyate iti tat samarthitam bhavati 
VNṬ_133,1^4	 atra evam kāpilena sva upagame samarthite sati tat uktasya tena sāṅkhyena uktasya hetoḥ anvaya darśanasya doṣam asiddha tā ādikam anudbhāvya saḥ evam uktavān paryanumujyate atha prakṛtiḥ nirvikāraḥ iti katham lakṣayitavyam iti evam vikāra prakṛtyoḥ lakṣaṇam pṛcchan svayam ayam akṣapādaḥ prakṛta asambandhena aniyamāt prakṛta artha uparodhāt kathāmpravarttayati yasmāt prakṛti vikārayoḥ iha lakṣaṇam na prakṛtam eva tat kintad abhidhāya paryanuyujyate tasmāt aprastuta paryanuyoktṛt tvāt akṣa pādaḥ eva nigraha arhaḥ itibhāvaḥ kintarhi atra uttara sambaddha vākyam iti āha tatra anvaya darśana hetau= idam syāt vācyam vyaktat nāma pravṛtti nivṛtti dharmakam na tathā vyakta vat sukha ādayaḥ pravṛtti nivṛtti dharmakāḥ iti liṅga vacana pariṇāmena sambandhaḥ 
VNṬ_133,1^5	 tathā ca vyaktasya sukha ādi anvaye asya vyākhyānam sukha ādi svabhāvatāyām satyām pravṛtti nivṛtti dharma tā lakṣaṇam vyaktasya avahīyate tat avyatirekeṇa teṣām api sadā avasthānāt iti tasmāt na tad rahita sukha ādi svabhāva tā vyaktasya tābhyām pravṛtti nivṛttibhyām rahitāḥ tathā uktāḥ te ca sukha ādayaḥ ca te svabhāvaḥ yasya tasya bhāvaḥ tad rahita sukha ādi svabhāva tā kasmāt iti āha vyakta lakṣaṇa virodhāt iti vyaktasya lakṣaṇam pravṛtti nivṛtti dharmaka tvam tasya tad viparītaḥ sukha ādibhiḥ paraspara parihāra sthiti lakṣaṇaḥ virodhaḥ tathā ca sādhanat na sadā avasthita rūpa sukha ādi svabhāvam idam te vyaktam prāpnoti tad viparīta dharma tvāt 
VNṬ_133,1^6	 kṣetrajña vat na ca sukha ādi vyaktayoḥ eka svabhāva tā paraspara viruddha dharma adhyāsita tvāt sattva rajaḥ tamasām iva caitanyānām iva vā evañca vyaktasya sukha ādi svabhāva tā yoge sukha ādi anvaya darśana siddhaḥ hetuḥ kasmāt idam sambaddham dūṣaṇam iti āha evam hi tasya sāṅkhyasya sādhana doṣa udbhāvanena hetu asiddha tā ācodanena eka prakṛti idam vyaktam iti ayam pakṣaḥ dūṣitaḥ bhavani sa punar naiyāyikaḥ sādhane doṣam asiddha tā ākhyam anupasaṃhṛtya apadarśya aprakṛta prakṛti vikāra lakṣaṇa paryanuyogena kathām pratānayati avimuñcam sva doṣa manyamāt kathā prasaṅgam paratra sāṅkhye tapasvini upakṣipati 
VNṬ_133,1^7	 paraḥ āha ayam eva asiddhatā ākhyaḥ doṣa ūnena prakāreṇa prakṛti vikāra lakṣaṇa paryanuyoga dvāreṇa asmābhiḥ api ucyate iti ācāryaḥ āha eṣa naimittikānāṃjyotiḥ jñāna vidām viṣayaḥ na ayam tvad uktasya vākyasya arthaḥ iti yāvat yatas na lokaḥ śabdaiḥ apratipāditam artham pratipattum samarthaḥ artha prakaraṇa ādibhiḥ vinā iti adhyāhāraḥ tasmāt saḥ eva ayam pratijñā virodha prastāve nirddiṣṭaḥ bhaṇḍālekhya nyāyotrā api apasiddhāntona kevalam tatra iti a api śabdaḥ yathā hi bhaṇḍāḥ prākṛtān vismāpayantaḥ śīghūmarddha candra ākārām alpīyasīm rekhām ālikhya bhaṇanti paśyata tāla mātreṇa hastī vilikhita usmābhiḥ iti tatra kecid manda matayaḥ tathā eva pratipadyante 
VNṬ_133,1^8	 kecid durvidagdha dhiyaḥ paryanuyuñjate nanu nosya karṇṇa pāda danta ādayaḥ pratīyante tat katham ayanta dvi kalaḥ hastī bhavati iti te pu nara āhuḥ satyam na pratīyante asmābhiḥ tu samāpta sakala kalaḥ kareṇuḥ ayam likhitaḥ tāḥ tasya sakalāḥ kalāḥ salile iva magna tvāt na upalabhyante kumbhaka deśa mātrantu idam asya upa labhyate iti tathā ajātīyakam etat parasya api dhārṣṭya vijṛmbhitam yadi nāma na ayam artha usmāt bāhyāt pratīyate tathā api anena prakāreṇa ucyate iti api ca ucyatām ayam eva artha ūnena prakāreṇa tathā api asiddhasya hetvābhāseṣu antarbhāvāt tat vacanena eva abhidhānam iti na apasiddhāntaḥ pathak upādeyaḥ bhavet iti etat upasaṃhāra vyājena āha yathā uktena nyāyene tyādi 
VNṬ_136,1^1	 hetvābhāsāḥ ca yathā uktāḥ iti sūtram idam ākṣepa pūrvakam vātsyāyanaḥ vyācaṣṭe kim punar iti hetvābhāsa lakṣaṇāt yat anyat lakṣaṇam tena sambandhāt nigraha sthāna tvam āpadyante kim iva iti āha yathā pramāṇāni prameyat tvam lakṣaṇa antara vasāt a āpadyante iti varttate tāni hipram iti kriyāyāḥ kāraṇa tvāt pramāṇāni pramāṇa antareṇa tu yadā pramīyante tadā karma tvāt prameyāni tatas eva padārtha tvāt prāptaḥ saṃśayaḥ atra āha muninā yathā uktaḥ iti asya eva vivaraṇam yathā ukta hetvābhāsa lakṣaṇena eva nigraha sthāna bhāvaḥ iti idam uktam bhavati 
VNṬ_136,1^2	 savyabhicāra viruddha prakaraṇa sama sādhya sama atīta kālāḥ iti hetvābhāsāḥ iti prabhedam upakramya yat pratyekam lakṣaṇam uktam anaikāntikaḥ savyabhicāraḥ siddhāntam abhyupetya tad virodhāt viruddham yasmāt prakaraṇa cintā sa nirṇṇaya artham apadiṣṭaḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ sādhya aviśiṣṭaḥ sādhya tvāt sādhya samaḥ kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ kāla atītaḥ iti tena eva lakṣaṇena eṣāt nigraha sthānattvam na punar tatas lakṣaṇa antaram apekṣyate iti atra apī tyācāryaḥ kathañcintyam iti āha kinte yathā bhavadbhiḥ lakṣita prabhedāḥ tathā eva te bhavanti āho svid anyathe ti 
VNṬ_136,1^3	 lakṣitaḥ prabhedaḥ yeṣām iti vigrahaḥ tat tarhi kintat cintyate iti āha tat tu cintyamānam iha ati prasajyate iti na pratanyate idam eva agūritam vidanti eva kecid atra hetvābhāsāḥ eva na yujyaṃte kecid tu hetvābhāsāḥ api na saṅgrahītā iti asmin= ca vicāre hetvābhāsa vārttikam sakalam avatārayitavyam iti śāstra antaram eva bhavet avadāta matayaḥ tu asmad vihita hetvābhāsa lakṣaṇa viparyayeṇa dūra antara tvāt tat vaisaśam tasmāt upekṣā eva yujyate iti tathā api mandam ati vibodhanāya api śāstram ucyate iti 
VNṬ_136,1^4	 kāla atīta prakaraṇa samayoḥ tāvat hetu ābhāsa tvam yathā na upapadyate tathā varṇyate tatra kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ kalā atītaḥ tat iha bṛddha naiyāyikānām apāsya matam ācārya diṅnāga pādaiḥ bhāṣita tvāt idāni intanā vātsyāyanā dayā umum eva sthipakṣam āhuḥ tatra evambrūmaḥ kāla atyayena yuktaḥ yasya artha eka deśaḥ apadiśyamānasya sa kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ kāla atītaḥ iti ucyate nidarśanam nityaḥ śabdaḥ saṃyoga vyaṃgya tvāt rūpa vat prāc ūdrdhvam ca vyakteḥ avasthitam rūpam pradīpa ghaṭa saṃyogena vyajyate tathā śabdaḥ vyavasthitaḥ bherī karṇṇa saṃyogena dāru parṇa yogena vā vyajyate 
VNṬ_136,1^5	 tasmāt saṃyoga vyaṃgya tvāt nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti ayam ahetuḥ kāla atyaya apadeśāt vyaṃjakasya saṃyogasya kālam na vyaṃgyasya rūpasya vyaktiḥ atyeti sati pradīpa saṃyoge rūpasya grahaṇam bhavati na nivṛtta saṃyogerūpaṅgṛhyate nivṛtte tu dāru parṇa saṃyoge dūra sthena śabdaḥ śrūyate vibhāga kāle na iyam śabdasya vyaktiḥ saṃyoga kālam atyeti iti saṃyoga nimittā bhavati kāraṇa abhāvāt hi kārya abhāvaḥ iti nanu ayam anaikāntikaḥ eva saṃyoga vyaṃgya tvāt iti anityam api saṃyogena vyajyamānam dṛṣṭam yathā ghaṭaḥ iti na saṃyoga vyaṃgya tvena avasthānasya sādhya tvāt na brūmaḥ nityaḥ śabdaḥ iti api tu avatiṣṭhate śabdaḥ iti ayam pratijñā arthaḥ tadā ca saṃyoga vyaṃgya tvāt iti ayam hetuḥ anaikāntikaḥ na hi anavasthitam kiñcid saṃyogena abhivyajyamānaḥ katham iti tadanena prakāreṇa saṃyoga vyaṅgya tvam eva śabdasya pratiṣiddhi ate iti na ayam asiddhāt vyāvartate anyathāneyam śabdasya vyaktiḥ saṃyogi kālam atyeti iti na saṃyoga nimittā abhavati iti vacanasya korthaḥ iti vaktavyam syāt buddhiḥ sarvadā dharmiṇya vidyamānasya asiddha tvam 
VNṬ_136,1^6	 ayantu na sarvathā dharmiṇī a siddhaḥ yena utpatti kāle saṃyoga vyaṅgya tvam asti natu upalabdhi kāle iti tat uktam eka deśa asiddhasya api asiddhattda parijñānāt yathā nityāḥ paramāṇavaḥ gandhava tvāt śvetanāḥ ca taravaḥ svāpāt iti yaḥ ca anityaḥ śabdaḥ iti pratijānīte sa kuṭhāra dāru saṃyoga ādeḥ śabdasya utpattim eva pratipadyate na punar avasthitasya abhivyaktam iti vyaktam asya anyatara asiddha tvam atha saṃyoge sati upalabdheḥ iti hetu artha abhyupagamāt na ayam asiddhaḥ hetuḥ iti samādhīyate 
VNṬ_136,1^7	 tathā api taila tejaḥ vartti saṃyoge kulāla mṛd piṇḍa daṇḍa saṃyoge ca sati dīpa ghaṭa ādayaḥ samupalabhyante na ca teṣa an tatra saṃyoga aprāpti avasthānam iti anena anaikāntikaḥ eva prāpnoti iti na kāla atītaḥ tad uttara kālam api avasthāne sādhyesamudāya antaravyaya vādinaḥ viruddhaḥ sa pakṣa abhāvāt eva tatra vṛtteḥ abhāvāt kṣaṇa sthiti dharmavati ca dharmiṇi rūpa ādike vidyamāna tvāt sthira bhāvavādinantu pratipratibandha vaikalyam sādhana vaiphalyañca anaṅgīkṛta siddhānte tu nyāya vādini prativādini pūrva pakṣa pratipāditaḥ doṣaḥ iti evam udāharaṇa anta repi dūṣaṇam utprekṣya vaktavyam iti 
VNṬ_137,1^1	 yasmāt prakaraṇa cintā sa nirṇṇaya artham apadiṣṭaḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ vimarśa adhiṣṭhānau pakṣa pratipakṣau= anavasitau prakaraṇantasya cintām avimarśāt prabhṛti prāk nirṇṇayāt parīkṣaṇam sā yatra kṛtā sa nirṇṇaya artham prayukta ubhaya pakṣa sāmyāt prakaraṇam anativarttamānaḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ na nirṇṇayāya kalpyate kasmāt punar prakaraṇa cintā tattva upalabdheḥ yasmāt upalabdhe tatverthe nivarttate cintā tasmāt sāmānyena adhigatasya yā viśeṣataḥ anupalabdhiḥ sā prakaraṇa cintām prayojayati iti udāharaṇam anityaḥ śabdaḥ nitya dharma anupalabdheḥ 
VNṬ_137,1^2	 anupalabhyamāna nitya dharmakam anityan dṛṣṭam sthālī ādi yatra samānaḥ dharmaḥ saṃśaya kāraṇa hetu tvena upādīyate saṃśaya samaḥ savyabhicāraḥ eva yā tu vimarśasya viśeṣa apekṣata ubhaya pakṣa viśeṣa anupalabdhau sā prakaraṇam pravartayati yathā ca śabde nitya dharmaḥ na upalabhyate tathā anitya dharma upi sā iyam ubhaya pakṣa viśeṣa anupalabdhiḥ prakaraṇa cintām prayojayati katham viparyaye prakaraṇa nivṛtteḥ yadi nitya dharmaḥ śabde gṛhyeta na syāt prakaraṇam yadi na nitya dharmaḥ gṛhyeta evam api nivarttate prakaraṇam 
VNṬ_137,1^3	 soyam hetuḥ ubhau pakṣau pravarttayan nānyatarasya nirṇṇayāya kalpyate iti na tu ayam sādhya aviśiṣṭaḥ eva na aviśiṣṭaḥ tasya eva prakaraṇa pravṛtti hetorddharmasya hetu tvena upādānāt yatrasādhyena samānaḥ dharmaḥ hetu tvena upādīyate sa sādhya aviśiṣṭaḥ yatra punar prakaraṇa pravṛtti hetuḥ eva sa prakaraṇa samaḥ iti atra api nitya anitya dharma anupalambhat va yāt eva prakaraṇa cintā na tu ekasmāt viparyaye prakaraṇa nivṛttiḥ iti vacanāt tat yadi nitya anitya dharma anupalabdheḥ iti hetuḥ syāt syāt prakaraṇa samaḥ 
VNṬ_137,1^4	 tad eka dharma anupalabdheḥ tu upādāne katham prakaraṇa samaḥ iti abhidhānīyam ubhaya dharma anupalambha upādānepi sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ anuvṛtti vyāvṛtyoraniścayāt asādharaṇa anaikāntikobhavati iti katham asya hetvābhāsa antara tvam bhavatu nāma eka dharma anupalabdhiḥ eva hetuḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ tathā api nitya śabda vādyavaśyam eva vyāmohāt nitya dharmān pratipadyatā eti prativādya siddhi iyam bhavati atha pramāṇena nitya dharmma pratikṣepāt nitya dharma anupalabdhiḥ pratipādyate tadā api niścāyaka tvāt samyak jñāna hetuḥ eva ayaṃ iti katham hetvābhāsaḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ 
VNṬ_137,1^5	 tadā hi viśeṣa upalabdhiḥ eva hetu arthaḥ vyavatiṣṭhate viśeṣāḥ ca nityasya kṛtaka tva ādayaḥ na ca tad kṛtā prakaraṇa cintā viparyaye prakaraṇa nivṛtteḥ iti vacanāt api ca nitya dharma anupalabdheḥ iti kim ayam prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ kim vā pratiyogi vidhānam yadi prasajya pratiṣedhaḥ tadā prameya tva ādi vat sādhāraṇānaikānti koyam nitya dharma upalabdhiḥ pratiṣedha mātrasya anitya tva rahiteṣu asatsu api sambhavāt atha pratiyogividhānanta dāpi anantara uditayā yuktyā hetu pratirūpa tva ayogaḥ anyaḥ tu anyathā idam sūtra dvayam vyācaṣṭe yaḥ hetuḥ hetu kāle apadiṣṭaḥ atyeti apaiti kasmāt apaiti pratyakṣeṇa āgamena ubhayena vāpīḍyamānaḥ sa kālam atītaḥ iti kāla atītaḥ iti ucyate kutas punar pratyakṣa āgama virodhaḥ labhyate iti ced catur lakṣaṇaḥ hetuḥ iti vacanāt tathā hi pūrvavat śeṣa vatsāmānyatas dṛṣṭaḥ ñca iti atra catū rūpaḥ hetuḥ iṣṭaḥ pūrvavat nāma sādhye vyāpakam śeṣavat iti tad samānā isti sāmānyatas ca dṛṣṭañca śabdāt aviruddhañcā iti tathā bhāṣya vacanam api asti yat punar anumānam pratyakṣa āgama viruddham nyāya ābhāsaḥ saḥ iti 
VNṬ_137,1^6	 tat evam trairūpye sati pratyakṣa āgamābhyām yaḥ vā adhyate sa kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ sa ca tridhā bhidyate pratyakṣa viruddhaḥ āgama viruddhaḥ ubhaya viruddhaḥ ca iti pratyakṣa viruddhaḥ yathā anuṣṇa ugniḥ dravya tvāt udaka vat āgama viruddhaḥ yathā brāhmaṇena surā pātavyāḥ drava tvāt kṣīra vat ubhaya viruddhaḥ yathā araśmivat cakṣuḥ indriya tvāt ghrāṇa ādi vat iti na ca ayam kila pakṣa virodhaḥ pakṣa virodhasya pratikṣepāt iti tat etat trairūpya lakṣaṇa anavavodha vaiśadyam trairūpyam hi yadāsvam pramāṇaiḥ pariniścitam pakṣa dharma tva ādikam trayam ca yatra bādhā tatra pratibandha usti bādhā vinā bhāvayoḥ viroghāt avinā abhāvaḥ hi sati eva sādhya dharme hetoḥ bhāvaḥ kathañcā asau tad lakṣaṇaḥ dharmiṇi hetuḥ syāt na ca atra sādhya dharmaḥ iti ādikam atra ābādhita viṣaya tva dūṣaṇa anusāreṇa vaktavyam yatra punar iyam bādha udāhṛtā nateṣām trailakṣaṇyam manāk api asti pratibandha vaikalyāt abhyupagata pakṣa prayogasya ca pakṣa doṣaḥ eva ayam yuktaḥ yat punar pakṣa doṣa tva parihārāya bahu asambaddham udgrāhitam tat atyantam asāram iti na iha avasīyate 
VNṬ_139,1^1	 yasmāt prakaraṇa cintā iti prakaraṇam bhāṣye nirūpitam tasya udāharaṇam aṇu raṇu antara kārya tvam pratipadyatenavā iti cintāya aṅkaḥ cid abhidhatte aṇu raṇu antara kāryaḥ rūpa ādima tvāt tad dvi aṇuka ādi vat iti yosāvaṇoḥ aṇuḥ kāraṇa tvena upādīyate tatra api rūpa ādim a tvam asti iti cintā kim iyam rūpa ādima tvāt aṇu antara kāryaḥ na vā iti cintā yāñca yadi tasya api aṇu antara kārya tvam rūpa ādima tvāt iti vakti tadā tasya api rūpa ādim a tvam asti iti punar api cintātadevam anavasthā rūpam prakaraṇam pravarttayati iti prakaraṇa samaḥ iti ucyate 
VNṬ_139,1^2	 atha aṇuraṇu antara kārya tvam na pratipadyate rūpa ādima tve sati tadā anaikāntikaḥ hetuḥ iti tasmāt bhidyate anaikāntikāt prakaraṇa samaḥ na ca ayam viruddhaḥ aviparyaya sādhaka tvāt na asiddhaḥ pakṣa dharma tva darśanāt na kāla atyaya apadiṣṭaḥ pratyakṣa āgamābhyām abādhyamāna tvāt atas artha antaram iti athavā pradeśe karaṇam prakaraṇañca iti kāraṇa siddhiḥ iti arthaḥ pradeśe siddhiḥ iti iyam cintā yasmāt hetoḥ apadiṣṭā bhavati sa prakaraṇa samaḥsa pradeśa sādhaka tvāt samaḥ yathā eka deśe asādhaka tvantathā itaratra api iti asādhaka tva sāmānyāt samaḥ tasmāt eka deśa varttī dharmaḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ 
VNṬ_139,1^3	 tat yathā pṛthivī ap tejaḥ vā yva ākāśāni a nityāni sattāva tvāt iti atra api yadyakṣa pāda mata anusārī tāvat evam pramāṇayati paramāṇuḥ paramāṇu antara pūrvvakaḥ rūpa ādima tvāt dvi aṇuka ādi vat iti tadā tasya abhyupeta virodhaḥ iti na ayam atīta kālāt bhidyate atha bauddhaḥ karoti tadā api hetoḥ asiddhiḥ paramāṇūnām rūpa ādi vyatirekeṇa anabhyupagamāt ayogāt cat vyadīnāñca abhāvāt ubhaya vikalaḥ dṛṣṭāntaḥ yadā api anapekṣita siddhāntaḥ nyāya vādī brūte tadā api dvitīya pakṣa udita doṣa anivṛttiḥ iti na ayam asiddhāt vyāvarttate yaḥ api anumeya eka deśa varttī dharmaḥ pṛthivī ādīni anityāni gandhava tvāt iti ayam api apasiddhānta antarbhūtaḥ eva iti na pṛthak vācyaḥ na asiddhaḥ pakṣa eka deśa dharma tvāt sa pakṣa eka deśa varttiva diti ced viṣamoyam upanyāsaḥ sa pakṣaḥ eva ca satvam iti atra hi samuccīyamāna avadhāraṇam eva na sakala sapakṣa dharma tām sādhanasya pratipādayati anumeye satva vacanam punar ayoga vyavacchedena niyantṛ bhūtam aśeṣa sādhya dharmi dharma tāyāḥ pratipādakam iti anena eva pakṣa eka deśa asiddha bhedānām apohaḥ kṛtaḥ iti apārthakam yatna antaram iti yat kiñcid etat 
VNṬ_140,1^1	 bhāvi viktaḥ pyatra eva khara rave patitaḥ prakaraṇa samam anyathā samarthayati yasmāt hetoḥ prakaraṇa cintā vipakṣasya api vicāraḥ paścāt bhavati sa evam lakṣaṇaḥ hetu nirṇayāya yā upadiśyamānaḥ prakaraṇa samaḥ bhavati prakaraṇe sādhye samaḥ tulyaḥ sattve asattve vā yathā sat sarvajña m itaratad viparīta vinirmukta tvāt rūpa ādi vat iti yasmāt ayam hetuḥ ubhayatra samānaḥ yopya satvam sādhayati tasya api samānaḥ katham asat sarvajña tvam itaratad viparīta vinirmukta tvāt khara viṣāṇa vat iti na ca ayam kila ubhaya dharma tvepi anaikāntikaḥ vipakṣa vṛttiḥ vaikalyāt tat idam ācāryeṇa svayam pramāṇa viniścaye pratiṣiddham 
VNṬ_140,1^2	 kampunar atra bhavān vipakṣam pratyeti sādhya abhāvam katham idānīm hetum vipakṣa vṛttiḥ ubhaya dharmeṇa eva ityādinā artha grahaṇa vyākhyāne ca yat uktam tat atra api vaktavyam viśeṣeṇa dūṣaṇañcā asya prapañcena uktam eva evam prakaraṇa sama atīta kālayoḥ anupapattiḥ sādhya vyabhicārasya tu yujyate hetvābhāsa tvaṃna tu yathā bhavatām abhyupagamaḥ tathā hi bhavantaḥ sandigdha vipakṣa vyāvṛttikasya anaikāntika tvam na pratipadyante adarśana mātreṇa eva vyatireka siddhi abhyupagamāt atas eva ca bhavadbhiḥ apa gata śaṅkaiḥ evam prayujyate prāpya kāriṇī cakṣuḥ śrotre bāhya indriya tvāt ghrāṇa ādi vat 
VNṬ_140,1^3	 sa vikalpam pratyakṣam pramāṇa tvāt anumāna vat ityādi na ca adarśana mātreṇa eva vinā pratibandhe na vyatireka siddhiḥ iti pratānitam anyatra ātma mṛd cetana ādīnām yaḥ bhāvasya aprasādhakaḥ saḥ eva anupalambhaḥ kim hetu abhāvasya sādhakaḥ ityādinā tathā sa pakṣa vipakṣayoḥ sandigdhaḥ sat asatvasya api samyak jñāna hetu tvam eva yuṣmābhiḥ iṣyate na anaikāntika tvam yathā sa ātmakam jīvat śarīramprāṇa ādimattvāt iti asya ca tad bhāvaḥ pratipāditaḥ pramāṇa viniścayāḥ dau viruddha prabhedaḥ tu bhāradvāja vihitaḥ pratijñā virodha prastāvaḥ eva nirākṛtaḥ 
VNṬ_140,1^4	 sādhya samepi yoyam anyathā siddhaḥ varṇyate yathā anityāḥ paramāṇavaḥ kriyāva tvāt ghaṭa ādi vat iti ayam api kila sādhya samaḥ yasmāt mūrti kriyā rūpa ādima tvāt aṇūnām kriyāva tvam na anitya tvāt iti sa na upapadyate dharmiṇi siddha tvāt na hi dharmiṇi vidyamānaḥ eva asiddhohetuḥ yujyate sarva hetūnām asiddha tā prasaṅgāt na etat evannahi pakṣeḥ ti iti etāvatā pakṣa dharma tvam sādhya vaśena hi dharmiṇaḥ pakṣa dharma tvam iṣyate kevalasya sādhya tvāt na ca sādhyaḥ dharmaḥ yadi dharmiṇi tena sādhanena vinā na sambhavati tasya ca sādhanasya sādhya dharma abhāve dharmiṇā sambhavaḥ tatas hetoḥ pakṣa dharma tvam 
VNṬ_140,1^5	 yadā punar anyathā api sādhanāya upātte dharmiṇi dharmaḥ upapadyate tadā hetuttvam evañca viśiṣṭam eva satvam pakṣa dharma tvena vivakṣitam anyathā siddha tvam yuktam eva sādhya samam tat idam atra pratividhān aṃyadi khalu sādhya dharma abhāve dharmiṇi asambhavaḥ hetoḥ evam vidhamā iva satvam pakṣa dharma tvena vivakṣitam na tu bhāva mātram tadā kintadittthaṃbhūtam pakṣa dharma tvam avijñātam eva anumeya prakāśakam āhosvit pariniścitam eva iti prakāra dvaye yadi avijñātam prakāśakam tat ājñāpaka hetu nyāyam ativarttate jñāpakaḥ hi hetuḥ sva ātmani jñāna apekṣaḥ jñāpyam artham prakāśayati 
VNṬ_140,1^6	 sattā mātreṇa ca hetavaḥ vipratipatti nirākāraṇa paṭavaḥ santi iti prativādinām paraspara parāhatam pravacana nānā tvam na bhavet vijñātasya api gamaka tve pramāṇāt vā tasya pariniścayaḥ pramāṇāt vā na tāvat apramāṇasya bhūta artha niścaya hetu tva abhāvāt apramāṇāt gatiḥ anyathā prāmāṇyam eva avahīyate yasmāt idam eva pramāṇasya pramāṇa tvam yat yatha avasthita vastu prakāśaka tvam tat ca idam apramāṇasya api asti tadā katham tada pramāṇāt sādhye dharmiṇi vinā sādhya dharmeṇa asat bhūṣṇoḥ hetoḥ sattvam pakṣa dharma tvena adhigamyatetadā api yatas eva pramāṇāt hetoḥ siddhiḥ tatas eva sādhya dharmasya api iyam jāyate iti kim artha m ayam akiñcitkaraḥ hetu rūpa ādīyate 
VNṬ_140,1^7	 na ca hetoḥ eva kevalasya tatas siddhiḥ sādhya dharmasya tu na iti yuktam vaktum hetoḥ api tatas asiddhi prasaṅgāt tathā hi evam ayam hetuḥ tatra dharmiṇi sidhyati yadi anena sādhya dharmeṇa vinā iha na upapadyate saha eva tu upapadyate iti sidhyet tathā ca kathantataḥ eva pramāṇāt sādhya dharmasya api na siddhiḥ san jātā iti cintanīyam etat evañca tena eva pramāṇena saha asya sādhya dharmasya gamya gamaka bhāvaḥ na tu anena hetunā iti mahat aniṣṭam āpadyate evamvidha pakṣa dharma tva samāśrayaṇe ca yāvat sādhyasya asiddhiḥ tāvat hetoḥ api yāvat ca hetoḥ asiddhiḥ tāvat sādhyasya api iti paraspara āśraya prasaṅgaḥ 
VNṬ_140,1^8–142,1	 pakṣa dharma tva niścaya velā yāñca sādhya dharma siddhiḥ sampadyate iti vyartham uttara liṅga rūpa anusaraṇam ittthañca na dvi lakṣaṇaḥ catur lakṣaṇaḥ pañca lakṣaṇaḥ ca hetuḥ vaktavyaḥ asmad mate tu dharmiṇi satva mātram vijñāya ca tad uttara kālam anvaya vyatirekayoḥ vijñānam anvaya vyatirekau vā sarvvā upasaṃhāreṇa vijñāyate uttara kālam dharmiṇi satva mātram vijñātam atas ca ānantaryeṇa eva tad sāmarthyāt sādhya dharmasya tatra pratītiḥ upapadyate tena idam atra sakalam doṣa jālam nabhasi iva amale jale na avasthāna m alam labhate iti alam apratiṣṭhita mithyā pralāpaiḥ iti viramyate yadi evam kim punar atra iṣṭam iṣṭam iti āha hetvābhāsāḥ tu yathānyāyam ityādiye nyāyāḥ hetvābhāsāḥ tad uktiḥ nnigraha sthānam bhavati te ca yesmābhiḥ uktāḥ eka aprasiddhi saṃdehe aprasiddha vyabhicāra bhāj dvayoḥ vviruddhosiddhau ca saṃdeha vyabhicāra bhāgi ti 
VNṬ_142,2^1	 nanu ca ayam vāda nyāya mārgaḥ sakala lokā nibandhana bandhunā vāda vidhānāt au= āryavasubandhunā mahā rāja pathīkṛtaḥ kṣuṇṇaḥ ca tadanu mahatyām nyāya parīkṣā yām kumati mata matta mātaṅga śiraḥ pīṭha pāṭana paṭubhiḥ ācārya dignāga pādaiḥ tat kim idam punar carvvita carvvaṇam āsthitam tvayā iti etat codya parihāra param imam ślokam upanyasyatipanyasyate lokaḥ ityādi timirañca paṭalañcā iti timira paṭalam avidyā eva timira paṭalam avidyā timira paṭalam bhūta artha darśana vibandhaka tvāt tasya ullekhanaḥ vāda nyāya iti sambandhaḥ ullekhana śabdaḥ kartṛ sādhanaḥ kasya punar avidyā timira paṭalam iti āha tattva dṛṣṭeḥ tatva darśanasya prajñā locanasya iti arthaḥ yaḥ eṣa samanantaram āveditaḥ vāda nyāyaḥ 
VNṬ_142,2^2	 sat bhiḥ pūrva ācāryaiḥ para hita rataiḥ karuṇā pāratantryāt lokān samyak varttmani vyavasthāpayitum praṇītaḥ parām prasiddhim nītaḥ loke suṣṭu sphuṭīkṛtaḥ iti arthaḥ na tu para sparddhayā na api yaśaḥ kāma tā ādibhiḥ yadi evantarhi tad avasthitam ca udyam iti atas āha tatvasya ālokam udyotamvāda nyāyamācā ācāryairūpa diṣṭam timirayati andhakārīkaroti kudūṣaṇa tamasā pracchādayati iti yāvat kaḥ punar asau= ati sāhasikaḥ yaḥ mahā nāgaiḥ kṣuṇṇam panthānam roddhum īhate iti āha duḥ vidagdhaḥ samyak viveka rahita tayā janoya mudyota kara prīti candra bhāvi vikta prabhṛtiḥ yatas ca evam tasmāt yatnaḥ kṛtaḥ iha vādanyāya prakaraṇe mayā tasya mahadbhiḥ udbhāvitasya anta rājataiḥ avadhūtasya samujvālanāya kudūṣaṇa parihāreṇa tat ni iti udyotanena mama vyāpṛta tvāt na mayā piṣṭam piṣṭam iti saṃkṣepa arthaḥ 
VNṬ_143,1–143,3	 anargha vanitā avagāhanam analpadhī śakti nā api adṛṣṭa parama artha sāram adhika abhiyogaiḥ api matam matitamaḥ sphuṭam prativibhajya samyak mayā ayat āptam akṛśam śubham bhavatu tena śāntaḥ janaḥ ahañca nairātmya bodha paripāṭita doṣa śaila sambuddha bhāra vahana kṣama bhūri śaktamañju śriyaḥ śriyam avāpya samasta sattva sarva āvṛti kṣaya vidhāna paṭuḥ bhaveyam mahārayena eva na kiñcid atra tyaktam viviktam na vibhajyam eva tathā api manda pratibodhana artham ālokaḥ eṣa jvalitaḥ pradīpaḥ 
VNṬ_143,4–143,9	 loke avidyā timira paṭala ullekhanaḥ tattva dṛṣṭe vāda nyāyaḥ para hita rataiḥ eṣa samyak praṇītaḥ tattva ālokam timirayati tam durviṃdagdhaḥ janoyantasmāt yatnaḥ kṛtaḥ iha mayā tad samujvālanāya iti vipañcitā arthā nāma vādanyāyaṭīkā samāptāḥ kṛtiḥ iyaṃśa anta ra kṣita pādānām iti samvataḥ ācū śrāvaṇa kṛṣṇaḥ ekādaśyāṃlikhitam mayā rāja adhirāja parameśvara parama bhaṭṭārakaḥ śrīmat ānanda deva pādīya vijaya rājye śubha dine granthasya asya pramāṇañca nipuṇaiḥ nnavaśatā adhikam sahasra dvitayam samyaksaṃkhyā tampūrvvasūribhiḥ śubham astu sarvu ajagatām i sarvaiḥ rakṣitavyam prayatnataḥ iti namaḥ sarvajñāya
